Amu kigonde eunekwak che chang’ kotet ng’alek agobo tuguchoto kigosulda eng’ kwenunnyo , 
ko u ye kigogonech , che ki baorinik che kigeer koboch taunet , ak che ki kiboitinik che bo ng’olyot , 
kiageer agane ale, mie atetun eng’ siret, ko kaanai agane ole kibiitunda tuguk tugul koboch taunet, ee, inye, ne i toogunot Teopilo; 
si kobiit inai eng’ iman , ng’alechato kiginetin .
Kimi eng’ betusiek che bo Herod , laitoriatab Judea , tisiindet age ne kigiguure Sakaria , ne bo ripsetab Abija : ak kitinyei osotiot ne kisalu gab Aron , ak kigiguure kainennyi Elisabet . 
Ak ki bo iman ichek tuwai eng’ taitab Jehovah , ak kibendate ng’atutik tugul ak karureiywek che bo Kiptaiyat , ama tinyei lelut . 
Ak kima kotinyei lakwa , amu ki son Elisabet , ak kiga koosegitu tuwai .
Ak ye kita koyaei boisietab tiseinatet eng’ taitab Jehovah , ko u tetetab ripsennyi , 
ko u biteetab boisietab tiseinatet , ko kigilewen inendet kwo hekalutab Kiptaiyat kobeel nyamdutik . 
Ak kimi sang’ tuiyet komugul ne bo bik , kosaei eng’ sait ne kibeele nyamdutik . 
Ak kimong’ji malakaiyatab Kiptaiyat kotonone komostab tai ne bo kapkorosut ne kibeele nyamdutik . 
Ak kingogeer Sakaria inendet koarogen ak koiyweis . 
Ago kilenji malaikaiyat inendet , Ameiyweisie , Sakaria : amu kogegasun someng’ung’ , ak ta kosigun osotiondeng’ung’ Elisabet werit , ak iguure kainennyi Johana . 
Ak inyoru boiboiyet ak kagasetab ge ; ak boiboitu bik che chang’ eng’ sigennyi . 
Amu tun egu ne o eng’ taitab Kiptaiyat , ama eei divaik anan maiyek ; ago kinyiiti Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , koboch komi moetab kamet . 
Ak koweekyi lagokab Israel che chang’ Kiptaiyat Jehovah nenywa . 
Ak kowendot eng’ taitab togennyi eng’ tamirmiriet ak kimnatetab Elija , si koweech mugulelwek che bo kwanisiek kotokyigei lagok , ak kowelel ngelelik si kobendat eng’ ng’omnatetab che bo iman ; si kochopchi Kiptaiyat bik che chobotin .
Ak kilenji Sakaria malaikaiyat, Anae nee ng’olyondonito? Amu koaositu , ak kigotar kenyisiek che chang’ osotiondennyu . 
Ak kiwolji malaikaiyat kolenji , A Gabriel , ne atononi eng’ taitab Jehovah ; kagiyokwa ang’alalun , ak aibun logoiywechu miachen . 
Ak keero , namoksein kut , amemuchi ing’alal , agoi tun betut ne biitu ng’alechu , amu ma iyan ng’alekyuk , che tun isuldoi eng’ betusiekwak .
Ak kiigen bik Sakaria , kot kokwong’io , amu kiigagei eng’ hekalut . 
Ak ye kingomong’ sang’ , koma komuch kong’alalji ichek , ak kinai ichek kole , kagogeer kaborunet ne bo kwong’et eng’ hekalut : ak king’alaljine bichoto eut , ak kiteb ko namat kut .
Ak ye kingogesgei betusiekab otisiennyi , kwo ga . 
Ak ye kingogesgei betusiechoto komanach osotiondennyi Elisabet ; ak kiunygei arawek mut , ak komwa kole , 
Koyaiywa ko u nito Kiptaiyat eng’ betusiek che kiibwata , si koistoena reng’sennyu eng’ bik .
Kiiyokto Jehovah malaikaiyat Gabriel eng’ arawetab lo kwo nganaset ne bo Galili , ne kiguure Nasaret , 
kwo oldab chepto bergeiyat ne kiga kechamji murenet age ne kiguure Josep , ne bo gotab Daudi ; ak kigiguure bergeiyandanato Maria . 
Ak kinyo ole mi cheboto , ak kolenji , Chamge , inye ne i chamat mising’ , mi Kiptaiyat koboten .
Ago kiimgei mising’ inendet eng’ mwaonato, ak kiibwat kole, egu nee kagatonikab ngalechu ? 
Ak kilenji malaikaiyat inendet , Ameiywei , Maria : amu kainyoru chamet eng’ Jehovah . 
Ak keero , imanachi , ak isich werit , ak tun iguure kainennyi JESU . 
Egu ne o inendet , ak tun kiguure Weritab Inendet ne Toror Mising’ : ak kigochin Kiptaiyat Jehovah ng’echeretab laitornatet ne bo kwandanyi Daudi : 
ak tun laitorane gotab Jakobo koigeny ; ama tinyei ole igesunegei bounatennyi .
Ak kilenji Maria malaikaiyat , Egundoi ano ng’olyondoni , amu mangen muren ? 
Ak kiwolji malaikaiyat kolenji , Nyonjinin Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ak kouurin kamuktaetab Inendet ne Toror Mising’ : noto anyun kiguure ne tilil , Weritab Jehovah , inendet ne tun kisichei . 
Ak keero , managat agine Elisabet tupcheng’ung’ , tun sichei werit eng’ osindanyi : ne bo lo arawani eng’ inendet ne kigiguure son . 
Amu mami ng’olyo ne bunu Jehovah ne ma kim . 
Ak kile Maria , Keero , a chepto ne otwogindetab Kiptaiyat ; ingeyaiywa ko u ng’olyondeng’ung’ . Ak kiwa malaikaiyat kobagakta inendet .
King’eet anyun Maria eng’ betusiechoto kwo kochakta emetab tulonok , agoi nganasetab Juda ; 
ak kiwa agoi gotab Sakaria ak kogat Elisabet . 
Ak ye kingogas Elisabet kagatetab Maria , koureren lakwet eng’ moennyi ; kinyi anyun Tamirmiriet ne Tilil Elisabet ; 
ak komwa eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Iberurot inye eng’ kobogorisiek , ak iberurot inendet ne isiche . 
Ak katepto ano kot anyoru nito , kot konyonja kametab Kiptaiyandennyu ? 
Amu , keero , ye kangoit itikyuk kutitab kagateng’ung’ , koureren lakwet eng’ moennyu eng’ boiboiyet . 
Ak baibai kobogoriondonoto iyani ; amu tun isuldoi tuguk che kigemwachi inendet che bunu Kiptaiyat .
Ak kile Maria , Itorori sobondanyu Kiptaiyat ,
Ak kagobaibait tamirmiriennyu eng’ Jehovah Yetindennyu .
Amu kagogeer nyerotietab otwogindennyi ne chepto : Amu , ogeero , koboch ra koguurena ibinwek tugul ne baibai .
Amu kagoyaiywa inendet ne bo kamuktaet tuguk che eechen ; Ak tilil kainennyi .
Tebyei rirenennyi eng’ ibinwek agoi ibinwek Eng’ icheget che konyiti inendet .
Kigobor kimnatet eng’ eunnyi ; Ak kigoiyesta che menotik eng’ kabwatutikab mugulelwekwak .
Kagochoor bounik eng’ ng’echerokwak , Ak kagoeet che nyerotin .
Kagobae che amei rubet tuguk che miachen : Ak kagoon magorek koba buch .
Kagotoret otwogindennyi Israel , Si kobwat rirenetab ge ,
Ko u ye king’alalji kwanisiekyok , Eng’ Abraham ak iyotennyi agoi koigeny .
Ak kitebi Maria koboto Elisabet ne negit arawek somok ; yeityo koweek kwo ga .
Kiit anyun betut ne sigisie Elisabet ; kosich werit . 
Ak kogas bikab kokwennyi ak bikab orennyi kole kagotesyi Kiptaiyat rirenennyi kwonyoto ; ak kiboiboitu koboto inendet .
Ak kingoit betut ne bo sisiit , kobwa ichek koyatita lakwet ; kimachei koguure Sakaria , kemwaitae kainetab kwandanyi . 
Ak kiwol kamet kole , Achicha ; kiguure Johana . 
Ak kilenji ichek inendet , Mami chi eng’ oreng’wong’ ne keguure kainanato . 
King’alaljine ichek eut kwanitab lakwet , koteebe kainet ne machei ketochi . 
Kosom kit ne kisirei , ak kisir , kole , Johana kainennyi . Ak kikwong’io tugul . 
Koyatak anyun kutinnyi ngunoto , ak kotiagak ng’elyeptanyi , ak kitwek kolos Jehovah . 
Ak kinyonji kaiyweisiet tugul che kimenyei komoswekwak ; ak kigimwaita ng’alechuto tugul koyom emetab tulonok ne bo Judea . 
Ak kigonore mugulelwekwak ng’alechato ichek tugul che kigas , kole , Tun egu nee anyun lakwani ? Amu kimi koboto inendet eutab Kiptaiyat .
Kinyi anyun Tamirmiriet ne Tilil kwandanyi Sakaria , ak kimaoten , kole ,
Iberurot Kiptaiyat , Jehovah ne bo Israel ; Amu kagorutochi bikyik ak koyachi katiaget ichek ,
Kagong’eetwech kuinetab yetunet Eng’ gotab Daudi kiboitiondennyi
(Ko u ye kimwa eng’ kutuswekab maotikyik che tililen che kimi koboch ko kagitoi ng’ony) ,
Si kosoruech eng’ bunikyok , ak eng’ eunekab tugul che wechech ;
Si korire kwanisiekyok , Ak kobwat kayomisennyi ne tilil ;
Kayosiet ne kiiyosiechi kwandanyo Abraham ,
Si kobiit kogonech , ko kagosoruech eng’ eunekab bunikyok , Keboisiechi inendet ama eng’ kaiyweisiet ,
Eng’ tililindo ak eng’ imanda eng’ tainnyi eng’ betusiekyok tugul.
Ee lakwani , kiguurenen maotiotab Inendet ne Toror Mising’ : Amu iwendi eng’ taitab Kiptaiyet indoi , si kobiit ichob ortinwekyik ;
Si igochi bikyik naet ne bo yetunet Eng’ nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogikwak ,
Amu muguleldo ne riregei ne bo Jehovah nenyo , Si kochorjech lapkeiyet ne bunu barak ,
Si koluuchi icheget che tebyei eng’ mesundeito ak che mi uruetab meet ; Si kondochi kelyekyok kot koit oretab kalyet .
Ak kiner lakwanato , ak kotesak kimnatet eng’ tamirmiriet , ak kimeng’oti surkwen agoi betut ne kiiborjigei Israel .
Kibun anyun ng’atutiet Kaisari Agusto eng’ betusiechoto , kole , kesir kainaikab bik tugul . 
Ne bo tai sirisioni ye ki bounindetab Suria , Kurenio . 
Kiba anyun tugul si kesir , chi tugul eng’ nganasennyi .
Kitogos agine Josep eng’ Galili , kobunu nganasetab Nasaret , agoi Judea , kot koit nganasetab Daudi , ne kiguure Betlehem , amu ki bo inendet gotab Daudi , ak ki bo orennyi ; 
si kobiit kesir inendet koboto murerennyi Maria , ne ki chio . 
Ak kiit sigetab lakwet , kota komi oloto . 
Ak kisich werinnyi ne bo tai ; ak kolaakyi ngoroikab lakwandit , ak komogonji kaptugut , amu kima komi boroindo eng’ gotab toek .
Ak kimi emonoto mestowek che kitebyei eng’ kewet koribei akwenywa ne bo kechirek kemoi . 
Ak kitonon malaikaiyatab Kiptaiyat eng’ ole negite ichek , ak kiiluuchi lilindab Kiptaiyat komoswekwak tugul : koiyweis anyun mising’ . 
Ak kilenji malaikaiyat ichek , Amoiyweisie ; ogeero , aibwok logoiywek che miach che bo boiboiyet ne o ne ityin bik tugul : 
amu kagisikwok Yetindet rani , eng’ nganaset ne bo Daudi , noto Kristo Kiptaiyat . 
Ak nit kaborunet eng’ okwek : Onyoru lakwet ko kagilaakyi ngoroikab lakwandit , korue moinget ne amisie tuga .
Ak kimi eng’ sainato koboto malaikaiyandanato chang’indab lugosiekab kipsengwet che kiilosu Jehovah kolen ,
Bo teegisto Jehovah , eng’ ole toror mising’ , Ak kalyet eng’ ng’ony eng’ bik che chamotin eng’ inendet .
Ak kingo kagoweek malaikaisiek koba kipsengwet , kolenjigei mestowechoto , Ongebe nguno agoi Betlehem , si kobiit kegeer ng’olyondonito kagoyaak , ne kagoboruech Kiptaiyat .
Ak kibwa anyun kochok , ak kinyor Maria ak Josep , ak lakwet korue moinget ne amisie tuga . 
Ak ye kingogeer kobarta mwaet ne kaga kemwachi agobo lakwanato . 
Ak kikwong’io tugul che kigas ng’alechato kimwachi mestowek . 
Ago kirib Maria ng’alechato tugul , kobwatoti eng’ muguleldanyi . 
Ak kiweek anyun mestowek , kotorori Jehovah ak kolosunoti eng’ tuguk tugul che kagogas ak che kagogeer , ko u ye kaga kemwachi .
Ak kingoit betusiek sisiit che kiyatitoe inendet , keguure kainennyi JESU , ko u ye kiga kotochi malaikaiyat kotomo kemanach .
Ak kingo kagobata betusiekab katililenywa ko u Ng’atutietab Musa , komut inendet konyo Jerusalem , si kogochi Kiptaiyat 
(ko u ye kigisir eng’ Ng’atutietab Kiptaiyat , kele , Kiguure ne itabanat agobo Kiptaiyat werit age tugul ne yatei iyotet) , 
ak kogoito korosiot ko u ye kigimwa eng’ Ng’atutietab Kiptaiyat , kele , Cheptugenik aeng’ , anan arek aeng’ che bo cheptugenik .
Ogeero , kimi chito age Jerusalem , ne kigiguure Simeon ; ak ki chito ne bo iman ak kigonyiti Jehovah , ne kiigeni kagaigaetab Israel : ak kitebe Tamirmiriet ne Tilil inendet . 
Ak kiga kong’ang’ji inendet Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , kole , mageerei meet , kotom kogeer Kristo ne bo Kiptaiyat . 
Kinyo anyun hekalut eng’ Tamirmiriet : ak ye kingomut sigik lakwet Jesu , si kobiit koyachi inendet ko u biteetab Ng’atutiet , 
konam anyun lakwet eng’ eunekyik , ak kolos Jehovah , kole ,
Ee , Kiptaiyat , ichamjini nguno otwogindeng’ung’ kwo Eng’ kalyet , ko u ng’olyondeng’ung’ ;
Amu kagogeer konyekyuk yetuneng’ung’ ,
Ne kiichob eng’ taitab bik tugul ;
Lapkeiyet ne bo ng’ang’utiet ne king’ang’jin Bororiosiek , Ak torornatetab biguk Israel .
Ak kikwong’io Josep ak kametab lakwet agobo tuguchoto kagimwa agobo inendet ; 
ak kiiberur Simeon ichek, ak kolenji Maria kamennyi , Keero , kaginde lakwani si kobutyo che chang’ ak kong’eetyo che chang’ eng’ Israel ; asi koek kaborunet ne tun kiesioi ; 
(ee agot inyendet ko tun torei rotwetab chok muguleldang’ung’ ;) si kobiit kong’ang’ogis kabwatutikab mugulelwekab bik che chang’ .
Ak kimitei agine Ana , chebo Panuel , ne ki maotio , ne bo oretab Aser (ne kiga koosit mising’ ; kitebi ak manong’otiot kenyisiek tisab koboch ngitun . 
Ak kitebi ko mosok kenyisiek tamanwogik sisiit ak ang’wan) , ko mamandoi eng’ hekalut , ak kolosu , koboto karugutetab ge , ak somutik , kemoi ak bet . 
Ak kinyo eng’ sainato ak kogochi Jehovah kongoi , ak king’alalji tugul che kiigeni katiaget eng’ Jerusalem agobo inendet .
Ak kingo kagoges tugul ko u Ng’atutietab Kiptaiyat , koweektagei koba Galili , agoi nganasenywa Nasaret . 
Ak kiner lakwet , ak kotesak kimnatet , ak kinyi ng’omnatet : ak kimi mieindab Jehovah koboto inendet .
Kicham kobendi sigikyik kenyit age tugul Jerusalem eng’ igorta ne bo paska . 
Ak ye ki bo kenyisiek taman ak aeng’ , kotogosta ichek koba Jerusalem ko u biteet ne bo igorta ; 
ak ye kingowong’ betusiek , ye kiweeksei , kong’et lakwet Jesu eng’ Jerusalem : ak kima nai sigikyik ; 
ago kilen mi koboto bik che kibendi tugul , koba anyun bandab betut komugul ; ak kicheng’ inendet eng’ kwenutab bikab orenywa ak che kiingengei : 
ak ye kimanyor inendet , koweektagei Jerusalem , kocheng’at .
Ak ye kingogesgei betusiek somogu , konyorji inendet hekalut , kotebyei eng’ kwenutab konetik , koepchin it ng’alekwak , ak koteepse icheget : 
ak kikwong’io ichek tugul che kiepchin it inendet amu naennyi ak wolunaikyik . 
Ak ye kingogeer inendet , kokwong’io : ak kilenji kamennyi inendet , Lakwani , kalya si iyaiywech ko u ni ? Keero , kogicheng’in ane ak kwandang’ung’ eng’ arogenet . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Amu nee si ocheng’a ? Ma onai ole kanyolja atebe boisietab Baba ? 
Kima iguiyo ichek ng’olyondonoto kamwachi .
Kichorgei anyun koboto icheget , ak kiit Nasaret ; ak kigase it ichek : ak kigonor kamet ng’alechato tugul eng’ muguleldanyi . 
Kitesak ng’omnatetab Jesu , ak etunatet , ak mieindo eng’ Jehovah ak eng’ bik .
Ak eng’ kenyit ne bo taman ak mut ne bo laitornatetab Tiberio Kaisari , ye ki bounindet ne bo Judea Pontio Pilato , ak Herod ko ki kiruogindet ne bo Galili , ak ki kiruogindetab Iturea ak Trakoniti Pilipu ng’etab kametab Herod , ak ki Lusania kiruogindet ne bo Abilene , 
eng’ betusiek che bo tiseinatet ne o ne bo Anas ak Kaiapa , koityi anyun ng’olyotab Jehovah Johana weritab Sakaria eng’ surkwen . 
Ak kinyo komoswek tugul che bo tabanwekab Jordan , koamdooti kabatisanetab sigunet agobo nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogik ; 
ko u ye kigisir eng’ bukuitab ng’alekab maotiot Isaia , kele , Kutitab chi ne ititeni eng’ surkwen kolen , Ochob oretab Kiptaiyat , Olititoti ole bunoti .
Tun kilong’u atebwet age tugul , Ak tun kiribribi tulwet age tugul ne o ak ne ming’in : Ak tun kilititi che kunuren , Ak kichaboi ortinwek che sing’ortot :
Ak tun keerei bik tugul yetunetab Jehovah.
Kimwachi anyun tuiyosiek che kibendi ole mi inendet , si kobatisan , kolenji , Ee okwek lagokab erenokab ng’wonet , ng’o ne kagoteeiywok omweune nereknatet ne tun nyonei ? 
Oii anyun logoek che nyoljin sigunet , amotau omwa eng’ mugulelwekwok ole , Kitinye kwandanyo Abraham : amu amwawok ale , eng’ koichu komuchi Jehovah kong’eetyi Abraham lagok . 
Agot nguno ko kaginde aiywet tigitikab ketik : noto anyun , ketit age tugul ne maiyei logoek che miach , keebei , ak kewirji ma .
Ak kiteebe inendet tuiyosiek kole , Kiyai nee anyun ? 
Ak kiwolji ichek kolenji , Inendet ne tinyei sumotik aeng’ , kogochi ne matinyei ; ak ingoyai ko u noto agine ne tinyei amitwogik . 
Ak kibwa agichek taagikab aisurut si kibatisan , ak kolenji inendet , Konetindoni , kiyai nee ? 
Ak kimwachi ichek kolenji , Amomage bik tuguk che siirei che kiging’at . 
Ak kiteebe askarik agichek kolenji , Kiyai nee anyun achek ? Ak kilenji , Amomu chi age tugul , anan orebe chi kiy ; ago ingoyamak melekwekwok .
Ak kingota kogeni bik kit ne biitu , ak kogereri met eng’ mugulelwekwak bik tugul agobo Johana , kolen ngo tos Kristo inendet ; 
kowolji Johana ichek tugul kolenji , Abatisanok eng’ beek iman ; ago nyonei inendet ne kim kosiira , ne manyoljina atiach anokab kweonikyik : ibatisanok inendet eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ak mat : 
tinyei keibet eng’ eunnyi , ak kotilili komie ruanyut , ak koyumji nganok chogennyi ; ago beelei metetek eng’ mat ne ma misoksei .
Kiamji anyun bik logoiywek che miach koboto kotigonutik alak che chang’ . 
Ago ye kingo kagoger kong’ Johana kiruogindet Herod agobo Herodia , osotiotab ng’etab kam , ak agobo tuguk tugul che yaachen che kiga koyai Herod , 
kotesyi nito anyun chun tugul , noto ko kiger Johana eng’ korgoret .
Ak ye kingo kagibatisan bik tugul , ak ko kagibatisan Jesu agine , ak ye kisaei , koyatak kipsengwet , 
ak kochorjigei inendet Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , eng’ kergeindab cheptuget , ak komong’une kutit kipsengwet kole , Inyendet ko i Werinnyu , chamanennyu ; abaibai mising’ eng’ inye .
Ak kingotau Jesu konetisiei , ko ki negit kenyisiek sosom , (kolen ichek abere) weritab Josep , weritab Heli , 
weritab Matat , weritab Lawi , weritab Melki , weritab Janai , weritab Josep , 
weritab Matatia , weritab Amos , weritab Nahum , weritab Esli , weritab Nagai , 
weritab Maat , weritab Matatia , weritab Semein , weritab Josek , weritab Joda , 
weritab Joanan , weritab Resa , weritab Serubabel , weritab Sealtiel , weritab Neri , 
weritab Melki , weritab Adi , weritab Kosam , weritab Elmadam , weritab Er , 
weritab Jose , weritab Elieser , weritab Jorim , weritab Matat , weritab Lawi , 
weritab Simeon , weritab Juda , weritab Josep , weritab Jonam , weritab Eliakim ,  
weritab Melea , weritab Mena , weritab Matata , weritab Natan , weritab Daudi , 
weritab Jesii , weritab Obed , weritab Boas , weritab Salmon , weritab Nason , 
weritab Aminadab , weritab Armi , weritab Hesron , weritab Peres , weritab Juda , 
weritab Jakobo , weritab Isak , weritab Abraham , weritab Tera , weritab Nahor , 
weritab Serug , weritab Reu , weritab Peleg , weritab Eber , weritab Sela , 
weritab Kainan , weritab Arpaksad , weritab Sem , weritab Noa , weritab Lamek , 
weritab Metusela , weritab Enok , weritab Jared , weritab Maalaleel , weritab Kainan , 
weritab Enos , weritab Set , weritab Adam , weritab Jehovah .
Ak kiweek Jesu kobunu Jordan ko nyiitat Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak kiimut Tamirmiriet kwo surkwen 
ak kotebi betusiek artam koyomei oindet . Ak ma am kiy eng’ betusiechoto : ak ye kingogesgei betusiechoto , koam rubet . 
Ak kilenji oindet , Ngo i Weritab Jehovah , ing’at koi koek makatiat . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu inendet kolenji , Kigisir kele , Masobei chi eng’ makatiat inegei .
Ak kiimut anyun oindet kotogosta , kwo koborji bororiosiek tugul che bo ng’ony eng’ sainato . 
Ak kilenji anyun oindet inendet , Agonin kimnatoni tugul , ak telunatenywa tugul ; amu kigigona ; ak agochini age tugul ne amakyini . 
Ngot iloswa anyun , eng’ tainnyu , kobunjinin tugul . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Kigisir kele , Ilosu Kiptaiyat Jehovah neng’ung’ , ak iboisiechi inendet inegei .
Kiimut anyun inendet Jerusalem , kwo kotonone kimonjogutab hekalut , ak kolenji , Ngo i Weritab Jehovah , iwirjige ng’ony eng’ yu : 
amu kigisir kele , Iyogu malaikaisiekyik agobo inye , si koribin :
ak Kotaachin eng’ eunekwak , Si marus koita keldang’ung’ .
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Kigimwa kele , Meyom Kiptaiyat Jehovah neng’ung’ . 
Ak ye kingoges oindet yomset age tugul , kobagakta inendet ne matia .
Koweek anyun Jesu Galili eng’ kimnatetab Tamirmiriet : ak kiyom logoiywek korotinwek tugul agobo inendet eng’ ole negite oloto . 
Ak kiinetisiei eng’ sunagogisiekwak , ak kiilos inendet bik tugul .
Kinyo anyun Nasaret , ole kinerjin : kiwa sunagogit , eng’ betutab sabato , ko u ye kicham kowendi , ak kotonon si kobiit kosoman . 
Ak kigigochi inendet bukuit ne mamanat ne bo maotiot Isaia . Ak king’any bukuit , konyor ole kigisir kele ,
Mi Tamirmirietab Kiptaiyat kobota , Ami kiila si kobiit aamji kibananok logoiywek che miach : Kiiyokwa si kobiit aamji luulenik katiaget, Asi kobiit kogeerto kipkoratinik , Ak atiach che kigiguoten .
Si kobiit aamda kenyit ne chamat eng’ Kiptaiyat .
Ak kimaman bukuit , ak koweekyi kogeny kiboitiot , ak koteb ng’ony : ak kiichiilji kong’ inendet bik tugul che kimi sunagogit . 
Ak kitoi kolenji bichoto , Kagosulda rani sirutioni eng’ itikwok . 
Ak kibaorianji tugul inendet , ak kokwong’io eng’ ng’alek che bo mieindo che kamong’une kutinnyi : ak kile ichek , Tos ma weritab Josep nito ?
Ak kiwolji ichek kolenji , Iman omwawa kalewenoni , Isoopge inye , chepkerichot : tuguk tugul che kigegas kele kiyaak eng’ Kapernaum , iyai choto agichek eng’ yu eng’ emoning’ung’ . 
Ak kilenji , Amwawok iman , ale , Mami maotiondo ne chamaksei eng’ emennyi . 
Ago amwawok iman ale , Kimi mosogik che chang’ Israel eng’ betusiek che bo Elija , yu kiga kiger kipsengwet kenyisiek somok ak arawek lo , yu kiga nyo rubet ne o emet tugul ; 
ago ma kiyokto Elija kwo oldab age eng’ ichek , kobate kiwa Sarepta eng’ emetab Sidon agoi oldab kwondo age ne ki mosok . 
Ak kimi che chang’ che kitinyei mogondosik eng’ Israel eng’ betusiekab maotiot Elisha ; ak kima kisoob chi eng’ ichek kobate Naaman inegei , Suriaindet . 
Ak kinyi neregek ichek tugul eng’ sunagogit ye kingogas ng’alechuto ; 
ak king’eetyo kotoorta inendet komanda eng’ nganaset , ak kiimut kwo tulwet barak ole kigiteech nganasenywa , kolen kotoortae chemng’esut . 
Ago kisiirtoe kwenunywa kwo .
Ak kichorjigei anyun Kapernaum , nganaset ne bo Galili . Ak kiinet bik eng’ betutab sabato : 
ak kikwong’io eng’ konetisiennyi ; amu kitinyei kimnatet ng’olyondennyi . 
Ak kimi chi sunagogit , ne kitinyei tamirmirietab oindet ne muruon ; ak kiwaach eng’ waagat ne o , 
kole , Bagaktech ! Kiting’ege nee ak inye , Jesu ne bo Nasaret ? Kenyo inye si ibarech ? Kaanain inye ale i Ne Tilil ne bo Jehovah . 
Ak kiger kong’ Jesu inendet, ak kolenji , Sis , ak imong’u eng’ inendet . Ak kingo kagowirji oindet kwenunywa , komong’une inendet anyun , komata koita kiy . 
Ak kikwong’io bichoto tugul , ak kong’alaljigei ichegei kole , Nee ng’olyondoni ? Amu kang’at eng’ kimnatet ak kamuktaet tamirmirik che muruonen , si komong’ . 
Ak kiyom anyun logoiywek komoswek tugul che bo emonoto agobo inendet .
Ak kimanda eng’ sunagogit ak kwo gab Simon . Kiamei kametab osotiotab Simon eset ne korom ; ak kisaisai bik Jesu agobo inendet . 
Ak kotonon eng’ ye negit , ak koger kong’ eset ; kibagakta anyun eset inendet : ak ngunoto kong’eet ak koboisiechi ichek .
Ak ye ki negit kororokta asista , komutyi bik tugul bikwak che kimiandos eng’ korotwek che terotin : ak kiigonoor eunekyik age tugul eng’ ichek , ak kosoob . 
Komong’une anyun oik bik che chang’ , kowaachei kolen , Inyendet ko i Weritab Jehovah . Koger kong’ Jesu icheget , ma chamji kotwek , amu kiingen ichek kole , inendet ko Kristo .
Ak ye kingo kagoeech , komong’ eng’ oloto kwo surkwen : ak kicheng’at tuiyosiek inendet , koba ole mi , komach icheget korany inendet kole , amat kwo kobagakta ichek . 
Ago kilenji ichek , Kanyolja aamda logoiywek che miach che bo bounatetab Jehovah eng’ nganasok alak agichek : amu kigiyokwa agobo noto . 
Ak kiamdaat anyun eng’ sunagogisiek che bo Galili .
Ak ye kingota kogiichi tuiyet inendet , ak kogasei ng’olyotab Jehovah , kotonon inendet eng’ ngegutab araraita ne bo Genesaret ; 
ak kigeer moingonik aeng’ che bo beek kotonondos eng’ ngegutab araraita : ago kiga kochorgei ramik koba komwet regereiywekwak che kiname njirenik . 
Ak kilany moinget age , ne ki bo Simon , kosom kole , konaktae kolooit kitigin eng’ ngegut . Ak kiteb ng’ony anyun ak konet tuiyosiek komi moinget .
Ak ye kingo kagoges ng’alalennyi , kolenji Simon , Ta ikweri moinget kwo ole chang’ beek , ak ochoorte regereiywekwok oramisie . 
Ak kiwol Simon kole , Kiptaiyandani , kogiboisie kemout komugul , ama kinyoru kiy : ago achoortoi regereiywot amu ng’olyondeng’ung’ . 
Ak ye kingo kagoyai ko u noto , konam njirenik ng’isiat ; kot kotoi kong’etyo regereiywekwak ; 
ak king’wech bik che kiboisiei tugul che kimi moinget age , kole kobwa kotoret . Kobwa anyun , ak konyiit moingonik tuwai , kot kotoi moingonik kosu .
Ago ye kingogeer Simon Petero , kobutyi kotung’oikab Jesu , ak kole , Istoenage , amu a chi ne bo tengek , ee Kiptaiyandani . 
Amu kikwong’ , ak tugul che kimi koboto inendet , agobo njirenik che kiga nam ; 
kikwong’io agichek Jakobo ak Johana , werikab Sebedi , che kiboisiei tugul koboto Simon . Ak kilenji Jesu Simon , Ameiyweisie ; koboch nguno iegu ne irame bik . 
Ak ye kingo kagoget moingonikwak kobwa ngegut , kobagakta tugul , ak kosub inendet .
Ak kingota komitei nganaset age , ogeero , chito ne ki nyiitat mogondosik : ak ye kingogeer inendet Jesu , kobut kosieb mo , ak kosaisai kole , Kiptaiyandani , ngicham , imuchi itilila .
Ak kiiyogoito Jesu anyun eunnyi , ak kotwa ak kole , Kaacham ; tililitu . Ak ngunoto kobagakta mogondosik inendet . 
Ak king’at anyun kolenji , Amat imwachi chi : ago ui ak iborjige tisiindet , ak igoite che bo katilileng’ung’ , ko u ye king’at Musa , koek baornatet eng’ icheget .
Ak kitesak mising’ koiyesta logoiywekyik : ak kiiyumgei tuiyosiek che chang’ kobwa si kogas ng’alekyik ak kisoob eng’ mianwekwak . 
Ago kiitabangei inegei kwo surkwen kosa .
Ak kiinetisiei eng’ betut age eng’ betusiechoto ; ak kimi Parisaik ak konetik che bo ng’atutik kotebyei eng’ oloto , che kibunu nganaset age tugul ne bo Galili ak ne bo Judea ak ne bo Jerusalem : ak kimi kamuktaetab Kiptaiyat koboto inendet kosoobe bik . 
Ak ogeero , kilau bik chito eng’ itogut ne ki meat borto : ak kicheng’ oret ne imute kwo go , ak konde inendet tainnyi . 
Ak ye kimata konyor ole imute kwo go amu chang’indab bik , kolany got barak , ak kochoortae inendet itogunnyi kobun ole kigisieb , agoi kwenut eng’ taitab Jesu . 
Ak kingogeer Jesu kayanenywa , kolenji , Chichi , kagenyoun kaat tengekwogiguk .
Ak kitoi sirik ak Parisaik kobwat agobo ng’olyondonoto kole , Ng’o nito mwaei ng’alechu yaachen ? Ng’o ne imuchi konyochi chi kaat tengekwogik kobate Jehovah inegei ? 
Ago ye kingonai Jesu anyun kabwatutikwak , kowolji kolenji , Obwati nee eng’ mugulelwekwok ? 
Nee ne nyamnyum , ngele , Kaginyoun kaat tengekwogiguk ; anan ngele , Ng’eet ak iwendote ? 
Ago si kobiit onai ole tinyei kimnatet Weritab chi eng’ ng’ony konyochi kaat bik tengekwogik (kolenji chito ne ki meat borto) , Amwaun ale , Ng’eet , ib itogung’ung’ ak iwe gong’ung’ . 
Ak king’eet ngunoto anyun eng’ tainywa , ak kiib kit ne karue , ak kwo gonnyi , kolosunoti Jehovah . 
Ak kokwong’io ichek tugul ak kolos Jehovah ; ak kinyi ichek kaiyweisiet , ak kole , Kagegeer rani tuguk che kikwong’e .
Ak kingobata tuguchu kwo kogeer taagindetab aisurut , ne kiguure Lawi , kotebyei eng’ ole kitaage aisurut , ak kilenji , Isubwa . 
Ak kibagakta tugul , ak kong’eet kosub inendet . 
Ak kichopchi Lawi inendet igorta ne o eng’ gonnyi ; ak kimi tuiyet ne o ne bo taagikab aisurut ak bik alak che kitebyei eng’ amisiet koboto inendet . 
Ak kiing’unyng’ung’ji Parisaik ak sirikwak alamalyennyi , kole , Kalya si oamisiei ak oeeisei koboto taagikab aisurut ak kiptengeginik ? 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Mamage kiy chepkerichot bik che chamegei ; kobate che miandos . 
Kima anyo aguur che bo iman , ago kiptengeginik , si kosik .
Ak kilenji inendet , Irugutegei konyil che chang’ alamalyetab Johana , ak kosaei , ak yaei ko u noto agichek che bo Parisaik ; ago amisiei cheguk ak koeeisei . 
Ak kilenji Jesu ichek , Tos omuchi ogochi korugutgei che kogiguurji katunisiet , kota komi sandet koboto icheget ? 
Ago bwanei betusiek che tun kiistoe ichek sandet , korugutgei anyun eng’ betusiechoto .
Ak kimwachi ichek anyun kalewenet kogeny kolenji , Mami chi ne kerei akwot ne bo ngoriet ne leel ak konapchi ngoriet ne os ; amu ngo yai ko u noto ko kereri noto leel , ak kogeny , manamegei akwot ne leel ak ne os . 
Ama mi chi ne indoi divaik che leelach lolotinwek che osen ; ngo yai ko u noto ko kereri divaik lolotinwek , ak kotumdagei , ak kong’emogis lolotinwek . 
Ago kanyol kinde divaik che leelach lolotinwek che leelachen . 
Ama mi chi ne ngo kagoee divaik che bo keny ko ta komach che leelach : amu mwaei kole , Miachen che bo keny .
Ak kibunei mbarenikab bek eng’ betutab sabato ; ak kibagat alamalyennyi mesisekab bek , kobirir ak konyei . 
Ago kimwa alage che bo Parisaik kole , Amu nee si oyai eng’ betutab sabato ne ma chamdaat eng’ ng’atutik ? 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Tom osoman agot ng’olyondoni , ne kiyai Daudi , ye kingoam rubet , koboto che kimitei ak inendet ; 
ak kiwa gotab Jehovah ak kocher makatinik che bo kabartaet , koam ak kobutyi che kimi koboto inendet agichek ; che ma chamdaat eng’ ng’atutik koam chi kobate tisiik ichegei ? 
Ak kimwachi ichek kolenji , Weritab chi ko kiptaiyatab sabato .
Ak kiwa sunagogit eng’ sabato age , ak konetis : ak kimi chi oloto , ne ki resot eunnyi ne bo tai . 
Ak kirib inendet sirik ak Parisaik kole , kogeer ngo tos isoob chi eng’ betutab sabato ; si konyor oret ne itaame . 
Ago kinai kabwatutikwak ; ak kolenji chichoto ne kitinyei eut ne resot , Ng’eet , tonon eng’ kwen . Ak king’eet kotonon . 
Ak kilenji Jesu ichek , Ateebenok , ale , Tos , chamdaat eng’ ng’atutik keyai ne mie eng’ sabato , anan keyai ne ya ? Kesor sobon , anan kebar ? 
Ak kigeerot Jesu bik tugul , yeityo kolenji chichoto , Chuul eung’ung’ . Ak kiyai ko u noto : ak kimieit eunnyi ko u ye konye . 
Ak kinerekso mising’ : ak king’alaljigei ichegei agobo kit ne itoi Jesu .
Kiwa Jesu anyun eng’ betusiechoto , tulwet kosa ; ak kisa Jehovah kemout komugul .
Ak ye kingoeech , koguur alamalyennyi : ak kilewen eng’ choto taman ak aeng’ , che kiguure kainenywa che kiyoktoi ; 
Simon , ne kiguure kainennyi ne bo aeng’ Petero , ak Andrea ng’etab kamet , ak Jakobo ak Johana , ak Pilipu ak Bartolomayo , 
ak Matayo ak Tomas , ak Jakobo weritab Alpayo ak Simon ne kigiguure Selote , 
Judas weritab Jakobo , ak Judas Iskariot , ne ki ng’wektaindet ;
ak kichortagei koboto icheget , ak kotonone ye ribrib , koboto tuiyet ne o ne bo alamalyennyi , ak bik che chang’ che kibunu Judea komugul ak Jerusalem , ak ngegutab nyanjet ole bo komostab Turo ak Sidon , che kibwanei kogasei inendet , ak kisoob eng’ mainwekwak ; 
ak kigisoob icheget che kiinyalili tamirmirik che muruonen . 
Ak kicheng’ tuiyet komugul kotwa inendet : amu kibunu inendet kamuktaet , ak kosoob ichek tugul .
Ak kigeerot alamalyennyi , ak kole , O boiboen okwek che o bonon : amu neng’wong’ bounatetab Jehovah . 
O boiboen okwek che amok rubet nguno : amu tun obiyong’dosi . O boiboen okwek che orirtosi nguno : amu tun ororitosi .
O boiboen okwek , ye wechok bik , ak kobesienogei , ak kochurok , ak kowirta kaineng’wong’ kole ya , agobo Weritab chi . 
Oboiboitu eng’ betunoto , ak otorombense eng’ boiboindo : amu , ogeero , o melektang’wong’ eng’ kipsengwet : amu kiyachi kwanisiekwak maotik ko u noto . 
Ago bwa okwek che o magore : Amu kaotaach kagaigaeng’wong’ . 
Bwa okwek , che o biyong’otin nguno : Amu tatun koamok rubet . Bwa okwek , che ororitosi nguno : Amu tatun oteitosi ak orirtosi . 
Bwa okwek , ye mwaei bik tugul che miach agobo okwek : Amu kigoyachi ko u noto kwanisiekwak maotik che bo lembech .
Ago amwawok okwek che ogase , ale , Ocham bunikwok , oyachi che miach ichek che wechok , 
oberur ichek che chubok , ak osachi ichek che usok . 
Ak inendet ne irabachin matanda age igochi matanda age ; ak inendet ne rebenen ngorieng’ung’ ko meete agot sumeng’ung’ . 
Igochi chi age tugul ne somin ; ak inendet ne rebenen tuguguk ko matata isom kogeny . 
Ak ko u ye omache koyaiywok bik , oyachi ak okwek ko u noto .
Ngocham anyun icheget che chamok , otinye kongoi nee ? Amu agot kiptengeginik kochamei agichek icheget che chamei . 
Ak ngoyachi che miach icheget che yaiywok che miach , otinye kongoi nee ? Amu agot kiptengeginik koyaei ko u noto . 
Ak ngobesendochi bik che omang’u ole tun onyorune , otinye kongoi nee ? Amu agot kiptengeginik ko besendochin kiptengeginik alak , si konyor che te chugicheta . 
Ago ocham bunikwok, ak oyai ne mie , ak obesende, amongen onyoru kogeny ; si koeet melektang’wong’ , ak oegu werikab Inendet ne Toror Mising’ : amu tala inendet eng’ icheget che matinyei kongoi ak che yaachen . 
Oegu che tinyei rirenetab ge , ko u Kwandang’wong’ ne tinyei rirenetab ge .
Amoruokyi , si tun koma kiruokwok : amogikyi , si tun koma kigikyok : otiach , si tun kitiachak : 
ogoite , si tun kegonok ; kerutiet ne mie , ne kigigony , ne kigisaisach , kot korara , choto che tun indoi bik tegetikwok . Amu kerutiet ne ogere ko noto ne tun kigerunenok ak okwek .
Ak kimwachi kalewenet kolenji , Imuchi kipkoratiat kondochi kipkoratiat ? Tos marorokyin tuwai keringet ? 
Masiirei alamalyet konetindennyi : ago inendet ne kigonetak kogergeitu ak konetindennyi . 
Ak amu nee si igeere betbetiat ne mitei kondab ng’etab komet , ago mebwati bambaniat ne mi kondang’ung’ inyendet ? 
Anan imuktoi ano ilenji ng’etab komet , Tupchennyu , inganemun betbetiat ne mitei kondang’ung’ , ago mebwati inye bambaniat ne mi kondang’ung’ inyendet ? Ee , chombilindoni ! inemu korok bambaniat ne mi kondang’ung’ inyendet , si ye kaigeerte komie imuch anyun inemu betbetiat ne mi kondab ng’etab komet .
Amu mami ketit ne mie ne yiei logoek che yaach ; ama mi ketit ne ya ne yiei logoek che miach . 
Amu kinae ketit age tugul logoekyik . Amu mabutei bik logoekab mogoonik eng’ katok , ak mabutei bik logoekab sabibuk eng’ ketitab katok . 
Inemu chito ne mie kit ne mie kobunu konoruet ne mie ne mi muguleldanyi ; ak inemu chito ne ya kit ne ya kobunu konoruet ne ya ne mi muguleldanyi : amu che mwaei kutinnyi ko che nyiitat muguleldo .
Amu nee si oguurena Kiptaiyat , Kiptaiyat , amoyae tuguk che amwae ? 
Chi age tugul ne nyonjina , ak kogas ng’alekyuk , ak koyai , aboruok chito ne kergei : 
kergei inendet ak chito ne teechei got , ne kibal kororokto mising’ , ak konde lumeiywot ruandet : ak ye kingo chang’a beek , korieb beekab mogoch goyoto , ama imuch kotumdum : amu kiga kiteech komie . 
Ago inendet ne kasei, ama yaei , ko kergei ak chito ne kiteech got ng’ung’unyek ama lumji ng’ony lumeiywot ; ak kirieb beekab mogoch , ak kilul ngunoto ; ak kieet luletab goyoto .
Ak kingo kagogesyi ng’alekyik tugul itikab bik , kwo anyun Kapernaum . 
Kimi kiptaiyatab bogol , ne kitinyei otwogindet ne kichamei kot, ak kimiani otwogindonoto ne ki negit kome . 
Ak ye kingogas agobo Jesu , koyokto inendet boisiekab Yahudik , koba komwachi konyo kosoob otwogennyi . 
Ak ye kingoit icheget ole mi Jesu , kosaisai inendet mising’ , kolenji , Nyoljin inendet iyachi ko u noto : 
amu chamei bororiennyo , ak kiteekwech inendet sunagoginnyo . 
Kwo anyun Jesu koboto icheget . Ak ye kima kota ko loo eng’ goyoto , koyokto kiptaiyandanato choronokyik koba ole mi inendet ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , amata iimge : amu ane , ko ma a chito ne nyolu inyo gonnyu : 
noto anyun , agot ane , ko ma aiitge ale nyolu anyonjin : ago mwa ng’olyot kityo , ak kosob otwogindennyu . 
Agot ane , nganda a chi ne kiboiywa , atinye askarik che abou , ak ngalenji ni , Ui , kwo ; ak ngalenji age , Nyo , konyo ; ak ngalenji otwogindennyu , Yai ni , koyai .
Ak ye kingogas Jesu ng’alechuto, kokwong’ agobo inendet , ak kiwelelgei ak kolenji tuiyet ne kiisubi inendet , Amwawok ale , tom anyoru kayanet ne o ne te ni , achicha , agot eng’ Israel . 
Ak kingoweek anyun che kiga kiyokto , koba ga , konyor otwogindonoto ko kagosob .
Ak ye kingo kagobata betunoto , kwo nganaset ne kiguure Nain ; ak kiba alamalyennyi koboto inendet , ak tuiyet ne o . 
Ak ye kiga rikta ormarichetab nganaset , ogeero , kigisutei musto , ne ki werit ne kii kamet inegei , ak ki mosok chebiosonato : ak kimi koboto inendet bik che chang’ che bo nganaset . 
Ak ye kingogeer Kiptaiyat inendet , korire , ak kolenji , Amat irir . 
Ak kirikta ye negit ak kotwa kit ne kigisute inendet : ak kitononso anyun che kisutei . Ak kilenji Jesu inendet , Neranani , kamwaun ale , Ng’eet . 
Ak king’eet anyun ne koga kome , ak kotoi kong’alal . Ak kiigochi kamet . 
Ak kiiyweis tugul : ak kolos Jehovah , kole, Kagong’eet eng’ kwenunnyo maotiot ne o : ak, Kagorutochi Jehovah bikyik . 
Ak kiyom ng’olyondonito agobo inendet Judea komugul , ak korotinwek tugul che kiyiem oloto .
Ak kimwachi alamalyetab Johana inendet tuguchuto tugul . 
Ak kiguurjigei Johana aeng’ che bo alamalyennyi ak koyokto koba ole mi Kiptaiyat , koteebe kole , Tos inyendet ni nyonei , anan kigeni age ? 
Ak ye kiga it bik ole mi inendet , kolenji , Kagoyokwech Johana Kabatisanindet kebwa ole imi , kole , Tos inyendet ne nyonei , anan kigeni age ?
Eng’ sainato kosoob che chang’ che kitinyei mianwek ak korotwek ak tamirmirik che yaachen ; ak kiigochi kipkoratinik che chang’ kogeerto . 
Kowolji kolenji , Oba omwachi Johana tuguk che kaogeer ak che kaogas ; kigochin kipkoratinik kogeerto , ak bendoti che koing’waldos , kitilili che tinyei mogondosik , ak kastoi che ming’otin , king’eeti che kigobek , kiamjin kibananok logoiywek che miach . 
Ak baibai age tugul ne manyorunena kanagut .
Kingo kagoba che kiga koyokto Johana , kotoi komwachi tuiyosiek agobo Johana , kole , Kiomande surkwen ogeer nee ? Tegat ne itumdumi usonet ? 
Ago kiomande ogeer nee okwek ? Chito ne ilaachi ngoroik che tangusen ? Ogeero , icheget che ilaachi ngoroik che bo lelesta , ak che meng’isiei eng’ talbisto , komitei gorikab laitorinik . 
Ago kiomande ogeer nee ? Maotiot ? Ee , amwawok ale , siirei maotiot . 
Nito ne kigisir agobo inendet , kele , Ogeero , ayoktoi kiboitiondennyu kondoenen , Ne chobei oreng’ung’ eng’ taing’ung’ .
Amwawok ale, Eng’ che kisich kobogorisiek ko mami ne o ne siirei Johana : kobate inendet ne ming’in eng’ bounatetab Jehovah ko o kosiir inendet .
Ak ye kingogas bik tugul , koboto taagikab aisurut , koiityi imanda Jehovah , amu kiga kibatisan eng’ kabatisanetab Johana . 
Ago kiesio Parisaik ak ng’omotikab Ng’atutik , kiruogutikab Jehovah , ma makyigei , amu kima ibatisan inendet icheget .
Ak kile Kiptaiyat , Aroge nee bikab ibini ? ak kergei ak nee ? 
Kergei ak lagok che tebyei eng’ oldab aldaisiet , ak koguuregei ; kolen , Kigegutwak ndurerusiek , ak ma oureren ; kigirirjok , ak ma oririe . 
Amu kinyo Johana Kabatisanindet ama am makatia anan divaik ; ak omwae anyun ole , Tinyei oindet . 
Kinyo Weritab chi koamis ak koeeiso ; ak omwae ole , Ogeero , kipkeiya chichi , ak eeindetab divaik , choruetab taagikab aisurut ak kiptengeginik! 
Ak naat ng’omnatet kele bo iman , eng’ lagokyik tugul .
Ak kimach age eng’ Parisaik kole koamis ak inendet . Ak kiwa gotab Parisaindonoto , ak koteb ng’ony koamis . 
Ak ogeero, kobogoriot age ne kimi nganaset , ne ki kiptengekyo ; ye kingonai kole , tebyei ng’ony Jesu koamisiei eng’ gotab Parisaindonoto , koib chubait ne mi mwaita ne nyamdut , 
ak kitonon eng’ let ole negite kelyekyik , korirei , ak kitoi kosachi beekab kong’ kelyekyik , ak kouuse sumeekyik , ak kong’utut kelyekyik ak koiile mwaata . 
Ak ye kingogeer noto Parisaindonoto ne kiguurei inendet , komwa eng’ orinnyi , kole , Nda ka maotio chichi , ta kagonai kole ng’o kobogoriondoni katwa inendet , ak chi ne u nee , kole kiptengekyot . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu inendet kolenji , Simon , atinye ng’olyot ne amache amwaun . Ak kile , Konetindoni , mwa anyun . 
Kole , Kimi besendoindet anum ne kitinyei besenikyik aeng’ : kibesen age denarisiek bogol mut , ak kibesen age konom . 
Ak ye kima kotinyei kiy ne yaakyin , konyochi kaat ichek tuwai . Ng’o anyun eng’ ichek tuwai ne chamei inendet kosiir ? 
Kowol Simon kole , Alen inendet ne kiginyochi kaat che chang’ . Ak kilenji , Kairuoch komie .
Ak kingoweleljigei kobogoriot , kolenji Simon , Igeere kobogoriondoni ? Kaanyo gong’ung’ ama inaga beek aune kelyekyuk : ago kagosachi kelyekyuk beekyik bo kong’ kobogoriondoni , ak kouuse sumeekyik . 
Ma ing’ututa ; ago inendet , koboch ngab anyo , kotomo kobagakta kong’utut kelyekyuk . 
Ma iile metinnyu mwaita : ago kagoiile ine kelyekyuk mwaita ne nyamdut . 
Noto anyun ne kamwaun ale , kagenyochi kaat tengekwogikyik , che ka chang’ ; amu chamei mising’ : ago inendet ne kinyochin kaat kitigin , kochamei agine kitigin . 
Kolenji kobogoriondonoto , Kagenyoun kaat tengekwogiguk .
Ak kitoi icheget che kimitei amisiet koboto inendet , komwa eng’ orinywa , kole , Ng’o ni kot konyochi kaat bik tengekwogik ? 
Ak kilenji kobogoriot , Kagosorun kayaneng’ung’ ; ui eng’ kalyet .
Ak kingobata noto , ne matianit , kowendote nganasok che eechen ak che mengechen koamdaati ak komwaitaati logoiywek che miach che bo bounatetab Jehovah , ak kimi tamanu ak aeng’ koboto inendet , 
ak kobogorisiek alak che kiga kosoob eng’ tamirmirik che yaachen ak mianwek , Maria ne kiguure Magdalene , ne kimandae oik tisabu , 
ak Joana osotiotab Kusa kiboitiotab Herod , ak Susana , ak kobogorisiek alak che chang’ , che kiboisiechin inendet eng’ tugukwak .
Ak kingo yomogei tuiyet ne o , ak kobwanji inendet che kibunu nganaset age tugul , kong’alal eng’ kalewenet kole : 
Kiwa kolindet koleta keswekyik : ak ye kita koletoi , kobutyi alak oret taban ; ak kigitiegat , ak koam taritik che bo barak . 
Ak kiibutyi alak ruandet ; ak ye kingobityo , koyaamnyo , amu manyor beek . 
Ak kiibutyi alak kwenutab katok ; ak kibityo katok koboto keswechoto , ak kogiich . 
Ak kiibutyi alak ng’ung’unyek che miach , ak kobityo , ak koi age tugul bogol . Ak ye kita komwaei tuguchu , komwa eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Inendet ne tinyei itik che kastoe , kogas .
Ak kiteebe alamalyennyi ole teptoi kalewenoni . 
Ak kile , kagigonok okwek onai ung’otik che bo bounatetab Jehovah : ago kimwachin alak eng’ kalewenaik ; si ye keertoi ko mageerei kiy , si ye kasei ko manaei .
Kalewenonoto ko ni : Keswek ko ng’olyotab Jehovah . 
Ak choto mi oret taban ko icheget che kigogas ; yeityo konyo oindet , ak konem ng’olyot eng’ mugulelwekwak , si manyor kayanet ak kesor . 
Ak icheget che mi ruandet barak , ko ye kagas ng’alek , koyan eng’ boiboiyet , ak matinyei tigitik , iyani ne matia , ak kochuchuigei eng’ betutab yomset . 
Ak che kiibutyi katok , ko icheget che kigas , ak ye kaba kogiich kererwekab met ak magornatosiek , ak boiboiyetab tugukab soboni , ama iyo logoek che nyiitotin . 
Ak che mi ng’ung’unyek che miach , ko icheget , che ye kagogas ng’olyot , konam komie , eng’ mugulelwek che bo telunatet ak ko miachen , ak koiiyo logoek eng’ kagiiletab ge .
Mami chi , ne , ye kagonaam tait , kotuge kiy , anan konde kureretab itogut ; ago indoi kit ne tonone tait , si kobiit kogeer lapkeiyet bik che bwanei go .
Amu mami kiy ne keunyei , ne matun ng’ang’oksei ; ama mi kiy ne bo ung’ot , ne matun naaksei eng’ ole lapkei .
Oripge anyun eng’ ole ogastoi : amu age tugul ne tinyei , ko tun kigochin ; ak inendet ne matinyei , ko tun kirebe agot ne len tinyei .
Ak kibwanji inendet kamet ak che tupcho , ago kima imuch korikyi amu chang’indab bik . 
Ak kigimwachi kelenji , Tonondos komet ak che otupche eng’ sang’ , machei kogeerin . 
Ago kiwolji kolenji , Kamennyu ak che kitupche ko chu kasei ng’olyotab Jehovah , ak koyai .
Ak kilany moingetab beek eng’ betut age eng’ betusiechoto , koboto alamalyennyi ; ak kilenji , Ongelandae araraita kebe bitonin : kotoi anyun koba . 
Ak kingota kobendi , koru Jesu konuuch : kochorjigei anyun usonet ne o araraita ; kot komachei konyi beek moinget ak kinyonji ng’oiyondit . 
Ak kibwa ole mi inendet , ak kong’eet , kolenji , Konetindoni , konetindoni , kagibegu . Kong’eet anyun , ak koger kong’ usonet ak wasetab ge ne bo beek : kosis anyun araraita komung’do . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Mi ano kayaneng’wong’ ? Kiiyweis ak kokwong’io , kolenjigei ichegei , Ng’o chichi anyun , ne ng’atei agot usonet ak beek , kot kogas it inendet ?
Kiit anyun emetab Gerasenik , ne tokyingei Galili . 
Ak ye kingonyo ngegutab araraita , kotuiyo ak inendet chito age ne kibunu nganaset , ne kitinyei oik ; ak kima kolaachi ngoroik koboch betusiek che chang’ , ak kima komenyei go , ago kitebote kererisiek . 
Ak kingogeer Jesu , kowaach ak kobutyi tainnyi , ak kimwa eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Ating’enen nee , Jesu Weritab Jehovah ne toror Mising ? Kasomin ale , amenyalila . 
Amu king’at tamirmiriet ne muruon komong’ eng’ chichoto . Amu kiga nam eng’ betusiek che chang’ : ak kigiribei mising’ , ak kiga kirate sirimwek ak mugurek ; ak king’etyei tuguk che kirate , ak kionei oindet inendet kwo surkwen . 
Ak kiteebe Jesu, kolenji , Kiguurenen nee ? Ak kile , Chang’indo ; amu kiga chut oik che chang’ inendet . 
Ak kisom kole , si mang’at koba keringet ne matinyei ole bochin .
Ak kimi oloto akwet ne o ne bo torok che kiagetos eng’ tulwet : ak kisom ichek mising’ kole , kochamji kochut torochoto . Kochamji anyun . 
Ak kimong’ anyun oik eng’ chichoto , ak kochut torok : ak kiruai akwet kochortaegei chemng’esut koba araraita , ak kobek .
Ak kingogeer che kiiyagisiei tuguk che kabiit , komwaei , ak koba komwaita eng’ nganaset ak eng’ emet agobo noto . 
Ak kiba kogeer kit ne kagoyaak ; ak kibwa ole mi Jesu , konyor chichoto ne kamandae oik , kotebyei eng’ kelyekab Jesu , kolaagat , ak kotinyei ng’omnatennyi : ak kiiywei . 
Ak kimwachi ichek che kageerei tuguk che kabiit , ole kagisoopto chito ne katinyei oik . 
Ak kisom anyun bik tugul che bo ole negite emetab Gerasenik kole , kwo kobagakta ichek : amu kiga nam ichek kaiyweisiet ne o : ak kilany moingetab beek , ak koweektagei . 
Ago kisom inendet chito ne kamandae oik kole , kotebi tuwai : ago kimwachi kwo , kolenji , 
Iweekyigei gong’ung’ , ak imwaite tuguk che eechen che kagoyaun Jehovah . Ak kiwa anyun, komwaitaat eng’ nganaset komugul tuguk che eechen che kagoyachi Jesu .
Ak ye kiweeksei Jesu , kotaach tuiyet ; amu kiigeni bik tugul inendet . 
Ak ogeero , kinyo chito age ne keguure Jairo ; ki bounindetab sunagogit : ak kiibutyi kelyekab Jesu , ak kosom inendet kole, konyo gonnyi : 
amu kitinyei chepto ne kigii inegei, ne ki bo olo bo kenyisiek taman ak aeng’ , ak ki negit kome . Ago kiigiigoti tuiyosiek inendet kowendi . 
Ak kimi kobogoriot age ne kimandae korotik kenyisiek taman ak aeng’ , ne kiga koboisie tugukyik tugul eng’ chepkerichinik , ama imuch kosoob inendet age tugul eng’ ichek . 
Kinyo anyun kobun let eng’ inendet , ak kotwa tabandab ngoriennyi : ak ngunoto kosisyo korotik . 
Ak kile Jesu , Ng’o ne katwaa ? Ak kingotiiyo tugul , kolenji Petero ak che kimi koboto inendet , Konetindoni , kariichin tuiyosiek ak kagogiichin . 
Ago kile Jesu , Kagotwaa chi : amu kaanai ale , kagomandaena kimnatet . 
Ak ye kingogeer kobogoriot kole , ma imuch koung’ak , konyo kobotanonu , ak kobutyi ng’ony eng’ tainnyi ak komwaita eng’ taitab bik tugul kit ne kaigochi kotwa inendet , ak ole kagisoopto ngunoto . 
Ak kilenji , Chebi , kagosoobin kayaneng’ung’ ; ui eng’ kalyet .
Ak ye kita kong’alali , konyo chi ne kibunu oldab bounindetab sunagogit , kole , Kagome cheptang’ung’ amatata iim Konetindet . 
Ago kingogas Jesu , kowolji kolenji , Ameiywei : iyan kityo , si kisoob .
Ak ye kingo kagoit got , koma kochamji chi age tugul kwo go koboto inendet , kobate Petero , ak Johana , ak Jakobo , ak kwandab cheboto ak kamet . 
Ak kirirtos bik tugul , ak koteeitos agobo inendet : ago kile, Morirtosi; amu ma me inendet, ago inuuchi. 
Ak kirorechi inendet anyun kochot , amu kiingen kole kagome . 
Ago kinam inendet eutab cheboto , ak koguur , kole , Chebi, ng’eet . 
Koweek anyun tamirmiriennyi , ak kong’eet ngunoto : ak king’at kole , kigochi kiy ne amei . 
Ak kikwong’io mising’ sigikyik : ak king’at inendet ichek kolenji , amomwachi chi age tugul kit ne kagoyaak .
Kiguur anyun taman ak aeng’ koyumgei, ak kogochi kimnatet ak bounatet koboi oik tugul , ak kosoob che miandos . 
Ak kiiyokto koamda bounatetab Jehovah , ak kosoob che miandos . 
Kolenji , Amoib kiy ne bo bandang’wong’ , agot kirokto, anan lolet , anan makatiat , anan fedaisiek ; amoibote sumotik aeng’ . 
Ak got age tugul ne omong’jini , otebe oloto agoi obe . 
Ak alak tugul che mataachak , ye omande eng’ nganasanato , olelekte temburiek eng’ kelyekwok si koek baornatet agobo ichek . 
Koba anyun kobunot nganasok , koamdaati logoiywek che miach , ak kosooboti eng’ oldo tugul .
Ak kigas anyun kiruogindet Herod tuguk tugul che kigoyaak : kiimgei mising’ , amu kimwaei alak , kole , kagong’eet Johana eng’ che kibek ; 
ak kilen alak , kogotook Elija : kolen alak , kong’eet age eng’ maotik chu ki bo keny . 
Ak kile Herod , Kiatil metitab Johana : ago ng’o anyun chichi , ne agase tuguk che u choto agobo inendet ? Ak kicheng’ kole kogeer inendet .
Ak ye kingoweek che kiyoktoi , komwachi inendet tuguk che kogoyai . Ak kiimut ichek koba taban ichegei agoi nganaset ne kiguure Betsaida . 
Ago kingonai tuiyosiek kosub : ak kitaach icheget , ak kong’alalji agobo bounatetab Jehovah , ak kiisoob ichek che kimachei kisoob .
Ak ye kimachei koimen , kobwa anyun tamanu ak aeng’ kolenji inendet , Ilenji tuiyet koba , si koit nganasok ak emet , si konyor ole ruitos , ak amitwogik : amu kimi surkwen . 
Ago kilenji ichek , Ogochi okwek amitwogik . Ak kile , Magitinye kiy kobate makatinik mut ak njirenik aeng’ ; kobate kebe kealji amitwogik bichu tugul . 
Amu ki olo bo murenik elfusiek mut . Ak kilenji alamalyennyi , Ochob kobuur ak ingobeate konom . 
Ak kiyai anyun ko u noto , ak kichob tugul koteb ng’ony . 
Ak kinam makatinichoto mut ak njirenichoto aeng’ , ak kiinyal kipsengwet , ak koberur , ak kotonaton ; ak kogochi alamalyet si kobiit kogochi kabuureito . 
Ak kiamis , kot kobiyong’so : ak kigiyum katuganik che king’et eng’ kererutik , ak kiek kerebonik taman ak aeng’ .
Ak ye kisaei inegei, ko kimi alamalyet koboto inendet : ak kiteebe icheget kolenji , Mwaei tuiyosiek kole a ng’o ? 
Ak kiwolji ichek kolenji , Len Johana Kabatisanindet ; kolen alage , Elija ; kolen alak , kagong’eet maotiot age eng’ chu ki bo keny . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Ago olen okwek a ng’o ? Ak kiwol Petero kole , I Kristo ne bo Jehovah .
Ago kiitigon ichek , ak kong’at kolenji , Amomwachi chi ng’olyondonito ; 
kole , Kanyolji Weritab chi konyalil eng’ tuguk che chang’ , ak koesio boisiek inendet ak tisiik che eechen ak sirik , ak kebar , ak king’eet eng’ betutab somok .
Kimwachi tugul kolenji , Ngo machei chi age tugul kosubwa , ko ingoesiogei , ak koib kimurtoiyondennyi betut age tugul , ak kosubwa . 
Amu age tugul ne machei kosor sobondanyi kobeeti ; ak age tugul ne ibeeti sobondanyi agobo ane , ko noto ne soru . 
Amu keljin nee chi , ngonyor ng’ony komugul ak kobeetgei anan kerebe sobondanyi ? 
Amu age tugul ne ililanjina ak ng’alekyuk ko tun ililanjin agine Weritab chi chichoto , ye tun nyonei eng’ torornatennyi , ak ne bo Kwanda , ak ne bo malaikaisiek che tililen . 
Ago amwawok iman ale , Mitei alak eng’ che tonondos eng’ yuto che magoi chamjam meet matiny , kot kogeer bounatetab Jehovah .
Ak kingogesgei olo bo betusiek sisiit , koboch ngomwa ng’alechato , komut Petero ak Johana ak Jakobo , kotogosta tulwet koba kosa . 
Ak ye kita kosaei , kowalak itondab togennyi , ak koleelagitu ngoroikyik kot kolil bich . 
Ak ogeero , king’alalyo ak inendet bik aeng’u ; ki Musa ak Elija ; 
che kigotook eng’ lilindo , ak kiga ng’alal agobo meenyi ne kimachei kosulda eng’ Jerusalem . 
Ak kiga birto met Petero koboto icheget che kimi ak inendet : ago ye kingogos , kogeer lilindanyi , ak bichoto aeng’ che kitonondos koboto inendet . 
Ak ye kimachei kobesio ak inendet , kolenji Petero Jesu , Konetindoni , mie amu kimi yuto : si keteech keriosiek somok ; neng’ung’ age , ko bo Musa age , ko bo Elija age : kimwaei ama nai kit ne mwaei .
Ak ye kita komwaei tuguchuto , konyo boldet , ak kotuch icheget : ak kiiyweis ye kingochut boldet . 
Ak kimong’ kutit eng’ boldet , ak kole , Ni Werinnyu , ne kialewen : ogas inendet . 
Ak ye kingobata kutinato , kotook Jesu inegei . Ak kosisyo anyun , ama mwachi chi eng’ betusiechoto kit age tugul ne kiga kogeer .
Ak betut ne kiisubi betunoto , ye kingochorugei eng’ tulwet , kotuiyo ak inendet tuiyet ne o . 
Ak ogeero , kibol chito age eng’ tuiyet , kole , Konetindoni , asain ale , rire werinnyu ; amu kigii inegei : 
ak keero , namei inendet tamirmiriet , ak ngunoto kowaach ; ak kobirabirto kot kobun bugat kutinnyi , konyalili mising’ ama chamei komanda . 
Ak koarirji alamalyeng’ung’ ale koon ; ago ma imuch . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Ee ibini matinyei kayanet ak komaasat , atebye kobotok , ak amuitoi agobo okwek kot kotianit ? Imutu wering’ung’ konyo yu . 
Ak kingota konyonei , kowirji ng’ony oindet inendet , ak kobirabirto mising’ . Ago kiger kong’ Jesu tamirmiriet ne muruon , ak kosoob lakwet , ak koweekyi kwanda . 
Ak kikwong’io tugul agobo oindab Jehovah . Ago kingota kokwong’dos tugul agobo tuguk che kayai Jesu , kolenji alamalyennyi , 
Ongochut ng’alechu itikwok : amu tun kigoitoi Weritab chi kwo eunekab bik . 
Ago ma iguiyo ichek mwaonato ; kiung’ak eng’ icheget , si manai : ak kiiywei koteebe inendet agobo mwaonato .
Kotoi anyun koteebegei kole , Ng’o ne egu ne o eng’ achek .  
Ak kingonai Jesu kabwatutikab mugulelwekwak , konam lakwet ne ming’in , ak konde ye negit inendet , 
ak kilenji ichek , Chi age tugul ne taachei lakwani ming’in eng’ kainennyu ko kataacha : ak chi age tugul ne taacha ko kataach inendet ne kiiyokwa : amu inendet ne ming’in eng’ okwek tugul , ko noto ne o .
Ak kiwolji Johana kolenji , Konetindoni , kogigeer chi koonei oik eng’ kaineng’ung’ ; ak kogiete , amu magibendoti tugul . 
Ago kilenji Jesu inendet , Amoete inendet : amu inendet ne magirindook ko neng’wong’ .
Ak ye ki negit mising’ koit betusiek che kitaage inendet eng’ barak , kogiiljigei kotokyi togennyi Jerusalem ; 
koyokto che ibei ng’alek koba kondoe inendet : koba anyun , komong’ji nganaset age ne bo Samarik , ak kochopchi oldo . 
Ak ma taach inendet , amu kiga kotokyi togennyi Jerusalem . 
Ak ye kingogeer noto alamalyennyi Jakobo ak Johana , kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , tos imache keng’at mat kochorgei eng’ kipsengwet , si kowong’ icheget [ko u ye kiyai Elija] ? 
Ago kiweleljigei ichek , ak koger kong’ . 
Koba anyun nganaset age .
Ak kingota kobendi eng’ oret , kolenji chito age , Asubun eng’ oldo tugul ole iwendi . 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Tineyi lelwek keringonik , ak kotinyei taritik che bo barak kesonok ; ago matinyei Weritab chi ole indoi metinnyi .
Ak kilenji age , Isubwa . Ago kilenji chichoto , Kiptaiyandani , chamwa awa korok atub baba .
Ago kilenji , Bagakte che begu kotub chechuak che begu ; ago ui inye ak iamdaate ng’alekab bounatetab Jehovah .
Kole age agine , Tun asubun, Kiptaiyat ; ago chamwa korok awa agochi bikab gonnyu saisere . 
Ago kilenji Jesu inendet , Mami chi ne namei mogombetab tuga , ak kogusgong’ kogeer let , ne nyoljin bounatetab Jehovah .
Kingobata tuguchu kolewen Kiptaiyat bik alak tamanwogik tisab agichek , ak koyokto kobee aeng’ kole , kondoe inendet koba nganaset age tugul ak komosta age tugul ole tun bunoti . 
Ago kilenji ichek , O kesisiet ago ng’ering’ kesik : noto anyun osom Kiptaiyat ne bo kesisiet , si kobiit koyokyi kesik kesisiennyi . 
Oba: ogeero kaayoktok ko u arekab kechirek eng’ kwenutab suik . 
Amoib lolet , anan suberet , anan kweonik : amogat chi eng’ oret . 
Ak got age tugul ne omong’jini , omwa ole , Ingoteb kalyet eng’ goi . 
Ak ngo mitei weritab kalyet yoto , kotebe kalyeng’wong’ inendet : ak ngo mami , koweekyinogei okwek . 
Ak otebe goyoto anyun , ak tuguk che konok , oam ak oee : amu nyoljin kiboitiot melektanyi . Amoitote gorik . 
Ak nganaset age tugul ne omong’jini , ak kotaachak , oam tuguk che kindoi taing’wong ; 
ak osoob che miandos eng’ oloto , ak olenji ichek , Kagorikyok bounatetab Jehovah . 
Ago nganaset age tugul ne omong’jini , ama taachak , omande obe ortinwekyik ak omwa ole , 
kagibukyok temburiek che bo nganaseng’wong’ , che kanam kelyekyok ; ago onai ni , ole , kagorik bounatetab Jehovah . 
Ago amwawok ale , Tun kaigaitu Sodom eng’ betunoto , kosiir nganasanato .
Bwa we , Korasin ! Bwa we , Betsaida ! Amu nda kiga kiyai eng’ Turo ak Sidon boisionik che bo kamuktaet ko u che kogiyai eng’ okwek , ta kiga kosik keny , ak kotebe orek kolaachi kuniok . 
Ago tun kaigaitu Turo ak Sidon eng’ kiruoget , kosiirok . 
Ak inye Kapernaum , tos tun kitororin iwe kipsengwet ? Kiwirjinin ng’ony kot iit oldab che kigobek .
Inendet ne kasok kogasa agane ; ak inendet ne esiok koesioa agane ; ak inendet ne esioa koesioi inendet ne kiiyokwa .
Kiweek anyun bichoto tamanwogik tisabu eng’ boiboindo , ak komwa kole , Kiptaiyandani , agot oik kogasech it eng’ kaineng’ung’ . 
Ak kilenji , Kiageer Setani kochorugei eng’ kipsengwet ko u kalyelet . 
Ogeero , kaagonok kamuget si kobiit otiech erenok ak melmelwek , ak oterter kimnatet tugul ne bo bunyot : ak mami kiy ne imuchi kong’emak . 
Ago amoboiboitu amu ng’olyondoni , amu kasok it oik ; ago oboiboitu amu sirotin kainaikwok eng’ kipsengwet .
Eng’ sainato kobaibait Jesus eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak kole , Aweegun kongoi , ee Baba , Kiptaiyat ne bo kipsengwet ak ng’ony , amu kiiung’e tuguchu che ng’omen ak che ingen , ak kiing’ang’ji manyurunik : ee , Baba ; amu kichamak ko u noto eng’ taing’ung’ .
Kigogona tuguk tugul Baba : ak mami chi ne ingen Werit kole ng’o , kobate Kwanda ; ama nai chi Kwanda kole ng’o , kobate Werit , ak chi age tugul ne chamei Werit , kong’ang’jin .
Ak kiweleljigei alamalyet , ak kolenji eng’ ung’ot , Iberurotin konyek che keerei tuguk che ogeere : 
amu amwawok ale , kimachei maotik che chang’ ak laitorinik kogeer tuguk che ogeere , ago kima keer ; ak kimachei kogas tuguk che ogase , ago kima kas .
Ogeero , kitonon ng’omotiot age ne bo ng’atutik koyom inendet , kole , Konetindoni , ayai nee si tun anyoru sobondab koigeny ? 
Ak kilenji , Kigisir nee eng’ Ng’atutik ? Isomandoi ano ? 
Ak kiwolji inendet kolenji , Cham Kiptaiyat Jehovah neng’ung’ eng’ muguleldang’ung’ komugul , ak eng’ sobondang’ung’ komugul , ak eng’ kimnateng’ung’ komugul , ak eng’ ng’omnateng’ung’ komugul ; ak icham chitab kokweng’ung’ ko u ye ichamdoige . 
Ak kilenji , Kewolu komie : yai ko u noto , si isob .
Ago ye kimachei komieitgei , kolenji Jesu , Ng’o chitab kokwennyu ?
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kichortaegei chito age Jerusalem kwo Jeriko ; ak kotuiyo ak rebik , che kirebe ngoroik ak kobir , ak koba , kobagakta ko negit kome . 
Ak kichortaegei tisiindet age oranato : ak kingogeer inendet korob taban . 
Ak ye kingoit Lawindet yoto , ak kogeer , korob taban agine ko u noto . 
Ago ye kita kowendi Samarindet age eng’ bandanyi , koit ye mi chichoto : ak ye kingogeer inendet , korire , 
kwo ole mi inendet , koratyi ole kagibir , ak kosachinot mwaita ak divaik ; ak kiganapchi chichoto sigiriennyi , ak komut kwo gotab toek , ak korib inendet . 
Ak mutai konem denarisiek aeng’ , kogochi chitab kobo got , ak kolenji , Rib inendet ; ak tuguk alak tugul che inyae che siirei chu , kotun kaweege , anyo ayaagun . 
Eng’ chuto somok , ilen ng’o ne kiek chitab kokwennyi eng’ chichoto kituiye rebik ? 
Ak kile , Inendet ne kiriregei chichoto . Ak kilenji Jesu , Ui , iyai ko u noto .
Ak ye kita komi bandanywa , komong’ji anyun nganaset age : ak kitaach eng’ gonnyi kobogoriot age ne keguure Marta . 
Ak kitinyei chepkamet ne kiguure Maria , ne kitebyei eng’ ole bo kelyekab Kiptaiyat , kogasei ng’olyondennyi . 
Ago kiimgei Marta eng’ boisionik che chang’ ; ak konyonji inendet ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , meiti kiy ak kabagakta tupchennyu abois anege ? Mwachi anyun kotoreta . 
Ago kiwolji Kiptaiyat kolenji , Marta , Marta , igereri met ak iimige agobo tuguk che chang’ : 
ago kit agenge ne kemachei : amu kagolewen Maria kebeberta ne mie , ne magirebe .
Ak ye kita kosaei eng’ oldo age , ak kingoges, kolenji age eng’ alamalyennyi , Kiptaiyandani , tos inetech kesa , ko u ye kiineti Johana alamalaikchik ?
Ak kilenji ichek , Ye osae , omwa ole , Kwandanyo , ingotililit kaineng’ung’ . Ingonyo bounateng’ung’ . [Ingoyaak mageng’ung’ ko u eng’ kipsengwet , ko u noto eng’ ng’ony .] 
Konech amitwogikyok eng’ betut age tugul . 
Ak inyoiywech kaat tengekwogikyok ; amu achek kenyochini kaat besenikyok . Amemutech ole mi yomset .
Ak kilenji , Ng’o eng’ okwek ne tinyei choruet , ak kwo ole mi kemoi kwen , ak kolenji , Choruani , kona makatinik somok abesen ; 
amu kagoit choruennyu ne bunu rutoi , amatinye kiy ne agochini ; 
kowolji ne mi go , kolenji , Amat iima : kaager kurget , ak kageruiye ak lagokyuk ; ma amuchi ang’eet agonin ? 
Amwawok ale , agot ngo mang’eet kogochi , amu choruennyi , ko amu somsennyi ko noto ne igochin kong’eet kogochi kiy tugul ne machei . 
Ak amwawok agane ale , Osom , si kegonok ; ocheng’ , si onyoru ; ogongony , si keyatwok . 
Amu age tugul ne somei , kigochin ; ak nyoru ne cheng’ei ; ak inendet ne igongonyi keyatyin . 
Ak ng’o eng’ okwek kwanda ne ngo som werit makatiat , ko tos igochi koita ? Anan ngo som njiriot, ko tos igochi erenet kogeere njiriot ? 
Anan ngo som koitab ingok , ko tos igochi melmeldo ? 
Ngongen okwek che o yaach ogochi lagokwok tuguk che miach , siirei anyun ne tia kagoitoet ne igochin Kwandang’wong’ ne mi kipsengwet Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ichek che somei inendet ?
Ak kion inendet oindet ne namat kut . Ak ye kingo kagomanda oindet , kong’alal anyun ne ki namat kut ; ak kikwong’io tuiyosiek . 
Ago kile alak , Onei oik eng’ Beelsebul , laitoriat ne bo oik . 
Ak kitiem alak inendet komage kaborunet ne bunu kipsengwet . 
Ago kinai inendet kabwatutikwak , kolenji , Bororiet age tugul ne pchegei ko ng’emaksei ; ak got age tugul ne pchegei kolulei . 
Ak ngo pchegei agine Setani , kotonondoi ano bororiennyi ? Amu omwae ole , aone oik eng’ Beelsebul . 
Ngot aone oik eng’ Beelsebul , koonei werikwok eng’ ng’o ? Noto anyun ne igochin icheget koek kiruogikwok . 
Ago ngot aone oik eng’ mornetab Jehovah , ko kanyonjok anyun bounatetab Jehovah .
Ak chi ne tinyei kimnatet ak kotinyei karikyik che ribe gonnyi , kotebyei tugukyik eng’ kalyet : 
ak ye nyonji chito ne kim kosiir inendet , ak koterter , korebe anyun inendet karikyik tugul che cham komang’u , ak kopcheita bareiywekyik . 
Inendet ne magimi tuwai kogirindaa ; ak inendet ne magiyumi tuwai koiyestooti .
Ye kagomanda tamirmiriet ne muruon eng’ chito , kosiir ole mami beek , kocheng’oti ole imuung’e ; ak ye mata konyor , komwa anyun kole , Kaweektege gonnyu ole kiabunu . 
Ak ye it , konyor kobugot ak ko chobot . 
Kwo anyun , komut tamirmirik tisab alak che yaachen kosiir inendet ; kochut anyun orit ak komeny oloto : ak yaitu kagesunetab chichoto kosiir ne bo tai .
Ak ye kita komwaei ng’alechu , komwa kobogoriot age eng’ tuiyet , kole, Iberurot moet ne kisichin , ak kinaik che kiirerie . 
Ago kile inendet , Iberurotin kosiir che kasei ng’olyotab Jehovah , ak korib .
Ak ye kingoyumjingei inendet tuiyosiek , kotoi komwa kole , Ibini , ko ibinda ne ya : cheng’ei kaborunet ; ago magigochin kaborunet kobate kaborunetab Jona . 
Amu ko u ye kiek kaborunet Jona eng’ bikab Ninebe , ko u noto Weritab chi eng’ ibini . 
Tun ng’eetei laitoriat kobogoriot ne bo murot ne bo tai eng’ kiruoget koboto bikab ibini , ak koruokyi ichek : amu kibun tabanwekab emet konyo kogas ng’omnatetab Solomon ; ak ogeero , mitei yu ne o kosiir Solomon . 
Tun tonondos bikab Ninebe ak ibini eng’ kiruoget , ak koruokyi : amu kisik ichek eng’ amdaetab Jona ; ak ogeero , mi yu ne o kosiir Jona .
Mami chi ne ngo kagonaam tait , konde ole ung’at , anan kitonget orit , ago indoi kit ne tonone , si kobiit kogeer lapkeiyet che bendi go . 
Taitab bortang’ung’ kondang’ung’ : ngo mie kondang’ung’ , ko nyiitat bortang’ung’ komugul lapkeiyet ; ago ngo ya kondang’ung’ ko nyiitat bortang’ung’ agine mesundeito . 
Keer anyun ngo lapkeiyet ne mi oring’ung’ ko mesundeito . 
Ngo nyiitat bortang’ung’ komugul lapkeiyet , ama tinyei ye imen , kolapkeitu anyun bortang’ung’ tugul , ko u ye konin lapkeiyet tait ne ikweng’sei komie .
Ak ye kita kong’alali , koguur Parisaindet age kwo koamis tuwai : ak kiwa go ak koteb ng’ony koamis . 
Ak ye kingogeer Parisaindet , kokwong’ , amu kiamis ama iun eut korok . 
Kolenji Kiptaiyat , Okwek Parisaik , ouni barak kikombet ak sanit ; ago nyiitat oring’wong’ rebisiet ak yaitiet . 
Okwek che o berber ! inendet ne kiyaei sang’ ko ma ne kiyaei orit agine ? 
Ogoite kagochinoik che bo tuguk che mi orit ; ak ogeero, tililitu tuguk tugul eng’ okwek .
Ago bwa okwek Parisaik ! Amu ogoitoi kebebertab taman ne bo heduosmon ak ketik che mengech che ng’uu , ak che bo sogek alak tugul , ak ometoi kiruoget ak chamnyetab Jehovah : ago kita nyolu oyai chuto , amomete chun alak .
Bwa okwek Parisaik ! Amu ochame ng’echerok che tororen eng’ sunagogisiek , ak kagatosiek che kigatok eng’ oldinwekab aldaisiet . 
Bwa okwek ! Amu o kerge ak kererisiek che matoogu , ama naei bik che bunoti barak .
Ak kiwolji ng’omotiot age ne bo ng’atutik , kolenji , Konetindoni , ngot imwa ko u noto ko ketewerech agachek . 
Ak kole , Bwa okwek ng’omotikab Ng’atutik ! Amu oganapchini bik lautik che bichien eng’ laiset , ago okwek ko motwae lautichoto agot eng’ mornet agenge . 
Bwa okwek ! Amu oteeche kererisiekab maotik , ago kibarei kwanisiekwok . 
Kioegu anyun baorinik ak ochamnyechini boisionikab kwanisiekwok : amu icheget che kibarei ak oteeche okwek kererisiekwak . 
Kile anyun ng’omnatetab Jehovah amu noto , Tun ayokyini maotik ak che kiyoktoi ; ak kobar alak eng’ ichek ak kousaus alak ; 
si kobiit komage ibini , korotikab maotik tugul , che kigitumda koboch ko kagilumda ng’ony ; 
koboch korotikab Abil agoi korotikab Sakaria , ne kime eng’ kwenutab kaptisisiet ak gotab Jehovah : ee , amwawok ale , tun kimage ibini .
Bwa okwek ng’omotikab ng’atutik ! Amu kioib yateiywot ne bo ng’omnatet ama obe orit okweget , ak kioger che kita mong’jin .
Ak ye kingomong’ eng’ oloto , kotoi sirik ak Parisaik koriich inendet mising’ , ak kogilgilye , si kobiit komwa ng’alek che chang’ ; 
korib kole tamangab konyor ng’olyo ne mong’une kutinnyi .
Eng’ saisiechoto , ye kingoyumgei bik ng’isiat che bo tuiyet , kot kotiech ge ichegei , kosib kotoi kolenji alamalyennyi , Oribege mermerekab Parisaik , noto chombilisiet . 
Ago mami kiy ne tugot , ne matun king’anyei , anan ne ung’at , ne matun naaksei . 
Amu kiy age tugul ne omwae eng’ mesundeito kotun kegasei eng’ ole lapkei ; ak che kiochaamji itit eng’ got orit kotun kemwaitoi eng’ got barak .
Ak amwawok choronokyuk ale , Amoiywei che barei borto , yeityo ko mata komuch koyai kiy age . 
Ago ateeiywok si onai inendet ne kanyol oiywei : Oiywei inendet , ne ngo kagobar komuchi kowirji Gehenna ; ee , amwawok ale , Oiywei inendet . 
Tos magialdae taritik mut che mengechen kebebertab mut ne bo denarit ? Ama utie Jehovah agot agenge . 
Ago iitotin sumeek tugul che bo metowekwok . Amoiywei anyun : osiire okwek taritik che chang’ che mengechen .
Ak amwawok ale , Age tugul ne ibortaa eng’ taitab bik , kotun ibortoi agine Weritab chi chichoto eng’ taitab malaikaisiek che bo Jehovah . 
Ago inendet ne esioa eng’ taitab bik kotun keesioi agine eng’ taitab malaikaisiek che bo Jehovah .
Ak age tugul ne mwaei ng’olyo ne ya agobo Weritab chi , kenyochin kaat : ago inendet ne chubei Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ko maginyochin kaat inendet .
Ak ye kimutak oldab sunagogisiek , ak taitab kiruogik , ak bounik , ko mat ogerer met agobo kit ne owolu anan omwae : 
amu inetok Tamirmiriet ne Tilil eng’ sainato kit ne nyolu omwa .
Kilenji anyun chito age eng’ tuiyet , Konetindoni , mwachi werit ne kitupche kopcheiywa tugukyok . 
Ago kilenji inendet , Chichi , ng’o ne kindea aek kiruogindet anan pcheindet eng’ okwek ?
Ak kilenji ichek , Ogeer , ak oripge eng’ kasetab miat tugul : amu matebyei sobondab chi eng’ chang’indab tuguk che tinyei . 
Ak kimwachi kalewenet kolenji , Kimi magoriot age ne kiga rur mbarennyi mising’ : 
ak kiibwat eng’ muguleldanyi kole , Ayae nee , amu matinye ole agonore bekyuk ? 
Ak kile , Ayae ko u ni : abute chogenikyuk , si ateech che eechen kosiir chu : si agonore bekyuk ak tugukyuk tugul che miach . 
Si alenji sobondanyu , Sobondanyu , itinye tuguk che chang’ che miachen che konorotin che yamei kenyisiek che chang’ ; imuuny , amisie , eeise , ak ibaibaitu . 
Ago kilenji Jehovah , I berber inye , kimachei sobondang’ung’ kemouni bo ra ; ara , si kobunji ng’o anyun , tuguchoto koichob ? 
U noto anyun chito ne konorjingei magornatet inegei , ne ma magorio eng’ Jehovah .
Kilenji anyun alamalyennyi , Noto anyun amwawok ale , Amogerer met agobo sobeng’wong’ , eng’ tuguk che oame ; anan agobo borwekwok , eng’ tuguk che olaachi . 
Amu siirei sobet amitwogik , ak siirei borto ngoroik . 
Obwat chepkuginik , amu magolei , ama kesei ; ama tinyei ole konore anan choget ; ago Jehovah ne baei : osiire taritik konyil ata ! 
Ak ng’o eng’ okwek ne imuchi kogerer met si kotes koindanyi eng’ kakwautiet agenge ne bo eut ? 
Ngo momuchi anyun oyai agot kiy kitigin , ko amu nee anyun si ogerer met agobo tuguk alak ? 
Obwat taptok , ole bititoi : maboisiei , anan koletis ; ago amwawok ale , Agot Solomon , eng’ talbistanyi tugul , ko kima kolumegei ko u age eng’ chuto . 
Ago ngolaaksechin Jehovah ko u noto suswek che bo kewet che mi ra , ak mutai kewirji ma , kotos siirei ne tia anyun kolaaksewok okwek , che otinye kayanet ne ming’in ?
Amocheng’ che oame , anan che oee , amosage . 
Amu cheng’ei tuguchuto tugul bororiosiekab ng’ony : ago ingen Kwandang’wong’ kole omakyinige tuguchuto . 
Ago ocheng’ okwek bounatetab Jehovah , si keteswok tuguchuto tugul .
Amoiywei , okwek akwet ne ming’in ; amu baibai Kwandang’wong’ kogonok bounatet . 
Oalde che otinye , si ogoite kagochinoik ; onapchige suberok che maosegitu , konoruet eng’ kipsengwetisiek ne mabegu , ole marikyin chorik , ama ng’emei kiptorotinik . 
Amu ole mi konorueng’ung’ , ko oloto ole mi muguleldang’ung’ agine .
Ongogermenogis suenutikwok , ak ongolalyo taisiekwok ; 
ak ogergeitu ak bik che igeni kiptaiyandenywa , kobunu igortab katunisiet : si ye nyo ak kogongony , koyatyi ngunoto . 
Boiboen otwogichoto , che nyoru kiptaiyandanato koripsei ye nyo : amwawok iman ale , kermenigei inendet , ak chobei bichoto koteb ng’ony eng’ ole amisie , ak kwo kobai ichek . 
Ak ngo nyo eng’ ripset ne bo aeng’ , anan ne bo somok , ak konyorta ko u noto , ko boiboen anyun otwogichoto . 
Ago onai ni ole , nda kiingen kiptaiyatab got sait ne nyonei chorindet , ta kiripsei , ta kima kobagaktoi gonnyi kobut chorindet . 
Ochopge ak okwek : amu nyonei Weritab chi eng’ sait ne mobwati .
Kilenji anyun Petero , Kiptaiyandani , imwawech achek kalewenoni , anan imwachini bik tugul ? 
Kole anyun Kiptaiyat , Ng’o anyun ribindet ne kiyani ak ko ng’om , ne indoi kiptaiyandennyi kotononji gonnyi , ak kogochi amitwogikwak che yamei eng’ betut ne makyin ? 
Baibai otwogindonoto , ne nyoru kiptaiyandennyi koyaei ko u noto . 
Amwawok iman ale , indoi chichoto kotononji tugukyik tugul . 
Ago ngo mwa otwogindonoto eng’ muguleldanyi , kole , Igaegei kiptaiyandennyu masib koitu ; ak kotoi kobir otwogik che murenik ak che tibik , ak koamis ak koeeiso , ak kobogit ; 
weeksei anyun kiptaiyat ne bo otwogindonoto eng’ betut ne kama kogeni , ak eng’ sait ne manaei , ak kobir mising’ , ak kopchechi kebebertanyi koboto che matinyei kayanet . 
Ak otwogindonoto , ne kiingen magetab kiptaiyandennyi , ama kochopgei , anan koyai ko u magennyi , kebire birutik che chang’ ; 
ago inendet ne kima kongen , ak koyai tuguk che nyoljin biret , kebirei birutik che ng’ering’en . Ak age tugul ne kigigochi che chang’ , kotun kimage che chang’ : ak inendet ne kigigochi korib tuguk che chang’ , kotun kimage inendet che siirei .
Kianyo awirji mat ng’ony ; nee anyun ne ta amache , ngo kagolal nguno . 
Ago atinye kabatisanet ne tatun kibatisanena ; kamarigitya ne tia agoi kosulda ! 
Tos olen kianyo agonu kalyet konyo ng’ony ? Amwawok ale , Achicha ; ago besiet : 
amu koboch nguno kopchegei bik mutu che mi got agenge , surie somogu aeng’ , ak kosurie aeng’ somok . 
Pchegei , kwanda ak werit , ak werit ak kwanda ; kamet ak cheptanyi , ak chepto ak kamet ; kametab werit ak osotiondennyi , ak osotiotab werit , ak kametab werit .
Kimwachi anyun tuiyet kolenji , Ye ogeer kotogosune boldet cherongo , ole , Machei korobon ; ak koyaak ko u noto anyun . 
Ak ye ogeer usonet ne usune murot ne bo tai , ole, Machei koit kemeut ne ng’wan ; ak koyaak ko u noto . 
Chombilichu ! ongen obesie ole teptoi ng’ony ak kipsengwet ; kalya anyun si monai ole teptoi betusiechu ?
Kalya si moruoch okwege agobo tuguk che bo imanda ? 
Amu ye ta obendi ak bunyondeng’ung’ taitab kiruogindet , igiilge obendi eng’ oret si kounden ; si mata komutin taitab kiruogindet , ak komutyin kiruogindet askarindet , ak kotoorjin askarindet korgoret . 
Amwaun ale , Magoi imong’une oloto , agoi iyaakte sendeiyot ne bo let .
Kimi bik alage eng’ betusiechoto che kimwachi inendet agobo Galilik , che kiburuch Pilato korotikwak ak tiseiywekwak . 
Ak kowolji kolenji , Tos olen ki kiptengeginik bichoto bo Galili kosiir Galilik tugul , amu kinyor nyalilwogichu ? 
Amwawok ale , Achicha : ago , ngot ko mosigu okwek , olustosi okwek tugul ko u noto . 
Anan choto taman ak sisiit , che kisieb got ne koi ne bo Siloam , ak kobar , tos olen ki kiptengeginik kosiir bik tugul che kimenyei Jerusalem ? 
Amwawok ale , Achicha : ago , ngot ko mosigu ak okwek , olustosi tugul ko u noto .
Ak kimwa kalewenoni , kolenji , Kimi chito age ne kitinyei mogoiywet ne kiga minji mbarennyi ne bo sabibuk ; ak kinyo kocheng’ logoekab ketoto , amanyorji kiy . 
Kolenji ribindetab mbaretab sabibuk , Keero , kenyini ko ne bo somok anyone acheng’e logoek eng’ mogoiywoni amanyorune kiy : eb kolul ; amu nee si koamei ng’ung’unyek buch ? 
Ak kiwolji kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , ingotebi kenyini agine , si kota asemberji ak ande ng’atatek : 
ak ngo ii logoek kong’eete nguno , ko mie ; ak ngo maii , ieb anyun kolul .
Ak kiinetisiei eng’ sunagogit age eng’ betutab sabato . 
Ak ogeero , kobogoriot age ne kitinyei tamirmiriet ne bo nyalulet kenyisiek taman ak sisiit ; ak kigarigak , ak kima kota komuchi kochuulgei agot kitigin . 
Ak kingogeer Jesu inendet , koguur ak kolenji , Kobogoriondoni , kagitiachin eng’ nyaluleng’ung’ . 
Ak kiigonoor eunekyik inendet : kochuulak ngunoto , ak kolos Jehovah . 
Kinerech anyun bounindetab sunagogit , amu kiisoob Jesu chito eng’ betutab sabato , ak komwachi tuiyet kolenji , Mitei betusiek lo che nyolu koboisie bik : obwa anyun eng’ betusiechoto si kisoobok , ama eng’ betutab sabato .
Ago kiwolji Kiptaiyat, kolenji , Okwek chombilik , tos mayatei age tugul eng’ okwek eitanyi anan sigiriennyi eng’ bii eng’ betutab sabato, ak kokweri koee beek ? 
Ak kobogoriondoni , ne cheptab Abraham , ne kigorat Setani kenyisiechu taman ak sisiit , tos manyol kitiach eng’ ratutioni eng’ betutab sabato ? 
Ak ye kingota komwaei tuguchu , kolilanso bunikyik tugul : ago kiboiboitu tuiyet komugul agobo tuguk che tororen che kiyaei inendet .
Kimwa anyun , kole , Kergei bounatetab Jehovah ak nee ? Ak tos aroge nee ? 
Kergei ak keswotab karadali , ne kinam chito , ak kominji mbarennyi ; ak kibit , agoi koek ketit ; ak kitebe taritik che bo barak temenikyik .
Ak kimwa kogeny kole , Aroge nee bounatetab Jehovah ? 
Kergei ak mermerek , che kinam kobogoriot , ak koburukto busiek che bo kitongok somok , agoi kogut tugul .
Ak kibunot nganasok che eechen ak che mengech , konetisioti, kobunei oret ne wendi Jerusalem . 
Ak kilenji chito age , Kiptaiyandani , tos ng’ering’ che tun kisoru ? Ak kilenji , 
Ogiilge obun kurget ne mariich : amu amwawok ale , cheng’ei tun che chang’ kobun yoto , ago matun imuchi . 
Ak ye tun kang’eet chitab kobo got , ak koger kurget , ak otau anyun otononse eng’ sang’ , ak ogongony kurget , ole , Kiptaiyandani , yatwech ; ak kowolwok inendet kole , Mangenok , ak ole obunu ; 
otau anyun ole , Kigiamisiei ak kigiee eng’ taing’ung’ , ak kiinetisiei eng’ ortinwekyok ; 
ak tun mwaei kole , Mangen ole obunu ; oba eng’ ane , okwek tugul yaikab tengek . 
Koek anyun rirek ak nyeetab kelek, ye tun ogeer Agraham, ak Isak, ak Jakobo, ak maotik tugul, eng’ bounatetab Jehovah, ak kewirjok okweget sang’ . 
Ak tun bwanei kobunu kong’asis ak cherongo , ak murot ne bo katam ak murot ne bo tai , ak koteb ng’ony koamis eng’ bounatetab Jehovah . 
Ak ogeero , mi che bo let che tun egu che bo tai , ak mitei che bo tai che tun egu che bo let .
Kibwa Parisaik alak eng’ sainato , ak kolenji , Ng’eet mande , ui eng’ oli : amu machei kobarin Herod . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Oba omwachi lelwandonoto , olenji , Keero , aone oik ak asoobi bik rani ak mutai , ak eng’ betutab somok abegechi . 
Ago kanyol awo bandanyu rani ak mutai ak betut ne bo somok : amu manyoljin komechi maotiondo oldo age kobate Jerusalem .
Ee , Jerusalem , Jerusalem , inye ne ibare maotik , ak ilage koik che kiyogun ! Kiamach konyil ata ayum lagoguk , ko u ngogiet ne iyumjin arekyik kebebaikyik , ago kima ocham ! 
Ogeero , kagebagakwok gong’wong’ koek kipkubere : ak amwawok ale , Maogeera , agoi tun ole , Iberurot ne nyonei eng’ kainetab Kiptaiyat .
Ak ye kingwo gotab age eng’ bounik che bo Parisaik eng’ betutab sabato , si koamis , koribot ichek inendet . 
Ak ogeero , kimi chi tainnyi ne ki lolosenot borto . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu ng’omotikab ng’atutik ak Parisaik , kolenji , Tos chamdaat eng’ ng’atutik kisoob chi eng’ betutab sabato , anan achicha ? 
Ago kisisyo . Ak kinam inendet , ak kosoob , ak kounda kwo . 
Ak kolenji icheget , Ng’o eng’ okwek ne tinyei sigiriet anan eito ne kagobutyo keringet , ama sutu eng’ sainato eng’ betutab sabato ? 
Ak kimata komuch anyun kowolji inendet kogeny agobo tuguchuto .
Ak kimwachi kalewenet che kiga kiguur , ye kingogeer ole lewendoi ng’echerok che bo tai ; kolenji ichek , 
Ye kaguurjin chi age tugul igortab katunisiet , ko metebe ng’echeret ne bo tai ; amu abere kagiguur age ne konyitot kosiirin , 
si ye nyo inendet ne kaguurok okwek tuwai , komwaun kole , Istochige chichi ; itau anyun iwe ole bo let eng’ kalilanet . 
Ago ye kiguurin , itebe olo bo let ; ak ye nyo anyun ne kaguurin , komuchi kolenjin , Choruani , ui olin bo tai : inyoru anyun teegisto eng’ che oamisiei tugul . 
Amu age tugul ne itororigei kiming’ini ; ak inendet ne iming’inegei kitorori .
Kimwachi anyun chichoto kiga kuurso agine , kolenji , Ye ichob amitwogik che bo bet anan che bo koskoleny , ko mat iguur choronoguk , anan che otupche , anan tilionutiguk , anan magorek che bo kokwet ; abere tos kuurin agichek , ak koweegun cheguk . 
Ago ye ichob igorta , iguur kibananok , ak che bo mugungon , ak che ing’waldos , ak che koriotin : 
si kiberurin ; amu matinyei icheget che weegun : amu tun kiweegun eng’ ng’eetyetab che bo iman .
Ak kingogas tuguchuto chito age ne kimi koboto inendet eng’ amisiet , kolenji , Baibai inendet ne tun amisiei eng’ bounatetab Jehovah .
Ago kilenji , Kichob chito age amitwogik che chang’ che bo koskoleny ; ak koguur bik che chang’ : 
ak kiiyokto otwogindennyi eng’ saitab amitwogik , koguur che kiga kemwachi , kolenji , Obwa ; amu kagochobogis tuguk tugul . 
Ak kotoi tugul eng’ maget agenge komwa kit ne karany . Kilenji chito ne bo tai , Kaal mbaret , kanyolja awo ageer : asomin ale nyoiywa kaat . 
Kole age , Kaal eik taman che bo chogit , kawe atiem ichek : asomin ale nyoiywa kaat . 
Kole age , Kaatunisie , noto anyun mamuchi anyo . 
Konyo anyun otwogindonoto , ak kotetyi kiptaiyandennyi ng’alechuto tugul . Konerech anyun chitab kobo got , ak kolenji otwogindennyi , Ui chakte ortinwek che eechen ak che mengechen che bo nganaset , ak imutu yu kibananok , ak che bo mugungon ak che koriotin ak che ing’waldos . 
Ak kile otwogindonoto , Kiptaiyandani , kagoyaak kit ne kageng’at , ago ta komi boroindo . 
Kolenji anyun kiptaiyat otwogindennyi , Ui ortinwek che eechen ak kiwotosiekab mbarenik , ak ichiich kobwa go , si konyi gonnyu . 
Amu amwawok ale , mami agot agenge eng’ che kiga kemwachi ne chamjami amitwogikyuk .
Ak kiba ak inendet tuiyosiek che chang’ : ak kiwelelgei inendet ak kolenji , 
Ngo nyonja chi , ama wech kwanda , ak kamet , ak osotiondennyi , ak lagokyik , ak werik che tupcho , ak chepkametinik , ee ak sobondanyi agine , ko maimuchi koek alamalyennyu . 
Ak chi age tugul ne maibei kimurtoiyondennyi , ak kosubwa , ko maimuchi koek alamalyennyu . 
Amu ng’o eng’ okwek , ne machei koteech got ne koi , ama toi koteb ng’ony korok ak koiit tuguk , ngo tinyei che yamei kogesune got ? 
Si ma ye kagotonon lumeiywot , ak koma komuch koges , kotoi kochurachur inendet tugul che keerei , 
kole , Kitoi chichi koteekso ago ma imuch koges .
Anan ng’o laitoriat ne wendi kobaregei ak laitoriat age , ama teb ng’ony korok ak korar ole teptoi , ngo tos imuchi inendet ak bik elfusiek taman kotuiyo ak ne setyin inendet ak bik elfusiek tiptem ? 
Anan , ye ta komi age ole loo , koyokto ng’olyot , si koteeb agobo kalyet .
