Noto anyun , chi age tugul eng’ okwek ne mabagaktoi tugukyik tugul , ko maimuchi koek alamalyennyu .
Miachen munyuk : ago ngo kagogesgei anyinyindanyi , ko ta kianyinye nee ? 
Ma kotilei kiy eng’ emet anan eng’ kapng’atat : kilaktoi . Inendet ne tinyei itik che kastoe , kogas .
Ak kirikyi inendet taagikab aisurut tugul ak kiptengeginik si kobiit kogas inendet . 
Ak kiing’unyng’ung’so Parisaik ak sirik , kole , Taachei chichi kiptengeginik , ak koamisiei tugul . 
Ak kimwachi ichek kalewenoni, kolenji , 
Ng’o chi eng’ okwek , ne tinyei kechirek bogol , ak ngobeet agenge eng’ choto , ko tos mabagaktoi choto tamanwogik sogol ak sogol eng’ surkwen , ak kwo kocheng’at noto kabet , agoi konyor ? 
Ak ye kigonyor , konde tigikyennyi , ak kobaibait . 
Ak ye kagoit ga , koguur choronokyik koboto bikab kokwennyi koyumgei , ak kolenji , Ongeboiboitu tugul , amu kaanyoru kechiriennyu ne koga bet . 
Amwawok ale , egu ko u noto tun agine boiboiyet eng’ kipsengwet agobo kiptengekyot agenge ne kasik , ne siirei bik che bo iman tamanwogik sogol ak sogol , che mamage kiy sigunet .
Ng’o kobogoriot ne tinyei fedaisiek taman , ak ngobeet fedaiyat agenge , kotos mainaami tait ak kobuch got , ak kocheng’ mising’ agoi konyor ? 
Ak ye kagonyor , koguur anyun choronokyik koboto bikab kokwennyi koyumgei ak kole , Ongeboiboitu tugul , amu kaanyoru fedaiyandennyu ne koga kobet . 
U noto anyun, amwawok ale , mi boiboiyet eng’ taitab malaikaisiekab Jehovah eng’ kiptengekyot agenge ne kasik .
Ak kimwa kole , Kimi chi anum ne kitinyei werik aeng’ : 
ak kilenji werit ne ming’in kwandanyi , Aba , kona tuguk che ka tatun bunjina . Ak kipchechi ichek tugukyik . 
Ak kingobata betusiek che matia koyum weroto ming’in tugukyik tugul , ak kwo emet ne loo ; kwo koserser eng’ oloto tugukyik eng’ atepto ne ya . 
Ak kingo kagogesta tugul , konyo rubet ne o emonoto ; kotoi anyun kobanan . 
Ak kiwa kogakta chito age ne bo emonoto ; ak kiiyokto kwo koyaga torok eng’ mbaret . 
Ak kimachei mising’ kole kobiyo metetek che kiamei torok : amu ma igochi chi kiy . 
Ak kingobwat , komwa kole , Tia otwogik che bo baba che tinyei amitwogik che yamei kot kosiir , ago ane , ko kabara rubo eng’ yu ! 
Ang’eete ak awe oldab baba , alenji , Baba , kiachalwogenji kipsengwet ak kiachalwogen eng’ taing’ung’ : 
ma ko nyoljina kota keguurena wering’ung’ : ingaek ko u age eng’ otwogiguk . 
King’eet anyun kwo oldab kwandanyi . Ago , ye kita komi ole loo , kogeer inendet kwandanyi , ak korire inendet , ak kilabat kwo kosuub kaatit , ak kong’utut .
Ak kilenji werit , Baba , kiachalwogenji kipsengwet , ak kiachalwogen eng’ taing’ung’ : ma ko nyoljina kota keguurena wering’ung’ . 
Ago kilenji kwanda otwogikyik , Oibu ochogune ngoriet ne kararan ne siirei tugul , ak olaakyi ; ak ondechi peteit mornennyi , ak olaakyi kweonik : 
ak ogetu moita ne nerat , ak oeny , si keam , ak keboiboitu : 
amu werinnyu ni , ne kiga kome , ago kagosob kogeny ; kiga kobet , ak kagobiit . Kitoi anyun koboiboitu .
Ak kimi werinnyi ne o mbar : ak kingorik ye negit got , kogas cheetab tiendo ak ureriet . 
Ak kiguur age eng’ otwogik , ak koteebe kole , nee tuguchu . 
Ak kilenji , Kagoit ng’etab komet ; ak kagoeng’ji kwandang’ung’ moita ne nerat , amu kagotaach inendet kochamegei . 
Ago kinerech , ak kiesio kwo go : ak kimong’ sang’ kwandanyi , kogaigai . 
Ago kiwolji kwandanyi kolenji , Keero , kiaotin eng’ kenyisiechu chang’ , ama abut ng’atutieng’ung’ : ak kima igona arua , si keboiboitu ak choronokyuk : 
ago ye kangonyo weritang’ung’et , ne kigoam tuguguk ak chepkugonik , ieng’ji anyun moita ne nerat . 
Ak kilenji , Weri , kimi tuwai kotugul , ak tugukyuk tugul ko cheguk . 
Ago kanyolu keboiboitu ak kigasge : amu kiga kome weri otupche , ago kagosob kogeny ; kiga kobet , ago kagobiit .
Ak kilenji inendet alamalyennyi kogeny , Kimi chi anum ne ki magorio , ne kitinyei ribindet ne kitononjin gonnyi ; ak kigimwaita chichoto eng’ tainnyi kele , iserseri tugukab magoriondonoto . 
Ak kiguur inendet kolenji , Nee ni agase agobo inye ? Konu koitetab ripseng’ung’ ; amu ma iegu ribindet kogeny . 
Ak kile ribindonoto eng’ muguleldanyi , Ayae nee anyun , amu kagoistaa kiptaiyandennyu eng’ boisiet ? Amatinye kimnatet ne abatisie ; ak ngale , Asomso , alilani . 
Kaanai kit ne ayae , si ye kageona eng’ boisiet , kotaacha eng’ gorikwak . 
Ak kingoguur age tugul eng’ besenikab kiptaiyandennyi , kolenji ne bo tai , Kiibesen ata tugukab kiptaiyandennyu ? 
Kole , Terenik bogol che bo mwanik . Ak kilenji , Nam kartasing’ung’ , ak iteb ng’ony si isir konom , ichokyi . 
Yeityo kolenji age , Kiibesen ata inye ? Kole , Terenik bogol che bo nganok . Kolenji , Nam kartasing’ung’ , si isir tamanwogik sisiit .
Ak kiichoi kiptaiyandennyi otwogindonoto kima ko bo imanda amu kayai eng’ ng’omnatet : amu ng’omen werikab ng’onyuni eng’ ibindanywa kosiir werikab lapkeiyet .
Ak amwawok ale , Oyachige choronok eng’ oretab magornatosiek che ma bo imanda ; si ye tun igesgei , ko tun kotaachak eng’ gorik che bo koigeny . 
Inendet ne kiyani eng’ che ng’ering’ , kiyani agine eng’ che chang’ : ak inendet ne magiyani eng’ che ng’ering’ ko magiyani agot eng’ che chang’ . 
U noto anyun , ngo kima oegu che kiyani eng’ magornatosiek che ma bo imanda , ko ng’o ne tos iyanak eng’ magornatosiek che bo imanda ? 
Ak ngo kimata oegu che kiyani eng’ tugukab chito age , ko tos ng’o anyun ne konok tuguk che chekwok ?
Ma mi otwogindet ne imuchi koot kiptainik aeng’ : amu tos wech age , ak kocham age ; anan konamgei ak age , kosas age . Momuchi oot Jehovah ak magornatet .
Ak kigas Parisaik tuguchuto tugul . Kichamei siling’isiek icheget , ak kororechi inendet . 
Ak kilenji , Okweget che omieitige eng’ taitab bik ; ago ingen Jehovah mugulelwekwok : amu kit ne itorori bik ko wegot mising’ eng’ taitab Jehovah .
Kitebi Ng’atutik ak maotik agoi koit Johana : koboch betunoto keamdoi logoiywek che miach che bo bounatetab Jehovah , ak komong’jin chi tugul eng’ kimnatet . 
Ago nyamnyum kosiirto kipsengwet ak ng’ony , kosiir kobut sirutiet agenge ne bo Ng’atutik .
Age tugul ne onei osotiondennyi , ak kotun age , ko kabaigei : ak chito ne ituni inendet ne kigoon manong’otiot ko kabaigei .
Ak kimi chi anum ne ki magorio ne kiilaachi ngoroik che arusen ne birir , ak che bo katanit ne kararan , ak kibaibai betut age tugul , ak kotalbisi : 
ak kimi kibanania ne kigiguure Lasaro ne kigimogoni eng’ kurgennyi , ak ki nyiitat mook bortanyi , 
ak kimachei kebae tuguk che ibutos eng’ mesetab magoriondonoto ; ee , kibwa agot sesenik ak komel mookyik .
Ak kime kibananiandanato betut age , komut inendet malaikaisiek konde tegetab Abraham : ak kime agine magoriondonoto , ak kigitub . 
Ak ye kimi oldab che kigobek konyal barak , komi nyalilda ne o , kogeer Abraham komi ole loo , komi Lasaro tegennyi . 
Ak kiite kole , Baba Abraham , rirena , ak iyogu Lasaro , koting’e beek walitab mornennyi , si kotiswa ng’elyeptanyu , amu ami ng’wanindo mising’ eng’ mai lalei . 
Ago kile Abraham , Weri , ibwat ile kingota isobe ko kiinyoru tuguguk che miach , ki u noto Lasaro , kinyoru tuguk che yaach : ago nguno kigoigoi inendet eng’ yu , ago inye , imi ng’wanindo ne o . 
Ak ne siirei chu tugul , ko kiginde chemng’eisut ne o ne ioitosech achek ak okwek , si che machei kolong’ olo omi ko maimuchi , ak che machei kolong’ ole kimi ko maimuchi . 
Ak kile , Asain anyun , baba , ale , iyokte inendet kwo oldab baba ; 
amu atinye che kitupche mut ; kwo koteechi ichek , si mabwa ole mi nyalilda ne o . 
Ak kilenji Abraham , Tinyei ichek Musa ak maotik ; ingogas ichek . 
Ago kile , Achicha , baba Abraham : ago ngot kwo chi ole mi ichek ne bunei oldab che kigobek , kosigu . 
Ak kilenji , Ngot ko magas Musa ak maotik , koesioi koyan agot chito ne ng’eetei eng’ che kigobek .
Kilenji alamalyennyi anyun , Bwanei kanagutik matiny : ago bwa eng’ chichoto bunu . 
Kita kaigai eng’ inendet kirooch kaatinnyi koitab bai ne o ak kewirji nyanjet , kosiir ye inachi age eng’ chu mengech . 
Oripge : ngochiliilun ne otupche , iger kong’ ; ak ngo sik , inyochi kaat . 
Ak ngo chalwogenjin konyil tisab eng’ betut agenge , ak ngo week ole imi konyil tisab kolen , Kaasigu ; inyochi kaat .
Ak kilenji che kiyoktoi Kiptaiyat , Teswech kayanennyo . 
Ak kile Kiptaiyat , Ndotinye kayanet ne u keswotab karadali , ko ye omwachi mogoiywoni , olenji , Kitutin , ak keminin eng’ nyanjet ; kogasok it .
Ago mi ng’o eng’ okwek ne tinyei otwogindet ne ibatisiei anan ne iyagi kechirek , ne lenjin , ye kait kobunu mbar , Nyo ngunoto ak itebi ng’ony iamisie , 
Tos ma kaigai kolenji inendet , Chobwa tuguk che aame , kermenge , ak iboisiewa , agoi aamisie ak aeeise ; si yeityo iamisie ak ieeise aginye ? 
Tos weekyin otwogindonoto kongoi amu kayai tuguk che kaga king’at ? 
U noto tun ak okwek , ye kaoyai tuguk tugul che kaging’atak , omwa ole , Ki otwogik che matilei kiy ; kageyai che kanyoljinech keyai .
Ak ye kimi oret kowendi Jerusalem , kobun kwenutab Samaria ak Galili . 
Ak kingomong’ji nganaset age , kotuiyo ak murenik taman che kiamei mogondosik , che kitonondos eng’ ole loo : 
ak kiwaach kole , Jesu Kiptaiyat , rirenech . 
Ak kingogeer ichek , kolenji , Oba oborjige tisiik . Ak ye kingab kaba , kotililitu . 
Ak kingogeer age eng’ ichek kole kagosob , koweek , kolosunonu Jehovah eng’ kutit ne o ; 
ak kiibutyi kelyekyik kogochi kongoi ; ak ki Samarindet chichoto . 
Ak kiwol Jesu kole , Kama kitilil taman ? Ago mi ano chugai sogolu ? 
Tos ma biit agot agenge ne kaweek kogochi kalosunet Jehovah , kobate toondoni ? 
Ak kolenji inendet , Ng’eet , si iwe : kagosoobin kayaneng’ung’ .
Ak kingoteebe Parisaik kole nyonei au bounatetab Jehovah , kowolji ichek kolenji , Manyonei bounatetab Jehovah kegeeronu : 
ama kimwaei kele , Ogeero , mi oli ! Anan mi olin ! Amu , ogeero , mi bounatetab Jehovah kwenung’wong’ .
Ak kilenji alamalyennyi , Tun bwanei betusiek , che tun omache ogeer betut agenge ne bo Weritab chi , ak mogeere . 
Ak tun lenjinok , Ogeero , mi olin ! Ogeero , mi oli ! Amat obe , anan osub ichek : 
amu u kalyelet , ne ilyelune komosta age eng’ kipsengwet , ak koluu agoi komosta age ne bo kipsengwet ; tun u noto Weritab chi agine eng’ betunnyi . 
Ago kanyol konyalil eng’ tuguk che chang’ ak koesio inendet ibini . 
Ak ko u ole kibiitunda eng’ betusiekab Noa , ko tun u noto eng’ betusiekab Weritab chi . 
Kiamisiei , kieeisei , kiitunisiei , ak kiigoitoi kitun , agoi betut ne kiwa Noa melit orit , ak kinyo maranet , ak kobar tugul . 
U noto agine , ole kibiitunda betusiekab Lot ; kiamisiei , kieeisei , kialisiei , kialdoisiei , kigolsei , ak kiteeksei ; 
ago eng’ betut ne kimanda Lot eng’ Sodom korobon mat ak koik che laldos che kibunu kipsengwet , ak kobar tugul : 
u noto eng’ betut ne kiboru Weritab chi .
Eng’ betunoto , ko mat kochorgei inendet ne mi got barak , koib tugukyik che mi go ; amat koweek agine inendet ne mi mbar . 
Obwat osotiotab Lot . 
Age tugul ne cheng’ei kosor sobondanyi kobeeti : ak age tugul ne ibeeti sobondanyi koribei . 
Amwawok ale , Tun ruitos bik aeng’u eng’ itogut agenge eng’ kemounoto ; kimuti age , kebagakta age . 
Tun ng’oisei kobogorisiek aeng’u kibagenge ; kimuti age , kebagakta age . 
Tun mi bik aeng’u mbar : kimuti age , kebagakta age .
Ak kiwolji inendet kolenji , Ano , Kiptaiyandani ? Ak kilenji , Ole mi musto , koyumjingei oloto motong’wek agichek .
Kimwachi anyun kalewenet kole , Kanyol kosa betusiek tugul , amat chorirenso ; 
kolenji , Kimitei nganaset age kiruogindo , ne kima koiywei Jehovah , ak kima koiiti chi : 
ak kimi mosoget age nganasanato ; ne kinyonei ole mi kotugul , kolen , Ibesiewa kiruoget ne bo iman eng’ bunyondennyu . 
Ak kiesio eng’ betusiek alak : ago eng’ let , komwa eng’ orinnyi kole , Agot ngo maiywei Jehovah , amaiiti chi ; 
ago amu inyalila mosogani , abesiechini anyun , si ma konyonei kotugul koiima .
Ak kile Kiptaiyat , Ogas kit ne kimwa kiruogindet ne ma bo imanda . 
Tos mayachin Jehovah imanda che lewenotin , che rirjin inendet bet ak kemoi , ak muitoi inendet eng’ ichek ? 
Amwawok ale , yachin inendet ichek imanda kochokyin . Ago ye tun nyo Weritab chi , ko tos nyoru kayanet eng’ ng’ony ?
Ak kimwachi kogeny kalewenoni alak che kiimang’ugei kole , ki bo imanda , ak kosasei bik tugul , 
kolenji , Kitogosta bik aeng’u hekalut koba kosa ; Parisaindet age , ko taagindetab aisurut age . 
Kitonon Parisaindet kosa kong’alal inegei ko u ni kole , Jehovah , amwaun kongoi , amu ma ki kergei ak bik alak , che rebik , che ma bo iman , che ibegei , anan taagindoni bo aisurut . 
Arugutige konyil aeng’ eng’ wigit ; agoitoi kebeberta ne bo taman eng’ tuguk tugul che anyoru . 
Ago kitonon taagindetab aisurut eng’ ye loo , ak ma cham agot konyal kipsengwet , ago kiluch tegennyi , kole , Jehovah , rirena , a kiptengekyo . 
Amwawok ale , kichortagei chichoto gonnyi ko kagoek ne bo imanda kosiir nin age : amu chi age tugul ne itororigei kiming’ini ; ak age tugul ne iming’inigei ko tun kitorori .
Ak kiimutyi bik inendet manyurunik , si kobiit kotwa ichek : ago ye kingogeer alamalyet , koger kong’ . 
Ago kiguur Jesu ichek kobwanji , ak kolenji , Ochamji lagok che mengech kobwanja , amat oete : amu bo che u chu bounatetab Jehovah . 
Amwawok iman ale , Age tugul ne mataachei bounatetab Jehovah ko u lakwet ne ming’in , ko magoi mong’ji oloto matiny .
Ak kiteebe inendet bounindet age , kole , Konetindoni mie , ayai nee si kobiit anyor sobondab koigeny ? 
Ak kilenji Jesu , Amu nee si iguurena ne mie ? Mami ne mie , kobate agenge , noto ko Jehovah . 
Ingen Ng’atutik , Amoipge , Amerumisie , Amechorse , Amebaorian lembech , Teech kwandang’ung’ ak komet . 
Ak kile, Kiarib tuguchuto tugul koboch ko a neran. 
Ak ye kingogas Jesu , kolenji , Ta ko rartaat kit agenge eng’ inye : alde tugul che itinye , ak ipchechi kibananok , si inyoru konoruet eng’ kipsengwet : ak inyo , isubwa . 
Ago ye kingogas inendet tuguchu , koarogen mising’ ; amu ki magorio kot .
Ak kingogeer Jesu inendet , komwa kole , Bichii ne tia eng’ che tinyei magornatosiek komong’ji bounatetab Jehovah ! 
Amu nyamnyum eng’ tambesiet kochut kondab katet , kosiir komong’ji magoriot bounatetab Jehovah . 
Kimwa anyun che kigasei , kole , Ng’o anyun ne kesoru ? 
Kile , Tuguk che maimugaksei eng’ bik komugaksei eng’ Jehovah .
Kole Petero , Keero , kigebagakte tugukyok , ak kisubun . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Amwawok iman ale , Mami chi ne kibagakta got , anan osotiot , anan che tupcho , anan sigik , anan lagok , agobo bounatetab Jehovah , 
ne manyoru che chang’ kosiir eng’ betusiechu , ak sobondab koigeny eng’ betusiek che tun bwanei .
Ak kiimut taman ak aeng’ kobwa ole mi , ak kolenji , Ogeero , kitogostoi Jerusalem , ak kosulda tuguk tugul che kisir maotik agobo Weritab chi . 
Amu kindoi inendet eunekab Bororiosiek , si kechurachur , ak kitewer , ak kesing’ilji : 
ak kobire kipcharitit , ak kobar : ak kong’eet kogeny eng’ betutab somok . 
Ak kima iguiyo icheget tuguchuto , agot agenge ; ak kiung’ak mwaonito eng’ ichek , ak kima ibesio tuguk che kiga kimwa .
Ak kingorikyi Jeriko , ko kitebyei ng’ony kipkoratia eng’ oret taban kosomsei : 
ak kingogas kosiirtoi tuiyet , koteeb kole , Nee chu ? 
Ak kimwachi ichek inendet kolenji , Jesu ne bo Nasaret ne siirtoi . 
Ak kiwaach , kole , Jesu , Weritab Daudi , rirena . 
Ak kiger kong’ inendet anyun che kiindoi , kole kosis : ago kites kowaach mising’ kole , Weritab Daudi , rirena . 
Ak kitonon Jesu , ak kong’at kimut inendet kwo ole mi : ak ye kiga rik , koteebe inendet , 
kole , Imache ayaun nee ? Ak kile , Kiptaiyandani , amache ageerto . 
Ak kilenji Jesu, Keerte : kagosoobin kayaneng’ung’ . 
Kigeerto anyun ngunoto , ak kosub inendet , kolosunoti Jehovah : ak kingogeer tuiyet komugul , kogonyit Jehovah .
Kimong’ji anyun Jeriko ak kobun kwenut . 
Ak ogeero , chito ne kiguure Sakayo ; ak ki ne o inendet eng’ taagikab aisurut , ak ki magorio . 
Ak kicheng’ei kole kogeer Jesu si konai kole ng’o inendet ; ago kima imuch amu tuiyet , amu ki nwach . 
Ak kilabat kondo , kwo kolany mogoiywet si kogeer inendet : amu kinyo kosiirtoe oranato . 
Ak ye kingoit Jesu yoto , konyal ketoto , ak kolenji , Sakayo , choruge , chogu ; amu kanyolja aru gong’ung’ ra . 
Ak kichok , kochorgei , ak kotaach inendet eng’ boiboindo . 
Ak ye kingogeer bichoto , kong’unyng’ung’so tugul , kole , Kawa kotebi eng’ gotab chito ne kiptengekyo . 
Ak kitonon Sakayo , ak kolenji Kiptaiyat , Keero , Kiptaiyandani , agochini kibananok kebebertab tugukyuk ; ak ngo kiaibe chi age tugul kiy eng’ ng’alset , aweekyini konyil ang’wan . 
Ak kilenji Jesu , Kagonyo yetunet rani goi , amu weritab Abraham agine inendet . 
Amu kinyo Weritab chi kocheng’ ak kosor ne kiga kobet .
Ak ye kingota kogasei ichek tuguchu , kotes komwa kalewenet , amu ki negit Jerusalem , ak kiibwati icheget kolen toogu bounatetab Jehovah ngunoto . 
Kimwa anyun kole , Kiwa chi anum ne toogunot emet ne loo , kwo konam bounatet kobunji , ak koweek . 
Yeityo koguur otwogikyik taman , ak kogochi fedaisiek taman , ak kolenji , Oboisie agoi tun aitu . 
Ago kiwech inendet bikab emennyi , koyokto ng’olyot kosube inendet , kole , Magimache chichi koboiywech .
Ak ye kingoweek kogeny , ko kagonam bounatet , kong’at keguur otwogichoto , chu kiga kigochi fedaisiek , kobwa ole mi inendet , si kobiit konai che kinyor bichoto eng’ boisiet . 
Ak kinyo tainnyi chito ne bo tai , kole , Kiptaiyandani , kigonyor fedaiyandeng’ung’ fedaisiek alak taman . 
Ak kilenji inendet , Kiiyai ne mie , otwogindoni mie : amu kiiegu ne kiyani eng’ kit ne ming’in mising’ , bou nganasok taman . 
Ak kinyo ne bo aeng’ , kole , Kiptaiyandani , kigonyor fedaiyandeng’ung’ fedaisiek mut alak . 
Ak kilenji noto agine , Bou nganasok mut aginye .
Ak kinyo age , kole , Kiptaiyandani , keero , ineni fedaiyandeng’ung’ ne kigaratyi anget ak agonor : 
amu kiaiywein , amu i chi ne kolgol : inemu ne kima inde ng’ony , ak igese che kima igol . 
Kolenji anyun inendet , Aruogun agobo ne kemwa eng’ kuting’ung’ , otwogindoni ya . Kiingen ile a chi ne kolgol , anemu ne kima ande ng’ony , ak agese che kima agol ; 
kilya anyun si mende fedaisiekyuk ole kiwalawale , ta kaanyoru ko kaitu koboto che kitesak ? 
Ak kimwachi ichek che kitonondos eng’ ye negit , kolenji , Orebe inendet fedaiyat , ak ogochi inendet ne tinye fedaisiek taman . 
Ak kilenji ichek inendet , Kiptaiyandani , tinyei inendet fedaisiek taman . 
Amwawok ale , chi age tugul ne tinyei , kigochin ; ago inendet ne matinyei , kerebe agot ne tinyei . 
Ago omutu anyun bunichuchuk kobwa yu , che machamei aboi , si obar eng’ tainnyu .
Ak ye kiga komwa ko u noto , kwo kondo , kotogostoi Jerusalem . 
Ak ye kingo kagorikta Betpage ak Betania , eng’ tulwet ne kiguure tulwetab Emitik , koyokto aeng’ che bo alamalyennyi , 
kolenji , Oba agoi oit nganaset ne mi taing’wong’ ; ak ye oit ogeer moitab sigiriet ne ratat , ne tom kolany chi : otiach , ak ogetu . 
Ak ngo teebenak chi age tugul , kole , Kalya si otiach ? Olenji anyun , Makyingei Kiptaiyat .
Koba anyun che kaga kiyokto , ak konyor ko u ye kaga mwachi inendet ichek . 
Ak ye kita kotiachi moitab sigiriet , kolenji bikab kobo , Kalya si otiach moitab sigiriet ? 
Ak kilenji , Makyingei Kiptiyat . 
Ak kiget konyo ole mi Jesu : yeityo koiito ngoroikwak eng’ moata bo sigiriet , ak koganapchi Jesu barak . 
Ak ye kiwendi , koiitoot ngoroikwak eng’ oret .
Ak kingorikta tegeiyatab tulwetab Emitik , kotoi tuiyet tugul ne bo alamalyet koboiboitu ak kolos Jehovah eng’ kutit ne o agobo boisionik tugul che bo kamuktaet che kiga kogeer ; 
kolen , Iberurot Laitoriat ne nyonei eng’ kainetab Kiptaiyat : kalyet eng’ kipsengwet , ak lilindo eng’ ole toror mising’ .
Ak kilenji Parisaik alage che bo tuiyet inendet , Konetindoni , ker kong’ alamalyeng’ung’ . 
Ak kiwolji kolenji , Amwawok ale , ngot kosisyo chu , koboldos koik .
Ak kingorik , kogeer nganaset ak korirji , 
kolen , Nda kengen eng’ betuni , agot inye , tuguk che bo kalyet ! Ago nguno ko kagoung’ogis eng’ konyeguk . 
Amu tun bwanjinin betusiek che teechei buniguk irimet koyiemin komoswek tugul , ak kogerjin go eng’ komosta age tugul , 
ak kowirjin ng’ony , ak lagoguk che mi oring’ung’ ; ama bagagun agot koita agenge ne mi baragutab age ; amu kima inai betutab rutochineng’ung’ .
Ak kiwa hekalut orit , ak kotoi koon komanda che kialdoisiei , 
kolenji ichek, Kigisir kele , Egu gonnyu gotab saet : ago kaoyai koek kebenetab rebik .
Ak kiinetisiei betut age tugul eng’ hekalut . Ago kicheng’ tisiik che eechen ak sirik ak che toogunotin eng’ bik , kobar inendet : 
ak manyor kit ne kiimuchi koyai ; amu kiepchin it bik tugul inendet mising’ .
Ak ye kiineti bik eng’ betut age eng’ hekalut , ak koamdoi logoiywek che miach , 
kobwanji inendet tisiik che eechen ak sirik koboto boisiek koche inendet ; ak kimwachi inendet kolenji , Mwawech ; iyae tuguchu kimnatetab ng’o Ak ko ng’o ne kigonin kimnatoni ? 
Ak kiwolji kolenji , Ateebenok agane ng’olyot ; ak omwawa : 
Kabatisanetab Johana ko kibunu kipsengwet , anan kibunu bik ? 
Ak king’alaljigei ichegei , kole , Ngot kemwa kele , Kibunu kipsengwet ; komwa kole , Ko kilya si moyan inendet ? 
Ago ngot kemwa kele , Kibunu bik ; kolachech bik tugul eng’ koik : amu kiiyani ichek kole , ki maotio Johana . 
Ak kiwol kole , Magingen ole kibunu . 
Ak kilenji Jesu ichek , Agot ane ko mamwawok kimnatet ne ayae tuguchu .
Ak kitoi komwachi bik kalewenoni , kole : Kimin chi sabibuk eng’ mbar , ak komanakyi meek , ak kwo emet age kotebi betusiek che chang’ . 
Ak kingoit betut koyokyi otwogindet meechoto , si kobiit kogochi ichek inendet logoekab mbaranato : ago kibir meek inendet , ak koon kwo buch . 
Ak kiiyokto kogeny otwogindet age : ak kibir noto agine , ak kotewer , ak koon kwo buch . 
Ak kiiyokto kogeny ne bo somok : ak kiiguoten agine ak kotoorji sang’ . 
Ak kile chitab kobo mbaret , Ayai nee anyun ? Ayoktoi werinnyu chamanennyu : tamangab kogonyit inendet . 
Ago ye kingogeer meek inendet , kong’alaljigei ichegei , kole , Nito ne tun bunjin tuguk : ongebar anyun , si kindii tuguk . 
Ak kitoorta komanda eng’ mbaretab sabibuk ak kobar . Itoi nee anyun chitab kobo mbaret bichoto ? 
Nyonei anyun inendet ak kobar meechoto tugul , ak kogochi bik alak mbaretab sabibuk . Ak ye kingogas ichek , komwa kole , Achicha , mat koek ko u noto .
Ak kiichiilji kong’ ichek ak kole , Nee anyun ne kigisir kele , Koita ne kiesio teegik , Kigiyai noto koek metitab luita ?
Ak chi age tugul ne ibutyin koyata koilei konyaknyaksei ; ak inendet ne ibutyin koyata , konyinyirsei .
Ak kicheng’ sirik ak tisiik che eechen konam inendet eng’ sainato ; ak kiiywei ichek bik : amu kinai kole mwaei kalewenoni agobo ichek . 
Ak kiriboti icheget inendet , ak koyokto segeik , che kiyaigei koek che bo imanda , si kobiit koname inendet ng’alekyik , si kogoito inendet kwo taitab bounatet ak kimnatetab bounindet . 
Ak kiteebe inendet kole , Konetindoni , kingen kele imwae ak inetisiei eng’ iman , ago metiytii chi , ak ineti iman oretab Jehovah : 
Tos chamdoi ng’atutik kigochi kodi Kaisari , anan achicha ?
Ago kinai ng’alsenywa , ak kolenji ichek , 
Oborua denarit , Bo ng’o itoni ak sirutik che tinyei ? Ak kile , Bo Kaisari . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Ogochi Kaisari tuguk che bo Kaisari , ak ogochi Jehovah tuguk che bo Jehovah . 
Ak kima imuch koname mwaonato eng’ taitab bik ; ak kikwong’io eng’ wolunennyi , ak kisisyo .
Ak kibwanji inendet Sadukaik alak , icheget che mwaei kole , mami ng’eetyet ; ak kiteebe inendet , 
kole , Konetindoni , kisirwech Musa , kole , Ngo me ng’etab kam , ago tinyei osotiot , ne tom kosich lakwa , kondii ng’etab kam osotiondonoto , si kolalji ma ng’etab kam . 
Kimi anyun werik tisabu che kitupcho : ak kiitunis ne bo tai , ak kime ama kisich lakwa ; 
ak kiindi ne bo aeng’ ; 
ak u noto ne bo somok ; ak kiigei noto tugul ko tisab , kibek ama sich lakwa . 
Ak kingobata kome agine kobogoriondonoto . 
Tun eng’ ng’eetyet anyun koegu osotiotab ng’o eng’ ichek ? Amu kiitun ichek tugul ko tisab .
Ak kilenji Jesu ichek , Itunisiei werikab betusiechu , ak kogoitoi kitun : 
ago che kiityin kele nyoljin konyor betusiechoto bwanei , ak ng’eetyet eng’ che kibek , ko matun itunisiei , ama kigoitoi kitun : 
amu ma komuchi kobek agoi : amu kergeitu ak malaikaisiek ; ak icheget ko werikab Jehovah , amu werikab ng’eetyet . 
Ago ng’eetos che kigobek , kiibor Musa agine eng’ ye kigisir agobo Ketit , ye kiguure Kiptaiyat , Jehovah ne bo Abraham , ak Jehovah ne bo Isak , ak Jehovah ne bo Jakobo . 
Inendet ko ma Jehovah ne bo che kigobek , ago bo che soptos : amu soptos tugul eng’ inendet .
Ak kiwolji sirik alak kolenji , Konetindoni , kaimwa komie . 
Amu kimata kogany ichek koteebe inendet teebut age tugul kogeny .
Ak kilenji ichek , Teptoi ano si komwaei ichek kole , Kristo ko weritab Daudi ? 
Amu kimwa Daudi inendet eng’ bukuitab Tienwogikab Kalosunet , kole , Kilenji Kiptaiyat Kiptaiyandennyu , Tebe eunnyu ne bo tai ,
Agoi ayai buniguk koek ng’echeretab kelyeguk .
Kuure anyun Daudi inendet Kiptaiyat , koegundoi ano anyun werinnyi ?
Ak kimwachi alamalyennyi kogasei bik tugul kolenji , 
Oripge eng’ sirik , che chamei kobendat kolaachi ngoroik che koen , ak kochamei kagatosiek eng’ oldinwekab aldaisiet , ak ng’echerok che bo tai eng’ sunagogisiek , ak oldinwek che bo tai eng’ igorwek ; 
ak korebe mosogik gorikwak , ak kosaei sautik che koen kong’alsei : tun nyoru chuto kiruoget ne o kosiir .
Ak kiyot met , kogeer magorek kondoi kagochinoikwak ole kiyumjin . 
Ak kigeer mosoget age ne kibanania kondoi sendeisiek aeng’ che u kebebertab pesaiyat . 
Ak kile , Amwawok iman ale , Kagonde mosogani banan che siirei cho tugul : 
amu kagonde chu tugul eng’ chang’indanywa ole kindoi kagochinoik ; ago kagonde inendet eng’ banandanyi tugul che tinyei , agot che kosobe .
Ak kingota kong’alali alak agobo hekalut , ole kigimusaganda eng’ koik che kororon ak kagochinoik , kole , 
Eng’ tuguchu ogeere , ko tun bwanei betusiek , che mang’etune koita agot agenge , baragutab age , ne ma tun kiwirjin ng’ony .
Ak kiteebe , kole , Konetindoni , egu anyun tuguchuto auyo ? Ak u nee kaborunet ye tun machei korik kosulda tuguchuto ?
Ak kile , Oripge si ma kibeetok : amu tun bwanei bik che chang’ eng’ kainennyu , kolen , A inendet ; ak , Kagorik betusiek : amosub ichek . 
Ak ye tun ogas agobo lugosiek ak chemarget , ko mat oarogense : amu kanyol kosib kosulda tuguchoto korok ; ago tom korik kagesunet .
Kolenji anyun ichek , Tun setyin bororiet age bororiet age , ak setyin bounatet age bounatet age : 
ak kobiit botanosiek che eechen che bo ng’ony , ak rubosiek eng’ oldinwek alak , ak korotwek ; ak kobiit kamuisosiek ak kaborunoik che eechen che bunu kipsengwet . 
Ago ye tom kobiit chuto , konamak eng’ eunekwak , ak kousok , ak komutak obe sunagogisiek ak korgorosiek , komutak taitab laitorinik ak bounik agobo kainennyu . 
Egu baornatet eng’ okwek . 
Oegu che begechinotin eng’ mugulelwekwok , si mosib ogerer met agobo ole owolundoi : 
amu agonok kutit ak ng’omnatet , ne maimuchi bunikwok tugul kota kowol kiy anan kogirindaak . 
Ak kong’wektak sigikwok , ak che otupche , ak che bo oreng’wong’ , ak choronok ; ak kebar alak eng’ okwek . 
Ak kowechok bik tugul agobo kainennyu . 
Ak mabetei sumeiyot agenge ne bo metowekwok . 
Ak eng’ muitaeng’wong’ onyoru sobonwekwok .
Ak ye tun ogeer lugosiek koyiem Jerusalem , onai anyun ole , kagorik ng’emisiennyi . 
Ingomwechi anyun chi mi Judea tulonok ; ak ingomanda che mi kwenutab nganasanato ; ak amat kota koba orit ichek che mi emonoto . 
Amu chuto ko betusiekab mugetut , si kobiit kosulda tuguk tugul che kigisir . 
Bwa eng’ ichek che chio ak che reritos eng’ besiosiechoto . Amu biitu bichiindo ne o eng’ ng’ony , ak nereknatet eng’ bichuto . 
Ak kobutyo ichek eng’ ng’atibindab rotwetab chok , ak kimut luulenik koba bororiosiek tugul : ak kotiech Bororiosiek Jerusalem , agoi kosulda betusiekab Bororiosiek .
Ak kobiit kaborunoik eng’ asista ak eng’ arawet ak eng’ kecheik ; ak kobiit eng’ ng’ony bichiindab bororiosiek , ak beng’jinet amu kamuutetab nyanjet ak beek che mildogei ; 
ak kobek mugulelwekab bik amu kaiyweisiet , ak amu kagenisietab tuguk che bwanjin ng’ony : amu kitumdum kimnatosiekab kipsengwetisiek . 
Ak eng’ betunoto kogeer anyun Weritab chi konyonei eng’ boldet koboto kimnatet ak lilindo ne o . 
Ak ye toi kosulda tuguchuto , ogeer barak , ak oyot metowekwok ; am karik katiageng’wong’ .
Ak kimwachi ichek kalewenet ; kole , Ogeer mogoiywet , ak ketik tugul : 
ye ing’atyo ogeere ak onae okwek ole , karik kesisiet . 
U noto anyun ak okwek , ye ogeer koyaagis tuguchuto , onai ole karik bounatetab Jehovah . 
Amwawok iman ale , Masiirtoi ibini , agoi kosulda tuguk tugul . 
Siirtoi kipsengwet ak ng’ony : ago magoi siirto ng’alekyuk .
Ago oripge anyun okwek , si manyi mugulelwekwok keiyandit , ak bogitet , ak kaiimutikab sobetab betusiechu , ak konyonjok betunoto kocheak ko u mestet : 
amu u noto tun nyonjin bik tugul che menyei ng’ony komugul . 
Ago oripge eng’ betut age tugul , ak osae , si kobiit oterterisie , ochilile tuguchuto tugul bwanei , ak otononse eng’ taitab Weritab chi .
Ak kiinetisiei eng’ hekalut betut age tugul ; ak kimandoi kemout age tugul , kowendi kotebyei eng’ tulwet ne kiguure tulwetab Emitik . 
Ak kimusyin bik tugul inendet eng’ hekalut , si kobiit kogas inendet .
Kirik anyun igorta ne bo makatinik che ma kinde mermerek , ne kiguure Paska . 
Ak kicheng’ tisiik che eechen ak sirik ole bartoi inendet ; amu kiiywei ichek bik .
Ak kichut Setani Judas ne kiguure Iskariot , ne ki age eng’ taman ak aeng’ . 
Ak kiwa kong’alal ak tisiik che eechen ak kiptainik , ole ng’wektochindoi inendet ichek . 
Kiboiboitu anyun bichoto , ak kochamnyechi kogochi inendet fedaisiek . 
Kocham anyun inendet , ak kocheng’ boroindo kong’wekyi inendet ichek eng’ ole mami bik che chang’ .
Ak kiit anyun betut ne bo makatinik che ma kinde mermerek , betut ne ki kanyol koeny aruetab paska . 
Ak kiiyokto Petero ak Johana , kole , Oba ochobwech paska , si kobiit keam . 
Ak kilenji , Imache kebe kechob eng’ ano ? 
Ak kilenji ichek , Ogeero , ye omong’ji nganaset , kotuiyenok chito ne ibei teretab beek ; osub inendet agoi got orit ole wendi . 
Ak omwachji chitab kobo got , olenji , Kateebenen Konetindet , kole , Mi ano gotab toek , ole anyone aame paska koboto alamalyennyu ? 
Koboruok anyun got ne o ne mi barak ne tetotin tuguk : ochob eng’ oloto . 
Ak kiba anyun , ak konyor ko u ye kaga kemwachi : ak kichob paska .
Ak ye kingoit sait , koteb ng’ony , koboto che kiyoktoi . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Eng’ maget ko koamach aam paskaini kobotok kotom anyalil : 
amu amwawok ale , Koboch nguno ko ma aame , agoi kosulda eng’ bounatetab Jehovah .
Ak kitaach kikombet , ak kingo kagogoito kongoi , kole , Onam ni , ak opchechige okwege : 
amu amwawok ale , Koboch nguno , ko ma aee che bo logoekab sabibuk , agoi koit bounatetab Jehovah .
Ak kinam makatiat , ak kingo kagomwa kongoi , kobutul , ak kogochi ichek , ak kole , Ni bortanyu ne kigoitoi agobo okwek : oyae ko u ni eng’ kabwatet ne obwatena . 
Ko u noto kikombet agine , kingo kagobata amitwogik che bo lagat , kole , Arorutiet ne leel kikombani eng’ korotikyuk , che kitumdoi agobo okwek .
Ago , ogeero , mi eutab inendet ne ng’wektaa kobota eng’ mesani . 
Amu wendi Weritab chi iman , ko u ye kiging’at : ago bwa eng’ chichoto ng’wektoi inendet !
Ak kitoi anyun koteebegei ichegei , kole ng’o eng’ ichek ne yaei kii .
King’eet anyun tiiyet eng’ kwenunywa , kole ng’o ne kiiti kele ne o eng’ ichek . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Laitorani laitorinik eng’ Bororiosiek : ak icheget che tinyei bounatet eng’ ichek keguure Toretik . 
Ago , ma u noto eng’ okwek : ago ingoigei ne o eng’ okwek ne ming’in ; ak inendet ne o koigei ne otisiei . 
Ng’o ne o anyun , inendet ne tebyei eng’ amisiet , anan inendet ne otisiei ? Tos ma inendet ne tebyei eng’ amisiet ? Ago ami kwenung’wong’ ko u chito ne otisiei .
Ago okwek ko o che kiotebi kobota eng’ yomsosiekyuk ; 
ak kaagonok bounatet , ko u ye kigogona Baba , 
si kobiit oamisie ak koeeise mesennyu eng’ bounatennyu , ak tun otebe ng’echerok che bo laitornatet , oruokyini ortinwek taman ak aeng’ che bo Israel .
Simon , Simon , keero , kagosom Setani kole konamak , si kosesak ko u nganok : 
ago kiasa agobo inye , si mabek kayaneng’ung’ : ak ye kaiwalage , igimit che otupche . 
Ak kolenji inendet , Kiptaiyandani , kaachoboge kebe tuwai korgoret agot meet . 
Ak kimwa kole , Amwaun Petero , kotom kote kipsoiywet rani , iesioa konyil somok ile , mengena .
Ak kilenji ichek , Kingayoktok ko motinye agot lolet , anan suberet , anan kweonik , ko tos kirarta kiy eng’ okwek ? Ak kile , Ma raruech kiy . 
Ak kilenji , Ago inendet ne tinyei lolet koibot nguno , ak u noto suberet agine : ak inendet ne matinyei rotwetab chok , koalda ngoriennyi , si koale . 
Amu amwawok ale , kit ne kigisir ko kanyol kosulda eng’ ane , kele , Kigiit inendet koboto kiptengeginik : amu tinyei kagesunet ng’alek che kigisir agobo ane . 
Ak kile , Kiptaiyandani , keero , mi yu rotokab chok aeng’u . Ak kilenji ichek , Kagoyam .
Komong’ sang’ anyun , ak kwo agoi tulwetab Emitik , ko u biteennyi ; ak kiisub alamalyet inendet . 
Ak ye kingo kagoit oloto , kolenji ichek , Osa si mochut yomset . 
Ak kiistoegei ichek ye te ye itei koita ngewirta ; ak kigutuny kosa , 
kole , Baba , ngicham , iistoena kikombani : ago ma ko u magennyu , ago ingoyaak ko u mageng’ung’ . 
Ak kimong’ji inendet malaikaiyat ne kibunu kipsengwet kogimit inendet . 
Ak ye kimi inendet nyalilda ne ng’wan , kotes kosa mising’ : ak kigergeitu kaotikyik ak korotik che sachin ng’ony .
Ak kingong’eet eng’ saennyi , konyo ole mi alamalyennyi , ak konyor koruitos amu arogenet , 
ak kilenji ichek , Kalya si oruiye ? Ong’eetye, osa , si mochut yomset .
Ak kingota ko ng’alali , ogeero , tuiyet , koboto inendet ne kiguure Judas , age eng’ taman ak aeng’ , kiindoune ichek ; ak korikyi inendet Jesu si kong’utut . 
Ago kilenji Jesu , Judas , ing’wektoi Weritab chi eng’ ng’ututet ? 
Ak kingogeer che kimi koboto inendet kit ne machei koyaak , kole , Kiptaiyandani , kieb eng’ rotwetab chok ? 
Ak kieb age eng’ ichek otwogindetab tisiindet ne o , kieb itinnyi ne bo tai . 
Ago kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Obagakte ; kagoyam . Ak kitwa itinnyi , kosoob .
Ak kilenji Jesu tisiik che eechen , ak kiptainikab hekalut , ak boisiek che kigabwa kogirinda inendet , Kobwa ak rotokab chok ak siarisiek , ko u ye obwanjini rebindet ? 
Ye kiami kobotok betut age tugul eng’ hekalut , ko ma oyogocha eunekwok : ago saing’wong’ ni , ak kimnatet ne bo mesundeito .
Kinam anyun inendet , ak komut kwo gotab tisiindet ne o . Ak kiisubi Petero eng’ ye loo . 
Ak ye kiga kolal mat eng’ kok , koteb ng’ony tugul , ak kitebe Petero kwenunywa . 
Ak kingogeer chepto age inendet kotebyei eng’ ye mi lapkeiyetab mat , kochiilji kong’ inendet , kole , Kimi chichi agine koboto inendet . 
Ago kitiiyo , kole , Kobogoriondoni , mangen inendet . 
Ak ne matia kogeer chito age , ak kole , I agenge aginye eng’ ichek . Ak kile Petero , Chichi , ma bo bichoto .
Ak ye kingogesgei olo bo sait agenge , kole chito age eng’ kimnatet , Iman kimi chichi agine koboto inendet : amu Galilindet inendet . 
Eng taunet ko kimi Ngolyondet , ak kimi Ngolyondet ak Jehovah , ak ki Jehovah Ngolyondet . 
Kimi inendet ak Jehovah eng taunet . 
Kigiyai tuguk tugul eng inendet ; ak kima kiyai kiy age tugul ne kiga keyai ne kima yai inendet . 
Kimi sobondo eng inendet ; ak ki lapkeiyetab bik sobonato . 
Amu iluu lapkeiyet eng mesundeito ; ak kima iterter mesundeito lapkeiyonoto .
Kinyo chi , ne kiiyok Jehovah , ne kigiguure Johana . 
Kinyo chichoto koek baoriat , si kobaorianji lapkeiyet , si kobiit koyan bik tugul amu inendet . 
Kima ko lapkeiyonoto inendet , ago kinyo si kobaorianji lapkeiyonoto . 
Kimi lapkeiyet ne bo iman , ne nyonei ngony , ne iluuchin chi tugul .
Kimi ngony inendet , ak kigiyai ngony eng inendet , ak kima nai ngony inendet . 
Kinyonji chechik , ak kima taach inendet bikyik . 
Ago tugul che kitaach inendet , ko kiigochi kamuget koek lagokab Jehovah , ichek che iyani kainennyi : 
che kigisich , ama eng korotik , anan eng magetab borto , anan eng magetab chi , ago eng Jehovah .
Ak kiek Ngolyot borto , ak komeny kwenunnyo (ak kigigeer torornatennyi , torornatet ne u ne bo ne kigii inegei kobunu Kwanda) , ko nyiitat mieindo ak imanit .
Kibaorianji inendet Johana , koititen kole , Inendet ni ne kiamwaitoi ale , Inendet ne isubwa koegu ne bo tai eng ane , amu ki bo tai inendet eng ane .
Amu kigitaach achek tugul che bo nyiiennyi , ak mieindo eng mieindo . 
Amu kigigon Ngatutiet eng Musa ; kibwa mieindo ak imanit eng Jesu Kristo . 
Mami chi ne kigeer Jehovah ole kigoi ; kigongangwech inendet Werit ne kigii inegei , ne mi tegetab Kwanda .
Ak ni ko baornatetab Johana , ye kingoyok Yahudik tisiik ak Lawik eng Jerusalem koba koteebe kole , I ngo inye ? 
Ak kingany inendet , ama tiiyo ; kingany kole , Ma a Kristo ane . 
Ak kiteebe inendet kole , Nee anyun ? I Elija ? Ak kile , Ma a inendet . I maotiondonoto ? Ak kiwol kole , Achicha . 
Kilenji anyun inendet , I ngo inye ? Si kobiit kewolji che koiyokwech . Imwae nee agobo inyege ? 
Kile , A kutitab chi ne ititeni eng surkwen , Olitit oretab Kiptaiyat , ko u ye kimwa maotiot Isaia .
Ak icheget che kigiyok ko ki bo Parisaik . 
Ak kiteebe inendet , kolenji , Kalya anyun si ibatisanisiei , ngo ma i Kristo , anan Elija , anan maotiondonoto ? 
Kowolji Johana bichoto kolenji , Abatisanisie beek : ago tononi eng kwenungwong age ne mongen , 
inendet ne isubwa , ne manyoljina atiach anokab kweonikyik .
Kiyaogis tuguchuto eng Betania Jordan komosin , ole kiibatisanisie Johana .
Eng betut ne bo aeng kogeer Johana Jesu konyonjin , ak kole , Ogeero , Aruet ne bo Jehovah , ne ibei tengektab ngony ! 
Inendet ni ne kiamwa ale , Isubwa chito ne egu ne tai eng ane : amu ki bo tai eng ane . 
Ak kima angen ane inendet ; ago si kobiit kibarta inendet eng Israel , kianyo anyun amu noto abatisane beek .
Ak kibaorian Johana , kole , Kiageer Tamirmiriet kochorugei eng kipsengwet ko u cheptuget ; ak kotebe inendet . 
Ak kima angen inendet : ago inendet ne kiiyokwa abatisane beek , ko inendet ne kimwawa kolenja , Chichoto igeere kochorjingei Tamirmiriet , ak kotebe inendet , ko noto ne ibatisane Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Ak kiageer , ak kiabaorian ale nito ko Weritab Jehovah .
Kogeny eng betut ne kiisubu betunoto , ko kitononi Johana , ak aeng che bo alamalyennyi ; 
ak kigeerot inendet Jesu kowendoti , ak kole , Ogeero , Aruet ne bo Jehovah ! 
Ak kigas choto aeng che bo alamalyennyi kongalali inendet , ak kosub Jesu . 
Ak kiwelelgei Jesu , ak kogeer ichek kosubu , ak kolenji , Ochenge nee ? Ak kilenji inendet , Rabbi (ye kiweech kele , Konetindet) , imenye ano ? 
Kolenji ichek , Obwa si ogeer . Kibwa anyun kogeer ole menyei , ak kitebi koboto inendet betunoto ; ki olo bo sait taman .
Ki Andrea , ne tupcho ak Simon Petero , age eng choto aeng che kigasei kongalali Johana , ak kiisub inendet . 
Kisib konyor Simon ne tupcho , ak kolenji , Kagenyoru Mesia ! (ye kiweech , ko Kristo) . 
Kiimutyi inendet Jesu . Kigeer Jesu inendet , ak kole , I Simon weritab Johana : ta keguurenen Kepa (ye kiweech , ko Petero) .
Kimach anyun kwo Galili eng betut ne kiisubi betunoto , ak kinyor Pilipu : ak kilenji Jesu inendet , Isubwa . 
Ak ki bo Pilipu Betsaida , nganaset ne bo Andrea ak Petero . 
Kinyor Pilipu Natanael , ak kolenji , Kagenyoru inendet , ne kisir Musa eng Ngatutiet , ak maotik , Jesu ne bo Nasaret , weritab Josep . 
Ak kilenji Natanael , Tos imuchi kobun Nasaret kiy age tugul ne mie ? Kolenji Pilipu inendet , Nyo si igeer . 
Kigeer Jesu Natanael konyonei ole mi inendet , ak kole agobo inendet , Ogeero , Israelindet iman , ne matinyei ngalset ! 
Kolenji Natanael inendet , Kenaena nee ? Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kageerin , ye kemi mogoiywet kel , kotom koguurin Pilipu . 
Kowolji Natanael kole , Rabbi , i Weritab Jehovah ; i Laitoriatab Israel ! 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Iyani amu kamwaun ale , kaagerin ye kemi mogoiywet kel ? Tatun igeere tuguk che eechen che siirei chu . 
Ak kilenji , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Tatun ogeere kipsengwet koyatoksei , ak kotogostoi malaikaisiek che bo Jehovah ak kochorjigei Weritab chi.
Ak kimi katunisiet eng betut ne bo somok eng Kana ne bo Galili ; ak kimi oloto kametab Jesu : 
ak kiga kiguurji katunisiet Jesu agine , koboto alamalyennyi . 
Ak ye kingorar divaik , kolenji kametab Jesu inendet , Ma kotinyei divaik . 
Ak kilenji Jesu inendet , Chebiosoni , kitingege nee ak inye ? Tom koit sainnyu . 
Kolenji kamet otwogik , Kiy age tugul ne kamwawok , oyai .
Ak kimi oloto terenik lo che eechen che bo beek , che bo koik , ko u biteetab katililetab Yahudik ; kiyamei age tugul debeisiek mut anan ko lo . 
Kolenji Jesu ichek , Onyiit beek terenichoto . Kiinyiit anyun mising . 
Ak kilenji , Osiilu nguno , ak oipchi bounindetab igorta . Ak kiipchi anyun . 
Ak ye kingochamjam bounindetab igorta beek che kagoek divaik , ama nai ole kabunu (ago kiingen otwogik che kasiilei beek) , koguur bounindonoto sandet , 
ak kolenji , Igoitoi chi tugul divaik che miach korok ; ak ye kagoee bik mising , kogon che ma miach : kaigonor divaik che miach agoi nguno .
Taunet nito ne bo kaborunoikyik ne kiyai Jesu eng Kana ne bo Galili , ak kiibortoi torornatennyi ; ak kiiyan inendet alamalyennyi .
Kingobata nito , kochortagei Kapernaum , koboto kamet , ak che tupcho , ak alamalyennyi : ak kibeni oloto betusiek che matia .
Ak kiga rik paska ne bo Yahudik , ak kitogosta Jesu Jerusalem . 
Ak kinyor kotebei eng hekalut che kialdoi eik ak kechirek ak cheptugenik , ak walikab silingisiek : 
ak kiyai kipcharitit ne bo rogoonik che kisach , ak koon tugul komanda eng hekalut , koboto kechirek ak eik ; ak koranda silingisiek che bo walik , ak kogabui mesosiekwak ; 
ak kilenji icheget che kialdoi cheptugenik , Oib tuguchu koba eng oli ; amoyai gotab Baba koek ole kiyae mungaret. 
Kiibwat anyun alamalyennyi kole kigisir kele , Ama ngetkonda agobo gongung .
Kiwolji anyun Yahudik kolenji , Iboruech kaborunet ngoro , amu iyae tuguchu ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ongem hekaluni , si angeet kogeny eng betusiek somok . 
Kile anyun Yahudik , Kigiteech hekaluni eng kenyisiek artam ak lo , ak ingeeti inye eng betusiek somok !
Ago kingalali inendet agobo hekalut ne noto ko bortanyi . 
Ye kingingeet anyun inendet komong eng che kibek , kobwat alamalyennyi kole kiga komwa ngolyondonito ; ak kiiyan sirutiet , ak ngolyot ne kiga mwa Jesu .
Ye kimi Jerusalem eng paska , komi igorta , koyan bik che chang , kainennyi , kogeerei kaborunoikyik che kiyai . 
Ago kima chamdagei Jesu , amu kiingen bik tugul , 
ak amu kima komage kiy chi ne baoriani agobo chi age ; amu kiingen inendet kit ne mi chi orit .
Kimi chi ne bo Parisaik , ne kigiguure Nikodemo , ki bounindet ne bo Yahudik : 
kinyo chichoto ole mi inendet kemoi , ak kolenji , Rabbi , kingen kele i konetindet ne bunu Jehovah : amu mami chi ne imuchi koyai kaborunoichu iyae inye , ngo mami Jehovah koboto inendet .
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Amwaun , iman , iman , ale , Ngot ko ma kisich chi eng siget ne leel , ko magoi imuch kogeer bounatetab Jehovah . 
Kolenji Nikodemo inendet , Kisiktoi ano chi ye kagoosit ? Imuchi kogetyigei moetab kamet kogeny , ak kesich ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Amwaun , iman , iman , ale , Ngot ko ma kisich chi eng beek ak Tamirmiriet , ko magoi imuch komongji bounatetab Jehovah . 
Ne kigisich eng borto ko borto ; ak ne kigisich eng Tamirmiriet ko tamirmiriet . 
Amekwong amu kamwaun ale , Kanyol kesichok eng siget ne leel . 
Usyin koristo ole machei , ak igase cheennyi , ago mengen ole bunu , anan ole wendi : ko u noto chi age tugul ne kagisich eng Tamirmiriet .
Kowolji Nikodemo kolenji , Imuchi kobiitunda ano tuguchu ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , I konetindetab Israel , ameguitosi tuguchu ? 
Amwaun , iman , iman , ale , Kimwae ne kingen , ak kebaorianjini ne kagegeer ; amotaache baornatennyo . 
Ngamwawok tuguk che bo ngony , amoyani , omuktoi ano ogan ngamwawok tuguk che bo kipsengwet ? 
Mami chi ne kitogosta kipsengwet , kobate inendet ne kichorgei eng kipsengwet , inendet ko Weritab chi ne mi kipsengwet .
Ak ko u ye kiigartat Musa erenet eng ongatet , kigartoti ko u noto Weritab chi matiny : 
si konyor sobondab koigeny eng inendet age tugul ne iyani . 
Amu kicham Jehovah ngony mising , kot kogoito Werinnyi ne kigii inegei , si malus age tugul ne iyani inendet , ago si konyor sobondab koigen . 
Amu kima iyokyi Jehovah Werit ngony koruokyi ngony ; ago si kesor ngony eng inendet .
Magiruokyin chi ne iyani inendet : ago inendet ne maiyani , ko kagiruokyi , amu ma iyan eng kainetab Weritab Jehovah ne kigii inegei . 
Ak ni kiruoget , amu kinyonji ngony lapkeiyet , ak kicham bik mesundeito kosiir lapkeiyet ; amu ki yaach boisionikwak . 
Amu wechei lapkeiyet chi tugul ne yaei yaitio , ama nyonei inendet ole mi lapkeiyet , si mangangogis boisionikyik . 
Ago nyonei ole mi lapkeiyet inendet ne yaei imanda , si kobiit kibarta boisionikyik , kele kigiyai eng Jehovah .
Kingobata tuguchu konyo Jesu ak alamalyennyi emet ne kiguure Judea ; ak kibeni oloto koboto ichek , ak kobatisanis . 
Ak kibatisanisiei Johana agine eng Aenon ne negite Salim , amu kimi beek che chang oloto : ak kibwa bik , ak kigibatisan . 
Amu kitom ketoorji Johana korgoret .
Kibiit anyun teebutiet eng alak che bo alamalyetab Johana ak Yahudiot agobo katililet . 
Ak kibwanji Johana , ak kolenji , Rabbi , ibatisanisiei inendet ne kimi koboten eng Jordan komosin , ne kiibaorian agobo inendet , ak bwanjin inendet bik tugul . 
Kowol Johana kole , Magoi imuch chi kotaach kiy , ngo ma kigochi eng kipsengwet . 
Kiobaorianja okweget kole , kiamwa ale , Ma a Kristo , ago olen kigiyokwa andoune inendet . 
Sandet inendet ne tinyei mureret : ago baibai mising choruetab sandet , ne tononi koepchin it inendet , amu kutitab sandet : isuldaat anyun boiboiyoninyu . 
Nyoljin inendet koeet ne matiny , ago aminginitu .
O inendet ne bunu barak kosiir tugul : inendet ne bo ngony ko bo ngony , ak ngalali che bo ngony : inendet ne bunu kipsengwet ko o kosiir tugul . 
Baorianjin inendet kit ne kigogeer ak ne kigogas ; ama mi chi ne taachei baornatennyi . 
Inendet ne kagotaach baornatennyi ko kagonde ngoksennyi , kole bo iman Jehovah . 
Amu ngalali ngalekab Jehovah inendet ne kiiyogu Jehovah ; amu magonu inendet Tamirmiriet eng karogendoet . 
Chamei Kwanda Werit , ak kigonde tuguk tugul eunnyi . 
Tinyei sobondab koigeny ne iyani Werit ; ama keerei sobondo ne magase it Werit , ago tebe neregekab Jehovah baragunnyi .
Ye kingonai Kiptaiyat kole kigogas Parisaik kole kiyaei Jesu bik koek alamalyet ak kobatisani che siirei che kiibatisan Johana 
(ago ma Jesu inendet ne kiibatisanisiei , ago alamalyennyi) , 
kongeet eng Judea , kwo kogeny Galili . 
Ak ki kanyol kobun Samaria .
Kiit anyun nganaset ne bo Samaria , ne kiguure Sukar , ne negite koret ne kiigochi Jakobo werinnyi Josep : 
ak kimi oloto keringetab beek ne bo Jakobo . Kitebyei anyun Jesu eng ye negite keringetab beek , amu ngetatetab bandanyi . Ki olo bo sait lo .
Kinyo kobogoriot ne bo Samaria kosiil beek : kolenji Jesu , Inaga aee . 
Amu kigaba alamalyennyi nganaset koal amitwogik .
Kilenji anyun kobogoriot ne bo Samaria , Katepto ano si isoma beek che iee , ak inye ko i Yahudiot , ak ane ko a kobogoriotab Samaria ? (Amu manamegei Yahudik ak Samarik .) 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Nda kengen konunetab Jehovah , ak inendet ne kalenjin , Inaga beek aee ; ta kaisom inendet , ak ta kagogonin beekab sobon . 
Kolenji kobogoriot , Kiptaiyandani , metinye kit ne isiile , ak loo keringet : inyorjini ano anyun beechoto bo sobon ? 
I o inye eng kwandanyo Jakobo , ne kigonech keringoni , ne kiee inendet , ak werikyik , ak tukyik ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Age tugul ne eei beechu ko ta koamei melel kogeny : 
ago age tugul ne eei beek che agochini ko ma koamei melel agoi ; ago egu beek che agochini kondab beek eng inendet , che kutu agoi sobondab koigeny . 
Kolenji kobogoriot , Kiptaiyandani , inaga beechoto , si ma koama melel , si ma anyone asiile beek eng oli loo . 
Kolenji Jesu kobogoriondonoto , Ui , iguur manongotiondengung , ak obwa yuto .
Kowolji kobogoriot kolenji , Matinye manongotiot . Kolenji Jesu , Kaimwa komie ile , Matinye manongotiot : 
amu kiotebi ak manongotaik mut ; ak inendet ne omi tuwai nguno ko ma manongotiondengung : kaimwa anyun iman nito . 
Kolenji kobogoriot , Kiptaiyandani , kaageer ale i maotio . 
Kisaei kwanisiekyok eng tulwoni ; ak olen okwek , Jerusalem ole kanyol kosae bik .
Kolenji Jesu , Kobogoriondoni , iyana , nyonei sait , ye ma kosae Kwanda eng tulwoni , anan eng Jerusalem . 
Osae ne mongen : kisae achek ne kingen : amu bunu yetunet Yahudik . 
Ago nyonei sait , ak kagoit nguno , ye saei Kwanda saik che bo iman eng tamirmiriet ak imanit : amu chengoti Kwanda che u choto koek che saei inendet . 
Jehovah ko Tamirmiriet : ak kanyol kosa inendet eng tamirmiriet ak iman che saei inendet . 
Kolenji kobogoriot , Angen ale nyonei Mesia (ne keguure Kristo) : ye nyo inendet , komwawech tuguk tugul . 
Kolenji Jesu , A inendet ne angalalun .
Kibwa anyun alamalyennyi ; ak kikwongio amu kingalali ak kobogoriot ; ago ma mwachi chi kole , Ichenge nee ? Anan , Kalya si ongalal ak inendet ?
Kibagakta anyun kobogoriot terennyi bo bei , ak kwo nganaset , ak komwachi bik kolenji , 
Obwa ogeer chito ne kamwawa tuguk tugul che kiayai atkinye kora ! tos Kristo nito ? 
Kimong anyun eng nganaset kobwa ole mi inendet .
Kingota kobwanei , kosom alamalyennyi , kole, Rabbi , amisie . 
Ago kilenji ichek , Atinye amitwogik che aame che mongen . 
Kolenjigei anyun alamalyennyi , Tos kagoipchi chi kiy ne amei ? 
Kolenji Jesu , Amitwogikyuk ko ayai magetab inendet ne kiiyokwa , ak agesu boisiennyi . 
Momwae okwek ole , Ta komi arawek angwanu , si koit kesisiet . Ogeero , amwawok ale , Oyot met , ak ogeer mbarenik , ole kagoleelagitu , kagoyam keges . 
Inendet ne kesei kotaachei melekto , ak koyumi logoek che bo sobondab koigeny ; si koboiboitu tuwai ne kolei ak ne kesei . 
Amu bo iman mwaoni eng ni , Kolei age , kogesei age . 
Kiayoktok oges che kima onyalilji : kigonyalilji alage , ak kaonam okwek uuindab boisienywa .
Kiiyan anyun inendet Samarik che chang che bo nganasanato amu ngolyotab kobogoriot , ne kibaorian kole , Kamwawa tuguk tugul che kiayai atkinye kora . 
Noto anyun , ye kingobwanji inendet Samarik , kosom kole kotebi koboto ichek : ak kibeni oloto betusiek aeng . 
Ak kiiyan alak che chang amu ngolyondennyi ; 
ak kilenji kobogoriot , Kiyani nguno , ma amu ngalelengung : amu kagegasyige ; ak kingen iman kele nito ko Yetindetab ngony .
Ak kingobata betusiechoto aengu kongeet eng oloto kwo Galili . 
Amu kibaorian Jesu inendet kole , matinyei maotiondo teegisto eng emennyi . 
Ak kingonyo anyun Galili , kotaach inendet Galilik , ko kagogeer tuguk tugul che kiyai inendet eng Jerusalem eng igorta : amu kigaba agichek igorta .
Kinyo anyun inendet kogeny Kana ne bo Galili , ole kiyae beek koek divaik . Ak kimi kiboitiot age ne bo kaplaitoriat , ne kimiani werinnyi eng Kapernaum . 
Ye kingogas kole kagomong Jesu eng Judea konyo Galili , kwo ole mi inendet , ak kisom kochorgei , kosoob werinnyi ; amu ki negit kome . 
Kolenji anyun Jesu inendet , Ngot ko mogeer kaborunoik ak kwongutik , ko magoi oyan matiny . 
Kolenji kiboitiondonoto , Kiptaiyandani , choruge kotom kome lakwennyu . 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Ui inye ; sobei weringung . Koyan anyun chichoto ngolyot ne kamwachi Jesu , ak kwo . 
Ak ye kita kochortagei , kotuiyo ak otwogikyik , ak kolenji , Sobei weringung . 
Koteebe anyun kole kogaigaitu ko tia . Kolenji anyun bichoto inendet , Kobagakta eset inendet amut sait tisab . 
Konai anyun kwanda kole ko sainato ne komwachin Jesu kolenjin , Sobei weringung : ak kiiyan inendet , ak gonnyi komugul . 
Noto kaborunet ne bo aeng ne kiyai Jesu koboch ngomong eng Judea konyo Galili .
Kingobata tuguchu kobiit igorta ne bo Yahudik ; ak kotogosta Jesu Jerusalem . 
Ak mitei Jerusalem tamboiyot , ne kainennyi ko Betesda eng kutitab Hebranik , ye negite ormarichetab kechirek ; kitinyei keterusiek mut . 
Kiruitos eng oloto bik che chang che kimiandos , che koriotin , che ingwaldos , che meiyotin , [kogeni wasetab beek : ]
Ak kimi yoto chito age , ne kiga komian kenyisiek sosom ak sisiit . 
Ak ye kingogeer Jesu chichoto koruei , ak konai kole ki u noto eng betusiek che chang , kolenji , Imache kisoobin ? 
Kowolji chito ne miani kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , matinye chi , ne indea tamboiyot , ko kawasgei beek : amu ye ta anyone , kosib kochortagei age . 
Kolenji Jesu anyun , Ngeet , ib itogungung , ak iwe . 
Ak kisob chichoto ngunoto , ak koib itogunnyi ak kwo . Ak ki sabato betunoto . 
Kilenji anyun Yahudik inendet ne kagisoob , Betutab sabato nito , ma chamdaat eng ngatutik iib itogungung .
Ago kiwolji ichek kolenji , Kamwawa inendet ne kagosooba , kolenja , Ib itogungung , ak iwe . 
Koteebe anyun bichoto inendet kole , Ngo chichoto kamwaun kole , Ib itogungung ak iwe ? 
Ago kima nai inendet ne kagisoobi kole ka ngo : amu kiga kwo Jesu , amu kimi bik che chang oloto . 
Kingobata noto konyorji Jesu inendet hekalut , ak kolenji , Keero , kagisoobin : amatata iyai tengek , si manyonjin kit age ne ya ne siirei ni . 
Kiwa anyun chichoto , ak komwachi Yahudik kole Jesu ne kagosoob inendet .
Kius anyun Yahudik Jesu amu ngolyondonito , amu kiyai tuguchu eng betutab sabato . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Boisiei Baba agoi kora , ak aboisiei agane .
Kicheng anyun Yahudik mising kole kobar inendet amu nito , amu kima bistoe sabato kityo , ago mwaei kole Jehovah Kwandanyi , koyaegei kogergeit ak Jehovah .
Kiwolji anyun Jesu ichek kolenji , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Mayaei kiy Werit inegei , ago ne keerei koyaei Kwanda : amu tuguk tugul che yaei inendet , koyaei choto agine Werit ko u noto . 
Amu chamei Kwanda Werit , ak koborjin tuguk tugul che yaei inendet : ak ta koborjin boisionik che eechen che siirei chu , si kobiit okwongie . 
Amu ko u ye ingeeti Kwanda che kigobek ak kosoobi , isoobi Werit ko u noto agine che machei . 
Amu ma iruokyin Kwanda chi age tugul , ago kigogochi Werit kiruoget tugul ; 
si kobiit koteech tugul Werit , ko u ye teechei Kwanda . Inendet ne mateechei Werit ko mateechei Kwanda ne kiiyok inendet .
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Inendet ne kasei ngolyondennyu , ak koyani inendet ne kiiyokwa , kotinyei sobondab koigeny , ama wendi ole mi kiruoget , ago kagomong eng meet komongji sobondo . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Nyonei sait , ak kagoit , ye kas che kigobek kutitab Weritab Jehovah ; ak soptos icheget che kasei . 
Amu ko u ye tinyei Kwanda sobondo inegei , u noto kigogochi Werit kotepto sobondo : 
ak kiigochi kimnatet koyai kiruoget , amu Weritab chi inendet . 
Amokwonge nito : amu nyonei sait , ne tun kasei kutinnyi tugul che mi kererisiek , 
ak komong ; ngeetyin sobondo che kiyaei ne mie ; ak kongeetyi kiruoget icheget che kiyaei ne ya .
Mamuchi ayai kiy anege : aruochi ko u ye agase , ak bo iman kiruogennyu ; amu machenge ayai magennyu , ago magetab inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Ngabaorianjinige , ko ma bo iman baornatennyu . 
Mi age ne baorianjina ; ak angen ale bo iman baornatet ne baorianjina . 
Kioyokyi ngolyot Johana , ak kibaorianji imanda . 
Ago baornatet ne ataache ko mabunu chi : ago amwae tuguchu , si kobiit kesoruok . 
Ki tait inendet ne kilalei kokwengsei : ak kiocham oboiboitune lapkeiyennyi eng betusiek che matia . 
Ago baornatet ne atinye ko o kosiir ne bo Johana : amu boisionik che kigona Kwanda ages , choto che ayae , ko che baorianjina , kole kiiyokwa Kwanda . 
Ak kibaorianja Kwanda inendet ne kiiyokwa . Tom ogas kutinnyi ole kinye kora , ak tom ogeer itondanyi . 
Ama tebyei eng okwek ngolyondennyi : amu moyani inendet ne kiiyogu Jehovah . 
Cham osiachi eng sirutik , amu olen otinye sobondab koigeny eng choto ; ago choto che baorianjina ; 
ago mochame obwanja , si kobiit konyoru sobondo .
Mataache kalosunet eng bik . 
Ago angenok ale motinye chamnyetab Jehovah eng oringwong . 
Kianyo eng kainetab Baba , ama otaacha : ngo nyo age eng kainennyi otaache inendet . 
Omuchi eng nee oyan , che otaagege kalosunet , amochenge kalosunet ne bunu Jehovah ne mi inegei ? 
Molen angandook eng Kwanda : mitei age ne ngandook , Musa noto , ne omangu . 
Amu nda kigoyan Musa , toyana ; amu kisir agobo ane . 
Ago ngo moyani sirutikyik , omuktoi ano oyan ngalekyuk ?
Kingobata tuguchu kwo Jesu bitet age ne bo araraitab Galili , noto ko araraitab Tiberia . 
Ak kiisub inendet tuiyet ne o , amu kigeer kaborunoik che kiyachi che miandos . 
Ak kitogosta Jesu tulwet , kwo koteb ngony eng oloto koboto alamalyennyi . 
Ak kiga rik paska , igorta ne bo Yahudik . 
Kingoyot met anyun Jesu , kogeer tuiyet ne o konyonjin inendet , kolenji Pilipu , Kiale ano makatinik si koam bichu ? 
Kimwaei ni kotieme inendet : amu kiingen inendet kit ne machei koyai . 
Kowolji Pilipu inendet kolenji , Mayamei ichek makatinik che bo denarisiek bogol aeng , si konyor age tugul kitigin . 
Kolenji inendet age ne bo alamalyennyi , Andrea , ngetab kametab Simon Petero , 
Mi yu werit age , ne tinyei makatinik mut che bo sairi , ak njirenik aeng : ago yamei nee anyun chuto eng bik che te chu ? 
Kimwa Jesu kole , Ochob bik kobuur . Ak kimi suswek che chang oloto . Kiibuur anyun bik ; ki olo bo elfusiek mut murenjoto . 
Kinam anyun Jesu makatinik ; ak kingo kagogoito kongoi , koropchi icheget che kitebyei ngony ; ak ko u noto agichek njirenik che te che machei . 
Ak ye kingobiyongso , kolenji alamalyennyi , Oyum katuganik che kanget , si mabet kiy . 
Koyum anyun katuganichato , ak konyiit kerebonik taman ak aeng katuganichato bo makatinik mut che bo sairi , che kangetune icheget che kaamisiei . 
Ye kingogeer anyun bichoto kaborunet ne kayai , kole , Ni maotiot iman ne nyonjin ngony .
Kingonai Jesu kole negit kobwa si konam inendet eng kimnatet , si koyai inendet koek laitoriat , kwo kogeny tulwet inegei .
Ak ye kingoek lagat , kochortagei alamalyennyi koba araraita ; 
ak kilany moingetab beek , kolandae araraita koba Kapernaum . Ak kiga koimenit , ak kitom koit Jesu ole mi ichek . 
Ak kiwasegei araraita amu kiusei usonet ne o . 
Ye kingo kagoba anyun eng araraita ole bo maelisiek somok anan ko somok ak kebeber , kogeer Jesu kowendoti eng araraita barak , ak korikyin moinget : ak kiiyweis . 
Ago kilenji ichek , Ane ; amoiywei . 
Kocham anyun kotaach inendet eng moinget : ak kiit moinget ngunoto emet ole kibendi .
Ki betut ne kiisubi noto kogeer tuiyet ne kitononi eng araraita bitonin , kole mami moinget age oloto , kobate agenge , ak kima lany Jesu moingonoto koboto alamalyennyi , ago kiba alamalyennyi ichegei . 
(ago kibwa moingonik alage eng Tiberia ye negite koret ole kiame makatinik ye kingo kagogoito Kiptaiyat kongoi) : 
Ye kingogeer tuiyet anyun kole mami Jesu oloto , anan alamalyennyi , kolany ichek moingonik , ak kobwa Kapernaum , kochengonu Jesu .
Ak ye kingonyor inendet eng bitet age ne bo araraita , kolenji , Rabbi , koinyone au oli ? 
Kowolji Jesu ichek kolenji , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ochenga , ma amu koogeer kaborunoik , ago amu kooam makatinik ak obiyongse . 
Amoboisie agobo amitwogik che begu , ago oboisie agobo amitwogik che tebyei agoi sobondab koigeny , che konok Weritab chi : amu kigongoch inendet Kwanda , ne inendet ko Jehovah . 
Kilenji anyun ichek inendet , Kiyai nee , si kobiit keyai boisionik che bo Jehovah ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ni boisietab Jehovah , ale , oyan inendet ne kiiyogu Jehovah .
Kilenji ichek inendet anyun , Nee kaborunet ne iyae , si kegeer , ak kiyanin ? Iyae nee ? 
Kiam kwanisiekyok mana eng ongatet ; ko u ye kigisir kele , Kiigochi ichek makatiat ne bunu kipsengwet koam .
Kolenji anyun Jesu ichek , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Kima ko Musa ne kigonok makatiandanato kibunu kipsengwet ; ago konok Baba makatiat ne bo iman ne bunu kipsengwet . 
Amu makatiat ne bo Jehovah ko noto chorugei eng kipsengwet , ak kogochi ngony sobondo . 
Kolenji anyun ichek inendet , Kiptaiyandani , konech makatiandanito koigeny ! 
Kolenji Jesu ichek , A makatiat ne bo sobon : inendet ne nyonjina ko magasei rubet agoi , ak inendet ne iyana ko maamei melel agoi . 
Ago kaamwawok ale , koogeera , ama oyan . 
Bwanjina tugul che kona Kwanda ; ak inendet ne nyonjina ko maone matiny . 
Amu kiachoruge eng kipsengwet , ma si ayai magennyu , ago magetab inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Ak ni magetab inendet ne kiiyokwa , ale , eng tugul che kigona inendet , ko mabetena agot agenge , ago tatun angeeti eng betutab let . 
Amu ni magetab Baba , ale chi age tugul ne keerei Werit , ak koyan inendet , konyoru sobondab koigeny ; ak angeeti inendet eng betutab let .
Kiingunyngungso anyun Yahudik , agobo inendet , amu kimwa kole , A makatiat ne kichorgei eng kipsengwet . 
Ak kile , Tos ma Jesu nito , weritab Josep , ne kingen kwandanyi ak kamet ? Lyon anyun si komwa kole , Kiachoruge eng kipsengwet ? 
Kowolji Jesu anyun kolenji , Amongunyngungse okwege eng okwege . 
Maimuchi chi konyonja , ama ichuut Kwanda ne kiiyokwa : ak angeeti inendet eng betutab let . 
Kigisir eng maotik , Ak kineti tugul eng Jehovah . Age tugul ne kagogas eng Kwanda , ak kagonetgei , konyonjina . 
Molen kigogeer chi age tugul Kwanda , kobate inendet ne kibunu Jehovah , kigogeer inendet Kwanda . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Inendet ne iyani , kotinyei sobondab koigeny . 
A makatiat ne bo sobon . 
Kiam kwanisiekwok mana eng ongatet , ak kibek . 
Ni makatiat ne chorugei eng kipsengwet , ne ngo am chi , ko mameei . 
A makatiat ne sobei ne kichorgei eng kipsengwet : ngo am chi age tugul makatiandani , kosobei koigeny : ee , ak bortanyu makatiat ne agoitoi agobo sobondo ne bo ngony .
Kiborio anyun Yahudik ichegei , kole , Imuktoi ano chichi kogonech bortanyi keam ? 
Kolenji Jesu anyun ichek , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ngot ko moam bortab Weritab chi ak oee korotikyik , ko motinye sobondo eng oringwong . 
Inendet ne amei bortanyu ak koeei korotikyuk kotinyei sobondab koigeny ; ak angeeti inendet eng betutab let . 
Amu amdit iman bortanyu , ak korotikyuk ko che kieei iman . 
Inendet ne amei bortanyu ak koeei korotikyuk komenya , ak amenye inendet . 
Ko u ye kiiyokwa Kwanda ne sobei , ak asobe amu Kwanda ; u noto inendet ne ama , sobei agine amu ane . 
Ni makatiandanato ne kichorgei eng kipsengwet : ma ko u ye kiam kwanisiek ak kobek : inendet ne amei makatiandani kosobei koigeny . 
Kimwa tuguchu eng sunagogit , kota konetisiei eng Kapernaum .
Ye kingogas ni che chang eng alamalyennyi , komwa kole , Uui ngolyondoni : imuchi ngo kogas ? 
Ago kinai Jesu eng orinnyi kole , Ingunyngungjin alamalyennyi ngolyondonito , kolenji ichek , Tos kagonachak nito ? 
Teptoi ano anyun ngot ko tun ogeer Weritab chi kotogostoi ole kimi atkinye ? 
Tamirmiriet ne igoitoi sobondo ; matilei kiy borto : tamirmiriet ak sobondo ngalek che kaamwawok . 
Ago mitei alak eng okwek che maiyani . Amu kinai Jesu koboch taunet icheget che maiyani , ak inendet ne kimachei kongwekta inendet . 
Ak kile , Noto kamwawok , ale , magoi imuch chi konyonja , kobate ne igochin Kwanda .
Koboch yoto kochuchuigei che chang che bo alamalyennyi , amata kobendat ak inendet . 
Kilenji anyun Jesu choto taman ak aeng , Obendi ak okwek ? 
Kowolji anyun Simon Petero , kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , kibendi ole mi ngo ? Itinye ngalek che bo sobondab koigeny . 
Ak kigiyan ak kingen kele i Ne Tilil ne bo Jehovah . 
Kowolji Jesu ichek kolenji , Kima alewenok taman ak aeng , ak oindet age eng okwek ? 
Kimwaei anyun agobo Judas ne bo gab Simon Iskariot , amu ine ne kimachei kongwekta inendet , ne ki agenge eng taman ak aeng .
Ak kingobata tuguchu kowendot Jesu eng Galili : amu ma cham kowendot eng Judea , amu kichengei Yahudik kobar inendet . 
Ak kiga rik igortab Yahudik , igorta ne bo keriosiek . 
Kilenji anyun tupchosiekyik , Ui eng oli , ui agoi Judea , si kogeer alamalyengung agichek boisioniguk che iyae . 
Amu mami chi ne yaei kiy eng ungot , ak kocheng kobartagei . Ngiyai tuguchu , iborjige ngony . 
Amu agot tupchosiekyik agichek , ko ma iyan inendet . 
Kolenji anyun Jesu ichek , Tom koit betunnyu ; ago mi betungwong kotugul . 
Maimuchi ngony kowechok ; ago wecha ane , amu abaoriani agobo ngony , ale , yaach boisionikyik . 
Otogosyi okwek igorta : tom atogosyini ane igorita ; amu tom kosulda betunnyu . 
Ak kingo kagomwachi tuguchuto , kota kotebi eng Galili .
Ago ye kingotogosta tupchosiekyik igorta , kotogosta agine , ago ma ibartaatgei , ago kiwa ko u ne ungotegei . 
Kicheng anyun Yahudik inendet eng igorta , ak kole , Mi ano inendet ?
Ak kimi kangunyngunyet ne o eng tuiyosiek agobo inendet : amu kile alak , Mie chichi ; kole alak , Achicha , ago imaasi tuiyet . 
Ago ma mwa chi ngolyo kotook agobo inendet amu kiiywei Yahudik .
Ago ye kingo kagoit kwenutab igorta kotogosta Jesu kwo hekalut , ak konetis . 
Kokwongio anyun Yahudik kole , Kinaita ano chichi sirutik , ago tom konetgei ? 
Kowolji anyun Jesu kolenji , Konetisiennyu ko ma nenyu , ago bo inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Ngo machei chi age tugul koyai magetab Jehovah , konai konetisioni , ngo bo Jehovah , anan ngamwae anege . 
Inendet ne mwaei che chechik inegei kochengei torornatennyi : ago ne chengei torornatetab ne kiiyok inendet ko bo iman , ama mi kiy ne ma bo imanda eng inendet . 
Tos kima konok Musa Ngatutiet , ago mami chi eng okwek ne yaei Ngatutiet ? Amu nee si ochenge obara ? 
Kowol tuiyet , kole , Itinye oindet : chengei ngo kobarin ?
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kiayai boisiet agenge , ak okwongie okwek tugul . 
Kigonok Musa kamuratanet amu noto (ago ma bo Musa , bo kwanisiek) ; ak omuratani chi eng saboto . 
Ngeyatitoi chi eng betutab sabato , si mabutok Ngatutietab Musa , ko tos onerekyina , amu kaasoob chi komie eng betutab sabato ? 
Amoruoch ko u ye ogeere , ago oruoch kiruoget ne bo imanda .
Kimwa alak eng choto bo Jerusalem kole , Ma inendet ni ne kochengei ichek kobar ? 
Ak ogeero , mwaitooti kotook , ama mwachi kiy ichek inendet . Tos ingen bounik komie kole , nito ko Kristo ? 
Ago kingen ole bunu chichi : ago ye nyo Kristo , ko manaei chi ole bunu .
Kingalal anyun Jesu eng kutit ne o eng hekalut , konetisiei , kole , Ongena , ak ongen ole abunu ; ak kama anyo anege , ago bo iman inendet ne kiiyokwa , ne mongen okwek . 
Angen inendet ; amu abunu inendet , ak kiiyokwa inendet .
Kicheng anyun bichoto konam inendet : ama nam chi inendet , amu kitom koit betunnyi . 
Ak kiiyan inendet che chang che bo tuiyet ; ak kile , Ye nyo Kristo , ko tos yai kaborunoik che siirei cho koyaei chichi ?
Kigasei Parisaik kongunyngungjin tuiyet tuguchuto agobo inendet ; ak kiiyok tisiik che eechen ak Parisaik kiptainik kobwa konam inendet . 
Kole Jesu anyun , Ta ami kobotok ne matia , si awa ole mi inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Tun ochenga , amonyorua : ak ole ami , ko momuchi obwa . 
Komwachigei anyun Yahudik kole , Wendi ano chichi si ma kinyoru inendet ? Tos wendi ole mi icheget che kigoiyestochi Yunanik , si konet Yunanik ? 
Nee anyun ngolyondoni kamwa , kole , Ochenga , amonyorua : ak ole ami , ko momuchi obwa ?
Eng betut ne bo let , betunoto o bo igorta , kotonon Jesu ak komwa eng kutit ne o , kole , Ngo amei chi melel , ko ingonyonja , ak koee . 
Inendet ne iyana , ko u ye kigomwa sirutiet , kole , bunu moennyi ainosiekab beek che sobei . 
Ago kimwaei nito agobo Tamirmiriet , ne tun taachei ichek che iyani inendet : amu kitom kegon Tamirmiriet ; amu kitom kitoror Jesu .
Ye kingogas alak che bo tuiyet ngalechuto , kole , Nito maotiot iman . 
Kole alak , Nito ko Kristo . Ago kile alage , Tos bunu Kristo Galili ? 
Ma mwa sirutiet , kole , mongune Kristo keswek che bo Daudi , ak kobun Betlehem , nganaset ole kimi Daudi ? 
Kibiit anyun toiyet eng tuiyet agobo inendet . 
Ak kimach alak konam inendet ; ago ma nam chi inendet .
Kibwa anyun kiptainik ole mi tisiik che eechen ak Parisaik ; ak kolenji , Kalya si momutu inendet ? 
Kowol kiptainik kole , Kitom kongalali chi ko u ni . 
Kowolji anyun Parisaik ichek , kolenji , Kagibeetok ak okwek ? 
Kigoyan inendet age tugul eng bounik , anan eng Parisaik ? 
Ago chubotin bichu che manaei Ngatutiet .
Kilenji Nikodemo (ne kigawa ole mi inendet atkinye tai , ne ki age eng ichek) , 
Tos iruokyin chi Ngatutiennyo , kotom kegas ngalekyik ak kenai kit ne yaei ? 
Kowolji anyun inendet kolenji , I bo Galili aginye ? Cheng , ak igeer amu mamongune Galili maotiondo .
Kiwa chi ktugul anyun gonnyi :
Ago kiwa Jesus tulwetab Emitik . 
Ak kimus karon konyo hekalut , ak kibwa bik tugul ole mi inendet ; ak kiteb ngony , konet ichek . 
Ak kiimut sirik ak Parisaik kobogoriot ne kiginamji ibetab ge ; ak ye kingo kaginde kwenut , 
kelenji , Konetindoni , kaginam kobogoriondoni eng ibetab ge , kota komi ibetab ge . 
Kingatech Musa eng Ngatutiet kole , kilage koik ne u nito : ara ilen nee inye ? 
Kimwaei ngolyondonito kotiemei inendet , si kosich kit ne kitaame . Ago kiinguruk Jesu , kosir ngony eng mornennyi . 
Ago ye kingota koteepse inendet , kotonon , ak kolenji , Ingotoi ne matinye tengek eng okwek kowir eng koita . 
Ak kiinguruk kogeny kosir ngony eng mornennyi . 
Ak ye kingogas ichek ngolyondonoto , komanda kobee agenge agenge , koboch ne o agoi ne bo let : ak kinget Jesu inegei , ak kobogoriondonoto eng ole kimi , kotononi eng kwen . 
Kotonon Jesu anyun , ak kolenji , Kobogoriondoni , mi ano ichek ? Ma igikyin chi ? 
Ak kile , Ma igikya chi , Kiptaiyandani . Ak kilenji Jesu , Magikyinin agane : ui anyun ; koboch nguno , komatata iyai tengek .
Kimwachi Jesu anyun ichek kogeny , kolenji , A lapkeiyet ne bo ngony : inendet ne isuba ko mawendoti eng mesundeito , ago nyoru lapkeiyetab sobondo .
Kolenji anyun Parisaik inendet , Ibaorianjinige : ma bo iman baornatengung . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Agot ngabaorianjinige , ko bo iman baornatennyu ; amu angen ole abunu , ak ole awendi ; ago mongen ole abunu , anan ole awendi . 
Oruochi ko u magetab borto ; maruokyini chi ane . 
Ee , agot ngaruoch , ko bo iman kiruogennyu ; amu mami anege , ago kimi ak Kwanda ne kiiyokwa . 
Ee , ak kigisir eng Ngatutiengwong kele , bo iman baornatetab bik aeng . 
A inendet ne abaorianjinige , ak baorianjina Kwanda ne kiiyokwa . 
Kolenji anyun ichek inendet , Mi ano Kwandangung ? Kowol Jesu kole , Mongena , anan Baba : nda kigonaa , ta kiongen Baba agine .
Kimwa inendet ngalechu eng ole kigonore silingisiek , ye kiinetisiei eng hekalut : ak ma nam chi inendet ; amu kitom koit sainnyi .
Kimwachi anyun icheget kogeny , kolenji , Awendi , ak tun ochenga , ak obegu eng tengektangwong : ole awendi , ko momuchi obwa . 
Kile anyun Yahudik , Tos bargei ? amu mwaei kole , Ole awendi , ko momuchi obwa ? 
Ak kilenji , O bo oli bo ngony , a bo barak : o bo ngonyuni ; ma bo ane ngonyuni . 
Noto kaamwawok , ale , obegu eng tengekwogikwok : amu ngo moyuani ole a inendet , obegu eng tengekwogikwok . 
Kilenji anyun ichek inendet , I ngo ? Kolenji Jesu , Noto kiamwawok koboch taunet . 
Atinye tuguk che chang che amwae ak che aruochi agobo okwek : ago bo iman inendet ne kiiyokwa ; ak amwachini ngony tuguk che kiagas eng inendet .
Ago ma iguiyo kole mwachin agobo Kwanda . 
Kilenji Jesu anyun , Ye kaouite Weritab chi , onai anyun eng betunoto ole a inendet , amayae kiy anege , ago amwae tuguchu ko u ye kiineta Kwanda . 
Ak kimi tuwai ak inendet ne kiiyokwa ; ma bagakta anege ; amu ayae kotugul tuguchoto chamaksei eng inendet . 
Ak ye kita komwaei tuguchu , koyan inendet che chang .
Kilenji Jesu anyun Yahudichoto kiga koyan inendet , Ngot otebye okwek eng ngolyondennyu , ko o alamalyennyu iman ; 
ak onai imanda , ak kotiachak imanda . 
Kowolji ichek inendet kolenji , Ki keswekab Abraham , ak tom keegu otwogikab chi age tugul ole kinye kora : imwaitoi ano anyun ile , Kitiachok ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Age tugul ne yaei tengek ko otwogindetab tengek . 
Ak matebyei otwogindet eng got koigeny : tebyei werit koigeny . 
Ngotiachak anyun Werit , ko otiagotin iman . 
Angen ale o keswekab Abraham ; ago ochenge obara , amu matinyei ngolyondennyu ole tebe eng okwek . 
Amwae tuguk che kiageer eng Baba : ak oyae tuguchoto kiogas eng kwandangwong .
Kowolji kolenji , Kwandanyo ko Abraham . Kolenji Jesu , Nda kio lagokab Abraham , ta kioyae boisiosiekab Abraham . 
Ago ngo ochenge obara , chito ne kamwawok ngalek che bo iman , che kiagas eng Jehovah : kima yai ko u noto Abraham . 
Oyae boisionik che bo kwandangwong . Kilenji anyun inendet , Kima kisichech eng sokset ; kitinye Kwanda agenge , noto ko Jehovah . 
Komwachi Jesu ichek kolenji , Nda ka Kwandangwong Jehovah , ta kaochama : amu kianyo abunu Jehovah ; kima anyo anege , ago kiiyokwa inendet . 
Amu nee si monai choto amwae ? Amu momuchi ogas ngolyondennyu . 
O bo kwandangwong oindet , ak ochame oyai magutikab kwandangwong . Ki rumindet koboch taunet , ama tononi eng imanit , amu mami imanit eng inendet . Ye mwaei lembech , komwaei agobo tugukyik : amu kiplembechwa inendet , ak kwanda ne bo noto . 
Ago moyana amu amwae imanit . 
Ngo eng okwek ne igikyina kole atinye tengek ? Ngot amwae imanit , ko amu nee anyun si moyana ? 
Inendet ne bo Jehovah kogasei ngalekab Jehovah : noto anyun mogase okwek , amu mobo Jehovah .
Kowolji anyun Yahudik kolenji , Magimwae achek iman kele , I Samarindet , ak itinye oindet ? 
Kowol Jesu kole , Matinye oindet ; ago agonyiti Baba , ak otewera . 
Ago machenge torornatennyu : mitei agenge ne chengei ak koruochi . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ngo rib chi ngolyondennyu ko mageerei meet agoi . 
Kolenji anyun Yahudik , Kingen nguno kele itinye oindet . Kigome Abraham , ak kigobek maotik ; ak imwae ile , Ngo rib chi ngolyondennyu , ko machamjami meet agoi . 
Tos i o isiir kwandanyo Abraham , ne kigome ? Ak kigobek maotik : iyaege iegu ngo ? 
Kowol Jesu kole , Ngot atororige , ko buch torornatannyu : Kwandanyu ne itorora ; ne omwae ole , inendet ko Jehovah nengwong ; 
ak tom onai inendet : ago angen inendet ; ak ngot amwa ale , mangen inendet , aegu kiplembechwa , ko u okwek : ago angen inendet , ak aribe ngolyondennyi . 
Kibaibai kwandangwong Abraham kogeer betunnyu ; ak kigeer , ak kogasgei . 
Kolenji Yahudik anyun , Tom iit kenyisiek konom , ak kiigeer Abraham ? 
Kolenji Jesu , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Kingotom kobiit Abraham , ami . 
Kiinem anyun koik komachei kowire inendet : ago kiunggei Jesu , ak komanda eng hekalut .
Ak ye kisiirtoi , kogeer chito ne ki korat koboch ko kagisich . 
Ak kiteebe inendet alamalyennyi , kolenji , Rabbi , ngo ne kiyai tengekto , chichi anan sigikyik , si kesich ko korat ? 
Kowol Jesu kole , Kima yai chichi tengekto , anan sigikyik ; ago si kobiit kotook boisiosiekab Jehovah eng inendet . 
Kanyol keyai boisiosiekab inendet ne kiiyokwa , ko ta ko bet : nyonei kemout , ye ma komuchi chi kobois . 
Ye ta ami ngony , ko a lapkeiyetab ngony . 
Ye kingo kagomwa ko u noto , kongutyi ngungunyek , ak kotangwar , ak koiile konyekyik ngungunyechato , 
ak kolenji , Ui iunde eng tamboiyotab Siloam (ye kiweech kele , Kiyokto) . Kiwa anyun , ak koun , ak konyo kogeertoi .
Kimwa anyun bikab kokwet , ak che kiga kogeer inendet eng tai kole somindet , kole , Tos ma inendet ni ne kicham kotebyei ak kosomsei ? 
Kole alage , Inendet : kole alage , Achicha , ago kerge ak inendet . Kole chichoto , A inendet . 
Kilenji anyun ichek inendet , Kagiyatita ano konyeguk ? 
Kowol kole , Katangwar ngungunyek chito ne keguure Jesu , ak koiile konyekyuk , ak kolenja , Ui Siloam , ak iunde : kaawe anyun ak aun , ak ageerte . 
Ak kilenji , Mi ano inendet ? Kole , Mangen .
Kiimut ichek chichoto ki korat eng tai , kwo ole mi Parisaik . 
Ki sabato betunoto ye kitangwari Jesu ngungunyek , si koyate konyekab chichoto . 
Koteebe anyun Parisaik kogeny inendet kole , Katepto ano si igeerte . Ak kilenji , Kagoiile konyekyuk ngungunyek che katangwar , ak kaaun , ak kaageerte . 
Kole alak che bo Parisaik anyun , Mabunu Jehovah chichi , amu maribei sabato . Ago kile alage , Imuktoi ano chi ne kiptengekyo koyai kaborunoik che u chu ? Ak kibiit toiyet eng kwenunywa . 
Kilenji anyun kogeny chito ne korat , Imwae nee agobo inendet , amu kayat konyeguk ? Ak kile , Maotio .
Ma iyan anyun Yahudik agobo inendet , kole , ko korat , ak , kagogeerto , agoi koguur sigikab chichoto kagogeerto , 
ak koteebe kolenji , Tos weringwong ni , ne omwae ole kigisich ko korat ? Katepto ano si kogeerto nguno ? 
Kowol sigikyik kole , Kingen kele werinnyo nito , ak kingen kele kigisich ko korat : 
ago magingen ole katepto si kogeerto nguno ; ak magingen inendet ne kayatei konyekyik : oteebe inendet ; kogoeet ; ingomwa inegei . 
Kimwa ngalechu sigikyik , amu kiiywei Yahudik : amu kiga sib kochamnyechi Yahudik , kole , ngo ngany chi age tugul kole Kristo inendet , kibeetoi eng sunagogit . 
Kimwa anyun sigikyik amu noto , kole , Oteebe , amu kogoeet inendet .
Kiguur anyun ne bo aeng bichoto chichoto ki korat , ak kolenji , Igochi Jehovah kalosunet : kingen kele kiptengekyo chichi . 
Kowol anyun inendet kole , Ngo kiptengekyo chichoto , ko mangen : angen kit agenge , ale , koa korat , ago ageertoi nguno . 
Kolenji anyun ichek inendet , Kayaun nee ? Kayatita ano konyeguk ? 
Kowolji ichek kolenji , Kaamwawok , ama ogas : kalya si omach ogas kogeny ? Omache koegu ak okwek alamalennyi ? 
Ak kingemji kut inendet kole , I alamalyennyi so ? Ago ki alamalyetab Musa achek . 
Kingen kele kigongalalji Jehovah Musa : ago magingen kole bo chichi . 
Kowolji chichoto icheget kolenji , Kwongut nito anyun ! amu mongen ole bunu , ago kagoyat konyekyuk . 
Kingen kele magasei Jehovah kiptengeginik : ago ngolosu chi age tugul Jehovah , ak koyai magennyi , kogasei inendet . 
Koboch ngetoi ngony ko ma kigas kele kiyat chi konyekab chito ne kigisich ko korat . 
Nda ma bunu Jehovah chichi ko magoi imuch koyai kiy . 
Kowolji inendet kolenji , Kigisikten iman tengekwogik , ak inetech ? Ak kitoorta inendet kwo sang .
Kigas Jesu kole kagetoorta inendet kwo sang ; ak kingonyor inendet , kolenji , Tos iyani Weritab Jehovah ? 
Ak kiwol kole , Ngo noto , Kiptaiyandani ? si kobiit ayan inendet . 
Kolenji Jesu , Kaigeer inendet , ak ko inendet ni ngalali koboten . 
Ak kile , Kiptaiyandani , ayani . Ak kogutungji kolos inendet .
Ak kile Jesu , Kianyo ngonyuni amu kiruoget , si kobiit kogeerto che mageertoi ; ak kogorio che keertoi . 
Kigas tuguchuto alak che bo Parisaik che kimi koboto inendet , ak kolenji , Ki koriotin agachek ? 
Kolenji Jesu , Nda o koriotin okwek , ta motinye tengek ; ago nguno omwae ole , Kigeertoi : noto anyun , tebyei tengektangwong .
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Chorin ak ko rebin inendet ne mabunei kurgetab biutab kechirek , ne lanyei oldo age . 
Ago mestowotab kechirek inendet ne bunei kurget . 
Yatyin inendet ribindetab kurget ; ak kasei kechirek kutinnyi : ak kuurei kechirekyik eng kainaikwak , ak kondoe ichek . 
Ak ye kagomaanda inendet chechiget tugul koba sang , kondoe , ak kosub kechirek inendet : amu ingen kutinnyi . 
Ak machamei kosub toondet , ago mwee : amu manaei kutuswekab toek . 
Komwachi Jesu ichek kalewenoni : ago ma iguiyo ichek kole nee tuguchoto kiga mwachi .
Kolenji anyun Jesu ichek kogeny , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , A kurgetab kechirek . 
Chorik ak ko rebik tugul che kiindounena : ago ma kas kechirek ichek . 
A kurget : ngwo chi age tugul go ne buna ane , kesoru , ak kwo go , ak komanda sang , ak konyor ole kiyage . 
Nyonei chorindet si kochor , ak kobar , ak kongem kityo : kianyo si kobiit konyor sobondo , ak kotepto sobonato inne .
A mestowot ne mie : igoitoi mestowot ne mie sobondanyi agobo kechirek . 
Ago inendet ne otwogin , ne ma mestowot , ne ma chitab kobo kechirek , kogeerei konyonei suiyot , ak kobagakta kechirek , ak komwei , ak konam anyun suiyot ichek , ak koiyesta : 
komwei inendet amu otwogin , ak mamage kiy kechirek . 
A mestowot ne mie ; ak angen chechuk , ak kongena chechuk ,
