ko u ye ingena Kwanda , ak angen Kwanda ; ak agoitoi sobondanyu agobo kechirek . 
Ak atinye kechirek alak , che ma bo biuni : kanyol aget choto agichek , si kogas kutinnyu : ak koek akwet agenge , ak mestowot agenge .
Chama anyun Kwanda amu noto , amu agoitoi sobondanyu , si kobiit anam kogeny . 
Marebena chi , ago agoitoi anege . Atinye kimnatet agoito , ak atinye kimnatet anam kogeny . Kiataach ngatutioni eng Baba .
Kibiit toiyet kogeny eng Yahudik agobo ngalechuto . 
Ak kile che chang eng ichek , Tinyei oindet , ak koamei iywek ; kalya si ogas inendet ? 
Kole alage , Ma bo ngalechu chi ne tinyei oindet . Tos imuchi oindet koyat konyekab chito ne korat ?
Ak kimi igortab katabanet eng Jerusalem : ak ki betusiekab kaititindo ; 
ak kiwendot Jesu eng hekalut eng keterut ne bo Solomon . 
Kibwa anyun Yahudik koyiem inendet , kolenji , Igonech kigenisie eng saget kot kotianit ? Ngo i Kristo , imwawech komie . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kiamwawok , amoyani : boisiosiek che ayae eng kainetab Baba ko choto che baorianjina . 
463 Ago moyani , amu mobo kechirekyuk . 
Kasei kutinnyu kechirekyuk , ak angen ichek , ak kosuba : 
ak agochini ichek sobondab koigeny ; ak magoi lusyo , ama rebena chi ichek eng eunnyu . 
O Baba , ne kigona ichek , kosiir tugul ; ama mi chi ne imuchi koreb ichek eng eutab Baba . 
Ane ak Kwanda , ko ki agenge .
Kinam anyun Yahudik koik kogeny kolen kolach inendet . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Koaboruok boisiosiek che chang che miach che bunu Kwanda ; olacha agobo boisio nee eng choto ? 
Kowolji Yahudik inendet kolenji , Magilachin amu boisiet ne mie , ago amu chotisiet ; ak amu inye ne i chi , iyaege iegu Jehovah . 
Kowolji Jesu bichoto , kolenji , Tos ma sirat eng Ngatutiengwong kele , Kiamwa ale , O cheptalelisiek ? 
Ngo kigoguure inendet ichek cheptalelisiek , icheget che kinyonji ngolyotab Jehovah (ama imugaksei kebut sirutiet) , 
tos omwae agobo inendet , ne kiitaban Kwanda ak koyokto kwo ngony , olenjini , Ichotisiei ; amu kiale , A Weritab Jehovah ? 
Ngot ko mayai boisiosiekab Kwandanyu , ko mat oyana . 
Ago ngayai , ko agot ngo moyana , oyan boisiosiek : si kobiit onai ak oyan ole mi Kwanda eng ane , ak ane eng Kwanda . 
Kicheng anyun kogeny konam inendet : ago kibetito eng eunekwak .
Ak kiwa kogeny Jordan komosin ole kiibatisanisie Johana eng tai ; ak kitebi eng oloto . 
Ak kibwanji che chang inendet ; ak kole , Kima yai Johana kaborunet ; ago tuguk alak tugul che kimwa Johana agobo chichi ko bo iman . 
Ak kiiyan inendet che chang eng oloto .
Ak kimian chito age ne kiguure Lasaro , ne bo Betania , ne bo nganasetab Maria ak chepkamet Marta . 
Ak ki Maria nito ne kiil Kiptaiyat eng mwaita , ak kouuse kelyekyik sumeekyik , ne kitinyei ngetab kamet , Lasaro , ne kimian . 
Kiiyokyi chepkametwogichato inendet ngolyot , kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , keero , miani inendet ne ichame .
Ago ye kingogas Jesu noto , kole , Ma bo meet mianoto , ago bo torornatetab Jehovah , ak kilosune Weritab Jehovah noto .
Ak kichamei Jesu Marta , ak chepkamet , ak Lasaro . 
Kingogas anyun kole miani , kota kotebi betusiek aeng eng ole kimi . 
Kingobatga nito anyun , kolenji alamalyet , Ongebe Judea kogeny . 
Kolenji alamalyet , Rabbi , kochengei Yahudik kolachin eng koik ; ak iwendi olindo kogeny ? 
Kowol Jesu kole , Tos mami saisiek tamanu ak aeng eng betut ? Ngo wendot chi bet , ko maginachi , amu keerei lapkeiyetab ngonyuni . 
Ago ngo wendot chi kemoi , kinachi , amu mami lapkeiyet eng inendet . 
Komwa tuguchu : ak ye ibata kolenji ichek , Inuuchi choruennyu Lasaro ; ago awendi , si angeet inendet eng ruondo . 
Kolenji anyun alamalyet inendet , Kiptaiyandani , ngot konuuchi , ko kaga ta kosobei . 
Ago kimwaei Jesu agobo meennyi : ak kilen ichek abere mwaei agobo ruondo ne kiga konuuch . 
Kimwachi anyun Jesu ichek komie , kolenji , Kogome Lasaro . 
Ago abaibai agobo okwek amu kima ami olindo , si kobiit oyan ; ago ongebe ole mi inendet . 
Kolenji anyun Tomas , ne kiguure Didumo , alamalyet chun alak , Ongebe ak achek , si kobiit kebegu ak inendet .
Ye kingoit Jesu anyun , konyor kole kiga kotebe kererit betusiek angwan . 
Ki negite Betania Jerusalem , ki bo olo bo maelisiek aeng ; 
ak kigabwanji che chang che bo Yahudik Marta ak Maria si kogaigai ichek agobo ngetab kamet .
Kingogas anyun Marta kole , nyonei Jesu , kwo kotorokta inendet ; ago kita kotebi Maria eng go . 
Kolenji Marta anyun Jesu , Kiptaiyandani , nda kiimi yu , ta kima komeei werit ne kitupche . 
Ago angen agot nguno ale , kit age tugul ne isome Jehovah , kogonin Jehovah . 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Ta kongeetei ngetab komet . 
Kolenji Marta inendet , Angen ale ngeetei eng ngeetyet ne bo betutab let . 
Kolenji Jesu , A ngeetyet , ak sobondo : inendet ne iyana , agot ngo me , ko ta kosobei : 
ak chi age tugul ne sobei ak koyanan ko mameei matiny . Tos iyani inye nito ? 
Kolenji , We , Kiptaiyandani ; kaayan ale i Kristo , Weritab Jehovah , ne nyonei ngony .
Ak ye kingo kagomwa nito cheboto , kwo , ak koguur Maria , chepkamet , eng ungot , kole , Mitei yu Konetindet ; kuurin . 
Ak ye kingogas noto , kongeet kochakta kwo ole mi inendet . 
Ago kitomo koit Jesu nganasanato , ago kita komi ole kiga tuiyechi ak Marta . 
Kiisub anyun Yahudik cheboto , icheget che kimi koboto inendet eng go kogoigoi , ye kingogeer kongeet Maria , ak kochakta komanda sang , kolen wendi kererit korirei eng oloto .
Ye kingoit anyun Maria ole mi Jesu , ak kogeer inendet , kobutyi kelyekyik , ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , nda kiimi yu , ta kima komeei werit ne kitupche . 
Ye kingogeer Jesu anyun inendet korirei , ak korirtos agichek Yahudik che kigabwa koboto inendet , kogas kingwan eng tamirmiriet , koarogen , 
ak kole , Kionde ano ? Kolenji , Nyo , Kiptaiyandani , keer . 
Korir Jesu . 
Kole anyun Yahudik , Ogeer anyun-o ole kichamdoi inendet ! 
Ago kile alak eng ichek , Kiga temene chichi , ne kiyatei konyekab chito ne ki korat , koger si mame agine chichi ?
Kogas anyun Jesu kingwan kogeny eng orinnyi konyonei kererit . Ki kebenet , ak kigegere koita kurget . 
Kole Jesu , Oiste koita . Kolenji Marta , chepkametab inendet ne kime , Kiptaiyandani , kogobul : amu koboch ngome ko betusiek angwan . 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Kama amwaun , ale , ngiyani , igeere torornatetab Jehovah ? 
Koisto anyun koita . Ak kiyot met Jesu ak kole , Baba, amwaun kongoi ale kaigasa . 
Ak kaanai ale igasa eng ui tugul : ago kaamwa ni amu tuiyoni tononi eng yuto , si kobiit koyan kole kiiyokwa . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa ko u noto , komwa eng kutit ne o , kole , Lasaro , mongu ! 
Komong anyun inendet ne kiga me , ko ratotin eunek ak kelyek eng ngoroik che bo kererit ; ak kiga kirate togennyi anget . Kolenji Jesu bichoto , Otiach , ak ounde kwo .
Kiiyan anyun inendet che chang che bo Yahudik che kigabwa ole mi Maria , ak kogeer tuguk che kayai Jesu . 
Ago kiba alak ole mi Parisaik , ak komwachi ichek tuguk che kagoyai Jesu .
Kiguur anyun kiruoget tisiik che eechen ak Parisaik , ak kole , Kiyai nee ? Amu yaei chichi kaborunoik che chang . 
Ngot kebagakte inendet ko u ni , koyani inendet bik tugul : asi kobwa Romanik korebenech emennyo ak bororiennyo . 
Ak kilenji age eng ichek , ne inendet ko Kaiapa ne ki tisiindet ne o kenyinoto , Mongen okwek kiy age tugul , 
mongen ole mieitu eng okwek ngo mechi bik chito agenge , si ma bet bororiet komugul . 
Kima komwaei inegei noto : ago kimaoten amu ki tisiindet ne o kenyinoto , kole , komechi Jesu bororiet ; 
ma agobo bororiet inegei , ago si kobiit koyum lagokab Jehovah che yestootin si kobiit koek agenge .
Koboch betunoto anyun ak kwo tai , koruogot agobo ole bartoi inendet . 
Mata kowendot Jesu anyun eng ole toogu eng ole mi Yahudik , ago kiwa eng oloto kwo emet ne negite surkwen , agoi nganaset ne kiguure Epraim ; ak kitebi eng oloto koboto alamalyet . 
Kiga korik paska ne bo Yahudik : ak kiba che chang eng emet kotogosta Jerusalem kotom koit paska , koba koanyinygei . 
Kicheng anyun Jesu , ak kolenjigei , kotonondos eng hekalut , Obwati nee okwek ? Tos olen manyonei inendet igorta ? 
Kiga ngat tisiik che eechen ak Parisaik , kole , ngo nai chi age tugul ole mitei , kobor , si kobiit konam ichek inendet .
Ak kingota komi betusiek lo si koit paska konyo Jesu Bertania , ole kimi Lasaro , ne kiingeeti Jesu komong eng che kibek . 
Kichopchi ichek eng oloto inendet amitwogik che bo lagat : koboisiechi Marta ; ago kimi Lasaro koboto ichek che kiamisiei ak inendet . 
Kiinem anyun Maria mwaita ne nyamdut ne bo ratilit agenge , ne bo kamanutiet ne o , ak koiile kelyekab Jesu , ak kouuse sumeekyik kelyekyik : ak kinyi got nyamdutiet ne bo mwaata . 
Ago kile Judas Iskariot , ne ki agenge ne bo alamalyennyi , ne kimachei kongwekta inendet , 
Ko amu nee si ma kialdae mwai denarisiek bogol somok , si kigochi kibananok ? 
Kimwa ni anyun , ma amu kirire kibananok ; ago amu ki chorin , ak kitinyei lolet , ak kiibei tuguk che mi orit . 
Kole Jesu , Obagakte kogonorji betutab tubennyu . 
Amu mi kibananok kobotok kotugul ; ago mami ane ak okwek kotugul .
Kinai anyun bik che chang che bo Yahudik kole mi oloto : ak kibwa , ma agobo Jesu inegei , ago si kobiit kogeer Lasaro agine , ne kiga kongeet inendet eng che kibek . 
Ago kiiruoch tisiik che eechen kole kobar Lasaro agine ; 
amu kiitabangei che chang che bo Yahudik , koba koyan Jesu amu inendet .
Ak eng betut ne kiisubi noto , ye kingogas tuiyet ne o ne bo bik che kigabwa igorta , kole nyonei Jesu Jerusalem , 
konam temenik che bo sosik , ak koba kotorokta inendet , ak komwa eng kutit ne o kole , Hosanna : Iberurot inendet ne nyonei eng kainetab Kiptaiyat , noto Laitoriatab Israel !
Ak ye kingo kagonyor Jesu moitab sigiriet , kolany ; ko u ye kigisir kele , 
Ameiywei , inye , ee , cheptab Sion : keero , nyonei Laitoriandengung , kobunu moitab sigiriet . 
Kima iguiyo alamalyennyi eng tai tuguchuto : ago kingo kagitoror Jesu , kobwat anyun ichek kole kigisir tuguchuto agobo inendet , ak kiga keyachi inendet tuguchuto .
Kibaorian anyun tuiyet ne kimi koboto inendet ye kiguurei Lasaro komong eng kererit , ak kiingeet inendet eng che kibek . 
Kiba anyun tuiyet amu noto kotorokta inendet , amu kigas kole kiga koyai kaborunoni . 
Kimwachigei anyun Parisaik ichegei kole , Ogeero , ma oterter eng kiy : ogeero , kagosub inendet bik tugul che bo ngony .
Ak kimi Yunanik alage eng che kigaba kotogosta kosa eng igorta . 
Kibwa choto anyun ole mi Pilipu , ne bo Betsaida ne bo Galili , ak koteebe inendet kole , Kiptaiyandani , kimache kegeer Jesu . 
Kinyo Pilipu komwachi Andrea : ak kibwa Andrea ak Pilipu komwachi Jesu . 
Ak kiwolji Jesu kolenji , Kait sait , ne kitorore Weritab chi . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ngo mame baiywat ne ibutyin ngungunyek , kotebyei inegei ; ago ngo me , koiyiei che chang . 
Inendet ne chamei sobondanyi kobeeti ; ak inendet ne wechei sobondanyi eng ngonyuni korib kot koit sobondab koigeny . 
Ngo boisiewa chi age tugul , ko nyolu kosubota ; ak si ole ami , komi oloto agine kiboitiondennyu : ngo boisiewa chi , koteechei inendet Kwanda .
Nyalili nguno sobondanyu ; amwae nee anyun ? Baba we , sorua eng saini ? Ago kianyonji saini amu ngolyondito . 
Baba , itoror kainengung . Kimong anyun kutit eng kipsengwet , kole , Kiatoror ak ta atorori kogeny .
Kimwa anyun tuiyet ne kitononi eng oloto kogasei , kole , Katul : kole alak , Kangalalji malaikaiyat . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kama nyo kutini agobo ane , ago agobo okwek . 
Kabiit nguno kiruogetab ngonyuni : ak kagitoorta anyun nguno ne o ne bo ngony komanda . 
Ak ye kiuita eng ngony , amutyige bik tugul . 
Ago kimwa ni , kobortoi meet ole meitoi .
Kiwolji anyun tuiyet inendet , kolenji , Kigegas eng Ngatutik kele tebyei Kristo koigeny : teptoi ano anyun si imwa ile , Kanyol keuito Weritab chi ? Ngo Weroto bo chi ? 
Kolenji Jesu anyun , Ta komi lapkeiyet eng kwenungwong eng betusiek che matia . Obendoti ye ta otinye lapkeiyet , si ma namak mesundeito : ak inendet ne wendoti eng mesundeito ko manaei ole wendi . 
Ye ta otinye lapkeiyet , oyan lapkeiyet , si kobiit oegu werikab lapkeiyet . Kimwa Jesu tuguchu , ak kwo koungegei ichek .
Ago nga kiga koyai kaborunoik che chang che te cho eng tainywa , ko ma iyan inendet : 
si kobiit kosulda ngolyotab maotiot Isaia , ne kimwa , kole , Kiptaiyandani , kiiyan ngo ngalekyok ? Ak kigengangji ngo eutab Kiptaiyat ?
Ma imuch anyun koyan amu ngolyondonito , amu kimwa Isaia kogeny , kole ,
Kigotuch inendet konyekwak , ak kigogochi inendet mugulelwekwak kouuegitu ; Si ma keere konyekwak , anan konai eng mugulelwekwak , Ak koweek , Ak asoob ichek .
Kimwa tuguchu Isaia , amu kigeer torornatennyi ; ak kingalal agobo inendet . 
Ago kiiyan inendet che chang agot eng bounik ; ago ma ngany inendet amu Parisaik , si ma kion ichek eng sunagogit : 
amu kichamei kalosunetab bik kosiir kalosunetab Jehovah .
Ak kimwa Jesu eng kutit ne o , kole , Inendet ne iyana , ko maiyana ane , ago iyani inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Ak inendet ne keera kogeerei inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Kianyo aegu lapkeiyet eng ngony , si ma kotebyei eng mesundeito chi age tugul ne iyana . 
Ak ngo kas chi age tugul ngalekyuk , ama rib , ko maruokyini inendet : amu kima anyo aruokyi ngony , ago kianyo asoru ngony . 
Inendet ne esioa , ama taachei ngalekyuk , kotinyei ne iruokyin : ngolyot ne kiamwa , noto ne iruokyin inendet eng betutab let . 
Amu kima amwae anege ; ago kigona Kwanda ne kiiyokwa , ngatutiet , ne kanyol amwa , ak ne kanyol aamda . 
Ak angen ale sobondab koigeny ngatutiennyi : tuguk che amwae anyun , ko ko u ye kimwawa Kwanda , amwae ko u noto .
Ak ye kingo tom koit igortab paska , konai Jesu kole kagoit sainnyi ne wendi eng ngony kwo ole mi Kwanda , ko kagocham chechik che mi ngony , kocham anyun agoi betutab let .
Ak eng saitab amitwogikab lagat , koga konde oindet ngwektaet muguleldab Judas Iskariot , ne bo gab Simon , 
ko kagonai Jesu kole kagonde Kwanda tuguk tugul eunekyik , ak kole kibunu Jehovah , ak wendi ole mi Jehovah , 
kongeet eng amitwogik , ak konde taban ngoroikyik , ak konam anget ne kiuusegei , kogermenegei . 
Ak korongji beek sanit , ak kotoi koun kelyekab alamalyet , ak kouuse anganato kiga kermenegei . 
Konyo anyun ole mi Simon Petero . Yeityo kolenji Petero , Kiptaiyandani , tos iuni inye kelyekyuk ? 
Kowolji Jesu inendet kolenji , Kit ne ayae , ko mengen nguno ; ago tatun inae . 
Kolenji Petero , Magoi iun kelyekyuk . Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ngo maunin , ko magitingege kiy . 
Kolenji Simon Petero inendet , Kiptaiyandani , ma kelyekyuk kityo , ago eunekyuk agichek ak metinnyu . 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Inendet ne kagoungei ko ma komachei koungei kogeny , kobate kelyekyik , amu iunot inne : ak ounotin okwek , ago ma okwek tugul . 
Amu kiingen ne kimachei kongwekta inendet ; kimwa amu noto kole , Ma ounotin tugul .
Ak ye kingo kagoun anyun kelyekwak , ak konem ngoroikyik , ak koteb ngony kogeny , kolenji , Tos ongen ne kayaiywok ? 
Oguurena Konetindet , ak Kiptaiyat : ak omwae komie ; amu a inendet . 
Ngo ane anyun ne a Kiptaiyat ak Konetindet , ne kaun kelyekwok , ko kanyoljok ak okwek ounjige kelyek . 
Amu kaboruok , si oyai ak okwek ko u ne kayaiywok . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ma o otwogindet kosiir kiptaiyandannyi ; ama o inendet ne kigiyok kosiir inendet ne kiiyogu . 
Ngonai tuguchu , ko oboiboi ngoyai .
Mamwae agobo okwek tugul : angen che kialewen : ago si kobiit kosulda sirutiet , ne kile , Inendet ne amei makatiandennyu , ko kagongeet kwariandennyi koyaiywa ne ya . 
Kasib amwawok koboch nguno kotom kosulda , si ye isulda , oyan ole a inendet . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Inendet ne taachei age tugul ne ayogu ko kataacha ; ak inendet ne taacha ko kataach kinendet ne kiiyokwa .
Kingo kagomwa Jesu ko u noto , konyor nyalilda eng tamirmiriennyi , ak kobaorian , kole , Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ngwektaa age eng okwek . 
Kogeergei anyun alamalyet , ama naei kole , ngo mwaei agobo ngo . 
Ak kimi meset agenge ne bo alamalyennyi ne kitiiegei tegetab Jesu ne ki chamat eng Jesu . 
Kongwech anyun Simon Petero inendet , kolenji , Mwawech , tos mwaei inendet agobo ngo ? 
Kolenji anyun ne kitiiegei tegetab Jesu , Kiptaiyandani , ngo noto ? 
Kowol Jesu anyun kole , Inendet ne agochini kererutiet , ye kaaburburte . Ak ye kingo kagoburburto kererutiet , kogochi Judas , ne bo gab Simon Iskariot . 
Ak kingo kagotaach kererutiet , kochut Setani inendet . Kolenji Jesu inendet anyun , Yai chokyi ne imache iyai . 
Koma konai chi eng che kimi amisiet kole kamwachi inendet agobo nee . 
Amu kilen alak eng ichek kalenji Jesu , Ial tuguk che kimachei eng igorta , amu kitingoti Judas lolet ; anan ko kalenji kogochi kiy kibanaok . 
Kingo kagotaach anyun inendet kererutiet , komanda ngunoto : ak ki kemoi .
Ye kingo kagomanda sang , komwa Jesu kole , Kagitoror nguno Weritab chi , ak kagitoror Jehovah eng inendet ; 
ak tun itorori Jehovah inendet eng orinnyi ; ak kotorori inendet eng sainato .
Lagochu mengech , ta atebye kobotok ne matia . Tun ochenga : ak ko u ye kiamwachi Yahudik , alenji , Ole awendi , ko momuchi obwa ; amwawok nguno ak okwek ko u noto . 
Agonok ngatutiet ne leel , ale , ochamnye ; ko u ye kiachamak , ochamnye ak okwek . 
Naei bik tugul kole o alamalyennyu , ngochamdosi .
Kilenji anyun Simon Petero , Kiptaiyandani , iwendi ano ? Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ole awendi , ko memuchi isubwa nguno ; ago tatun isubwa . 
Kolenji Petero , Kiptaiyandani , kalya si mamuchi asubun agot nguno ? Agoitoi sobondanyu agobo inye . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Igoitoi sobondangung agobo ane ? Amwaun , iman , iman , ale , Kotom kote kipsoiywet , iesioa konyil somok .
Amogochi mugulelwekwok koiimgei : oyani Jehovah , oyana agane . 
Mitei gorik che chang eng gotab Baba ; nda kima ko u noto , ta kiamwawok ; awendi achobwok koret ? 
Ak ye awe achobwok koret , anyone kogeny amutok ; si ole ami omite ak okwek . 
Ak ole awendi , ongen oret .
Kolenji Tomas , Kiptaiyandani , magingen ole iwendi ; kinaitoi ano anyun oret ? 
Kolenji Jesu , A oret , ak iman , ak sobondo : manyonjin chi Kwanda , ama eng ane . 
Nda kionaa , ta kionai Baba agine : ak kaonai inendet anyun koboch nguno , ak kaogeer inendet .
Kolenji Pilipu , Kiptaiyandani , iboruech Kwanda , si koyamech . 
Kolenji Jesu , Kigitebi tugul ak okwek betusiek che chang , ak tom inaa , Pilipu ? Inendet ne kigogeera ko kigogeer Kwanda : imwae eng nee anyun , ile , Iboruech Kwanda ? 
Tos meyani ile ami eng Kwanda , ak Kwanda eng ane ? Ngalek che amwawok ko mamwae anege : ago Kwanda ne menya ne yaei boisionikyik . 
Iyana amu ami eng Kwanda , ak Kwanda eng ane : anan oyana agobo boisionik icheget . 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Inendet ne iyana , koyaei agine boisionik che ayae ; ak koyaei boisionik che eech eng chuto ; amu awendi ole mi Kwanda . 
Ak kit age tugul ne osome eng kainennyu , ayae , si kegonyit Kwanda eng Werit . 
Ngot osom kiy age tugul eng kainennyu , ayae kioto .
Ngot ochama , oribe ngatutikyuk . 
Ak asom Kwanda , ak kogonok Kagaigaindet age , si kotebi kobotok koigeny , 
noto Tamirmiriet ne bo imanit : ne maimuchi ngony kotaach ; amu mageerei inendet , ama naei inendet : ago ongen inendet : amu tebyei kobotok , ak tun tebyei eng oringwong .
Mabagaktook ko u kibananok : anyonjinok . 
Ta ko mi kitigin , si ma kogeera ngony ; ago ogeera : amu asobe , osoptosi ak okwek . 
Eng betunoto onai ole ami eng Baba , ak okwek eng ane , ak ane eng okwek . 
Inendet ne tinyei ngatutikyuk , ak koribei , ko noto ne chama : ak inendet ne chama ko chamat eng Baba , ak achame inendet , ak angangjige inendet .
Kolenji Judas (ma Iskariot) , Kiptaiyandani , kalya si ingangweige , ama ingangjige ngony ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ngo chama chi , korib ngolyondennyu : ak kocham Baba inendet , ak kebwanji inendet , ak kemeny koboto inendet . 
Inendet ne machama ko maribei ngalekyuk : ak ma nenyu ngolyot ne ogase , ago bo Kwanda ne kiiyokwa .
Kaamwawok tuguchu , kota ami kobotok . 
Ago inetok tuguk tugul Kagaigaindet , Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ne iyogu Kwanda eng kainennyu , ak kobwatwok tugul che kaamwawok .
Abagakwok kalyet ; agonok kalyennyu : magonok ko u ye konu ngony . Amongoiimgei mugulelwekwok , anan koiyweis . 
Kaogas ko u ye kaamwawok ale , Awendi , ak anyone ole omi . Ngot ochama , ko oboiboi , amu awendi ole mi Kwanda : amu o Kwanda eng ane . 
Ak kaamwawok nguno kotom koyaak , si ye kagoyaak , oyan . 
Mangalalwok mising , amu nyonei ne o ne bo ngony : ama tinyei kiy eng ane ; 
ago si konai ngony kole achame Kwanda , ak ko u ye kigona Kwanda ngatutiet , ayae ko u noto . Ongeetye , kebe .
A ketit ne bo iman ne bo sabibuk , ak semberindet Baba . 
Tilei temet age tugul ne mi eng ane ne maiyiei logoek , ak kotilili temet age tugul ne yiei logoek si koi logoek alak . 
O tililen nguno amu ngalek che kaamwawok . 
Omenya , ak amenyok . Ko u ye maimuchi temet koi logoek inegei , ngot ko mamenyei ketit ; ko momuchi ak okwek , ngot ko momenya .
A ketitab sabibuk , ko o temenik : inendet ne menya , ak amenye inendet , ko noto ne yiei logoek che chang : amu momuchi oyai kiy okwege ngo mami ane kobotok . 
Ngo mamenya chi , kewirtoi inendet ko u temetab ketit , si koyaam ; ak koyum bik , ak kowirji ma , ak kolalyo . 
Ngot omenya , ak komenyok ngalekyuk , osom anyun kiy age tugul ne omache , si keyaiywok . 
Kigonyiti Baba eng nito , ye oiyie logoek che chang ; si oegu alamalyennyu . 
Ko u ye kichama Kwanda , ko u noto kiachamak agane : otebi eng chamnyennyu . 
Ngot oribe ngatutikyuk , otebye anyun eng chamnyennyu ; ko u ye kiarib ngatutik che bo Baba , ak atebye eng chamnyennyi . 
Kaamwawok tuguchu , si kotebi eng okwek boiboiyennyu , si kobiit kosulda boiboiyengwong . 
Ngatutiennyu ni , ale ochamnye , ko u ye kiachamak . 
Matinyei chi chamnyet ne siirei ni , ale kogoito chi sobondanyi agobo choronokyik . 
O choronokyuk , ngot oyai tuguk che angatok . 
Ma aguurenok otwogik ; amu manaei otwogindet kit ne yaei kiptaiyandennyi : ago kaaguurenok choronok ; amu kaangangwok tuguk tugul che kiagase Baba . 
Kima olewena , ago kialewenok , ak kiandeak , ale obe ak oii logoek , si kobiit kotebi logoekwok : si kobiit kogonok Kwanda kit age tugul ne osome eng kainennyu . 
Angatwok tuguchu , ale ochamnye .
Ngo wechok ngony , onai ole kigowecha kotom kowechok . 
Nda o bo ngony , ta chamei ngony chechik : ago amu mobo ngony , ago kialewenok eng ngony , kowechok ngony anyun amu noto . 
Obwat ngolyot ne kiamwawok , Masiirei otwogindet kiptaiyandennyi . Ngot ko kiusa ane , kousok ak okwek ; ngot ko kinam ngolyondennyu , konami nengwong agine . 
Ago yaiywok tuguchu tugul agobo kainennyu , amu ma nai inendet ne kiiyokwa . 
Nda kima anyo angalalji ichek , ta matinyei tengek : ago nguno ko matinyei kit ne itiagegei agobo tengektanywa . 
Inendet ne wecha ko kawech Baba agine . 
Nda kima ayai eng kwenunywa boisionik che kima yai chito age , ta kima kotinyei tengek : ago nguno ko kagogeerech ak kagowechech ane ak Baba . 
Ago , si kosulda ngolyot ne kigisir eng Ngatutikwak , kele , Kigowecha buch .
Ago ye kagoit Kagaigaindet , ne tun ayokwok kobunu Kwanda , Tamirmiriet ne bo imanit , ne bunu Kwanda , konyo kobaorianja : 
ak obaoriani ak okwek , amu kiomi kobota koboch taunet .
Kaamwawok tuguchu , si ma kinachak . 
Onok eng sunagogisiek : ee , nyonei sait , ne ibwati chi tugul ne barok kole , Ayachini Jehovah boisiet . 
Ak yaei tuguchu , amu ma nai Kwanda , anan ane . 
Ago kaamwawok tuguchu , si ye nyo sainywa , omuchi obwat ole kiamwawok agobo chuto . Ago kima amwawok tuguchu eng taunet , amu kiami kobotok . 
Ago kawe nguno ole mi inendet ne kiiyokwa ; ama mi age eng okwek ne teebena kole , Iwendi ano ? 
Amu kaamwawok tuguchu , ko kanyi mugulelwekwok arogenet . 
Ago amwawok ne bo iman : mie eng okwek ngawe : amu ngo mawe , ko manyonjinok Kagaigaindet ; ago ngot awe , ayokwok inendet . 
Ak ye kagonyo inendet , kogikyi ngony agobo tengekto , ak imanda , ak kiruoget : 
agobo tengekto , amu ma iyana ; 
agobo imanda , amu awendi ole mi Kwanda , ama ogeero kogeny ; 
agobo kiruoget , amu kigiruokyi ne o ne bo ngonyuni .
Ta atinye tuguk che chang che kata ta amwawok , ago ma omuchi omuite nguno . 
Ago ye tun kagonyo inendet , Tamirmiriet ne bo imanit , kondoiywok agoi oit imanda tugul : amu mamwaei inegei ; ago mwaei tuguk tugul che kasei : ak kongangwok tuguk che bwanei . 
Itorora : amu namei chechuk , ak kongangwok . 
Chechuk tuguk tugul che tinyei Kwanda : noto kaamwa , ale , namei chechuk , ak koboruok .
Tomo kitigin , si ma ogeera kogeny ; ak mi kitigin kogeny , si ogeero . 
Kongalaljigei anyun alak eng alamalyennyi kole , Nee ni kamwawech kole , Mi kitigin , si ma ogeera ; ak mi kitigin kogeny , si ogeera : ak , Amu awendi ole mi Kwanda ? 
Kole anyun , Nee ni kamwa kole , Mi kitigin ? Magingen kit ne mwaei . 
Kinai Jesu anyun kole , machei koteebe bichoto inendet , ak kilenji , Tos oteebege okwege agobo ngolyondoni kaamwa ale , Mi kitigin , si ma ogeera , ak mi kitigin kogeny , si ogeera ? 
Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Orirtosi ak oteitosi , ago baibai ngony : oarogendosi , ago kiweechi arogenengwong koek boiboiyet . 
Arogeni tamonet ye machei kosigis , amu kait sainnyi : ago ye kagosich lakwet , ko ma kobwati ngwanindo kogeny , eng boiboiyet amu kagesikyi chi ngony . 
Noto anyun otinye arogenet nguno : ago ta ageerok kogeny , ak boiboi mugulelwekwok , ama rebenok chi boiboiyengwong . 
Ama oteebena kiy eng betunoto . Amwawok , iman , iman , ale , Ngot osom Kwanda kiy age tugul , kogonok eng kainennyu . 
Tom osom kiy eng kainennyu : osom , si onyoru , si kobiit kosulda boiboiyengwong .
Kaamwawok tuguchu eng kalewenaik : ago nyonei sait , ye ma angalalwok eng kalewenaik , ago aboruok komie agobo Kwanda . 
Osome betunoto eng kainennyu : amamwawok , ale ateebe Kwanda kiy agobo okwek ; 
amu chamok inendet Kwanda , amu kiochama , ak kioyan ole kiabunu Kwanda . 
Kiabunu Kwanda , anyonji ngony : abagaktoi ngony kogeny , ak agetitege ole mi Kwanda .
Kolenji alamalyennyi , Keero , ingalali nguno komie kotook , ama imwae kalewenet . 
Kingen nguno kele ingen tuguk tugul , ama nyoljin chi koteebenen kiy : kiyani eng nito kele kiibunu Jehovah . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Oyani nguno ? 
Ogeero , nyonei sait , ee , kagonyo nguno , ye kiyestook , kwo chi tugul oldanyi , ak obagakta anege : ago mami anege , amu mi Kwanda kobota . 
Kaamwawok tuguchu , si kobiit onyorunena kalyet . Otinye nyalilda eng ngony : ago onyiganitu ! amu kaaterter ngony .
Kimwa Jesu ngalechu ; ak konyal kipsengwet , ak kole , Baba , kagonyo sait ; itoror Weringung , si kotororin Werit ; 
ko u ye kiigochi inendet kimnatet koboi bik tugul , si kobiit kogochi sobondab koigeny tugul che kiigochi inendet . 
Ak ni sobondab koigeny , ale konain Jehovah ne inyendet inyege ne bo iman , ak Jesu Kristo , ne kiiyogu . 
Kiatororin eng ngony , amu kaagesu boisiet ne kiigona ayai . 
Ak nguno , ee Baba , itorora eng inyendet inyege eng torornatet ne kiatinye kemi tuwai kotom kobiit ngony .
Kiaborji kainengung bik che kiigona eng ngony : ki cheguk , ak kiigona ; ak kigorib ngolyondengung . 
Kagonai nguno kole bunun tuguk tugul che kiigona ; 
amu kiagochi ichek ngalek che kiigona ak kigotaach , ak kigonai iman kole kiabunu ole imi , ak kigoyan kole kiiyokwa .
Asae agobo ichek : masae agobo ngony , ago agobo ichek che kiigona ; amu cheguk : 
ak tuguk tugul chechuk ko cheguk , ak cheguk ko chechuk : ak kiitorora eng ichek . 
Ak ma amite ngony , ago mi ngony chu , ak anyone ole imi . Baba ne Tilil , rib eng kainengung ichek che kiigona , si kobiit koek agenge , ko u achek . 
Kiarib eng kainengung ichek che kiigona , ye kota kemi ak ichek : kiarib ichek , ama bet agot agenge eng ichek , kobate weritab luset ; si kobiit kosulda sirutiet . 
Ak kanyonjin nguno ; ak amwae tuguchu eng ngony , si kobiit kosulda boiboiyennyu eng ichek . 
Kiagochi ngolyondengung ; ak kawech ngony ichek , amu ma bo ngony , ko u ye ma bo ngony ane . 
Masae ale imut ichek eng ngony , ago ale irib ichek eng inendet ne ya . 
Ma bo ngony ichek , ko u ye ma bo ngony ane . 
Itilil ichek eng imanit : imanit ngolyondengung . 
Ko u ye kiiyokwa anyo ngony , ko u noto kaayokte ichek koba ngony . 
Ak atabanige agobo ichek si kobiit kitaban ichek eng imanit .
Amasae agobo chu kityo , ago asae agobo ichek che tun iyana amu ngolyondenywa ; 
si kobiit koek ichek tugul agenge ! ko u ye imi inye Baba , eng ane , ak ane eng inye , si kobiit koteb ichek eng achek : si kobiit koyan ngony kole kiiyokwa . 
Ak kaagochi ichek torornatet ne kiigona ; si kobiit koek agenge ko u ye ki agenge achek ; 
ane eng ichek , ak inye eng ane , si kobiit koek ichek che igesunotingei eng agenge ; si kobiit konai ngony kole kiiyokwa , ak ichame ichek , ko u ye ichama .
Baba , amache ale kotebi kobota eng ole ami , ichek che kiigona ; si kobiit kogeer torornatennyu ne kiigona ; amu kiichama kotom kelumda ngony . 
Ee Baba ne bo imanda , kima kongenin ngony , ago kiangenin ; ak kigonai chu kole , kiiyokwa ; 
ak kiangangji ichek kainengung , ak ta angangjini ; si kobiit kotebe ichek chamnyet ne kiichamena , ak ane eng ichek .
Ye kingo kagomwa Jesu ngalechu , koba ak alamalyennyi kolanda eng kererut ne kiguure Kedron , ole kimi mbaret , ole kiwa inendet , koboto alamalyennyi . 
Ak kiingen koronoto Judas agine , ne kingwektoi inendet : amu kicham kowendi Jesu yoto koboto alamalyennyi . 
Ak kingo kagonyor Judas lugetab askarik , ak kiptainik che bunu tisiik che eechen ak Parisaik , kobwa kotinyei taisiek ak kegenganik ak karik che bo luget . 
Kwo anyun Jesu , ko kagonai tuguk tugul che bwanjin inendet , ak kolenji , Ochenge ngo ? 
Kowolji kolenji , Jesu ne bo Nasaret . Kolenji Jesu , A inendet . Ak kitononi koboto ichek Judas agine , ne kingwektoi inendet .
Ye kingomwachi anyun kole , A inendet , kobee batai , ak kobutyo . 
Kiteebe anyun ichek kogeny , kole , Ochenge ngo ? Ak kole , Jesu ne bo Nasaret . 
Kowol Jesu , kole , Kaamwawok ale a inendet ; noto anyun ngochenga ounde chu koba ; 
si kosulda ngolyot ne kimwa kole , Ma betena agot agenge eng choto kiigona . 
Kingus anyun Simon Petero rotwetab chok ne kitinyei , ak koeb otwogindetab tisiindet ne o , koeb itinnyi ne bo tai . Kigiguure otwogindonoto Malko . 
Kolenji Jesu anyun Petero , Weekyi rotwet choget : tos maee kikombet ne kagona Kwanda ?
Konam anyun luget ak kiptaiyat ne o , ak kiptainik che bo Yahudik , Jesu ak korat inendet , 
ak komutyi Anas korok ; amu ki kabyugoit ne bo Kaiapa , ne ki tisiindet ne o kenyinoto . 
Kaiapa noto ne kiiborji Yahudik kole , nyolu komechi chito agenge bik .
Kiisub anyun Simon Petero Jesu , ak age ne bo alamalyet . Ak kiingengei tisiindet ne o ak noto ne bo alamalyet , ak kiba got orit koboto Jesu agoi kapkiruogetab tisiindet ne o ; 
ago kitononi Petero eng sang ye negit kurget . Kimanda anyun chichoto , age ne bo alamalyet , ne kiingengei ak tisiindet ne o , ak kongalalji chepto ne kiribei kurget , ak kiimut Petero konyo go . 
Kolenji anyun chepto ne kiribei kurget Petero , Ma i age eng alamalyetab chichi ? Kole , Ma ane .
Ak kitonondos eng yoto otwogik ak kiptainik , che kiga kolaal mat ne bo nesek , amu ki kaitit ; ak kiyue mat : ak kitononi Petero agine koboto ichek , koyue mat .
Kiteebe anyun tisiindet ne o Jesu agobo alamalyennyi ak konetisiennyi . 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kiangalalji ngony , amauny ngolyo ; kianetisie kotugul eng sunagogisiek , ak eng hekalut , ole tuiyechin Yahudik tugul ; amamwa kiy eng ungot . 
Amu nee si iteebena? Teebe ichek che kigas kit ne kiamwachi ichek: keero, ingen chu tuguk che kiamwa. 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa ko u nito , korabach Jesu age eng kiptainik che kitonondos eng yoto , kole , Iwoljini tisiindet ne o ko u noto ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Ngot ko kaamwa ne ya , ibaorian agobo noto ya : ago ngot ko mie , ko amu nee si irabacha ? 
Kiiyokto anyun Anas inendet ko ratat kwo oldab Kaiapa , tisiindet ne o .
Ak kitononi Simon Petero koyue mat . Kolenji anyun ichek inendet , Ma i age aginye ne bo alamalyennyi ? Kotiiyo kole , Ma a inendet . 
Kole otwogindet age ne bo tisiindet ne o ne ki tilionut ak chichoto kiebei Petero itinnyi , Koma ageerin eng mbar omi ak inendet . 
Kotiiyo anyun Petero kogeny ; ak eng sainato kote kipsoiywet .
Kiimut Jesu anyun kongeete gab Kaiapa kwo Praitorium : ak kita ko karon mising ; ak maba icheget Praitorium orit , si ma ngwonegitu , ago si kobiit koam paska . 
Kimanda Pilato anyun kwo ole mi ichek , ak kole , Nee ngolyo ne oruokyine chichi ? 
Kowolji kolenji , Nda ko ma ko chalwogin chichi , ta ko ma kimutu inendet konyo taingung . 
Kolenji Pilato ichek anyun , Onam inendet okwek , ak oruokyi ko u ngatutiengwong . Kolenji anyun Yahudik , Ma chamdaat eng achek kebar chi age tugul : 
si kobiit kosulda ngolyotab Jesu , ne kimwa , koboru meet ole meitoi inendet . 
Kiwa anyun kogeny Pilato Praitorium orit , ak koguur Jesu , kolenji , Tos i Laitoriatab Yahudik ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Imwae ngolyondoni inyege anan komwaun alak agobo ane ? 
Kowol Pilato kole , A Yahudiot ? Kagomutun tainnyu bororiengung ak tisiik che eechen : kiiyai nee ? 
Kowol Jesu , kole , Ma bo ngonyuni laitornatennyu : nda bo ngonyuni laitornatennyu , ko kata yaei boriet kiboitinikyuk , si ma kindea eunekab Yahudik : ago nguno ko ma bo laitornatennyu oli . 
Kolenji anyun Pilato inendet , Ara , i laitoriat so ? Kowol Jesu kole , Imwae ile a laitoriat . Kigisicha amu nito , ak kianyo ngony amu nito , si kobiit abaorianji imanit . Kasei kutinnyu chi age tugul ne bo imanit . 
Kolenji Pilato , Nee imanit ? Ak ye kingo kagomwa ko u ni , komanda kogeny ole mi Yahudik , ak kolenji , Ma anyorji ane lelut inendet . 
Ago otinye biteet , ole atiakwok age eng paska : ara omache atiakwok Laitoriatab Yahudik ? 
Kobolyo anyun kogeny , kole , Ma chichi , ago Baraba . Ago anyun , ki rebindet Baraba .
Kinam anyun Pilato Jesu , ak kobire kipcharitit . 
Ak kitaa askarik ngatiet ne bo katok , ak konde metit , ak kolaakyi inendet ngoriet ne arus ne birir ; 
ak kobwa ole mi inendet kole , Kigatin , Laitoriatab Yahudik ! Ak korabach inendet . 
Ak kimanda Pilato kogeny , ak kolenji ichek , Ogeero , kamutwak inendet konyo taingwong , si onai ole ma anyorji ane lelut inendet . 
Komong Jesu anyun konyo sang , ko kerat metit eng ngatietab katok , kolaagonu ngorionoto arus ne birir . Ak kolenji Pilato bichoto , Ogeer chichi anyun-o ! 
Ye kingogeer anyun inendet tisiik che eechen ak kiptainik , kobolyo , kole , Igartat ! igartat ! Kolenji Pilato , Omut okwek inendet ak ogartat : amu ma anyorji lelut . 
Kowolji Yahudik kolenji , Kitinye ngatutiet , ak kanyol kome amu ngatutionoto , amu kiyaigei koek Weritab Jehovah .
Ye kingogas anyun Pilato mwaonato , koiywei mising ; 
ak kiwa Praitorium orit kogeny , ak kolenji Jesu , Ibunu ano ? Ago ma wolji Jesu inendet . 
Kolenji Pilato anyun inendet , Metwekwa ? Mengen ile atinye kimnatet atiachin , ak atinye kimnatet agartatin ? 
Kowolji Jesu kolenji , Kama ko tetinye kimnatet iyaiywa kiy , nda kama kigonin eng barak ; noto anyun , tinyei inendet ne koindea euneguk tengekto ne o kosiir . 
Koboch yoto kocheng Pilato kotiach inendet : ago kibolyo Yahudik , kole , Ngot itiach chichi , ko ma i choruet ne bo Kaisari : renyei Kaisari chi age tugul ne yaegei koek laitoriat . 
Ye kingogas anyun Pilato ngalechuto , komut Jesu komong sang , ak koteb ngony eng ngecheretab kiruoget eng ole kiguure Tetetab Koik , ago kiguure eng kutitab Hebranik , Gabata .
Ki Chobetab paska betunoto : ak ki olo bo sait lo . Ak kilenji Yahudik , Ogeero , Laitoriandengwong ! 
Kobolyo bichoto , kole , Iste inendet ! iste ! igartat inendet ! Kolenji Pilato anyun ichek , Agartat Laitroriandengwong ? Kowol tisiik che eechen , kole , Magitinye laitoria kobate Kaisari . 
Kogoito anyun Pilato inendet kigartat . Konam anyun ichek Jesu ak komut : 
ak komanda , koibei inegei kimurtoiyot , agoi koit ole kiguure Koretab terta , ne kiguure eng kutitab Hebranik , Golgota : 
ole kiigartate ichek inendet , koboto aeng alak , age komosi ak age komosi , ak kimi Jesu kwen . 
Ak kisir anyun Pilato siret , ak konde kimurtoiyot . Kigisir kele , JESU NE BO NASARET , LAITORIAT NE BO YAHUDIK . 
Kosoman anyun Yahudik che chang sironito : amu ki negite nganaset ole kigigartate Jesu : ak kigisir eng kutitab Hebranik , ak Romanik , ak Yunanik . 
Kolenji anyun tisiik che eechen che bo Yahudik Pilato , Amesir ile , Laitoriat ne bo Yahudik : ago , kimwa kole , A Laitoriat ne bo Yahudik . 
Kowol Pilato kole , Kit ne kaasir ko kaasir .
Ye kingo kagogartat anyun askarik Jesu , konam ngoroikyik , kopchei koek kebeberwek angwan , koib askarindet age tugul kebeberta age ; ak ko u noto sumet agine : ak kima kotinyei sumet ole kigituiye , kiginab koek agenge kongeete barak agoi kapkelyen . 
Kolenjigei anyun ichegei , Amongegerer , ago ongeser barbarek , si kenai chito ne bunjin : si kosulda sirutiet ne mwaei kole , Kipchechigei ngoroikyuk , Ak kolotyigei ngoriennyu . Kiyai anyun askarik tuguchuto .
Ago kitonondos eng ye negite kimurtoiyotab Jesu kamet , ak chepkametab kamet , Maria ne bo Klopa , ak Maria Magdalene . 
Ye kingogeer Jesu anyun kamet , ak noto ne bo alamalyet ne kichamei Jesu kotonondos eng yoto , kolenji kamet , Chebiosoni , keer weringung ! 
Kolenji anyun noto ne bo alamalyet , Keer komet ! Ak koboch sainato komut inendet chebiosonato kwo gonnyi .
Kingobata choto , ko kagonai Jesu kole kagogesgei tuguk tugul , si kobiit kosulda sirutiet , komwa kole , Ama melel . 
Kiga kinde yoto teret ne nyiitat siki : konyiit anyun sibonjit siki ak koyogochine husop , konde kutinnyi . 
Ye kingo kagotaach Jesu siki , komwa kole , Kagogesgei : ak koabuch metinnyi , ak kogoito tamirmiriennyi kwo .
Amu ki Chobet ak kima kemakyin muswek kotebe kimurtoiyot eng sabato (amu ki o betunoto bo sabato) , kosom Yahudik Pilato kole keiri kelyekwak , si kesutei . 
Kobwa anyun askarik , ak koiri kelyekab ne bo tai , ak ne bo age ne kiga kigartat koboto inendet . 
Ago ye kingobwa ye mi Jesu , ak kogeer kole kagome , ko mata koiri kelyekyik : 
ago kitoore ngotit karastanyi age eng askarik , ak ngunoto komong korotik ak beek . 
Ak kibaorian inendet ne kigeer , ak ko bo iman baornatennyi : ak ingen inendet kole mwaei iman , si kobiit oyan ak okwek . 
Kiyaak tuguchu , si kobiit kosulda sirutiet ne kile , Magiiriei kowennyi . 
Ak kogeny mwaei sirutiet age kole , Tun keerei ichek inendet ne kitoorei .
Ak kingobata tuguchu , kwo Josep ne bo Arimatea , ne ki age eng alamalyetab Jesu eng ungot , amu kiiywei Yahudik , kosom Pilato kole kosut mustab Jesu : ak kichamji Pilato . Konyo anyun koib bortanyi . 
Ak kinyo agine Nikodemo , ne kinyonji Jesu kemoi atkinye tai , koibu tuguk che u igomoik che kigiburukto nyamdutik alak , che ki olo bo ratilisiek bogol . 
Kisut anyun mustab Jesu , ak kotaa eng ngoroik che bo katanit koboto nyamdutik , ko u biteetab Yahudik ye tubisiei . 
Kimi mbaret ole kigigartate inendet ; ak kimi mbaranato kererit ne leel ne kitom ketupchi chi . 
Kiinde anyun Jesu oloto amu betutab Chobetab Yahudik , amu ki negit kererit .
Kinyo kererit Maria Magdalene , karon , ko kairir emet , eng betut ne bo tai ne bo wigit , ak kogeer koita ko kageisto eng kererit . 
Kolabat kot koit ole mi Simon Petero , ak noto age ne bo alamalyet , ne kichamei Jesu inendet , ak kolenji ichek , Kageib Kiptaiyat eng kererit , ama kingen ole kaginde . 
Koba anyun Petero , ak nin age ne bo alamalyet , kotokyigei kererit . 
Kiruai tuwai kibagenge : ak kilabat nin age ne bo alamalyet kondoe Petero , ak kosib koit kererit ; 
ak kingonguruk kogeer orit , kogeer ngoroikab katanit ko itootin ; ago mawa orit . 
Konyo anyun Simon Petero agine , kosubu inendet , ak kwo kererit orit ; ak kogeer ngoroik che bo katanit ko itootin ; 
ago anget ne kimitei metinnyi ko kima komi , koboto ngoroik che bo katanit , ago ki mamanat inegei eng oldo age . 
Kiwa orit agine noto age ne bo alamalyet ne kiga sib koit kererit , ak kigeer ak kiiyan . 
Amu kitom konai sirutiet ne kile , ngeetei kogeny matiny eng che kibek . 
Koba ga anyun kogeny choto bo alamalyet .
Ago kitononi Maria eng kererit sang , korirei : ak ye kita korirei , konguruk koiit kererit ; 
ak kigeer malaikaisiek aeng che leelach ngoroik kotebyei ngony , age eng ole bo metit , ak age eng ole bo kelyek , eng ole kimi bortab Jesu . 
Ak kilenji , Kobogoriondoni , kalya si irir ? Kolenji , Amu kageib Kiptaiyandennyu , amangen ole kaginde inendet .
Ak ye kingo kagomwa ko u noto , kowelelgei , kogeer Jesu kotononi , ama konai kole Jesu noto . 
Kolenji Jesu , Kobogoriondoni , kalya si irir ? Ichenge ngo ? Kiibwati kolen inendet ko ribindetab mbaret , ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , ngo kaiib inendet eng oli , imwawa ole kainde , si aib inendet . 
Kolenji Jesu , Maria ! Kowelelgei , ak kolenji eng kutitab Hebranik , Rabboni ! ye kiweech kele , Konetindoni . 
Kolenji Jesu , Ametwaa ; amu tom atogosyi oldab Kwanda : ago ui ole mi tupchosiekyuk , ak ilenji , Atogosyini oldab Baba , ago Baba nengwong , Jehovah nenyu , ago Jehovah nengwong . 
Konyo Maria Magdalene kolenji alamalyet , Kaageer Kiptaiyat : ak kagomwachi tuguchu inendet .
Ak ye kingoek lagat eng betunoto bo tai ne bo wigit , ye kiga keger kurgotik eng ole kimi alamalyet , amu kiiywei Yahudik , konyo Jesu kotonone kwenunywa ak kolenji , Ingoteb kalyet eng okwek ! 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa nito , koborji eunekyik ak karastanyi . Koboiboitu anyun alamalyet , ye kingogeer Kiptaiyat . 
Kolenji Jesu anyun kogeny , Ingoteb kalyet eng okwek ! ko u ye kiiyokwa Kwanda , ayoktook ak okwek ko u noto . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa nito , kobusyi , ak kolenji , Otaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil : 
bik alak tugul che onyochini kaat tengekwogikwak , kenyochin kaat ; ak alak tugul che oesioi onyochi kaat , keesioi kenyochi kaat .
Ago kima komi Tomas ne kigiguure Didumo , ne ki age eng taman ak aeng , koboto ichek ye kinyonei Jesu . 
Kolenji anyun chun alage che bo alamalyet , Kagegeer Kiptaiyat . Ago kilenji Tomas ichek , Ngot ko mageer eng eunekyik berutik che bo kipchumarisiek , ak ande mornennyu berutikab kipchumarisiek , ak ande eunnyu karastanyi , ko mayani .
Ak kingobata betusiek sisiitu ko kimi go alamalyennyi kogeny , ak kimi Tomas koboto ichek . Kinyo anyun Jesu , ko kerotin kurgotik , ak kotonon eng kwenunywa , ak komwa kole , Ingoteb kalyet eng okwek ! 
Kolenji Tomas , Iyogou mornengung , ak igeer eunekyuk ; ak iyogou eungung ak inde karastanyu ; si meegu ne matinyei kayanet , ago iyan . 
Kowolji Tomas kolenji , Kiptaiyandennyu ak ko Jehovah nenyu ! 
Kolenji Jesu inendet , Kaiyan amu kaigeera : iberurotin ichek che iyani ama keer !
Kiyai Jesu kaborunoik alak che chang eng taitab alamalyet che ma sirotin eng bukuini : 
ago kigisir chu , si kobiit oyan ole Jesu ko Kristo , Weritab Jehovah ; ak si kobiit ye oyani onyoru sobondo eng kainennyi .
Kingobata tuguchu koborjigei Jesu kogeny alamalyet eng araraita ne bo Tiberia ; kiiborjigei ko u ni . 
Kimi tugul , Simon Petero ak Tomas ne kiguure Didumo , ak Natanael ne bo Kana ne bo Galili , ak werikab Sebedi , ak aeng alak che bo alamalyennyi . 
Kolenji Simon Petero , Kawe aram njirenik . Kolenji chun alage , Kibendi agachek koboten . Koba anyun ak kolany moingetab beek : ak ma nam kiy kemounoto . 
Ago ye kimachei koeech , kotonon Jesu eng ngegut : ago ma nai alamalyet kole Jesu . 
Kolenji Jesu anyun , Lagochu , otinye kiy ne oame ? Kowolji kolenji , Achicha . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Owirji regereiywot ne kiname njirenik komostab tai ne bo moinget , si onyoru . Kowirji anyun , ak mata komuch kochuut amu changindab njirenik . 
Komwachi age ne bo alamalyet , noto ne chamei Jesu , Petero , kolenji , Kiptaiyat nito . Ye kingogas anyun Simon Petero kole Kiptaiyat , kolaach kotit anyun (amu kimi ach ngor) ak kochorjigei araraita . 
Ago kibwa chun alage che bo alamalyet kobunu moinget ne mingin (amu kima ko looen eng ngegut , ago ki olo bo kakwautik che bo eut bogol aeng) , kochuutu regereiywondonoto mi njirenik . 
Noto anyun , ye kingoit ngegut , kogeer eng yoto mat ne bo nesek , ak kiwatanat njiriot eng yoto , ak makatiat . 
Kolenji Jesu , Oibu njirenik alak chu korame nguno . 
Kolany Simon Petero moinget , ak kochuut regereiywot konyo ngegut , ak ki nyiitat njirenik che eechen , bogol agenge ak konom ak somok : ak nganda ki chang njirenik mising , ko kima kerer regereiywondonoto . 
Kolenji Jesu ichek , Obwa oamisie . Ak ma kany age tugul eng alamalyet koteebe kole , I ngo ? Amu kiingen kole , inendet ko Kiptaiyat . 
Konyo anyun Jesu ak konam makatiat , ak kogochi , koboto njirenik agichek .
Nito ko ne bo somok koborjingei Jesu alamalyet , ko kagongeet inendet komong eng che kibek .
Ye kingo kagoamis anyun , kolenji Jesu Simon Petero , Simon , weritab Johana , tos ichama kosiir chu ? Kolenji inendet , Ee , Kiptaiyandani , ingen ile achamin . Kolenji , Bai arekyuk .
Kolenji kogeny ne bo aeng Simon , weritab Johana , ichama ? Kolenji , Ee , Kiptaiyandani , ingen ile achamin . Kolenji , Iyage kechirekyuk .
Kolenji ne bo somok , Simon , weritab Johana , ichama ? Koarogen Petero amu kamwachi ne bo somok , kolenji , Ichama ? Ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , ingen tuguk tugul ; ingen ile achamin . Kolenji Jesu inendet , Bai kechirekyuk . 
Amwaun , iman , iman , ale , Ye kita ko i mingin , ko kiilaaksechinige , ak iwendi ole imache : ago ye tun iositu , iitoi euneguk , ak kolaakseun age , ak komutin ole memache . 
Komwa ni , kobortoi ole teptoi meet ne konyite Jehovah . Ak ye kingo kagomwa nito , kolenji , Isubwa .
Kowelelgei Petero , kogeer noto bo alamalyet ne chamei Jesu , kosubi ; ne kitiiegei tegetab Jesu eng amisietab lagat , ak kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , ngo inendet , ne ngwektoin ? 
Kingogeer Petero inendet , kolenji Jesu , Kiptaiyandani , lyon chichi ? 
Kolenji Jesu , Ngot amach kotebi agoi tun anyo , image nee ? Isubwa inye . 
Kiyom anyun ngolyondoni tupchosiek , kole mameei chichoto age ne bo alamalyet : ago kima mwachi Jesu inendet , kolenji , mameei ; ago kilenji , Ngot amach kotebi agoi tun anyo , image nee ?
Nito anyun ko noto bo alamalyet ne baorianjin tuguchu , ak ne kisirei tuguchuto : ak kingen kele bo iman baornatennyi .
Ak mi kogeny tuguk alak che chang che kiyai Jesu , che , nda kisirei age tugul , alen ta mayamei ngony bukusiek che kata kisirjin .
Ee Teopilo , kiatet eng baruet ne bo tai , tugul che kitoi Jesu koyai ak konet , 
agoi betut ne kigimuti kwo barak , ye kingo kagogochi ngatutiet eng Tamirmiriet ne Tilil che kiyoktoi che kiga kolewen , 
icheget che kiiborjigei kosobei ye kingobata nyalildanyi , eng kaborunoik che chang , kongangjingei ichek eng betusiek artam , ak kongalaljin ichek agobo tuguk che bo bounatetab Jehovah : 
ak , kingo kagoyumgei koboto icheget , kongat kolenji , amat obe eng Jerusalem , ago ogen kayomiset ne bo Kwanda , noto kiogasena : 
amu kiibatisanis Johana iman eng beek ; ago kibatisanok eng Tamirmiriet ne Tilil kotom kogesgei betusiek che chang .
Noto anyun , ye kingo kagoyumgei , koteebe inendet , kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , iweekyini Israel bounatet eng betusiechuto ? 
Kolenji ichek , Mabotok onai betusiek anan kenyisiek , che kigonde Kwanda eng bounatennyi inegei . 
Ago otaache kamuktaet , ye tun kanyonjok Tamirmiriet ne Tilil : ak oegu baorinikyuk eng Jerusalem , ak eng Judea komugul ak Samaria , ak agoi tabandab ngony . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa tuguchuto , ye kita kogeerei kimut inendet kwo barak ; ak kitaach boldet inendet ak kobetito eng tainywa .
Ak ye kingota konyali kipsengwet kochiiljin kong kota kowendi , ogeero , kitononso bik aengu eng ye negite icheget kolaachi ngoroik che leelachen : 
che kimwa agichek , kole , Okwek bikab Galili , kalya si otononse ak onyali kipsengwet ? Tun nyonei Jesu nito , ne kagimut kwo kipsengwet kobunei olingwong , ko u yu kogeere kowendi kipsengwet .
Koweek anyun koba Jerusalem kobunu tulwet ne kiguure tulwetab Emitik , ne negite Jerusalem , ne yamegei ak bandab betutab sabato . 
Ye kingo kagoba go , kolany got ne bo barak , ole kitebe ; agot Petero , Johana , Jakobo , Andrea , Pilipu , Tomas , Bartolomayo , Matayo , Jakobo ne bo gab Alpayo , Simon Selote , ak Judas ne bo gab Jakobo . 
Kitebi chu tugul eng kabwatet agenge eng kagiiletab ge ne bo saet , koboto kobogorisiek , ak Maria kametab Jesu , ak tupchosiekab Jesu .
Ak kitonon Petero eng kwenutab che tupcho eng betusiechoto (ki chang bik che kiga tuiyo , ki olo bo bogol agenge ak tiptem) , ak kile , 
Che kitupche , ko nyolu kosulda sirutik , che kiga mwa Tamirmiriet ne Tilil eng tai eng kutitab Daudi agobo Judas , ne ki kandoindet ne kiindochin ichek che kinamei Jesu . 
Amu kigiititech , ak kinyor kebebertanyi eng boisioni .
Ak kinyor chichi mbaret eng melektab tengektanyi ; ak kingobut kosieb mo , kobetak moet , komong agutanikyik tugul . 
Ak kinaak ngolyondonoto eng tugul che menyei Jerusalem ; kot keguure mbaranato Akeldama eng kutinywa , noto ko , Mbaret ne bo korotik . 
Amu sirat eng bukuit ne bo Tienwogikab Kalosunet , kole , Ingoguber ole menyei , Ak amat komeny chi oloto : ak Ingonam chito age boisiennyi .
Ingobiit age eng bik che kicham kebendoti tugul eng betusiek tugul ye kicham komongu Kiptaiyat Jesu ak komandoi eng kwenunnyo , 
kotaune kabatisanetab Johana , agoi betut ne kigimuti kwo barak kobunei olinyo , kanyol koek age eng bichuto baoriat kobotech agobo ngeetyennyi .
Ak kilewen bik aeng , Josep ne kigiguure Barsaba , ne kigiguure kainennyi ne bo aeng Justo , ak Matia . 
Ak kisa , kole , Inye , Kiptaiyat , ne ingen mugulelwekab bik tugul , iboruech eng bichu aeng , ne kailewen , 
si kobiit konam kebeberta eng boisioni ak kayoktaoni , ne kiibute Judas , si kobiit kwo oldanyi . 
Ak kiser barbarek agobo ichek ; ak kiibutyi barbariat Matia ; ak kigiitito che kiyoktoi taman ak agenge .
Ee Teopilo, kiatet eng’ baruet ne bo tai , tugul che kitoi Jesu koyai ak konet , 
agoi betut ne kigimuti kwo barak , ye kingo kagogochi ng’atutiet eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil che kiyoktoi che kiga kolewen , 
icheget che kiiborjigei kosobei ye kingobata nyalildanyi , eng’ kaborunoik che chang’ , kong’ang’jingei ichek eng’ betusiek artam , ak kong’alaljin ichek agobo tuguk che bo bounatetab Jehovah : 
ak , kingo kagoyumgei koboto icheget , kong’at kolenji , amat obe eng’ Jerusalem , ago ogen kayomiset ne bo Kwanda , noto kiogasena : 
amu kiibatisanis Johana iman eng’ beek ; ago kibatisanok eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil kotom kogesgei betusiek che chang’ .
Noto anyun , ye kingo kagoyumgei , koteebe inendet , kolenji , Kiptaiyandani , iweekyini Israel bounatet eng’ betusiechuto ? 
Kolenji ichek , Mabotok onai betusiek anan kenyisiek , che kigonde Kwanda eng’ bounatennyi inegei . 
Ago otaache kamuktaet , ye tun kanyonjok Tamirmiriet ne Tilil : ak oegu baorinikyuk eng’ Jerusalem , ak eng’ Judea komugul ak Samaria , ak agoi tabandab ng’ony . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa tuguchuto , ye kita kogeerei kimut inendet kwo barak ; ak kitaach boldet inendet ak kobetito eng’ tainywa .
Ak ye kingota konyali kipsengwet kochiiljin kong’ kota kowendi , ogeero , kitononso bik aeng’u eng’ ye negite icheget kolaachi ngoroik che leelachen : 
che kimwa agichek , kole , Okwek bikab Galili , kalya si otononse ak onyali kipsengwet ? Tun nyonei Jesu nito , ne kagimut kwo kipsengwet kobunei oling’wong’ , ko u yu kogeere kowendi kipsengwet .
Koweek anyun koba Jerusalem kobunu tulwet ne kiguure tulwetab Emitik , ne negite Jerusalem , ne yamegei ak bandab betutab sabato . 
Ye kingo kagoba go , kolany got ne bo barak , ole kitebe ; agot Petero , Johana , Jakobo , Andrea , Pilipu , Tomas , Bartolomayo , Matayo , Jakobo ne bo gab Alpayo , Simon Selote , ak Judas ne bo gab Jakobo . 
Kitebi chu tugul eng’ kabwatet agenge eng’ kagiiletab ge ne bo saet, koboto kobogorisiek, ak Maria kametab Jesu, ak tupchosiekab Jesu.
Ak kitonon Petero eng’ kwenutab che tupcho eng’ betusiechoto (ki chang’ bik che kiga tuiyo , ki olo bo bogol agenge ak tiptem),  ak kile , 
Che kitupche , ko nyolu kosulda sirutik , che kiga mwa Tamirmiriet ne Tilil eng’ tai eng’ kutitab Daudi agobo Judas , ne ki kandoindet ne kiindochin ichek che kinamei Jesu . 
Amu kigiititech , ak kinyor kebebertanyi eng’ boisioni .
(Ak kinyor chichi mbaret eng’ melektab tengektanyi ; ak kingobut kosieb mo , kobetak moet , komong’ agutanikyik tugul . 
Ak kinaak ng’olyondonoto eng’ tugul che menyei Jerusalem ; kot keguure mbaranato Akeldama eng’ kutinywa , noto ko , Mbaret ne bo korotik .) 
Amu sirat eng’ bukuit ne bo Tienwogikab Kalosunet , kole , Ingoguber ole menyei , Ak amat komeny chi oloto : ak Ingonam chito age boisiennyi .
Ingobiit age eng’ bik che kicham kebendoti tugul eng’ betusiek tugul ye kicham komong’u Kiptaiyat Jesu ak komandoi eng’ kwenunnyo , 
kotaune kabatisanetab Johana , agoi betut ne kigimuti kwo barak kobunei olinyo, kanyol koek age eng’ bichuto baoriat kobotech agobo ng’eetyennyi .
Ak kilewen bik aeng’ , Josep ne kigiguure Barsaba , ne kigiguure kainennyi ne bo aeng’ Justo , ak Matia . 
Ak kisa , kole , Inye , Kiptaiyat , ne ingen mugulelwekab bik tugul , iboruech eng’ bichu aeng’ , ne kailewen , 
si kobiit konam kebeberta eng’ boisioni ak kayoktaoni , ne kiibute Judas , si kobiit kwo oldanyi . 
Ak kiser barbarek agobo ichek ; ak kiibutyi barbariat Matia ; ak kigiitito che kiyoktoi taman ak agenge .
Ak kingoitei betutab Pentekost , ko kimi tugul komosta agenge . 
Ak kimong’ eng’ sainato cheet ne bunu kipsengwet ko u usonet ne usei eng’ kimnatet ne o , ak kinyi got komugul ole kitebe . 
Ak kimong’ji ng’elyebwek che pcheotin , ko u che bo mat ; ak kitebe age tugul eng’ ichek . 
Ak kinyi ichek tugul Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak kitoi kong’alale kutuswek alak , ko u ye kiigochi Tamirmiriet kong’alal .
Ak kimi Yahudik che kimenyei Jerusalem , bik che kigonyiti Jehovah , che kibunu bororiet age tugul ne mi kureretab kipsengwet . 
Ak kingogas cheonoto , koyumgei tuiyet , ak kokwong’io , amu kigas chi tugul bichoto kong’alali eng’ kutinnyi . 
Ak kitang’any tugul ak kokwong’io , kolen , Ogeero , tos ma Galilik chu tugul ng’alaldos ? 
Ak katepto ano si kegas achek chi tugul eng’ kutinnyo , ne kigisiktech ? 
Partik ak Medoik ak Elamik , ak che menyei Mesopotamia , ak Judea ak Kapadokia , ak Ponto ak Asia , 
ak Prugia ak Pampulia , ak Misri ak komoswek che bo Libya che negite Kurene , ak toek che bunu Rom , Yahudik koboto che kibunji Yahudik eng’ kayanenywa , 
Kretik ak Marabuk , kigase ichek kong’alali eng’ kutuswekyok boisionik che eechen che bo Jehovah . 
Ak kitang’any tugul , ak kogerer met , kolenjingei ichegei , Egu nee ng’olyondoni ? 
Ago kichombil alak kole , Kabogityo eng’ divaik che leelach .
Ago kitonon Petero koboto taman ak aeng’ , ak kolenji , eng’ kutit ne o , Okwek , bikab Judea , ak okwek tugul che omenye Jerusalem , ingonaak ni eng’ okwek , ak oepchi it ng’alekyuk . 
Amu ma bogityo bichu , ko u ye obwati ; amu ta ko sait somok kityo ; 
ago nito ne kimwaei maotiot Joel ; kole ,
Mwaei Jehovah kole , Tun eng’ betusiek che bo let , Arong’jini bik tugul Tamirmiriennyu , Ak komaoten werikwok ak tibikwok , Ak kogeer murenikwok ng’ang’utik , Ak koruotyi boisiekwok karuotitaosiek :
Arong’jini Tamirmiriennyu eng’ betusiechoto ; Ee , agot otwogikyuk murenik ak tibik , si komaoten .
Ak abarte kwong’utik eng’ kipsengwet barak , Ak kaborunoik eng’ oli bo ng’ony ; Korotik , ak mat , ak koiyenetab iyeto :
Kiwalei asista koek mesundeito , Ak kewal arawet koek korotik , Kotom koit betutab Kiptaiyat , Betut ne o agobo ne toogunot :
Ak tun kisoru age tugul ne kuurei kainetab Kiptaiyat .
Okwek bikab Israel , ogas ng’alechu : Jesu ne bo Nasaret , chito ne kiibarta Jehovah eng’ okwek eng’ boisionikab kimnatet ak kwong’utik ak kaborunoik , che kiyai Jehovah eng’ inendet eng’ kwenung’wong’ , ko u ye ongen okwek ; 
inendet ne kiigoito Jehovah eng’ begechinetab ng’olyondennyi ak naet ne kiga kechob eng’ tai , kiogartat okwek inendet ak obar eng’ eunekab bik che bistoe ng’atutik : 
inendet ne kiing’eet Jehovah ko kagotiach eng’ ng’wanindo ne bo meet : amu kima komuchi meet konam inendet . 
Amu kimwa Daudi agobo inendet , kole , Kiageere Kiptaiyat kotugul komi tainnyu : Amu mi inendet eunnyu ne bo tai , si ma kitumduma :
Amu noto anyun kiigasgei muguleldanyu , ak kibaibait ng’elyeptanyu ; Ak koboto noto komeng’isiei bortanyu agine eng’ kamang’unet :
Amu mebagakyini sobondanyu oldab che kigobek , Amegoitoi neng’ung’ Ne Tilil kogeer nunet .
Kiigona anai ortinwekab sobondo ; Inyiitwa boiboiyet eng’ taing’ung’ .
Che kitupche , amwawok komie agobo boiyot ne o Daudi , ale , kime ak kigitub , ak mitei kererinnyi kwenunnyo agoi ra . 
Ak amu kimaotio , ak kiingen kole kiga koyosiechi Jehovah inendet kole , indoi Jehovah ng’echerennyi chito ne tun bunu iyotennyi ; 
kingogeer nito anyun kong’alal agobo ng’eetyetab Kristo kole , ma kibagakyin inendet oldab che kibek , ama nunei bortanyi . 
Kiing’eet Jehovah Jesu nito , ne ki baorinikyik achek tugul . 
Amu itororot inendet eng’ eutab tai ne bo Jehovah , ak ko kagetaach eng’ Kwanda kayomiset ne bo Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ko kagorong’ anyun nito ogeere ak ogase . 
Amu kima togosta Daudi kipsengwetisiek : ago kimwa inendet kole , Kilenji Kiptaiyat Kiptaiyandennyu , Tebe eunnyu ne bo tai ,
Agoi ayai buniguk koek ng’echeretab kelyeguk .
Ingonai anyun komie got komugul ne bo Israel , kole , kigoyai Jehovah inendet koek Kiptaiyat ak ko Kristo , Jesu nito ne kiogartat .
Kingogas anyun nito , kotoor mugulelwekwak , ak kolenji ichek Petero ak che kiyoktoi chun alak , Che kitupche , kiyai nee ? 
Kolenji Petero ichek , Osigu , si kibatisan age tugul eng’ okwek eng’ kainetab Jesu Kristo agobo nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogikwok ; si otaach konunetab Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Amu neng’wong’ kayomisoni , ak lagokwok , ak tugul che mi ole loo , ak tugul che ta koguurei Kiptaiyat Jehovah nenyo kobwanji inendet .
Ak kibaorian eng’ ng’alek alak che chang’ , ak kogiil , kolenji , Osoruge eng’ ibini kunur . 
Kigibatisan anyun icheget che kitaach ng’olyondennyi : ak kigitesyi ichek betunoto bik olo bo elfusiek somok .
Ak kiigiiljingei ichek tugul konetisietab che kiyoktoi ak yamdaet , eng’ butuletab makatiat ak sautik .
Ak kinyor chi tugul kaiyweisiet : ak kiyaak kwong’utik che chang’ ak kaborunoik eng’ che kiyoktoi . 
Ak kimi tugul kibagenge che kiga koyan , ak kiyamdoi tuguk tugul ; 
ak kialda mbarenikwak ak tuguk alak che kitinyei ak kopchechi ichek tugul che te che kinyalili chi age tugul . 
Ak kimi hekalut betut age tugul kotebyei eng’ kabwatet agenge , ak eng’ butuletab makatiat eng’ ga , ak kiamisiei eng’ kagasetab ge , ak eng’ muguleldo agenge , 
kolosu Jehovah , ak kiiboiboi ichek bik tugul . Ak kitesyin Kiptaiyat betut age tugul icheget che nyoru sorunet .
Ak kitogostoi Petero ak Johana hekalut eng’ sait ne bo saet , sait sogol . 
Ak kigiganabi chito ne ki solomwo koboch komi moetab kamet , ne kicham kindoi betut age tugul kurgetab hekalut ne kigiguure Kararan , si kosomei tuguk bik che kibendi hekalut orit ; 
ko ye kingogeer inendet Petero ak Johana komachei koba hekalut orit , kosom kole kogochi kagochinet . 
Ak kiichiilji kong’ Petero inendet koboto Johana , ak kolenji , Keerech . 
Ak kiinyal inendet ichek , kolen nyorune kiy . 
Ago kile Petero , Matinye feda ak tahabu ; ago agonin ne atinye . Ng’eet eng’ kainetab Jesu Kristo ne bo Nasaret , ak iwendote . 
Konam anyun inendet eut ne bo tai , ak kong’eet : ak kinyor kimnatet ngunoto kelyekyik ak kowekab ng’woniot . 
King’eet kochokyi , ak kotonon , ak kotoi kowendot ; ak kiba hekalut orit koboto icheget , kowendoti , kotorombenoti , ak kolosu Jehovah . 
Ak kigeer bik tugul inendet kowendoti ak kolosu Jehovah : 
ak kinai icheget kole , inendet ne kicham kotebyei kosomei konunoik eng’ Kurget ne kiguure Kararan ne bo hekalut : ak kikwong’io mising’ ak kotang’any agobo noto kagoyaak eng’ inendet .
Ak kingota konamoti chichoto Petero ak Johana , koruai bik tugul ole mi ichek eng’ keterut ne kiguure ne bo Solomon , kokwong’dos mising’ . 
Ak ye kingogeer Petero , kowolji bik kolenji , Okwek bikab Israel , kalya si okwong’ie agobo ni ? Anan kalya si ochiiljech kong’ ko u ne olen achek che kagigochi inendet kowendot eng’ kamugennyo anan eng’ imandanyo ? 
Jehovah ne bo Abraham , ak ne bo Isak , ak ne bo Jakobo , Jehovah ne bo kwanisiekyok , ko kagotoror Kiboitiondennyi Jesu , ne kiogoite ak kiotiiye inendet eng’ taitab Pilato , ye kiga kobegechi kotiach inendet . 
Ago kiotiiye okwek Inendet ne Tilil ak ko bo Imanda , ak osom ole kegonok rumindet , 
ak kiobar Ne O ne bo sobondo ; ne kiing’eet Jehovah eng’ che kibek ; ki baorinikab noto achek . 
Ak kagogochi kainennyi chichi kimnatet , amu kayanet eng’ kainennyi , chichi ogeere ak ongen okwek : ee , kayanet ne mi eng’ Jesu ko kagogochi chichi sobet ne igesunotgei eng’ taing’wong’ okwek tugul .
Ak nguno anyun , che kitupche , angen ale , kioyai noto amu kima ongen , ko u ye kiyai bounikwok agichek . 
Ago tuguk che kiga kobor Jehovah eng’ tai eng’ kutuswekab maotik tugul , kole tun nyalili Kristo nenyi , ko kagoyai noto kosulda . 
Osigu anyun ak owalage , si kobiit kibukto tengekwogikwok , si kobwa anyun betusiek che bo kamuung’et che bunu taitab Kiptaiyat ; 
si koyok Kristo ne kigilewenwok , inendet Jesu : 
ne kanyol kotaach kipsengwet agoi betusiek che kiwale tuguk tugul komiagitu , che king’alale Jehovah eng’ kutuswekab maotikyik che tililen che kimi koboch taunetab ng’ony . 
Kimwa Musa iman , kole , Ing’eetwok Kiptaiyat Jehovah maotiot ne bunu che otupche , ne u ane ; ogas it inendet eng’ tuguk tugul che te che mwawok . 
Ak tun king’emei kiwong’u eng’ kwenutab bik , chito age tugul ne magase it maotiondonoto . 
Ee , ak maotik tugul koboch Samuel , ak ichek che kibwanei let eng’ inendet , tugul che te che king’alal , ko kimwa agichek agobo betusiechu . 
O werikab maotik , ak che bo kayomiset ne kiiyomisgei Jehovah ak kwanisiekwok . Kilenji Abraham , Kiberuri bororiosiek tugul che bo ng’ony eng’ keswondeng’ung’ . 
Ak ye kingo kagong’eet Jehovah Kiboitiondennyi , koyokwok okwek korok si koberurok , ak koistoe chi age tugul eng’ okwek tengekwogikyik .
Ak kingota kong’alaljin ichek bik , kobwanji icheget tisiik ak kiptaiyatab hekalut ak Sadukaik , 
kotinyei neregek amu kiinet bik ak koamda eng’ Jesu ng’eetyetab che kibek . 
Ak kinam icheget , ak kotoorji korgoret agoi mutai : amu kiga koimen . 
Ago kiiyan che chang’ eng’ ichek che kigas ng’olyot ; ak kiek koitetab murenik olo bo elfusiek mut .
Ak eng’ betut ne kiisubi noto koyumgei bounik ak boisiek ak sirik eng’ Jerusalem ; 
ak Anas tisiindet ne o , ak Kaiapa , ak Johana , ak Aleksandro , ak tugul che bo oretab tisiindet ne o . 
Ak kingo kagonde ichek kwenunywa , koteebe kole , Nee kamuget ne koyae ni , anan eng’ kainetab ng’o ?
Kingonyi anyun Petero Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , kolenji ichek , Okwek bounikab bik ak boisiek , 
ngemachei keginenech rani agobo boisiet ne mie ne kogiyachi chito ne nyalulat , ole kogisoopto chichito ; 
ingonaak anyun eng’ okwek tugul , ak eng’ bik tugul che bo Israel ole , eng’ kainetab Jesu Kristo ne bo Nasaret , ne kiogartat okwek , ne kiing’eet Jehovah eng’ che kibek , tononi chichi eng’ yu , eng’ taing’wong’ , ko kagosob eng’ inendet . 
Inendet koita ne kiosas okwek teegik , ne kiga kiyai koek metitab luita . 
Ama mi yetunet eng’ chito age : amu mami kainet age eng’ kureretab kipsengwet , ne kigigochi bik , ne kanyol kesorunenech .
Ak kingogeer nyiganatetab Petero ak Johana , ak konai kole bik che ma kinet , ama toogunotin , kokwong’io ; ak kinai kole , kicham komi koboto Jesu . 
Ak kingogeer chito ne kogisoob kotononi koboto ichek , ko mata komuch komwa kiy agobo noto . 
Ago ye kingo kagong’at ichek komanda eng’ kapkiruok , kong’alal ichegei , 
kole , Kiitoi nee bichu ? Amu naat eng’ bik tugul che menyei Jerusalem kele koyaak iman eng’ ichek kwong’utiet ne o , ama kimuchi ketiiye . 
Ago si mata koiyestaat eng’ kwenutab bik , konyolu keger kong’ ichek , si mata kong’alalji chi age tugul eng’ kainanito kogeny .
Ak kiguur ichek , ak kong’at ichek , kolenji , amatata kong’alal agot kitigin anan konetis eng’ kainetab Jesu . 
Ago kiwolji Petero ak Johana ichek kolenji , Ngo mie eng’ taitab Jehovah kegasak kosiir Jehovah , oruoch okwek : 
amu magimuchi kesisye kobate kemwa tuguk che kigegeer ak che kigegas . 
Ak kingo kagoger kong’ ichek kogeny , kounda koba , ko mata konyor ng’olyot ne iruokyine , amu bik ; amu kiitoror bik tugul Jehovah agobo noto koyaak . 
Amu kisiirei artam kenyisiekab chichoto kiyaak eng’ inendet kwong’utionito bo kasoobet .
Ak kingo kageunda , koba ole mi bikwak , ak komwaita tugul che kamwachi tisiik che eechen ak boisiek . 
Ak kingogas ichek komwachi Jehovah eng’ kutit ne o eng’ kabwatet agenge , kolenji , Ee Kiptaiyat , inye ne kiiyai kipsengwet ak ng’ony ak nyanjet , ak tugul che mi oloto : 
ne kiimwa eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil eng’ kutitab kwandanyo Daudi kiboitiondeng’ung’ , ile , Kilya si kobolyo Bororiosiek , Ak kobwatoti bik tuguk che manamegei ak kiy ?
Kitetegei laitorinikab ng’ony , Ak koyumegei bounik , Agobo Kiptaiyat , ak Kristo nenyi :
amu iman kituitos eng’ nganasani Herod ak Pontio Pilato agine koboto Bororiosiek ak bikab Israel , kole kogirinda Kiboitiondeng’ung’ ne Tilil Jesu , ne kiil , 
si koyai kit age tugul ne kisib kong’at eung’ung’ ak ng’omnateng’ung’ kole kosulda . 
Ak nguno anyun , Kiptaiyandani , keer kertaenywa bo kong’ : ak igochi otwogiguk komwa ng’olyondeng’ung’ eng’ nyiganatet tugul , 
ye iitoi inye eung’ung’ isoobi bik ; si koyaak kaborunoik ak kwong’utik eng’ kainetab Kiboitiondeng’ung’ ne Tilil , noto ko Jesu .
Ak kingo kagosa , kotumdumgei ole kiga koyumjigei ; ak kinyi ichek tugul Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak kimwa ng’olyotab Jehovah eng’ nyiganatet .
Ak ki bo muguleldo agenge ak sobondo agenge tuiyet ne kiga koyan : ak ma mwa chi agot agenge kole , nenyi kiy age tugul ne kitinyei ; ago kiyamdoi tugukwak tugul . 
Ak kibaorian che kiyoktoi eng’ kimnatet ne o agobo ng’eetyetab Kiptaiyat Jesu : ak kitebe mieindo ne o ichek tugul . 
Amu kima komi agot agenge eng’ kwenunywa ne kibanani kiy : amu tugul che kitinyei korotinwek anan gorik , ko kialda , ak koib tuguk che kiga aldae kobwa ,
konde kelyekab che kiyoktoi : ak kigipchechi chi age tugul ne kinyalili .
Ak kialda Josep mbaret ne kitinyei , inendet ne kitochi che kiyoktoi kainet ne bo aeng’ koguure Barnaba (ne ye kiweech , ko Weritab kagaigaet) , Lawindet , chito ne kisalu Kupro , 
ak kiib siling’isiek konde kelyekab che kiyoktoi .
Ago kialda chito age ne kigiguure Anania , ak osotiondennyi Sapira , korennyi , 
ak kiituuch kebebertab che kigialdae , kongen agine osotiondennyi , ak kiib kebeberta age , konde kelyekab che kiyoktoi . 
Ago kile Petero , Anania , kalya si konyi Setani muguleldang’ung’ kot iberber Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak ituuch kebebertab che kigialdae koret ? 
Kingota komi , ko kima ko neng’ung’ ? Ak kingo kagealda , ko kima ibou ? Kalya si ichob kii eng’ muguleldang’ung’ ? Ma iberber chi , ago Jehovah . 
Ak kingogas Anania ng’alechu , kobut ak kome : ak kinyonji kaiyweisiet ne o tugul che kigas . 
Ak king’eetyo murenik ak kotaae musto anget , ak kisut kwo sang’ ak kotub .
Ak ye ki negit kogesgei saisiek somogu , koit osotiondennyi agine , ak kima kongen kit ne kagoyaak . 
Ak kiwolji Petero kolenji , Mwawa ngo kioaldae koret tuguk che te choto ? Kole , Ee , te choto . 
Ago kilenji Petero inendet , Katepto ano kot ochamnyechi tuwai oyom Tamirmirietab Kiptaiyat ? Keero , mi kurgat kelyekab icheget che katubei manong’otiondeng’ung’ , ak sutin aginye imande . 
Ak kiibutyi kelyekyik ngunoto , ak kome : kobwa go anyun murenik konyor ko kagome , ak kisut kwo sang’ ak kotupchi ye negite manong’otiondennyi . 
Konyonji anyun kaiyweisiet ne o kaniset komugul , koboto tugul che kigas tuguchoto .
Ak kiyaogis eng’ eunekab che kiyoktoi kaborunoik ak kwong’utik che chang’ eng’ kwenutab bik ; ak kimi tugul eng’ kabwatet agenge eng’ keterut ne bo Solomon . 
Ago eng’ bik alak ko kimata kobiit chi ne kita kogany konamgei ak icheget ; ago kiitoror bik ichek ; 
ak kitesak kayanik eng’ Kiptaiyat kosiir , kichang’a murenik koboto kobogorisiek ; 
kot komut ichek che miandos kobwa ortinwek , ak komogonji itogusiek ak kiplusisiek , kole, tamangab kokwer uruetab Petero alak eng’ ichek , kosiirtoi . 
Ak kiiyomogei tuiyet ne bunu nganasok che negite Jerusalem , komutu che miandos , koboto che kiinyalili tamirmirik che muruonen : ak kigisoob age tugul eng’ ichek .
Ago kitonon tisiindet ne o , ak tugul che kimi koboto inendet (kasubikab Sadukaik choto) , ak ki nyiitat ichek ng’et konda , 
ak kinam che kiyoktoi , ak kotoorji korgoret ne bo bik tugul . 
Ago kiyat malaikaiyatab Kiptaiyat kurgotikab korgoret kemoi ak komut ichek komong’ sang’ , ak kolenji , 
Oba , ak otonon eng’ hekalut ak omwachi bik ng’alek tugul che bo Soboni . 
Ak kingogas ko u noto , koba hekalut ko kaech , ak konetis . Ago kinyo tisiindet ne o , ak che kimi koboto inendet , ak koguur kiruoget , ak boisiek tugul che bo lagokab Israel , ak koyokto kimut ichek kobwa eng’ ole kigiratyi . 
Ago kingoit askarik korgoret ko manyor ichek : ak kiweektagei , ak komwaita , 
kole , Kaginyoru ko kerat komie korgoret , ak kotonondos ribik eng’ kurgotik : ak ye kangeyat , koma kenyorji chi orit . 
Ak kingogas ng’alechu kiptaiyatab hekalut ak tisiik che eechen , koiimgei mising’ agobo ichek kole egu nee anyun ng’alechu . 
Ak kinyo chi ak kolenji , Ogeero , bicho kogotoorji korgoret , kotonondos eng’ hekalut ak koneti bik . 
Kwo anyun kiptaiyat koboto askarik , ak komut kobwa , ago ma eng’ kimnatet ; amu kiiywei bik kole si ma kilach ichek eng’ koik .
Ak kingo kagomut ichek kobwa , konde taitab kapkiruok . Koteebe tisiindet ne o ichek , 
kole , Kigeetenak inne kele , amatata onet bik eng’ kainani : ak ogeero , kionyiit Jerusalem konetisieng’wong’ , ak omache oibwech korotikab chichito kobwanjech .
Ago kiwol Petero ak che kiyoktoi kole , Kanyol kegas it Jehovah kosiir bik . 
Kiing’eet Jehovah ne bo kwanisiekyok Jesu , inendet ne kiobar ogartat eng’ ketit . 
Inendet ne kiitoror Jehovah eng’ eunnyi ne bo tai koek Ne O ago Yetindet , si kogochi Israel sigunet , ak nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogik . 
Ak ki baorinik achek che bo tuguchu ; ak Tamirmiriet ne Tilil agine , ne kigogochi Jehovah ichek che kase it inendet .
Ak kingogas ichek nito , kong’wanit mising’ eng’ mugulelwekwak , kot komach kobar ichek . 
Ago kitonon chito age eng’ kapkiruok , Parisaindet , ne kigiguure Gamaliel , konetindetab Ng’atutik , ne kigonyiti bik tugul , ak kong’at kole kimut bichoto koba sang’ ne matia . 
Ak kilenji ichek , Okwek bikab Israel , oripge eng’ bichu , eng’ kit ne omache oyai . 
Amu kingo tom koit betusiechu , koit Teudas kochoigei kole , a chito ne o ; ak konamgei ak inendet bik che itei olo bo bogol ang’wan : ak kigibar inendet ; ak kiyesta tugul che kigase it inendet , ak kibetyo . 
Kingobata chichoto kong’eet Judas ne bo Galili eng’ betusiek che bo sirisietab kainaikab bik , ak kochuut bik alak kosub inendet : kime agine ; ak kiyesta tugul che kigase it inendet . 
Ara anyun , amwawok nguno , ale , Oistoege bichu , ak obagakte ichek : amu ngo bo bik ng’alechu anan boisioni , kowong’ugei : 
ago ngot ko bo Jehovah , ko momuchi owong’u ; si ma kinyoruok obortosi ak Jehovah . 
Kocham anyun ng’alekyik : ak kingo kagoguur che kiyoktoi kobwa ole mi ichek , kobir ak kong’at kolenji , amatata ong’alale kainetab Jesu , ak kiunda koba . 
Koba anyun eng’ taitab kapkiruok koboiboi amu kagiit kele nyoljin konyor katewerisiet agobo Kainanato . 
Ak kima sisyo eng’ betut age tugul konetis ak koamdoi eng’ hekalut ak eng’ gorik , kole Jesu ko Kristo .
Eng’ betusiechoto anyun , ye ki tesoksei koitetab alamalyet , kong’eet kang’unyng’ung’et eng’ Yahudik che ki kutinywa ko Yunanik , kong’unyng’ung’ji Hebranik , amu kiginyasta mosogikwak eng’ tuguk che kicham kigochin kotugul . 
Koguur anyun tamanu ak aeng’ tuiyet ne bo alamalyet , ak kolenji , Ma mie kebagakte ng’olyotab Jehovah ak keboisie eng’ mesosiek . 
Ocheng’ anyun che kitupche bik tisab eng’ okwek che toogunotin kele miachen , che nyiitotin Tamirmiriet ak ng’omnatet , che kimuchi kinde boisioni . 
Ago si kigiiljige achek saet , ak konetisietab ng’olyot .
Kicham anyun tuiyet komugul ng’olyondonoto : ak kilewen Stepano , chito ne nyiitat kayanet ak Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak Pilipu , ak Prokoro , ak Nikanor , ak Timon , ak Parmena , ak Nikola ne bo Antiokia ne kiwalak koek Yahudiot : 
kiinde choto anyun taitab che kiyoktoi : ak ye kingo kagosa , kogonoor ichek eunekwak .
Kitesak anyun ng’olyotab Jehovah ; ak kotesak mising’ koitetab alamalyet eng’ Jerusalem ; ak kogas it kayanet tuiyet ne o ne bo tisiik .
Ak kinyiitat Stepano mieindo ak kamuget , koyai anyun kwong’utik che eechen ak kaborunoik eng’ kwenutab bik . 
Ago king’eetyo alak che bo sunagogit ne kiguure ne bo Che Itiagotin , ak ne bo Kurenik , ak ne bo Aleksandrianik , ak ne bo bikab Kilikia ak Asia , ak kobelgei ak Stepano . 
Ak kima imuch ichek kogirinda ng’omnatet ak Tamirmiriet ne king’alale inendet . 
Kogaigai anyun bik komwa kole , Kigegas komwaei inendet ng’alek che bo chubisiet agobo Musa , ak Jehovah . 
Kong’eetng’eet anyun bik konerekso ak boisiek , ak sirik , kobwanji inendet , ak konam ak komut kwo kapkiruok , 
ak konde baorinik che bo lembech , che kimwa kole , Mabagaktoi chichi komwa ng’alek che yaach agobo yu tilil , ak Ng’atutiet : 
amu kigegas inendet komwaei kolen , tatun kong’emei yuto Jesu nito bo Nasaret , ak kowal bitonwek che kigonech Musa . 
Kiichiilji kong’ anyun inendet bik tugul che kitebyei eng’ kapkiruok , kogeer togennyi ko u togetab malaikaiyat .
Kole anyun tisiindet ne o , Tos u choto tuguchu ? 
Kole Stepano , Che kitupche ak kwanisiekyok , ogaso . Kimong’ji Jehovah ne bo torornatet kwandanyo Abraham , ye kimi Mesopotamia , kotomo komeny Haran , 
ak kolenji , Mong’u eng’ emeng’ung’ ak eng’ ole mi biguk , ak inyo emet ne ta aborun . 
Komong’ anyun eng’ emetab Kaldeik , ak komeny Haran : ak kingo kagome kwandanyi , kouu Jehovah inendet , konyo emonito omenye rani : 
ak kima igochi inendet borotet eng’ oloto , acha , agot ole indoi keldanyi : ak kiiarorji kole , tun igochin inendet ak iyotennyi eng’ let , ye kitom kosich lakwa . 
Ak kimwa Jehovah ko u ni , kole , Egu lagokyik bunotik eng’ emetab bik alak , ak koyai ichek koek otwogik , ak koyachi ne ya eng’ kenyisiek bogol ang’wan . 
Ak kimwa Jehovah , kole , Aruokyini bororionoto ne tun ratei ichek : ak ye ibata noto komong’ ak koboisiewa eng’ olito . 
Ak kiigochi arorutiet ne bo kamuratanet : kosich anyun Abraham Isak , ak komuratan inendet eng’ betut ne bo sisiit ; ak kosich Isak Jakobo , ak kisich Jakobo kwanisiekyok taman ak aeng’ .
Ak ye kingoam ng’et kong’ boisiechoto agobo Josep , koalda inendet kwo Misri : ak kimi Jehovah koboto inendet , 
ak kisor inendet eng’ nyalilwogikyik tugul , ak kogochi chamet ak ng’omnatet eng’ taitab Parao laitoriatab Misri ; ne kiinde inendet koek bounindet eng’ Misri ak gonnyi tugul . 
Kinyo anyun rubet Misri komugul ak Kanan , ak nyalilda ne o : ak manyor kwanisiekyok amitwogik . 
Ago ye kingogas Jakobo kole mitei bek Misri , koyokto kwanisiekyok eng’ banda ne bo tai . 
Ak eng’ banda ne bo aeng’ koborjigei Josep tupchosiekyik ; ak kinaak eng’ Parao bikab Josep . 
Ak kiiyokto Josep kole keguur kwandanyi Jakobo , ak bikyik tugul , bik tamanwogik tisab ak mut . 
Kochortagei anyun Jakobo kwo Misri ; ak kime , inendet , ak kwanisiekyok ; 
ak kigila ichek koba Sekem , ak kigitupchi kererit ne kiga al Abraham eng’ kamanutietab feda eng’ werikab Hamor eng’ Sekem .
Ak ye kingorik betut ne bo arorutiet , ne kiiyosiechi Jehovah Abraham , koyabak bik ak kotesogis eng’ Misri , 
agoi kobiit laitoriat age eng’ Misri , ne kima kongen Josep . 
King’omenji inendet bororiennyo , ak koyachi ne ya kwanisiekyok , si kolakta manyurunikwak si masopcho . 
Ak kigisich Musa eng’ betusiechoto , ak ki kararan inendet mising’ ; ak kigigu eng’ gotab kwandanyi arawek somok ; 
ak kingo kagemeto , konyo chebo Parao , komut , ak kogu koek werinnyi . 
Ak kiginet Musa ng’omnatet tugul ne bo Misrik ; ak ki kim eng’ ng’alekyik ak boisionikyik .
Ak ye kingoit olo bo kenyisiek artam , kobwat eng’ muguleldanyi korutochi tupchosiekyik , lagokab Israel . 
Ak ye kingogeer kinyalili age eng’ ichek , kotoret inendet , ak koyaaktochi mugetut inendet ne kaginyalili , kokwer Misrindet kobar : 
ak kilen inendet naei tupchosiekyik kole igochin Jehovah ichek sorunet eng’ eunnyi ; ago ma nai . 
Ak eng’ betut ne isubi noto kochunji ichek kobortos , ak iimachei kooiyo ichek , kolenji , Murenju , otupche okwek ; kalya si oyachige ne ya ? 
Ago kitoorta inendet ne kiyachi nin age ne ya , ak kole , Ng’o ne koindein iegu bounindet ak kiruogindet kot iruokwech ? 
Imache ibara ko u ye koibar Misrindet amut ? 
Kimwee Musa anyun ng’olyondonoto , kwo koek bunotyo eng’ emetab Midian , ole kisikyi werik aeng’ .
Ak kingobata kenyisiek artamu , komong’ji inendet malaikaiyat eng’ ong’atet ne bo tulwetab Sinai , eng’ mat ne lalei eng’ ketit ne samum . 
Ak kingogeer Musa , kokwong’ eng’ kioto kageer : ak kingorikta kole kogeer , kotwek kutitab Kiptaiyat , 
kole , A Jehovah ne bo kwanisieguk , Jehovah ne bo Abraham , ak ne bo Isak , ak ne bo Jakobo . Kobotan Musa , ko mata kogany kogeer . 
Kolenji Kiptaiyat anyun inendet , Icheru kweoniguk eng’ kelyeguk : amu tilil ng’onyut yoto itonone . 
Kiageer iman nyalildab bikyuk che mitei Misri , ak kiagas tigenenywa , ak kaachoruge si kobiit asor ichek : nyo anyun nguno , ayokten iwe Misri .
Musa nito ne kiesio ichek , kolen , Ng’o ne koindein iegu bounindet ak kiruogindet ? Inendet ne kiiyokto Jehovah eng’ eutab malaikaiyat ne kimong’ji inendet eng’ ketit si kobiit koek bounindet , ak katiagindet . 
Kiimut chichi anyun ichek komanda , ye kingo kagoyai kwong’utik ak kaborunoik eng’ Misri , ak eng’ Nyanjet ne Birir , ak eng’ kenyisiek artam eng’ ong’atet . 
Musa nito ko noto ne kilenji lagokab Israel , Ing’eetwok Jehovah maotiot ne tun bunu che otupche , ne u ane . 
Nito ko inendet ne kimi kaniset eng’ ong’atet koboto malaikaiyat ne king’alalji inendet eng’ tulwet ne bo Sinai , ak koboto kwanisiekyok : ne kitaach ng’alek che soptos si kogonech :
ak kima kas it kwanisiekyok inendet , ago kiesio inendet , ak kiweektagei mugulelwekwak Misri , 
kolenji Aron , Yaiywech kanamonik kondoenech : amu magingen ole katepto Musa nito , ne kiimutwech kemong’une emetab Misri . 
Ak kiyai anyun moita eng’ betusiechoto , ak koipchi tiseiywot kanamwonoto , ak koboiboitu eng’ boisionikab eunekwak . 
Ago kiituktochi batai Jehovah ichek , ak kogoito ichek koot lugetab kipsengwet ; ko u ye sirat eng’ bukuitab maotik , kele , Tos kiogona che kiyagi che kageeny ak tiseiywek Eng’ kenyisiek artam eng’ ong’atet , Ee gotab Israel ?
Ak kioib okwek emait ne bo Molok . Ak kecheiyat ne bo kanamwet Repan , Kanamonik che kioyai si osa : Ak autok obe Babulon bitonin .
Kitinyei kwanisiekyok emait ne bo baornatet eng’ ong’atet , ko u ye kiga koaror inendet ne kimwachi Musa , kolenji , koyai ko u kergeindo ne kiga kogeer . 
Ne kiib kwanisiekyok agichek eng’ betusiekwak , koboto Josua , ye kinamei Bororiosiek , che kion Jehovah eng’ taitab kwanisiekyok , agoi betusiekab Daudi ; 
ne kinyor chamet eng’ taitab Jehovah , ak kosom konyor meng’otetab Jehovah ne bo Jakobo . 
Ago Solomon ne kiteekyi got .
Ago mamenyei Inendet ne Toror Mising’ gorik che kiyae eunek ; ko u ye mwaei maotiot , kole , 
Ng’echerennyu ne bo laitornatet kipsengwet , Ak ng’ony ko ng’echeretab kelyekyuk : Tos oteekwa got ne u nee ? Mwaei Kiptaiyat : Anan ano ole amuung’e ?
Tos ma eunnyu ne kiyaei tuguchu tugul ?
Okwek che uui kaat che ma kimuratan mugulelwek ak itik , ogirindoi Tamirmiriet ne Tilil kotugul : ko u ye kiyaei kwanisiekwok , oyae ak okwek ko u noto . 
Ng’o eng’ maotik ne ma us kwanisiekwok ? Ak kibar che kisib kobor nyonunetab Chito ne bo Imanda ; ne kaoegu okwek nguno ng’wektoik ak rumik . 
Okwek che kiotaach Ng’atutiet ko u ye kiging’at eng’ malaikaisiek , ak ma orib .
Ak ye kingogas ng’alechuto kong’wonegitu mising’ eng’ mugulelwekwak , ak konyei kelek agobo inendet .
