Ago kiinyal kipsengwet kochiilji kong’ ko nyiitat inendet Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak kigeer lilindab Jehovah , ak Jesu kotononi eng’ eutab tai ne bo Jehovah , 
ak kile , Ogeero , ageere kipsengwetisiek ko kagoyatogis , ak kotononi Weritab chi eng’ eutab tai ne bo Jehovah .
Ago kibolyo eng’ kutit ne o , ak koger itikwak , ak kotorombenji kibagenge ; 
ak kitoorta inendet komanda eng’ nganaset , ak kolage koik : ak kiinde baorinik ngoroikwak kelyekab muren age ne kigiguure Saul . 
Kolach anyun Stepano , koguurei Kiptaiyat , kolen , Kiptaiyat Jesu , taach tamirmiriennyu . 
Ak kigutuny , ak komwa eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Kiptaiyat , ameiityi ichek tengegi . Ak kingo kagomwa nito , konuuch .
Ak kichamei Saul agine meennyi . Ak king’eet betunoto usisiet ne o agobo kaniset ne kimi Jerusalem ; ak kiyesta ichek tugul koyom emotinwekab Judea ak Samaria , kobate che kiyoktoi . 
Kotub anyun Stepano bik che kigonyiti Jehovah , ak koteiyo mising’ agobo inendet .
Ago kiinyalil mising’ Saul kaniset , ak kowendi got age tugul , kochuutu murenik ak kobogorisiek ak kotoorjin korgoret .
Kiba anyun ichek che kiga koyesta , koamdaat ng’olyot . 
Ak kichortagei Pilipu nganaset ne bo Samaria , ak koamji ichek Kristo . 
Ak kiepchi it tuiyosiek eng’ yamdaet agenge ng’alek che kimwaei Pilipu , ye kingogas ak kogeer kaborunoik che kiyai . 
Amu kimanda tamirmirik che muruonen , eng’ che chang’ che kitinyei , kowaaktos eng’ kutit ne o : ak kigisoob che chang’ che meiyotin borwek , ak che kiing’waldos . 
Ak kibiit boiboiyet ne o eng’ nganasanato .
Ak kimi chito age ne kigiguure Simon, ne kicham kong’orsei eng’ betusiek alak eng’ nganasanato , ak kiigochi bororietab Samaria kokwong’io , komwaei inendet kole , a chito ne o : 
kiepchin it tugul inendet , koboch ne ming’in agoi ne o , kolen , Kimnatetab Jehovah chichi , ne kiguure Ne O . 
Ak kiepchin it inendet , amu kicham kogochin kokwong’io eng’ betusiek che chang’ eng’ ng’orsosiekyik . 
Ago ye kingoyan ng’alekab Pilipu ye kiamdoi logoiywek che miach agobo bounatetab Jehovah ak kainetab Jesu Kristo , kibatisan anyun murenik koboto kobogorisiek . 
Ak kiiyan Simon agine : ak kingo kagibatisan kotebi koboto Pilipu : ak kingogeer koyaogis kaborunoik ak boisionikab kimnatet kokwong’ .
Kingogas anyun che kiyoktoi che kimi Jerusalem kole , kogotaach Samaria ng’olyotab Jehovah , koyokyi Petero ak Johana : 
ak ye kingo kagochorgei ichek , kosa agobo ichek , kole , si kotaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil : 
amu kitom kochorjigei agot agenge eng’ bichoto : kiga kibatisan ichek eng’ kainetab Kiptaiyat Jesu kityo . 
Yeityo kogonoor ichek eunekwak , ak kitaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Ye kingogeer anyun Simon kole kaga ngo konoor alamalyet chi eunekwak , kigochi Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , kogochi ichek siling’isiek , 
kole , Ogona agane kimnatoni , si ngagonoor chi age tugul eunekyuk , kotaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil .
Ago kilenji Petero inendet , Ingobetyo siling’isieguk koboten , amu kelen inyoru konunetab Jehovah eng’ siling’isiek . 
Metinye kebeberta anan motwet eng’ ng’olyondoni : amu ma mie muguleldang’ung’ eng’ taitab Jehovah . 
Sigu anyun eng’ tengeging’ung’et , ak isa Kiptaiyat , tamangab kenyoun kaat amu kabwatetab muguleldang’ung’ . 
Amu ageere ale imi eng’ ng’wanindo ak eng’ ratutietab tengekto . 
Ak kiwol Simon kole , Osaiywa Kiptaiyat , si mabwanja agot agenge tuguk che kaomwawa .
Ye kingo kagobaorian anyun ak komwa ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat , koweektagei Jerusalem , ak koamji logoiywek che miach nganasok che chang’ che bo Samarik .
Ago kimwachi Pilipu malaikaiyatab Kiptaiyat , kolenji , Ng’eet ak iwe murot ne bo tai agoi oret ne chortogei ne wendi Gasa kong’eete Jerusalem : ne surkwen . 
Ak king’eet anyun kwo : ak keero, chitab Etiopia , ne kigimoch , ne kitinyei bounatet ne o eng’ eutab Kandake , laitoriat kwondo ne bo Etiopik , ne kiribei tugukyik tugul che bo kamanutiet ne o , ne kiga nyo Jerusalem kosa ; 
kiweeksei anyun , kotebe karinnyi , ak kosomani bukuitab maotiot Isaia . 
Ak kilenji Tamirmiriet Pilipu anyun , Ui rikte , onamge ak karina . 
Ak kilabat Pilipu ak kogas inendet kosomani bukuitab maotiot Isaia , ak kilenji , Iguitosi kit ne isomani ? 
Ak kile , Amuktoi ano , ngo maiborua chi ? Ak kiigaigai Pilipu kole , kolany karit ak kotebi tuwai . 
Ak chu sirutik che kisomanoti , Kigimut ko u kechiriet ne kikweriei kwo eng’set ; Ak ko u aruetab kechiriet ne sisei eng’ taitab chito ne tilei kororikyik , U noto agine mang’any kutinnyi :
Kigiisto kiruogennyi eng’ kaming’inennyi bo ge : Ng’o ne tun mwaitoi ibindanyi ? Amu kinemu sobondanyi eng’ ng’ony .
Ak kiwolji chichoto kigimoch , Pilipu , kolenji , Asomin ale , mwaei maotiot ng’olyondoni agobo ng’o ? Agobo inendet , anan agobo chito age ?
Kong’any anyun Pilipu kutinnyi , ak kotoi eng’ sirutioni koamji inendet agobo Jesu . 
Ak ye kingota kobendi eng’ oret , koit ye mi beek ; kole chichoto, Keer beek-o ; nee ne kera si ma kibatisana ?  
Kong’at anyun kotonon karit : ak kichortagei tuwai koba beek , Pilipu ak chichoto ; ak kiibatisan inendet . 
Ak ye kingolong’ eng’ beek , komut Tamirmirietab Kiptaiyat Pilipu ; ak mata kogeer anyun chichoto kigimoch Pilipu , amu kiwa chichoto eng’ boiboindo . 
Ak kitook Pilipu eng’ Asoto : ak kosiirto , koamjinoti logoiywek che miach nganasok tugul , agoi koit Kaisaria .
Ak ye kita konerechi Saul koboisie kamuiset ak barisiet agobo alamalyetab Kiptaiyat , kwo oldab tisiindet ne o , 
ak kosom inendet baronok che ibei koba Damasko agobo sunagogisiek , kole ngonyor alak tugul che bo Oranato , ngo murenik anan kobogorisiek , komuchi komut kobwa Jerusalem ko ratotin .
Ak ye kita kowendi , ko karikta Damasko : koluu ngunoto lapkeiyet ne kibunu kipsengwet koluuchi inendet komoswek tugul : 
ak kiibutyi ng’ony , ak kogas kutit kolenji inendet , Saul , Saul , amu nee si iusa ? 
Ak kile , I ng’o , Kiptaiyandani ? Ak kile , A Jesu ne iuse : 
ago ng’eet , ui nganaset , si kemwaun kit ne kanyol iyai . 
Ak kitononso ko nam kut bik che kibendi koboto inendet , kogasei twegunet , ama keerei chi . 
Kong’eet anyun Saul ; ak kingo kagoyatogis konyekyik , ko ma kogeerei kiy ; komut anyun ichek inendet konamoti eut , agoi Damasko . 
Ak kitar betusiek somok ama keerei kiy , ama amisiei anan koeeiso .
Ak kimi alamalyet age Damasko , ne kigiguure Anania ; ak kilenji Kiptaiyat inendet eng’ ng’ang’utiet , Anania . Kowol kole , Ami yu , Kiptaiyandani . 
Kolenji Kiptaiyat , Ng’eet , ui oret ne kiguure Ne Litit , ak iteeb eng’ gotab Judas chito ne kiguure Saul , chitab Tarso : keero , saei ; 
ak kagogeer inendet chito ne kiguure Anania , konyonei agoi go , ak kogonoor inendet eunekyik , si kogeerto . 
Ago kiwol Anania , kole , Kiptaiyandani , kiagas eng’ bik che chang’ agobo chichito , ole te yaitiet ne kigoyachi biguk che tililen eng’ Jerusalem : 
ak tinyei eng’ yuto kimnatet ne bunu tisiik che eechen si korat tugul che kuurei kaineng’ung’ . 
Ago kilenji Kiptaiyat , Ui inye : amu kinnyu inendet ne aboisie ne kialewen , si koib kainennyu taitab Bororiosiek ak laitorinik , ak lagokab Israel : 
amu aborjini inendet ole te chang’indab tuguk che kanyol konyorune nyalilda agobo kainennyu .
Kiwa anyun Anania , ak kiwa agoi go ; ak ye kiigonoor inendet eunekyik , kolenji , Tupchennyu Saul , kagiyokwa Kiptaiyat , inendet Jesu , ne kichunjin eng’ oret ne kiibunu , kole igeerte , ak kinyiitun Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Ak eng’ sainato , kobutyo eng’ konyekyik tuguk che u berik , ak kigeerto ; ak king’eet anyun ak kigibatisan ; 
ak kiamis ak kinyor kimnatet . Ak kitebi betusiek alak koboto alamalyet che kimi Damasko . 
Ak ne matianit koamda agobo Jesu eng’ sunagogisiek kole , Inendet ko Weritab Jehovah . 
Ak kikwong’io tugul che kigas inendet , ak kole , Tos ma chichi ne kotar bik eng’ Jerusalem , icheget che cham koguurei kainani ? Ak kogonyo oli agobo ng’olyondonito , si kobiit komut ichek ko ratotin koba taitab tisiik che eechen .
Ago kitesak Saul kogimit , ak kiigochi kokwong’io Yahudik che kimenyei Damasko , koborjin ichek komie kole , Nito ko Kristo . 
Ak ye kingogesgei betusiek che chang’ , kotuiyo Yahudik koruoch kole kobar inendet : 
ago kinaak eng’ Saul chobenywa ne bo ung’ot . Ak kirib ormarichok bet ak kemoi , kole kobar : 
ago kiimut alamalyennyi kemoi , ak kochoorta kosiir irimet , komitei mesendet orit .
Ak ye kingonyo Jerusalem kotiem kole koyomogei ak alamalyet : ago kiiywei ichek tugul inendet , ama iyan kole alamalyet inendet . 
Ago kiimut Barnaba inendet kwo ole mi che kiyoktoi , ak kotetyi anyun ole kigeerto inendet Kiptaiyat eng’ oret , ak kole kiga kong’alalji inendet , ak ko u ye kigoamda eng’ nyiganatet eng’ Damasko eng’ kainetab Jesu . 
Ak kimi koboto ichek eng’ Jerusalem , komandoi ak komong’u , 
koamdoi eng’ nyiganatet eng’ kainetab Kiptaiyat : ak kong’alal ak kobeligei koboto Yahudik che ki kutinywa ko Yunanik ; ago kicheng’ei kotugul kole kobar inendet . 
Ak ye kingonai tupchosiek , komut inendet kochortagei kwo Kaisaria , ak koyokto kwo Tarso .
Konyor anyun kamuung’et kaniset ne mi Judea komugul ak Galili ak Samaria , koteegak ; ak ye kibendoti eng’ kaiyweisietab Kiptaiyat ak eng’ kagaigaet ne bo Tamirmiriet ne Tilil, kotesak .
Ak ye kiwendote Petero komoswek tugul , kochortagei ole kimi che tililen che kimenyei Luda . 
Ak kinyorji oloto chito age ne kigiguure Ainea , ne kiga korue itogunnyi kenyisiek sisiit ; amu ki meat borto . 
Kolenji anyun Petero inendet , Ainea , isoobin Jesu Kristo : ng’eet , ak iite itogung’ung’ . Kong’eet anyun ngunoto . 
Ak kigeer inendet tugul che kimenyei Luda ak Saron , ak koyan Kiptaiyat .
Ak kimi age ne bo alamalyet Jopa ne kigiguure Tabita , ne ye kiweech kele Dorkas : kitinyei kobogoriondoni boisionik che chang’ che miach ak kagochinoik che kiigoitoi . 
Ak kimian eng’ betusiechoto , ak kime : ak kingo kagoun , konde got age ne mi barak . 
Ak amu ki negityin Luda ak Jopa , ko ye kingogas alamalyet kole , mi Petero oloto , koyokyi bik aeng’ inendet , kosom kole , Nyonjech , amegage . 
Kong’eet anyun Petero ak koba ak ichek . Ak kingo kagoit , komut inendet kwo got ne bo barak : ak kitonondos mosogik tugul korirtos eng’ ye negit inendet , ak koborji sumotik ak ngoroik che kinabei Dorkas , ye kita komi koboto ichek . 
Komaanda Petero tugul koba sang’ , ak kogutuny , kosa ; ak kingoweleljigei musto , kolenji , Ng’eet , Tabita . Ak kiyat konyekyik : ak kingogeer inendet Petero , kong’eet koteb ng’ony . 
Ak kogochi inendet eunnyi , ak konam inendet kong’eet ; ak ye kingo kagoguur che tililen ak mosogik , konde inendet tainywa ko kagosob . 
Ak kinaak eng’ Jopa komugul : ak kiiyan che chang’ Kiptaiyat . 
Ak kitebi eng’ Jopa betusiek che chang’ koboto chito age ne kigiguure Simon ne teiteindetab muiywek .
Kimi chito age Kaisaria , ne kigiguure kainennyi Kornelio , ne ki kiptaiyatab bogol ne bo luget ne kigiguure luget ne bo Italia , 
chito ne kigonyiti Jehovah ak koiywei inendet koboto gonnyi tugul , ne kiigochin bik kagochinoik che chang’ , ak kosaei Jehovah kotugul . 
Kigeer eng’ ng’ang’utiet kimni , olo bo sait sogol ne bo bet , malaikaiyatab Jehovah konyonjin inendet , ak kolenji, Kornelio ! 
Ak kingogeer inendet mising’ eng’ kaiyweisiet , kole , Tos nee , Kiptaiyandani ? Kolenji , Kigoit barak sautiguk ak kagochinoiguk koek kabwatet eng’ taitab Jehovah . 
Iyokte nguno anyun bik koba Jopa , koguur chi ne kiguure Simon , ne kainennyi ne bo aeng’ ko Petero : 
inendet ko toondetab Simon ne teiteindetab muiywek , ne mi gonnyi ngegutab araraita . 
Ak ye kingo kakwa malaikaiyat ne king’alalji inendet , koguur otwogik aeng’ che bo gonnyi , ak askarindet ne kigonyiti Jehovah ne ki age eng’ che kiboisiechin inendet kotugul ; 
ak kingo kagomwachi ichek ng’alek tugul , koyokto koba Jopa .
Ak eng’ betut ne kiisubi betunoto ye kita kobendi , ko karikta nganaset , kotogosta Petero got barak , eng’ olo bo sait lo , kwo kosa : 
ak kiam rubet , ak kimach koamis : ak ye kigichobei amitwogik , kobutyi kiy ne u ruon ; 
ak kigeer kipsengwet koyatak , ak kochorugei kit ne u anget ne o kot , kechooru eng’ kuinoik ang’wan agoi ng’ony : 
kimi orit tiong’ik alak tugul che bo kelyek ang’wan ak tuguk che ichuutegei che bo ng’ony ak taritik che bo barak . 
Kinyonji anyun kutit , kolenji , Ng’eet , Petero ; eny ak iam . 
Ago kile Petero , Ma u noto , Kiptaiyandani ; amu tom aam kiy ne ma tilil anan ne ng’wan koboch atkinyei kora .
Kinyonji anyun kutit kogeny ne bo aeng’ , kolenji , Kit ne kagotilil Jehovah , ko mata ile ng’wan . 
Ak kiyaak kiito konyil somok ; ak ngunoto ketaach kioto eng’ kipsengwet .
Ak ye kita koiimegei Petero mising’ eng’ muguleldanyi kole , iboru nee ng’ang’utioni kagogeer , ogeero , kotononso eng’ kurgat bik che kiga koyok Kornelio , ko kagoteeb ole mi gotab Simon , 
ak koguurso ak koteeb ngo mi Simon oloto , ne kainennyi ne bo aeng’ ko Petero .
Ak ye kita kobwati Petero agobo ng’ang’utionoto , kolenji Tamirmiriet inendet , Keero , cheng’in bik somogu . 
Ago ng’eet , ak ichortege , ak obe tugul , amesage kiy : amu kaayogu ichek . 
Ak kichortagei anyun Petero kwo ole mi bichoto , ak kole , Ogeero , a inendet ne ocheng’e : nee ne kagonok obwa ? 
Ak kile , Kiiborji komie Jehovah Kornelio , eng’ malaikaiyat ne tilil , koyok bik kobwa koguurin iwe gonnyi ne inendet ko kiptaiyatab bogol , chito ne bo imanda ak koiywei Jehovah , ak baorianjin bororiet tugul ne bo Yahudik kole mie inendet , kole si kogasenen ng’alek .
Koguur anyun kobwa go ak kochopchi ichek ole ruitos . Ak king’eet karon koba koboto bichoto ak tupchosiek alak che kibunu Jopa . 
Ak betut ne kiisubi betunoto koit Kaisaria . Ak kiigeni ichek Kornelio , ko kagoguur tupchosiekyik ak choronokyik che kiingengei komie . 
Ak ye kingwo go Petero , kotoroch Kornelio inendet , ak kobutyi kelyekyik , kogutung’ji . 
Ago kiing’eet Petero inendet kolenji , Tonon ; anendet ko a chito agane . 
Ak kingota kong’alaljindos tuwai , kwo go , ak konyor bik che chang’ che kagoyumgei : 
kolenji anyun ichek , Ongen okwek ole kiy ne etan eng’ ng’atutik eng’ chi ne Yahudio konamgei ak chi ne bo boror age anan konyo ole mi ; ago kagoborua ane Jehovah kole , si mata aguure chi age ne ma tilil anan ne ng’wan : 
noto anyun kaanyo amata asich kiy ne amwae , ye kingo kageguura . Noto anyun ateebe ale nee ne koguurja . 
Kole anyun Kornelio , Betusiek ang’wan rani koboch yoto agoi saini , ye kiasae eng’ sait sogol eng’ gonnyu ; ak keero, kitonon eng’ tainnyu mureno ne ilaachi ngoroik che lilei bich , 
ak kole , Kornelio , kigegas saeng’ung’ , ak kigoek kabwatet eng’ taitab Jehovah kagochinoiguk . 
Iyokte anyun bik koba Jopa , koguurun Simon ne kainet ne bo aeng’ ko Petero ; mitei inendet ko toondet eng’ gotab Simon teiteindetab muiywek , ye negite ngegutab nyanjet . 
Kiayogu anyun bik eng’ sainato kobwa ole imi ; ak kaiyai ne mie amu kainyo . Kimi anyun yu nguno achek tugul eng’ taitab Jehovah , si kegas tuguk tugul che king’atin Kiptaiyat .
Ak king’any anyun Petero kutinnyi , kole , Iman ageere ale machamei Jehovah bik alak kosiir alak : 
ago taachaksei eng’ inendet chito ne iywei inendet , ak koyaei iman eng’ bororiet age tugul . 
Ng’olyot ne kiiyokyi inendet lagokab Israel , ko koamda ng’alek che miach che bo kalyet eng’ Jesu Kristo (inendet ko Kiptiyat ne bo tugul)- 
ongen okwek ng’olyondonoto , ne kigiamda eng’ Judea komugul ketaune Galili , kingobata kabatisanet ne kiamdoi Johana ; 
ko u ye kiil Jehovah Jesu ne bo Nasaret , eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ak eng’ kamuktaet : ne kiwendot ak koyaei ne mie , ak kosoobi tugul che kiinyalili oindet ; amu kimi Jehovah koboto inendet . 
Ak ki baorinik achek che bo tuguk tugul che kiyai eng’ emetab Yahudik , ak eng’ Jerusalem ; ne kibar ichek inendet kogartat eng’ ketit . 
Kiing’eet Jehovah inendet eng’ betutab somok , ak kogoito kotook , 
ma eng’ bik tugul , ago eng’ baorinik che kiga sib kolewen Jehovah , acheget choto che kigiamisiei ak keeisei koboto inendet ko kagong’eet komong’ eng’ che kibek . 
Ak king’atech keamji bik , ak kebaorian kele nito ko inendet ne kiinde Jehovah koek Kiruogindet ne bo che soptos ak che kigobek . 
Baoriani maotik tugul agobo inendet , kole , nyoru nyoetab kaat amu tengekwogikyik eng’ kainennyi age tugul ne iyani inendet .
Ye kita komwaei Petero ng’alechu , kochorjigei Tamirmiriet ne Tilil tugul che kigasei ng’olyot . 
Ak kikwong’io ichek che bo kamuratanet che kiiyani , tugul che kibwanei koboto Petero , amu kagerong’ji Bororiosiek agichek konunetab Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Amu kigasei ichek kong’alali eng’ kutuswek che terotin , ak kotorori Jehovah . Kowol anyun Petero kole , 
Imuchi chi koete beek , si ma kibatisan bichu , che kagotaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ko u achek ? 
Ak king’at kole kibatisan ichek eng’ kainetab Jesu Kristo . Kosom anyun ichek inendet kole kota kobeni betusiek alak .
Ak kigas anyun che kiyoktoi ak tupchosiek che kimi Judea kole kogotaach agichek Bororiosiek ng’olyotab Jehovah . 
Ak kingo kagonyo Petero Jerusalem , kobelgei ak inendet ichek che bo kamuratanet , 
kolen , Kiiwe oldab bik che ma kimuratan ak iamisie koboto ichek . 
Ago kitoi Petero kotetyi ichek komie ng’alechato , kolenji ,
Kiami nganasetab Jopa asae : ak kingobutya kiy ne u ruon ageer ng’ang’utiet , ne bo kiy ne kichorugei , ne u anget ne o kot , ne kigichoor kobunu kipsengwet eng’ kuinoik ang’wan ; ak kinyo agoi ole ami : 
ak ye kingageer mising’ , abwat , ageer tiong’ikab ng’ony che bo kelyek ang’wan ak tiong’ik che bo timin ak tuguk che ichuutegei ak taritik che bo barak . 
Ak kiagas kutit kolenja , Ng’eet , Petero ; eny ak iam . 
Ak kiamwa ale , Ma u noto , Kiptaiyandani : amu tom kochut kutinnyu kiy ne ma tilil anan ne ng’wan . 
Ago kiwol kutinato ne bo aeng’ kobunu kipsengwet kole , Amata ing’wanit kit ne kagotilil Jehovah . 
Ak kiyaak kioto konyil somok : ak kigichuut kogeny tugul koba kipsengwet . 
Ak ogeero , kitonondos eng’ sainato bik somogu eng’ taitab got ole kigimi , che kigiyok eng’ Kaisaria kobwa ole ami . 
Kong’ata anyun Tamirmiriet , kole , kebe tugul , amat isage . Ak kigibe tugul ak tupchosiechu lo agichek ; kebe agoi gotab chichoto : 
ak kimwawech ko u ye kiga keer malaikaiyat kotononi eng’ gonnyi , kole , Iyokte bik koba Jopa koguur Simon , ne kiguure kainennyi ne bo aeng’ Petero ; 
konyo komwaun ng’alek , che kisorunenen , inye ak gong’ung’ tugul . 
Ak ye kingatau kang’alal , kochorjigei Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ichek , ko u ye kichorjech ge agachek eng’ taunet . 
Abwat anyun ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat , ko u ye kimwa , kole , Kiibatisanis Johana eng’ beek ; ago kibatisanok okwek eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Ngo kiigochi anyun Jehovah ichek konunet ne kergei ak ne kigonech ye kingiyan Kiptaiyat Jesu Kristo , ko tos , kia ng’o anyun , kot amuch agirinda Jehovah ? 
Ak kingogas ng’alechuto , kosisyo , kolos Jehovah , ak komwa kole , Kaga kagogochi Jehovah Bororiosiek agichek sigunet ne ibu sobondo .
Kiba anyun ichek che kiga yesta amu usisiet ne king’eet agobo Stepano agoi koit Poinike , ak Kupro , ak Antiokia , ko mang’alaljin chi age ng’olyot kobate Yahudik . 
Ago kimi alak eng’ ichek , bikab Kupro ak Kurene , che kingobwa Antiokia kong’alalji Yunanik agichek , koamdoi Kiptaiyat Jesu . 
Ak kimi eutab Kiptaiyat koboto ichek : ak kiiyan bik che chang’ konam ng’alekab Kiptaiyat . 
Ak kigas ng’alek agobo ichek kaniset ne kimi Jerusalem : ak kiiyokto Barnaba kwo kot koit Antiokia : 
ak kingoit inendet , ak kogeer mieindab Jehovah , kobaibait ; ak kogiil ichek tugul konamgei ak Kiptaiyat eng’ mugulelwek che bekyinotin : 
amu ki chi ne mie , ak ko nyiitat Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ak kayanet : ak kitesak bik che chang’ kobunji Kiptaiyat . 
Ak kiwa agoi Tarso kocheng’ Saul : 
ak kingo kagonyor , komut konyo Antiokia . Ak kiiyumgei eng’ kenyit agenge koboto kaniset , ak konet bik che chang’ ; ak kigitoi keguure alamalyet Kristianik eng’ Antiokia .
Ak kichorgei maotik eng’ betusiechoto eng’ Jerusalem kobwa Antiokia . 
Ak kitonon age eng’ ichek ne kigiguure Agabo , ak kobor eng’ Tamirmiriet kole tun biitu rubet ne o ng’ony komugul : ne kiisulda eng’ betusiekab Klaudio . 
Ak kichopgei komie alamalyet koyokyi toretet tupchosiek che kimenyei Judea , chi tugul ko u ye kiimuchi : 
kiyai anyun ko u noto , kiiyokyi boisiek eng’ eunekab Barnaba ak Saul .
Ak ye ki negit betusiechoto kotoi laitoriat Herod kous alak che bo kaniset . 
Ak kibar Jakobo ng’etab Kametab Johana eng’ rotwetab chok . 
Ak ye kingogeer kole kiibaibai noto Yahudik , kotoi konam Petero agine . Ak ki betusiekab makatiat ne ma kinde mermerek , betusiechoto . 
Ak kingo kagonam inendet , konde korgoret , ak kogochi askarik ang’wan konyil ang’wan korib inendet ; kolen ye ibata Paska komutyi bik . 
Kigirib Petero anyun eng’ korgoret : ago kisa kaniset Jehovah mising’ agobo inendet .
Ak ye kimachei komoong’ Herod inendet , ko kirue Petero kwenutab askarik aeng’ eng’ kemounoto , koratate sirimwek aeng’ : ak kirib korgoret ribik eng’ taitab kurget . 
Ak ogeero , kitonon malaikaiyatab Kiptaiyat eng’ ye negite inendet , ak kiikweny lapkeiyet got : ak kiirabach karastab Petero , ak kong’eet kolenji , Ng’eet chokyi . Ak kiibutyo sirimwek che kimi eunekyik . 
Ak kolenji malaikaiyat inendet , Ratge , indege kweoniguk ak irat . Ak kiyai ko u noto . Ak kilenji , Ilaach ngorieng’ung’ , ak isubwa . 
Ak kiwa sang’ ak kosub ; ak kima nai kole iman kit ne kayai malaikaiyat , ago kilen kageer ng’ang’utiet . 
Ak kingo kagosiir ripset ne bo tai ak ne bo aeng’ , kobwa agoi ormarichet ne bo karnet ne kibunei kebendi nganaset ; koyatak inegei : ak kimanda sang’ , ak koba kobun oret agenge ; ak eng’ sainato kobagakta inendet malaikaiyat kwo .
Ak ye kingobwat Petero , komwa kole , Kaanai nguno iman , ale , kagoyok Kiptaiyat malaikaiyandennyi ak kasorua eng’ eutab Herod , ak eng’ kagenisiet tugul ne bo bikab Yahudik .
Ak ye kingo kagobwat komie , konyo gotab Maria kametab Johana ne kiguure kainennyi ne bo aeng’ Mariko ; ole kiga koyumjigei che chang’ ak kosaei . 
Ak ye kingogongony kurgetab ormarichet , konyo chepto ne kigiguure Roda kogas . 
Ak kingonai cheboto kutitab Petero , koma koyat ormarichet amu boiboiyet , ago kilabat go , ak komwaita kole tononi Petero eng’ ormarichet . 
Ak kilenji ichek inendet , Amin iywek . Ago kimwa eng’ kimnatet kole , u noto . Ak kimwa ichek kole , Malaikaiyandennyi . 
Ago kites Petero kogongony : ak kingo kagoyat , kogeer inendet , ak kokwong’io . 
Ago kiiborjine inendet ichek eut kosisyo , ak kotetyi ole kagomutunda Kiptaiyat inendet komong’ eng’ korgoret . Ak kimwa kole , Omwachi ng’alechu Jakobo , ak tupchosiek . Ak kiwa agoi komosta age .
Ak kingo kagoeech , kotoptobenso askarik mising’ , kole, katepto ano Petero . 
Ak ye kingo kagocheng’ Herod inendet , ama konyor , kogin ribik , ak kong’at kole kanyol kebar . Ak kichortagei eng’ Judea kwo Kaisaria , ak kotebe oloto .
Ak kinerekyi mising’ Herod bikab Turo ak Sidon : ak kobwanji inendet eng’ kabwatet agenge , ak , kingonam chorua ak Blasto , ne kiribei ole kirue laitoriat , kosom kalyet , amu kibaei emetab laitoriat emenywa .
Ak eng’ betut ne kiging’at , kolaach Herod ngoroikab laitornatet , ak kotebe ng’echeretab kiruoget , ak kong’alalji bichoto . 
Ak kibolyo bik , kole , Kutitab cheptalelit nito , ma bo chi . 
Eng’ sainato anyun kobir inendet malaikaiyatab Kiptaiyat , amu ma konyit Jehovah : ak kiam inendet kutik , ak kime . 
Ago kiner ng’olyotab Jehovah , ak kotesak .
Kiweektagei Barnaba ak Saul Jerusalem , ye kingo kagoges boisienywa , komuti Johana , ne ki kainennyi ne bo aeng’ ko Mariko .
Ak kimi kaniset ne kimi Antiokia , maotik ak konetik , Barnaba , ak Simion ne kigiguure Niger , ak Lukio ne bo Kurene , ak Manaen ne kigigui koboto kiruogindet Herod , ak Saul . 
Ak ye kiboisiechin Kiptaiyat ak korugutegei , kole Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , Otabanwa Barnaba ak Saul agobo boisiet ne kiaguurji . 
Ak ye kingo kagorugutgei ak kosaei ak kogonoor ichek eunekwak , koyokto koba .
Ak kingo kagoyokto ichek Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , kochorjigei Seleukia ; ak kiba eng’ oloto kobun melit agoi Kupro . 
Ak ye kimitei Salamis , koamda ng’olyotab Jehovah eng’ sunagogisiekab Yahudik : ak kimi koboto Johana ne kiboisiechinoti .
Ak kingo kagobun emet komugul ne kiikwen beek agoi koit Papos , konyorji oloto bonin , maotio ne bo lembech , ne Yahudiot , ne kigiguure Bar-Jesu ; 
ne kimi koboto bounindet , Sergio Paulos , chito ne ng’om . Kiguur chichito Barnaba ak Saul koba ole mi inendet , ak kimachei kogas ng’olyotab Jehovah . 
Ago kigirinda ichek Eluma ng’orindet (amu u noto kainennyi ye kiweech) , kigirinda bounindonoto , kocheng’ei komaas kole si manyor kayanet . 
Ago kinyi Tamirmiriet ne Tilil Saul , ne kiguure Paulo , ak kiichiilji kong’ , 
ak kole , Ee inye ne nyiitat ng’alset tugul ak ng’omnatet tugul ne bo kabeetet , inye weritab oindet , inye bunyotab imanda tugul , mebagaktoi imaas ortinwek che lititen che bo Kiptaiyat ? 
Ak keer nguno anyun-o , mi eutab Kiptaiyat baragung’ung’ , ak iegu kipkoratia , si mata igeer asista eng’ betusiek alak . Ak kiibutyi ngunoto mirmirindo ak mesundeito ; ak kiwendot kocheng’at bik che namoti inendet eut . 
Kingogeer anyun bounindet kit ne kayaak , koyan , kokwong’ agobo konetisietab Kiptaiyat .
Kiba anyun Paulo ak che kimi koboto inendet kobun melit eng’ Papos , ak koit Perga eng’ Pampulia : ak kiwa Johana koweektagei Jerusalem kobagakta ichek . 
Ak kingobun ichek Perga , koit Antiokia ne bo Pisidia ; ak kiba sunagogit eng’ betutab sabato , ak koteb ng’ony .
Ak kingobata somanetab Ng’atutiet ak sirutikab maotik koyokto bounikab sunagogit bik koba ole mi ichek , kolenji , Che kitupche , ngotinye ng’olyo age tugul ne imuchi kotoret bichu , omwa . 
Kotonon anyun Paulo , ak koborjine eut , kole , Ogaso okwek bikab Israel , ak okwek che oiywei Jehovah . 
Kilewen Jehovah ne bo bichu Israel kwanisiekyok , ak kotoror bichoto ye ki bunotik eng’ emetab Misri , ak kiimut ichek komong’ eng’ eut ne kim . 
Ak kimuitochi ichek eng’ atebosiekwak eng’ olo bo kenyisiek artam eng’ ong’atet . 
Ak kingo kagong’em bororiosiek tisab eng’ emetab Kanan , kogochi ichek emenywa koek borotet , eng’ olo bo kenyisiek bogol ang’wan ak konom : 
ak kingobata tuguchu kogochi ichek kiruogik agoi Samuel maotiot . 
Ak kingobata kosom laitoriat : ak kiigochi Jehovah ichek Saul weritab Kis eng’ kenyisiek artam , chito ne bo oretab Benjamin . 
Ak kingo kagoisto inendet , kong’eetyi Daudi koek laitoriandenywa ; ne kibaorianji agine kole , Kaanyoru Daudi weritab Jesii , chito ne iboiboi muguleldanyu , ne tun yaei magutikyuk tugul . 
Ak kiimutyi Jehovah Israel Yetindet , Jesu , eng’ keswekab chichito , ko u arorutiet ; 
ye kiga sib koamji Johana bik tugul che bo Israel , kabatisanet ne bo sigunet , ye kitomo konyo inendet . 
Ak ye ki negit koges Johana bandanyi , komwa kole , Olen a ng’o ? Ma a inendet . Ago ogeero , isubwa age , ne manyoljina atiakyi kweonikab kelyekyik .
Che kitupche , lagokab keswek che bo Abraham , ak alak che mi kwenung’wong’ che iywei Jehovah , kagiyokwech achek ng’olyondoni bo yetunet . 
Ichek che menyei Jerusalem , koboto bounikwak , amu kima nai inendet , anan kutuswekab maotik che kisomani eng’ sabato age tugul , kosuldae kutuswechuto kiruoget ne kiiruokyi inendet . 
Ak nganda kimanyor eng’ inendet ng’olyot ne igochin kome , ago kisom ichek Pilato kole , kebar inendet . 
Ak ye kingo kagoges tuguk tugul che kiga kisir agobo inendet , kochoor inendet eng’ ketit , ak konde kererit . 
Ago kiing’eet Jehovah inendet komong’ eng’ che kibek : 
Ak kigeer inendet eng’ betusiek che chang’ ichek che kitogosu koboto inendet kobunu Galili kobwanei Jerusalem , che nguno ko baorinik eng’ bik . 
Ak kiibwok logoiywek che miach che bo arorutiet , ne kigigochi kwanisiekyok , 
ko u ye kigosuldochi Jehovah lagokyok noto , amu kiing’eet Jesu ; ko u ye sirat eng’ Tiendab Kalosunet ne bo aeng’ , kole , I werinnyu , kaasichin rani . 
Ak ko u ye kiing’eet inendet komong’ eng’ che kibek , ma koweekyingei amu inendet kogeny nunet , kimwa ko u ni , kole , Tun agonin kaberuroik che tililen , ak ko bo iman , che bo Daudi . 
Amu kimwa agine eng’ Tiendo age , kole , Matun igochini neng’ung’ Ne Tilil kogeer nunet . 
Amu ye kingo kagoboisiechi Daudi kiruogutikab Jehovah eng’ ibindanyi , konuuch , ak kigitub koboto kwanisiekyik , ak kogeer nunet : 
ago ma keer nunet inendet ne kiing’eet Jehovah . 
Ingonaak anyun eng’ okwek , che kitupche , kele , kimwawok eng’ chichi nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogik : 
ak kiityin imanda eng’ inendet age tugul ne iyani , eng’ tuguk tugul , che koma komuchi koiityok imanda Ng’atutietab Musa . 
Oripge anyun , si manyonjok ne kigimwa eng’ maotik ; kele ,
Ogeero , okwek sasik , okwong’ie , ak olusye ; Amu ayae boisiet eng’ betusiekwok , Boisiet ne magoi oyan matiny , agot ngo mwawok chi .
Ak kingota komandoi ichek , kosom kole , tun ko ta koamji ichek ng’alechato eng’ sabato ne nyonei . 
Ak kingo kagomanda tuiyet eng’ sunagogit , kosub Paulo ak Barnaba che chang’ che bo Yahudik ak che konyiti Jehovah che kiwalak kobunji Yahudik : ye kingong’alaljin ichek , kogiil kole koba tai eng’ mieindab Jehovah .
Ak eng’ sabato ne isubi noto , koyumgei nganaset che negit tugul kole kogas ng’olyotab Jehovah . 
Ago ye kingogeer Yahudik tuiyosiek , koam ng’et kong’ , ak koesio eng’ kimnatet ng’alek che kimwaei Paulo , ak komwa ng’alek che yaachen kochubis . 
Kong’alal anyun Paulo ak Barnaba eng’ nyiganatet , kolen , Konyolu kemwawok korok ng’olyotab Jehovah . Amu ogirindoi , ak oruokyinige okwege ole manyolu onyoru sobondab koigeny , ogeero , kagibe oldab Bororiosiek . 
Amu king’atech Kiptaiyat ko u noto , kole , Kaandein iegu lapkeiyet ne bo Bororiosiek , Si kobiit iegu yetunet agoi tabandab ng’ony .
Ak kingogas Bororiosiek ng’olyondonito , koboiboitu , ak kogonyit ng’olyotab Jehovah : ak koyan tugul che kiga kelewenji sobondab koigeny .
Ak kiyom ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat koronoto tugul . 
Ago kiinde Yahudik ng’alekab chaamset kobogorisiek che konyiti Jehovah ak ko toogunotin , ak bik che eechen che bo nganaset , ak kiing’eet usisiet kous Paulo ak Barnaba , ak koon komanda eng’ kiwotosiekwak .
Ago kilelekyi ichek temburiek che mi kelyekwak , ak kiit Ikonio . 
Ak kinyi alamalyet boiboindo ak Tamirmiriet ne Tilil .
Ak ye kimi Ikonio , koba tuwai agoi sunagogitab Yahudik , ak kong’alal kot koyan tuiyet ne o ne bo Yahudik ak Yunanik . 
Ago kiim Yahudik che ki bistoik sobonwekab Bororiosiek kot kogochi kowech tupchosiek . 
Kitebe oloto anyun betusiek che chang’ ak kong’alali eng’ nyiganatet agobo Kiptaiyat , ne kibaorianji ng’olyotab mieindanyi , ak kogochin koyaak kaborunoik ak kwong’utik eng’ eunekwak . 
Ago kipcheigei tuiyet ne bo nganaset ; ak kinamgei alage ak Yahudik , konamgei alage ak che kiyoktoi .
Ak ye kimachei Bororiosiek ak Yahudik koboto bounikwak kobokyi ichek , kole koyachi ne ya , ak kolach eng’ koik , 
kosib konai , ak kimwechi Lustra ak Derbe , nganasok che bo Lukaonia , ak korotinwek che negite oloto : 
ak kiamda logoiywek che miach eng’ oloto .
Ak kitebyei chito age eng’ Lustra , ne kima ko kimen kelyekyik , ne ki solomwo koboch komi moetab kamet , ne kitomo kowendot . 
Kigas chichoto Paulo kong’alali : ak kingochiilji kong’ inendet chichoto , ak kogeer kole tinyei kayanet ne kimuchi kisoob , 
komwa eng’ kutit ne o kole , Tonon komie eng’ kelyeguk . Ak kitoromben ak kowendot . 
Ak kingogeer tuiyosiek kit ne kayai Paulo , kobolyo eng’ ng’alekab Lukaonia , kole , Kachorjech ge cheptalelisiek eng’ kergeindab bik . 
Ak kiguure Barnaba , Seu ; koguure Paulo , Herme , amu ki ng’alalindet ne o inendet . 
Ak kiget tisiindetab Seu ne kimi hekalunnyi taitab nganaset , tuga ak sinendoik kobwa kurgotik , ak kimachei inendet koboto tuiyosiek kogoito tisieywot .
Ago ye kingogas agobo noto che kiyoktoi Barnaba ak Paulo , kogerer ngoroikwak , ak koruai koba kwenutab tuiyet , koboldos , 
kolen , Murenju , kalya si oyai tuguchu ? Ki bik agachek , che kergei ak okwek , ak kagiibwok logoiywek che miach , si kobiit oweige omete tuguchu matilei kiy ak obwanji Jehovah ne sobei , inendet ne kiyaei kipsengwet ak ng’ony ak nyanjet , ak tugul che mi oloto : 
kibagakyi inendet bororiosiek tugul eng’ ibinwek che kigosiirto , kobendat eng’ ortinwekwak . 
Ago kima tebi buch inendet ama tinyei baoria , amu kiyai ne mie , ak kogonok ropta ne bunu kipsengwet ak betusiekab ruratet , kogochin kobiyong’so mugulelwekwok eng’ amitwogik ak kagasetab ge . 
Ak ki negit kotemene koger tuiyosiek eng’ ng’alechu si mata kogochi tiseiywot .
Ago kibwa Yahudik che kibunu Antiokia ak Ikonia : ak kingo kagolom tuiyosiek , kolach Paulo eng’ koik , ak kochuut komanda eng’ nganaset , kolen kagome . 
Ago ye kitonondos alamalyet ko kayiem inendet , kong’eet , ak kwo nganaset : ak eng’ betut ne kiisubi noto koba Derbe ak Barnaba .
Ak ye kingo kagoamji logoiywek che miach nganasanato , ak ko kagoyai che chang’ koek alamalyet , koweektagei koba Lustra , ak Ikonia , agoi Antiokia , 
kogimitoti sobonwekab alamalyet , kogiili koba tai eng’ kayanet , ak kolenji , kanyol keit bounatetab Jehovah eng’ nyalilwogik che chang’ . 
Ak kingo kagolewenji ichek boisiek eng’ kaniset age tugul , ak kosa eng’ karugutetab ge , konde ichek eutab Kiptaiyat , ne kiga koyan .
Ak kibun Pisidia , ak koit Pampulia . 
Ak kingo kagoamda ng’olyot eng’ Perga , kochortagei Atalia ; 
ak kibun melit eng’ oloto agoi Antiokia , oloto ole kigindae ichek mieindab Jehovah agobo boisiet ne kiga koyai kosulda .
Ak kingo kagobwa , koyum kaniset komugul , komwachi tuguk tugul che kiga koyai Jehovah eng’ ichek , ak ko u ye kiga koyatyi Bororiosiek kurget ne bo kayanet . 
Ak kitebi betusiek che chang’ koboto alamalyet .
Ak kichorgei bik alak che kibunu Judea ak konet tupchosiek , kole , Ngot ko magimuratanak ko u biteetab Musa , ko momuchi onyoru sorunet . 
Ak ye kingo kagotiiyo Paulo ak Barnaba mising’ ak koteebegei mising’ koboto ichek , kolewen tupchosiek Paulo ak Barnaba , ak alak eng’ ichek , kotogosta koba Jerusalem ole mi che kiyoktoi ak boisiek agobo ng’olyondonito .
Ak kingo kagoyomis anyun ichek kaniset eng’ bandanywa , kobun Poinike ak Samaria , komwaitaati agobo che kigowalogis koyan Jehovah eng’ Bororiosiek : ak kiigochi ng’olyondonoto tupchosiek tugul boiboiyet ne o . 
Ak kingo kagoit Jerusalem , kotaach ichek kaniset ak che kiyoktoi ak boisiek , ak komwachi ichek tuguk tugul che kiga koyai Jehovah koboto icheget . 
Ago kitononso alak eng’ kasubikab Parisaik che iyanotin , kole , Kanyol kimuratan ichek , ak keng’at ichek korib Ng’atutietab Musa .
Ak kiiyumgei che kiyoktoi ak boisiek si kobiit kogeer ole teptoi ng’olyondonito . 
Ak kingo kagoteebegei mising’ , kotonon Petero ak komwachi ichek , kole , Che kitupche , ongen okwek ole kigolewen Jehovah eng’ kwenung’wong’ koboch ye bo ui , kole , kogas Bororiosiek ng’olyot ne bo logoiywek che miach eng’ kutinnyu , ak koyan . 
Ak kibaorianji ichek Jehovah ne ingen mugulelwekab bik , kogochi ichek Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ko u ye kigonech ; 
ak kima ibesiech ak icheget , ye kiitilili mugulelwekwak eng’ kayanet . 
Kalya nguno anyun si otiem Jehovah kot onde chogit kaatitab alamalyet , ne kima imuch koib kwanisiekyok anan achek ? 
Ago kiyani kele kisoruech eng’ mieindab Kiptaiyat Jesu , ko u ye kisoru agichek .
Kosisyo anyun tuiyet komugul ; ak koepchi it Barnaba ak Paulo kotetyin ichek kaborunoik ak kwong’utik che kiga koyai Jehovah eng’ ichek eng’ kwenutab Bororiosiek . 
Ak kingo kagosisyo , kowol Jakobo , kole , Che kitupche , ogaso . 
Kagomwa Simion ko u ye kirutochi Jehovah Bororiosiek eng’ tai , si kobiit kolewenji kainennyi bik eng’ ichek . 
Ak kanamgei nito ak ng’alekab maotik ; ko u ye sirat , kole , 
Ye ibata tuguchu aweege , Ak ateech kogeny gotab Daudi , ne kigolul ; Ak ateech kogeny komoswek che kigolulyo , Ak alum kotonon : 
Si kocheng’ bik che ng’etunotin Kiptaiyat , Ak Bororiosiek tugul che kiguurtoe kainennyu . 
Mwaei Kiptaiyat , ne yaei tuguchu si konaak koboch taunetab ng’ony .
Noto anyun , atile kiruoget ko u ni ale , amata kinyalil achek ichek che bo Bororiosiek che bwanjin Jehovah ; 
ago ongesirji ichek , kelenji kotabanegei muruonindab kanamonik , ak sokset , ak ne bo tuguk che kagiget , ak korotik . 
Amu kitinyei Musa koboch ibinwek che bo keny eng’ nganasok tugul , icheget che amdoi agobo inendet , che kisomani eng’ sunagogisiek eng’ sabato age tugul .
Kogeer anyun che kiyoktoi ak boisiek , koboto kaniset komugul , kole mie kolewen bik alak eng’ ichek , ak koyokto koba Antiokia koboto Paulo ak Barnaba ; choto ko Judas ne kigiguure Barsaba , ak Sila , bik che eechen eng’ tupchosiek : 
ak kisir ko u ni ak koyoktoe ichek , Kisirjini achek che kiyoktoi ak tupchosiek che boisiek , tupchosiek che bo Bororiosiek che mi Antiokia ak Suria ak Kilikia , kigatok : 
amu kogegas kele , inyalilok eng’ ng’alek bik alak che kibunei kwenunnyo , kong’emei sobonwekwok ; bik che kima king’at ko u noto ; 
kagigeer kele mie eng’ achek , che kagechamnyechi , kelewen bik ak kiyokwok koboto chamanikyok Barnaba ak Paulo , 
bik che kigogoito sobonwekwak amu kainetab Kiptaiyandennyo Jesu Kristo . 
Kagiyogu anyun Juda ak Sila , si komwawok icheget agichek tuguchuto eng’ kutuswekwak . 
Amu kigeere kele mie eng’ Tamirmiriet ne Tilil , ak eng’ achek kele , magigesenjok milet ne nyigis kosiir tuguchu nyolu ; 
kele otabanege tuguk che kieng’jin kanamonik , ak korotik , ak banyekab che kagiget , ak sokset ; ngotabanege choto , komieitu eng’ okwek . Saisere .
Ye kingo kagiyokto koba anyun , kochortagei koba Antiokia ; ak kingo kagoyum tuiyet , kogochi baruet . 
Ak kingo kagosoman koboiboitu agobo kagaigaet . 
Ak kiigiil Juda ak Sila , tupchosiek eng’ ng’alek che chang’ , ak kogimit amu ki maotik agichek . 
Ak kingo kagotebe oloto betusiek alak , kounda tupchosiek ichek eng’ kalyet koba ole mi ichek che kiiyogu . 
Ago kitebe Paulo ak Barnaba Antiokia , koneti ak koamdoi ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat , koboto bik alak che chang’ agichek .
Ak kingobata betusiek alak kolenji Paulo Barnaba , Ingeweege nguno kerutochi tupchosiek eng’ nganaset age tugul ole kigeamdaate ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat , ak kegeer ole teptoi . 
Ak kimachei Barnaba mising’ komut Johana , ne kigiguure Mariko , koba tugul . 
Ago kiibwat Paulo kole , ma mie kimut inendet ne kiga kobagakta ichek eng’ Pampulia , ama cham koba boisiet koboto ichek . 
Ak king’eetyo ng’alek che koromen , kot kopcheigei ichegei , ak kiimut Barnaba Mariko , ak kobun melit agoi Kupro ; 
ago kilewen Paulo Sila , ak koba, ko kagonde tupchosiek ichek mieindab Kiptaiyat . 
Ak kobun Suria ak Kilikia , kogimitoti kanisosiek .
Ak kinyo agine Derbe ak Lustra : ak ogeero , kimi age ne bo alamalyet oloto , ne kigiguure Timoteo , weritab Chebyahudiot ne kiiyani ; ago ki Yunanindet kwandanyi . 
Kibaorianjin inendet tupchosiek che kimi Lustra ak Ikonio kole mie . 
Kimachei Paulo chichito koba tuwai ; ak kiimut inendet ak komuratan amu Yahudik che kimi komoswechoto : amu kiingen tugul kole Yunanindet kwandanyi . 
Ak ye kibendi bandanywa kobunoti nganasok kogochi ichek ng’atutik , che kiga ng’at che kiyoktoi ak boisiek che kimi Jerusalem , si korib . 
Kigigimit anyun kanisosiek eng’ kayanet , ak kotesak koitenywa betut age tugul .
Kiba anyun kobun koret ne bo Prugia ak Galatia , ko kagoete ichek Tamirmiriet ne Tilil komwaita ng’olyot eng’ Asia ; 
ak ye kingotorjigei Musia , kotiem koba Bitunia ; ago ma chamji ichek Tamirmirietab Jesu ; 
ak kingosiir Musia , kochortagei Troa . 
Kinyonji anyun ng’ang’utiet Paulo kemoi ; kimi chitab Makedonia ne kitononi , kogoigoi inendet , kolen , Long’u Makedonia , nyo toretech . 
Ak ye kingo kagogeer ng’ang’utiet , eng’ sainato kemach kebe Makedonia , ko kagenai kele kogoguurech Jehovah si kobiit keamji ichek logoiywek che miach .
Kigibun anyun melit kebunu Troa , kitorjige Samotrake , ak betut ne kiisubi noto keit Neapoli : 
ak keng’eetyo oloto kebe Pilipi , ne nganasetab Makedonia , ne ki toogunot eng’ emonoto , ne kiuchi Romanik : ak kigitebe nganasanato betusiek alak . 
Ak eng’ betutab sabato kemandae ormarichet kebe ole negite ainet , ole kigilen oldab saet ; ak kigiteb ng’ony ak keng’alalji kobogorisiek che kiga tuiyo . 
Ak kigasech kobogoriot age , ne kigiguure Ludia , aldaindetab ngoroik che arusen ne birir , ne bo nganaset ne kiguure Tuatera , ne kiilosu Jehovah : ne kiyat Kiptaiyat muguleldanyi , si koepchi it tuguk che kimwaei Paulo . 
Ak ye kiga kibatisan inendet , ak bikab gonnyi , kogaigaech , kole , Ngo kaogeer ole ayani Kiptaiyat , obwa gonnyu , ak otebi . Ak kibirjech kebe .
Ak ye kigibendi oldab saet , kotuiyenech chepto ne kitinyei tamirmiriet ne ng’orsei ne kiipchi kiptainikyik tuguk che chang’ amu ng’orset . 
Kiisubot Paulo kebendi tugul , ak komwaei eng’ kutit ne o , kolen , Bichu ko otwogikab Jehovah ne Toror Mising’ , che mwawok oretab yetunet . 
Ak kiyai inendet ko u noto eng’ betusiek che chang’ . Ago kiarogen Paulo mising’ , ak kowelelgei ak kolenji tamirmirionoto , Kang’atin eng’ kainetab Jesu Kristo ale , mong’u eng’ inendet . Ak kimong’ eng’ sainato .
Ago kingogeer kiptainikyik kole kagobet kamang’unetab keljinenywa , konam Paulo ak Sila , ak kochuut koba taitab bounik eng’ oldab aldaisiet , 
ak kingo kagomut ichek kobwa taitab kiruogik , komwa kole , Inyalili bichu nganasennyo mising’ , ago icheget ko Yahudik , 
ak ineti bitonwek che ma chamdaat eng’ ng’atutik ketaach , anan kisub , amu achek ko ki Romanik . 
Ak king’eet tuiyet kibagenge kobokyi ichek : ak kogerer kiruogik ngoroikab bichoto , ak kong’at kebir eng’ kirokwek . 
Ak kingo kagobir ichek mising’ , kotoorji korgoret , ak kong’at ribindetab korgoret korib komie : 
ak kingo kagonyor ng’atutiet ne u noto , kotoorji ichek got ne bo orit , ak koratyi kelyekwak temeleiywek .
Ago kisaei Paulo ak Sila ak kotienjin Jehovah tienwogik olo bo kemoi kwen , ak kiepchin it ichek kimonjororinik ; 
ak kibotan emet mising’ eng’ sainato , kot kotumdumgei lumeiywekab korgoret : ak eng’ sainato koyatogis kurgotik tugul ; ak kiitiagogis tuguk che kigirate chi tugul . 
Ak kingosiir eng’ ruondo ribindetab korgoret , ak kogeer kurgotikab korgoret ko yatotin , kong’us rotwennyi bo chok , ak ki negit kobargei , kolen kagochililyo kimonjororinik . 
Ago kimwa Paulo eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Ameyachige kiy ne ya : amu kimi yu achek tugul .
Ak kiguur keib taisiek , ak kotoromben kwo orit , ak kiibutyi kelyekab Paulo ak Sila kobotananu eng’ kaiyweisiet , 
ak kiimut komong’ sang’ , ak kole , Kiptainichu , ayai nee si kesorua ? 
Kolenji , Iyan Kiptaiyat Jesu , si kesorun , inye ak gong’ung’ . 
Ak kimwachi inendet ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat , koboto tugul che kimi gonnyi . 
Ak kiimut ichek sainato bo kemoi , ak kounji birutikwak ; ak kigibatisan inendet ak bikyik eng’ sainato . 
Ak kiimut koba gonnyi ak kogochi amitwogik , ak kiboiboitu mising’ , koboto gonnyi tugul , amu kagoyan Jehovah .
Ak ye kingoeech , koyokto kiruogik kiptainikab askarik , kole , Ounde bicho koba . 
Ak kimwachi ribindetab korgoret Paulo ng’alechato , kole , Kagoyok kiruogik kole keundak obe : omong’u anyun ak obe eng’ kalyet . 
Ago kilenji Paulo ichek , Kagobirech eng’ taitab bik , ama kiruokwech , achek bik che ki Romanik , ak kogotoorjech korgoret ; ak nguno komachei koonech eng’ ung’ot ? Achicha , ma u noto ; ago ingobwa icheget komutech kemande . 
Ak kimwachi kiptainikab askarik ng’alechuto kiruogik : ak kiiywei , kingogas kole icheget ko Romanik : 
ak kibwa kogaigai ichek ; ak kingo kagomut ichek kobwa sang’ , kosom , kolenji , Oba eng’ nganaset . 
Ak kimanda eng’ korgoret , ak kiba agoi gotab Ludia : ak kingo kagogeer tupchosiek , kogaigai ichek , ak koba .
Ak kingo kagobun Ampipoli ak Apolonia , koit Tesalonike , ole kimi sunagogitab Yahudik : 
ak kiwa Paulo ole mi ichek , ko u ye kicham koyaei , ak kong’alal koboto bichoto eng’ sabatosiek somok eng’ sirutik , 
kong’ang’jin ak koborjin komie kole kiga nyolji Kristo konyalil , ak kong’eet kogeny eng’ che kibek ; ak kole Jesu nito aamwok , ko Kristo . 
Kiiyan anyun alage eng’ ichek , ak konamgei ak Paulo ak Sila ; ak tuiyet ne o ne bo Yunanik che kigonyiti Jehovah , ak che chang’ eng’ kobogorisiek che toogunotin .
Ago ye kingoam ng’etkonda Yahudik , konamgei ak bik che yaachen che matilei kiy , ak kiiyum tuiyet , ak kong’eet ichek bolatet eng’ nganaset ; ak kibut gotab Jason , komachei kole komut ichek sang’ koba ole mi bik . 
Ak ye kimata konyor , kochuut Jason ak tupchosiek alak koba taitab kiruogikab nganaset , koboldos , kolen , Kagobwa oli kogeny bichu kogowal ng’ony ; 
bik che kagotaach Jason : ak yaei bichuto tugul , tuguk che etei ng’atutikab Kaisari , komwaei kolen mitei laitoriat age , ne inendet ko Jesu . 
Ak ye kingogas tuguchuto , koiim tuiyet ak kiruogikab nganaset . 
Ak kingo kagoname Jason ak bik alak , tuguk , kounda koba .
Ak ne matianit koyokto tupchosiek Paulo ak Sila kemoi koba Berea : ak kingoit oloto , koba sunagogitab Yahudik . 
Ak ki miachen bichu kosiir choto bo Tesalonike , amu kitaach ng’olyot ak kocham mising’ , kosiachi sirutik betut age tugul , si kobiit konai ngo iman tuguchu . 
Kiiyan anyun che chang’ eng’ icheget ; ak kobogorisiek che bo Yunanik che toogunotin , ak murenik che chang’ .
Ago kingonai Yahudik che bo Tesalonike kole , amdoi Paulo ng’olyotab Jehovah eng’ Berea agine , koba oloto agine , ak kowas ak konyalil tuiyosiek . 
Koyokto anyun ngunoto tupchosiek Paulo kot koit nyanjet : ak kita kotebi eng’ oloto Sila ak Timoteo . 
Ago icheget che kiimuti Paulo ko kiimut agoi Atene : ak kingotaach ng’atutiet koipchi Sila ak Timoteo kole koba ole mi inendet kochok , koba anyun .
Ak kingota kogeni Paulo ichek eng’ Atene , koiimak tamirmiriennyi eng’ orinnyi , ye kingogeer nganaset ko nyiitat kanamonik . 
Kong’alal anyun eng’ sunagogit koboto Yahudik ak bik che konyiti Jehovah , ak eng’ oldab aldaisiet eng’ betut age tugul koboto che kituitos ak inendet . 
Ak kituiyo koboto inendet alak che bo ng’omotikab Epikurio ak Stoiko . Ak kole alak , Mwaei nee kipchang’alaini ? Kole alak , U kabartaindet ne bo cheptalelisiek che ter : amu kiamdoi Jesu ak ng’eetyet . 
Ak konam inendet , ak komut kwo Areopago , kole , Tos kimuchi kenai kele nee konetisioni leel , imwae ? 
Amu keipchi itikyok tuguk alak che leelach : noto anyun kimache kenai kit ne iboru tuguchuto . 
(Ak kima kotinyei bik tugul che bo Atene , ak toek che kimi oloto , boroindo ne bo kiy age kobate komwa anan kogas ng’al che too .)
Ak kitonon Paulo eng’ kwenutab Areopago , ak kole , Okwek bikab Atene , kaageer ale eng’ tuguk tugul ogiilige mising’ eng’ sautik . 
Amu ye kiasiirtoi , ak ageer tuguk che osae , anyoru agine kapkorosut ne tinyei sirutichu , BO CHEPTALELIT NE MANAEI CHI . Noto anyun ne osae amongen , aboruok anyun nito . 
Mamenyei hekalusiek che kigiyae eunek Jehovah ne kiyai ng’ony ak tuguk tugul che mitei oloto , amu inendet ko Kiptaiyatab kipsengwet ak ng’ony . 
Ama kiboisiechin eng’ eunekab bik , ko u ne banani kiy , amu inendet ne igochin tugul sobondo , ak kabuset , ak tuguk tugul ; 
ak kiyai eng’ chito agenge bororiet age tugul ne bo bik si komeny ng’ony komugul , ko kagoborji kenyisiek che kiging’at , ak kiwotosiekab meng’otenywa ; 
si kobiit kocheng’ Jehovah , komang’u kole tamangab kotamdamat , ak konyor inendet , nganda ma loo eng’ age tugul eng’ achek : 
amu kisoptosi eng’ inendet , ak kebendoti , ak kemi ; ko u ye kigomwa alage eng’ sirikwok che bo ng’alek che kergei ak tienwogikab kalosunet , kole , Amu ki lagokyik ak achek . 
Ngo ki lagokab Jehovah anyun , ko manyoljech kibwat kele kergei Jehovah ak tahabu , anan feda , anan koita , che kigiyai eng’ musoknatet ak eng’ ng’omnatetab bik . 
Kima mage kiy anyun Jehovah betusiek che kima komi naet ; ago kang’at nguno kole kosik bik tugul eng’ komosta age tugul : 
amu kigochob betut , ne tun iruokyine ng’ony eng’ imanda eng’ chichoto kigonde ; ak kigoborji komie bik tugul agobo noto , amu kiing’eet inendet komong’ eng’ che kibek .
Ye kingogas anyun agobo ng’eetyetab che kibek , kochombil alage ; ago kile alak , Ta kegasun nito betut age . 
Kimanda anyun Paulo eng’ kwenunywa .  
Ago kinamgei bik alak ak inendet , ak koyan ; ki age eng’ icheget Dionusio Areopagindet , ak kobogoriot ne kiguure Damaris , ak alak che kimi koboto icheget .
Kingobata tuguchu kwo Paulo eng’ Atene , ak koit Korinto . 
Ak kinyor Yahudiot age ne kiguure Akula , chito ne bo Ponto , ne kita kobunu Italia , koboto osotiondennyi Prisila , amu kiga ng’at Klaudio kole koba Yahudik tugul eng’ Rom : ak kinyo ole mi ichek ; 
amu ki kergei boisiennyi ak nenywa , kotebi anyun koboto ichek , ak kobois tugul ; amu ki nabik che bo emaisiek icheget . 
Ak king’alali eng’ sunagogit sabato age tugul , ak kochuutu Yahudik ak Yunanik .
Ago ye kingochorgei Sila ak Timoteo kobunu Makedonia , konyonji Paulo kachirjiret ne bo ng’olyot , kobaorianjin Yahudik kole Jesu ko Kristo . 
Ak ye kingogirindagei ak inendet , ak komwa ng’alek kochubis , koleglekta ngoriennyi , ak kolenji , Ingotebi korotikwok eng’ metowekwok ; a tilil ane : koboch nguno ko kawe oldab Bororiosiek . 
Ak kiwa eng’ oloto , ak kwo gotab chito age ne kiguure Tito Justo , chito ne kiilosu Jehovah , ne kinamegei gonnyi ak sunagogit . 
Ak kiiyan Krispo Kiptaiyat , ne ki bounindetab sunagogit , koboto gonnyi tugul ; ak kingogas che chang’ che bo Korintoek , koyan , ak kigibatisan .
Ak kilenji Kiptaiyat Paulo kemoi eng’ ng’ang’utiet , Ameiywei , ago ng’alal inye , amat isis : 
amu ami koboten , ama mi chi ne twain koyaun ne ya : amu atinye bik che chang’ eng’ nganasani . 
Ak kimeny oloto kenyit agenge ak arawek lo , koneti ng’olyotab Jehovah eng’ kwenunywa .
Ago ye kingo kiruogindetab Akayo Galio , kong’eetyi Yahudik Paulo eng’ maget agenge , ak komut inendet kwo taitab ng’echeretab kiruoget , 
kole , Ichuuti chichi bik kole kolos Jehovah eng’ oret ne etei Ng’atutiet . 
Ago ye kimachei Paulo kotwek , kolenji Galio Yahudik , Okwek Yahudichu , nda bo yaitio ng’alechu iman , anan ko bo chalwok ne ya , ta nyolu agaswok : 
ago ngo teebutik agobo ng’alek ak kainaik ak ng’atutieng’wong’ okweget , oyai okwege ; mamache aek kiruogindetab ng’alechuto . 
Ak kion ichek koba eng’ oldab ng’echeretab kiruoget . 
Ak kinam tugul Sostene , bounindetab sunagogit , ak kobir inendet eng’ taitab ng’echeranato bo kiruoget . Ak kima mage kiy Galio ng’alechato tugul .
Ak kingobata ni , ak ko kagotebi Paulo betusiek che chang’ , kobagakta inendet tupchosiek kobun melit kwo Suria , koboto Prisila ak Akula ; ye kiga kocher metit eng’ Kenkrea : amu kiga koarorta kiy eng’ kayosiet . 
Ak kiit Epeso ak kobagakta ichek eng’ oloto : ago kiwa inendet sunagogit , ak kong’alal ak Yahudik . 
Ak kingomwachi kole , kota kotebi ak ichek , koma kocham ; 
ago kingobagaktoi ichek , komwa kole , Aweekyinoge kogeny ngo cham Jehovah , ak kibun melit kwo Epeso .
Ak ye kingo kagolanda Kaisaria , kotogosta kwo kogat kaniset , ak kochortagei kwo Antiokia . 
Ak kingo kagotebi eng’ oloto betusiek alak , kwo kobunot koret ne bo Galatia ak ne bo Prugia , ko u ye rubegei , kogimitoti alamalaik tugul .
Ak kinyo Epeso Yahudiot age , ne keguure Apolo , ne bo Aleksandria , chito ne ng’om ; ak ki kim eng’ sirutik . 
Kiga kinet chichito oretab Kiptaiyat ; ak amu kitinyei kagiiletab ge eng’ tamirmiriennyi , kong’alal ak konet komie ng’alek agobo Jesu , kongen kabatisanetab Johana kityo : 
ak kitoi kong’alal eng’ nyiganatet eng’ sunagogit . Ago ye kingogas Prisila ak Akula , komut inendet kwo oldanywa , ak koborji inendet oretab Jehovah komie kosiir . 
Ak ye kimachei kolanda kwo Akaya , kogimit tupchosiek inendet , ak kosirji alamalyet kole kotaach inendet : ak ye kingo kagoit , kotoret inendet , ichek mising’ che kiga koyan eng’ mieindo : 
amu kiiguiyechi Yahudik komie eng’ kimnatet , eng’ taitab bik , koborjin eng’ sirutik kole Jesu ko Kristo .
Ak ye kita komi Apolo Korinto , ko kagobun Paulo emet kwen , koit Epeso , ak konyor alamalyet : 
ak kilenji ichek , Tos kiotaach Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ye kingoyan ? Kolenji , Achicha , tomo agot kegas ngo mitei Tamirmiriet ne Tilil . 
Ak kilenji , Kigibatisanjok nee anyun ? Ak kile , Kigibatisanjech kabatisanetab Johana . 
Kole Paulo , Kiibatisanis Johana eng’ kabatisanetab sigunet , kolenjin bik kanyol koyan inendet ne isubu inendet , noto ko Jesu . 
Ak ye kingogas nito , kibatisan eng’ kainetab Kiptaiyat Jesu . 
Ak ye kingo kagogonoor Paulo eunekyik icheget , konyonji anyun Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ichek ; ak king’alal eng’ kutuswek che terotin , ak koamda . 
Ak ki olo bo taman ak aeng’ bichoto tugul .
Ak kiwa sunagogit orit , ak kong’alal eng’ nyiganatet eng’ arawek somok , kong’alali ak kolomei agobo tuguk che bo bounatetab Jehovah . 
Ago ye kingouuegitu mugulelwekab alak ak kobistoe , ak komwaei ne ya agobo Oranato eng’ taitab tuiyet , kwo eng’ ole mi , ak kotaban alamalyet , kong’alaljin betut age tugul eng’ skulitab Turano . 
Kiyaak ko u noto eng’ kenyisiek aeng’ ; kot kogas ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat tugul che kimenyei Asia , Yahudik koboto Yunanik .
Ak kiyai Jehovah boisionikab kimnatet che ter eng’ eunekab Paulo : 
kot keipchi che miandos kitambaok ak angok che kiga kotiiny bortanyi , ak kiistogei mainwek eng’ bichoto , ak kimanda tamirmirik che yaachen eng’ ichek . 
Ak kitoi Yahudik alage che kiombenoti , che kilen koon oik , komwa kainetab Kiptaiyat Jesu eng’ icheget che kitinyei tamirmirik che yaachen , kolen , Ayosiewok eng’ Jesu ne amdoi Paulo . 
Ak kimi werik tisabu che bo Skeba , inendet Yahudiot , tisiindet ne o , che kiyai ng’olyondonito . 
Ak kiwolji tamirmiriet ne ya ichek , kolenji , Angen Jesu , ak angen Paulo : ago okwek ko o ng’o ? 
Ak kitorombenji chichoto kitinyei tamirmiriet ne ya ichek , ak konenet ichek , ak koterter , kot komwei komanda eng’ goyoto ach ngor ko kagiguoten . 
Ak kinaak nito eng’ tugul , Yahudik koboto Yunanik , che kimenyei Epeso ; ak kinyor kaiyweisiet ichek tugul , ak kinyor teegisto kainetab Kiptaiyat Jesu . 
Kibwa agichek che chang’ che kiiyan , kong’anyei , ak kobortoi boisionikwak . 
Ak kiib bukuisiekwak bik che chang’ eng’ ichek che kiyaei ng’orset , ak kobeel eng’ taitab bichoto tugul : ak kiit kamanutienywa , konyor kole kiitei fedaisiek elfusiek konom . 
Kotesak ko u noto anyun ng’olyotab Kiptaiyat eng’ kimnatet ak koterter .
Kingobata anyun tuguchuto , komach Paulo eng’ tamirmiriennyi kwo Jerusalem , ko kagobun Makedonia ak Akaya , kolen , Ye kaawe oloto , ko kanyol ageer Rom agine . 
Ye kingo kagoyokto aeng’ eng’ ichek che kiboisiechin inendet koba Makedonia , Timoteo ak Erasto , kota kotebi inendet eng’ Asia ne matia .
Ak king’eet bolatet ne o eng’ betusiechoto agobo Oranato ; 
amu chito age ne kiguure Demetrio , kitang’indet ne bo feda , ne kiitanyi kanamonik che bo feda che bo Artemi , ne kiipchin tuguk che chang’ kitang’ik ; 
che kiiyum kibagenge koboto bik che kitinyei boisiet ne u noto , ak kolenji , Murenju , ongen okwek ole , bunu magornatennyo boisioni . 
Ak ogeere ak ogase ole , ma eng’ Epeso kityo , ago negit Asia tugul , kagochuut bik che chang’ Paulo-inito , ak koweechi , kolenjin , choto kigiyae eunek ko ma cheptalelisiek : 
ak ma kele kityo biitu bichiindab sasisiet ne kisasei boisiennyo ; ago kiiti kele ma kiy hekalutab cheptalelit ne o ne kobogoriot Artemi , ak keistoe inendet teegistannyi , ne koilosu Asia tugul koboto ng’ony .
Ak ye kingogas nito , konerekso inne , ak kobolyo , kole , O Artemi ne bo Epesoek . 
Ak konyi anyun nganaset bolatet : ak koruai kibagenge oldab ureriet , ko kagonam Gaio ak Aristarko , bikab Makedonia , che kibendoti ak Paulo . 
Ak ye kimachei kwo Paulo orit ole mi bik , ko ma kochamji alamalyet . 
Ak kiiyokto ng’olyot bik alage che eechen che bo Asia , amu ki choronokyik , si mat kogoitogei kwo oldab ureriet orit . 
Kiboldos anyun alage , komwaei ni , komwaei alage kit age : amu kibiit bolatet eng’ tuiyet ; ak kima kongen che chang’ kit ne kiigochi kotuiyo . 
Ak kiimut Aleksandro komong’ eng’ tuiyet , kogoito Yahudik inendet . Ak kiiborji Aleksandro bichoto eng’ eut , ak kimachei kosorgei eng’ bichoto . 
Ago ye kingonai kole inendet ko Yahudiot , kobolyo tugul eng’ kutit agenge , eng’ olo bo saisiek aeng’ , kolen , O Artemi ne bo Epesoek . 
Ak kingo kagomwachi sirindetab nganaset tuiyet kosisyo , kole , Okwek bikab Epeso , tos mi ng’o ne maingen kole nganasetab Epesoek ko ribindetab hekalutab Artemi ne o , ak kanamwet ne kiibut kobunu barak ? 
Ak ngo magimuchi ketiiyo agobo tuguchu , ko kanyol osisye , mat osartae ng’olyo . 
Amu kaomutu bichu , che ma rebikab hekalusiek ama chubei cheptalelinnyo ne kobogorio . 
Ngo tinyei anyun Demetrio ak musogik che mi koboto inendet , ng’olyo agobo chi , ko yatotin kapkiruogutik , ak mitei bounik: ingoruokyin anyun ichegei . 
Ago ngocheng’ okwek ng’olyo agobo tuguk alak , ko tun kilititi eng’ tuiyet ne cham komi . 
Amu mi bichiindo ne tos kiruokwech agobo bolatet ne bo rani , amu mami kito ne bo : ak magimuchi ketetu kiy agobo tuiyoni . 
Ak kingo kagomwa ko u noto , komwachi tuiyet koba .
Ak kingobata bolatet , ko kagoyokto Paulo alamalyet kobwa ak kogimit ichek , koyomisgei , si kwo Makedonia . 
Ak kingo kagobun komoswechoto , ko kagogimit ichek eng’ ng’alek che chang’ , koit emetab Yunanik . 
Ak kingo kagotebe oloto arawek somok , kochob Yahudik ng’alek eng’ ung’ot agobo inendet , ye kimachei kobun melit kwo Suria , komachei kole koweegegei oretab Makedonia . 
Ak kiba koboto inendet agoi Asia Sopatro ne bo Berea , ne bo gab Puro ; ak che bo Tesalonikek Aristarko ak Sekundo ; ak Gaio ne bo Derbe , ak Timoteo ; ak Tukiko ak Tropimo che bo Asia . 
Ago kiga kondo chuto , ak kiigenech eng’ Troa . 
Ak kigibun melit eng’ Pilipi ko kagobata betusiekab makatiat ne ma kinde mermerek , ak keit ole mi ichek eng’ Troa eng’ betusiek mut ; ole kigitebe eng’ betusiek tisab .
Ak eng’ betutab tai ne bo wigit ye kiga kiyumge si kebutul makatiat , koamji Paulo ichek , ye kimachei kwo eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ ; kong’alal koek keny agoi kemoi kwen . 
Ak kimi taisiek che chang’ eng’ got ne bo barak , ole kiga kiyumjige . 
Ak kitebe tirisiet neranet age ne kigiguure Eutuko ak kibirto met ; ak kita koamji Paulo koek keny , ak kingobirto met , kotururtogei kong’eete got ne bo somok , ak kigisut ko kagome . 
Ak kichortagei Paulo , ak koitaegei inendet , ak kosuube eunekyik , komwa kole , Moiimge ; amu ta kosobei . 
Ak kingotogosta , ak kobutul makatiat , ak koam , ak kong’alal keny koboto ichek , agoi koeech , kwo anyun . 
Ak kiimut nerananato ko kagosob , ak kinyor kagaigaet ne o .
Ago kigindoi achek kebe melit , kebe Asos , amu kigimache kimut Paulo eng’ oloto : amu kiga kong’at inendet ko u noto , komach inendet kole kobun keldo . 
Ak ye kingetuiye ak inendet eng’ Asos , kimut inendet konyo melit , ak keit Mitulene . 
Ak kigibe eng’ oloto kebun melit , keit Kio eng’ betut ne bo tai ; ak betut ne bo aeng’ keit Samo ; ak betut ne bo somok keit Mileto . 
Amu kiga kobegechi Paulo kwo kosiirtoe Epeso eng’ melit , si ma igagei eng’ Asia ; amu kiigirgiri , kole tamangab koit Jerusalem eng’ betutab Pentekost .
Ak kiiyokto eng’ Mileto keguur boisiekab kaniset eng’ Epeso . 
Ak ye kingobwa ole mi inendet , kolenji , Ongen okweget koboch betut ne bo tai ye kingatau atiech Asia , ole kiateptoi kobotok tugul , 
aboisiechini Kiptaiyat eng’ kaming’inetab ge tugul , ak eng’ beekab kong’ , ak eng’ tiemisiosiek che kibwanja eng’ chobutik che bo ung’ot che bo Yahudik ; 
ko u ye kima ariny amwawok kiy age tugul ne imuchi kotoretok , ak anetak eng’ taitab bik , ak ang’eete got age agoi got age , 
abaorianjini Yahudik koboto Yunanik sigunet eng’ taitab Jehovah ak kayanet eng’ Kiptaiyandennyo Jesu Kristo . 
Ak ogeer anyun , nguno , awendi Jerusalem korata tamirmiriet , amangen tuguk che bwanjina eng’ oloto : 
kobate kityo baorianjina Tamirmiriet ne Tilil eng’ nganaset age tugul , kolen , igena ratisiosiek ak nyalilwogik . 
Ago maiiti sobondanyu ale kiy ne achame kot , si kobiit ages bandanyu , ak boisiet ne kiataach eng’ Kiptaiyat Jesu , abaorianji logoiywek che miach che bo mieindab Jehovah .
Ak nguno anyun , ogeero , angen ale okwek tugul che kiaamdaate bounatetab Jehovah kwenung’wong’ , koma ogeere togennyu kogeny . 
Abaoriani anyun eng’ taing’wong’ betuni , ale , a tilil eng’ korotikab bik tugul . 
Amu ma ariny amwawok magutik tugul che bo Jehovah . 
Oripge anyun okweget , koboto akwet tugul , ne kigonok Tamirmiriet ne Tilil oegu ribik , obai kanisetab Jehovah , ne kiale korotikyik . 
Angen ale ye kaawe komong’jok suik che koromen , ama rire akwet : 
ak tun ng’eetos alage eng’ kwenung’wong’ komwaei ng’alek che imaasi bich , si kochuut alamalyet kosub ichek . 
Oripse anyun , ak obwat ole ma abagakte atigon chi age tugul eng’ beekab kong’ eng’ kenyisiek somok kemoi ak bet .
Ara anyun , kabagakyok nguno eutab Jehovah , ak ng’olyotab mieindanyi , ne imuchi koteechak , ak kogonok borotet koboto ichek tugul che kitilili . 
Ma agase miat feda che bo chi age tugul , anan tahabu , anan ngoroik . 
Ongen okwek ole kibois eunechu agobo tuguk che kianyalili , ak agobo ichek che kimi kobota . 
Kiagonok kaborunet eng’ tuguk tugul , ale ye oboisiei ko nyolu otoret che matinyei kimnatet , ak obwati ng’alekab Kiptaiyat Jesu , ko u ye kimwa inendet kole , Tinyei boiboiyet kagoitoet kosiir taaget .
Ak kingo kagomwa ko u noto , kogutuny , kosa koboto ichek tugul . 
Ak kiririo ichek tugul mising’ , ak kosuub kaatitab Paulo , ak kong’utut inendet , 
koarogendos kosiir agobo ng’olyot ne kiga komwa , kole matun kogeerei togennyi kogeny . Ak kiiyomis inendet kowendi kolanyei melit .
Ak ye kingo kagebesie ak icheget , ak ketau kebe eng’ melit , kilitit banda , kitorjige Kos , ak betut ne kiisubi noto keit Rodo , ak kebe eng’ oloto agoi keit Patara : 
ak ye kingenyoru melit ne landoi kowendi Poinike , kelany , ak kebe . 
Ak ye kiga kegeer Kupro , kesiirtoe komi eut ne bo katam , kebe agoi Suria , ak kechoruge eng’ melit eng’ Turo : amu yoto ye kinemune tugukab melit . 
Ak ye kiga kenyoru alamalyet , ketebi eng’ oloto betusiek tisab : ak kimwachi ichek Paulo eng’ Tamirmiriet kolenji , amat kotiech Jerusalem . 
Ak kingo kagigesu betusiechoto , kebe bandanyo ; ak kiiyomisech ichek tugul koboto osotik ak lagok , agoi kemande eng’ nganaset : ak kegutung’se eng’ ngegut , kesa ,
ak kigochige saisere ; kelany anyun melit koweek ichek koba ga .
Ak ye kiga kigesu banda ne bo melit kebunu Turo , keit Ptolemai ; ak kigat tupchosiek , ak ketebi koboto ichek betut agenge . 
Ak eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ kebe , agoi keit Kaisaria : ak kebe gotab Pilipu amdoindet ne bo logoiywek che miach , inendet ko agenge eng’ bik tisab , ak kigitebi ak inendet . 
Kitinyei chichito tibik ang’wan , bergeinik , che kimaoteni . 
Ak ye kita ketebye eng’ betusiek che chang’ eng’ oloto , konyo kochorgei maotiot age ne bunu Judea ne kigiguure Agabo . 
Ak kingo kagoit ole kimi , konam birenetab Paulo , ak korate kelyekyik ak eunekyik , ak kole , Mwaei Tamirmiriet ne Tilil ko u ni kole , Ratei ko u nito Yahudik che mi Jerusalem chitab kobo birenoni , ak tun indoi inendet eunekab Bororiosiek .
Ak kingegas ng’alechuto , kigaigai inendet , achek ak bikab oloto , si matogosta Jerusalem . 
Kowol Paulo kole , Oyae nee , orirtosi ak obare muguleldanyu ? Amu a chobot , ma kerata kityo , ago ame eng’ Jerusalem agobo kainetab Kiptaiyat Jesu . 
Ak ye kimata kocham ko u noto , kesisye , kemwa kele , Ingoyaak magetab Kiptaiyat .
Ak kingobata betusiechoto kenam tugukyok ketogoste Jerusalem . 
Ak kigibe koboto alamalyet che kibunu Kaisaria , komutu Mnason ne bo Kupro , ne agenge ne bo alamalyet ne bo keny , ne kigibendi ketebe gonnyi .
Ak kingeit Jerusalem , kotaachech tupchosiek eng’ boiboiyet . 
Ak betut ne kiisubi betunoto kebe achek ak Paulo gab Jakobo ; ak kimi boisiek tugul . 
Ak kingo kagogat ichek , kotetyi tuguk tugul agenge agenge che kiga koyai Jehovah eng’ boisiennyi eng’ Bororiosiek . 
Ak kingogas ichek ng’olyondonoto , kogonyit Jehovah ; ak kolenji ichek inendet , Igeere anyun , ne kitupche , ole te elfusiek ng’isiat eng’ kwenutab Yahudik che kigoyan ; ak tinyei tugul kagiiletab ge agobo Ng’atutiet : 
ak kigiborji ichek agobo inye , kele , ineti Yahudik tugul che mi oldab Bororiosiek kobagakta Musa , ilenjini amat komuratan lagokwak , anan kosub bitonwek . 
Nee anyun nguno ? Magogas ichek iman kole kaiitu . 
Yai anyun ni kimwaun : Kitinye bik ang’wan che kigoarorta kiy eng’ kayosiet ; 
imut anyun bichu , ak ianyinyge koboto ichek , ak igamanji feda , si kobiit kicherji metowekwak : si konai tugul kole mami imanit eng’ tuguchoto kigiborji agobo inye ; ago inye iwendoti komie , iribe Ng’atutiet . 
Ago eng’ Bororiosiek che kigoyan , ko kigesir ketil kiruoget kele , kotabanegei tuguk che kieng’jin kanamonik , ak korotik , ak banyek che bo che kagiget , ak sokset . 
Komut anyun Paulo murenjoto , ak eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ koanyinygei koboto icheget ak kwo hekalut orit , kobortoi kasuldaetab betusiek che bo kaanyinyet , agoi kigoito kagochinet ne bo age tugul eng’ ichek .
Ak ye kimachei kogesgei betusiek tisabu , kowas tuiyet Yahudik che kibunu Asia , ye kingogeer inendet komi hekalut , ak konam inendet , 
koboldos , kolen , Okwek bikab Israel , otoretech ! Chichito ne ineti bik tugul eng’ komosta age tugul kowech bik , ak Ng’atutiet , ak yuto : ak koboto noto koimut Yunanik agichek kobwa hekalut , ak kagong’wanit yuto tilil . 
Amu kiga kogeer Tropimo Epesoindet komi koboto inendet eng’ nganaset , ne kilen kiimutu Paulo konyo hekalut .
Kowasgei anyun nganaset komugul , ak kiruai bik kibagenge : ak konam Paulo , ak kochuut komong’ eng’ hekalut : ak kigiger kurgotik eng’ sainato . 
Ak ye kicheng’ei kobar inendet , koityi ng’alek kiptaiyat ne o ne bo murenikab luget kole , mitei chemarget Jerusalem komugul . 
Komut ngunoto askarik ak kiptainikab bogolwogik , koruai kochortagei ole mi ichek : ak kingogeer ichek kiptaiyat ne o ak askarik , kobagakta biret ne kibirei Paulo . 
Konyo anyun kiptaiyat ne o korik , ak konam inendet , ak kong’at kole , kerat inendet eng’ sirimwek aeng’ ; ak koteebe kole , ng’o nito ? Ak kayai nee ? 
Ak kobolyo alak eng’ tuiyet komwaei kit age komwaei alage kit age : ak ye kima imuch konai komie kit ne bo bolatet , kong’at kole kimut inendet kwo irimet . 
Ak kingoit long’eiywot , koganab askarik inendet amu koromnatetab tuiyet ; 
amu kiisubi tuiyet ne bo bik , koboldos , kolen , Oiste inendet !
Ak ye kigimachei kimut Paulo kwo irimet , kolenji kiptaiyat ne o , Ichamwa amwaun ng’olyo ? Kolenji , Tos ingen kutitab Yunanik ? 
Tos ma i Misrindet ne kiing’eet lomset yaginye ak komut bik elfusiek ang’wan koba ong’atet , bik che kiguure Rumik ? 
Ago kile Paulo , A Yahudiot ne bo Tarso eng’ Kilikia , a bo nganaset ne ma nyerat : ak asomin ale , chamwa ang’alalji bik . 
Ak ye kingo kagochamji , kotonone Paulo long’eiywot , ak koborji bik eng’ eut kosisyo ; ak ye kingo kagosisyo inne , kong’alalji ichek eng’ kutitab Hebranik , kole ,
Che kitupche ak kwanisiekyok , ogas ng’alek che amwae nguno eng’ taing’wong’ che asorunege . 
Ak kingogas kole ng’alaljin ichek eng’ kutitab Hebranik , kosisyo mising’ : ak kile , 
A Yahudiot , kigisikya Tarso ne bo Kilikia , ago kianerji nganasani , ak kiineta Gamaliel , ak kigineta komie ko u ole teptoi Ng’atutietab kwanisiekyok , ak kiatinye kagiiletab ge eng’ Jehovah , ko u ole oteptoi okwek tugul rani : 
ak kiausausi Orani agoi meet , arate ak atoorjini korgoret murenik ak kobogorisiek . 
Ko u ye baorianjina tisiindet ne o , ak kapkiruoget tugul ne bo boisiek : che kianyorune baronok , che kiaibe koba oldab tupchosiek , ak kiawe Damasko , ale amut ichek che kimi oloto kobwa Jerusalem ko ratotin , si kobiit kebir .
Ak ye kiawendi , ko karikyi Damasko , ko katonon asis , koluu eng’ sainato lapkeiyet ne o ne kibunu kipsengwet koluucha komoswek tugul . 
Ak kiabutyi ng’ony , ak agas kutit kolenja , Saul , Saul , amu nee si iusa ? 
Ak kiawolu ale , I ng’o inye , Kiptaiyandani ? Ak kilenja , A Jesu ne bo Nasaret , ne iuse . 
Ak kigeer lapkeiyet iman che kimi kobota , ago kima kas kutitab inendet ne king’alalwa . 
Ale , Ayai nee anyun , Kiptaiyandani ? Kolenja Kiptaiyat , Ng’eet , ui Damasko ; si kemwaun eng’ oloto tuguk tugul che kigeng’at iyai . 
Ak ye kima kota amuchi ageer kiy amu liletab lapkeiyonoto , ait Damasko , konamota eut ichek che kimi kobota .
Ak kinyo ole ami , chito age ne keguure Anania , chito ne bo iman eng’ ribetab Ng’atutiet , ne kibaorianjin Yahudik tugul che kimenyei oloto kole mie . 
Ak ye kitononi eng’ ye negitena , kolenja , Ne kitupche Saul , keerte . Ak eng’ sainato ageer inendet . 
Ak kile , Kigolewenin Jehovah ne bo kwanisiekyok si kobiit inai magennyi , ak igeer Inendet ne bo Imanda , ak igas ng’olyot ne bunu kutinnyi . 
Amu iegu baoriandennyi eng’ bik tugul agobo tugul che koigeer ak che koigas . 
Ta igeni nee anyun nguno ? Ng’eet kibatisanin , ak kiundo tengekwogiguk iguure kainennyi .
Ak kingo kaaweektege Jerusalem , ak kingota asae eng’ hekalut , kobutya kit ne u ruon , 
ageer inendet kolenjina , Igirgir , chakte , mande eng’ Jerusalem : amu mataachei baornatet eng’ inye agobo ane . 
Ak kiale , Kiptaiyandani , ingen icheget kole kiarate ak abire eng’ sunagogit age tugul ichek che kiiyanin : 
ak ye kingetumdoi korotikab Stepano baoriandeng’ung’ , ko , kiatononi agane eng’ yoto , ak achame , ak aribe ngoroikab icheget che kibarei inendet . 
Ak kilenja inendet , Ui : amu ayoktoin iwe ole loo agoi oldab Bororiosiek .
Koepchi it anyun ichek inendet agoi ng’olyondonito ; yeityo komwa eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Oiste chito ne u nito kwo eng’ ng’ony : amu manyolu kosob . 
Ak ye kita koboldos , ak kowirtoi ngoroikwak , ak kowastoi temburiek koba barak , 
kong’at kiptaiyat ne o kole kimut inendet kwo irimet , kong’at kole , Ogine eng’ biret ne bo kipcharitisiek , si konai inendet kit ne kabolji ichek ko u noto agobo inendet . 
Ak ye kingo kagorate inendet anok , kolenji Paulo kiptaiyatab bogol ne kitononi eng’ yoto , Tos chamdoi ng’atutik eng’ okwek obir chi ne Romanindet , ama kiruokyi ? 
Ak kingogas kiptaiyandanato bo bogol noto , kwo ole mi kiptaiyat ne o , ak komwachi inendet kolenji , Imache iyai nee nguno ? Amu Romanindet chichi . 
Konyo anyun kiptaiyat ne o , ak kolenji inendet , Mwawa , tos i Romanin ? Ak kile , Ee . 
Kowol kiptaiyat ne o kole , Kiaegu chitab bororioni eng’ alyet ne o . Ak kile Paulo , Kigisikya bororionito . 
Koba anyun eng’ sainato ichek che kimachei kogine inendet : ak kiiywei agine kiptaiyat ne o , ye kingonai kole kaga Romanindet inendet , ak amu kiga korat inendet .
Ago ye kimachei konai komie eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ , kit ne koitaame Yahudik , kotiach inendet , ak kong’at tisiik che eechen ak kapkiruoget tugul kotuiyo , ak komut Paulo kochorgei , ak konde inendet tainywa .
Ak kingogeer Paulo kapkiruogonoto komie , komwa kole , Che kitupche , kiatebe kotugul kabwatet ne mie eng’ taitab Jehovah agoi rani . 
Kong’at Anania , tisiindet ne o , ichek che kitonondos eng’ yoto kole , korabach kutinnyi . 
Kolenji anyun Paulo inendet , Tun birin Jehovah , inye inatut ne kigisal koleelit : itebye ak iruokwa ko u ye mwaei Ng’atutiet , ak ing’ate kebira ama chamdoi Ng’atutiet ? 
Komwa ichek che kitonondos eng’ yoto kole , Ichube tisiindet ne o ne bo Jehovah ? 
Kole anyun Paulo , Kama anai , che kitupche , ale inendet ko tisiindet ne o : amu kigisir kele , Amemwa ne ya agobo bounindetab biguk .
Ago ye kingonai Paulo kole , Sadukaik alage , ko Parisaik alage , komwa eng’ kutit ne o eng’ kapkiruok kole , Che kitupche , a Parisaindet , weritab Parisaik : kagiruokwa agobo kamang’unet ak ng’eetyet ne bo che kigobek . 
Ak kingo kagomwa ko u noto , kong’eet anyun toiyet eng’ Parisaik ak Sadukaik : ak kipcheak tuiyet . 
Amu mwaei Sadukaik kole , mami ng’eetyet eng’ che kibek , anan malaika , anan tamirmiriet : ago iyani tugul Parisaik . 
Kong’eet anyun bolatet ne o : ak kitononso sirik alak che bo Parisaik , ak koborio kolen , Ma kinyoru yaitio eng’ chichi : ak tos nee eng’ okwek ngot ko kang’alal ak inendet tamirmiriet, anan malaika ?
Ak ye kingong’eet toiyet ne o , koiywei kiptaiyat ne o kole , abere togot kotonaton bichu Paulo , kong’at anyun askarik kochortagei ak komut inendet eng’ kimnatet eng’ kwenunywa , ak komut konyo irimet .
Ak eng’ kemout ne kiisubi noto kotonon Kiptaiyat eng’ ye negite inendet ak kolenji , Nyiganitu : amu ko u ye kiibaorianja eng’ Jerusalem , ko u noto kanyol ibaorian eng’ Rom agine .
Ak kingoeech koyumgei Yahudik , ak korategei kayosiet , kole magiame kiy ama kiee agoi kebar Paulo . 
Ak kisiirei artam icheget che kiyosio . 
Ak kibwa ole mi tisiik che eechen ak boisiek , ak kolenji , Kageratge eng’ kayosiet ne o kele , magichamjami kiy agoi kebar Paulo . 
Oborji anyun okwek ak boisiek kiptaiyat ne o komut inendet kochorgei konyo ole omi , ko u ne omache ogin komie ng’alekyik : ak ki chobotin achek kebar inendet agot kotom korikyech .
Ago kigas weritab chepkametab Paulo agobo setyinenywa , ak kinyo kwo irimet ak komwachi Paulo . 
Koguur anyun Paulo age eng’ kiptainikab bogolwogik , ak kolenji , Imut murenoni kwo ole mi kiptaiyat ne o : amu tinye ng’olyo ne machei komwachi inendet . 
Komut anyun inendet kwo ole mi kiptaiyat ne o , ak kolenji , Kaguura Paulo , kimonjororiot , awa ole mi inendet , ak komwawa amutun murenoni konyo ole imi , tinyei ng’olyo ne machei komwaun . 
Konam anyun kiptaiyat ne o eutab weroto , ak komut taban , ak koteebe eng’ ung’ot kole , Nee noto imache imwawa ? 
Kole , Kagochamnyechi Yahudik kole , kosomin imutu Paulo kochorgei mutai konyo kapkiruok , ko u ne imache iteepse inendet komie . 
Ameyanji anyun : amu mitei eng’ ichek che siirei artam che setyin inendet , che kagoratgei eng’ kayosiet , kole maamei kiy anan koee agoi kobar inendet : ak chobotin ichek nguno kogeni ng’atutiet ne bunun . 
Kounda anyun kiptaiyat ne o murenonoto kwo , ak kong’at inendet kolenji , Amemwachi chi agot agenge ilenji , Kaimwa tuguchu .
Ak kiguur kiptainik aeng’ che bo bogolwogik koba ole mi inendet , ak kolenji , Ochob askarik bogol aeng’ koba agoi Kaisaria , ak askarik tamanwogik tisab che lanyei mbartanyisiek , ak murenikab ng’otwek bogol aeng’ , eng’ sait somok ne bo kemoi : 
ak kimwachi kochob mbartanyisiek , si kobiit komute ichek Paulo , ak komut kot koit ole mi Peliki bounindet kochamegei . 
Ak kisir baruet ko u ni :
Ane Klaudio Lusia , agatin inye bounindet Peliki , ne i toogunot .
Konam Yahudik chichi , ak ki negit kobar ichek inendet , awe anyun ak askarik ole mi ichek , ak asoru inendet , ko kaanai ale kaga Romanin inendet . 
Ak ye kiamache anai kit ne kiitaame ichek inendet , amutu anyun kochorgei kapkiruogenywa : 
ageer ale , kigitaam inendet agobo ng’alekab ng’atutikwak , ago mami ng’olyo ne kigiityi inendet ne nyoljin meet anan ratutik . 
Ak ye kongiborua kele kogechob ng’alek eng’ ung’ot agobo inendet , ayogu inendet konyo olong’ung’ achogune , ak ang’at che kataamikyik si komwa ng’alek eng’ taing’ung’ , che itaame inendet .
Komut anyun askarik Paulo , ko u ye kaga king’at , ak komut kemoi kwo Antipatris . 
Ago mutai kobagakta murenik che kilanyei mbartanyisiek koba koboto inendet , ak koweektagei koba irimet : 
ak kingo kagoit Kaisaria , ak kogochi bounindet baruet , konde Paulo agine tainnyi . 
Ak ye kiga kosoman baruet , koteebe ichek kolenji , Ano emetab chichi ? Ak kingogas kele , bo inendet Kilikia , 
kole , Tun agasun ng’aleguk ko kait bik che kiitaamin : ak king’at kerib inendet eng’ gotab kiruoget ne bo Herod .
Ak kingobata betusiek mutu , kochorgei Anania tisiindet ne o ak boisiek alak , ak ng’alalindet age , ne kiguure Tertulo ; ak koborji bounindet ng’alek che kogitaame Paulo . 
Ak kingo kageguur , kotoi Tertulo kotaam inendet kole , Amu kiboiboitune kalyet ne o eng’ inye , ak kiistoi yaitwogik eng’ bororioni amu ng’omnateng’ung’ , 
kitaach anyun eng’ ortinwek tugul ak eng’ komoswek tugul , koboto kongoi tugul , ee inye ne i toogunot , Peliki . 
Ago si mata again mising’ , asomin ale igasech eng’ ng’alek che ng’ering’ eng’ mieindang’ung’ , 
amu kigegeer chichi kele inendet ko chi ne itoitos bich , ne ing’eeti chemereret eng’ Yahudik tugul eng’ ng’ony tugul , ak kandoindet ne bo kasubikab Nasaretik : 
ak kogeny , ko kigotiem kong’wanit hekalut : ak kiginam inendet : 
imuchi inai tuguchu tugul eng’ inendet ye igine inyendet , agobo tuguchoto kogitaame . 
Ak kiiyomechigei Yahudik kataamsonato , kogimit kole , u noto ng’alechuto .
Ak kingo kagoborjine bounindet Paulo eut , kole kong’alal , kowol Paulo kole , Angen ale , i kiruogindet ne bo bororioni eng’ kenyisiek che chang’ , amu noto asoruge eng’ boiboindo : 
amu imuchi inai ile , tom kosiir betusiek taman ak aeng’ koboch ngab atogoste Jerusalem awe asa : 
ama nyorua ichek eng’ hekalut kibelige ak chi age tugul , anan awase tuiyet , anan eng’ sunagogisiek , anan eng’ nganaset . 
Amaimuchi ichek koborun komie tuguk che itaamena . 
Ago kang’ang’un nito , eng’ Oranato kuure ichek biteet age , aote Jehovah ne bo kwanisiekyok , ak ayani tuguk tugul ko u ye mwaei Ng’atutiet , ak che kigisir eng’ maotik : 
atinye kamang’unet eng’ Jehovah , ne cheng’ei bichu agichek , ale , tatun komi ng’eetyetab che bo imanda ak che ma bo imanda . 
Ak achobege anyun agane eng’ ng’olyondoni atebe kotugul kabwatet ne matinyei kanagut eng’ taitab Jehovah ak bik .
Ak kingobata kenyisiek che chang’ anyo aipchi bikab bororiennyu kagochinoik ak tuguk che kigoitoi : 
ak kinyortaa kitilila eng’ hekalut , ama mi tuiyet , anan bolatet : ago kimi Yahudik alak che kibunu Asia , 
mie nda kami yu ichek eng’ taing’ung’ si komwaitaa ngo ting’ena ichek ng’olyo . 
Anan ingomwa bichu icheget boisiet ne ya ne kinyor , ye kingatonon eng’ taitab kapkiruoget , 
kobate twegunet agenge ne kiarirji atononi eng’ kwenunywa , ale , Kagiruokwa rani eng’ taing’wong’ agobo ng’eetyetab che kigobek .
Amu kiingen Peliki komie agobo Oranato , kolenji , Ogen , ye tun kachorgei kiptaiyat ne o Lusia , atil anyun ng’alekwok . 
Ak kong’at kiptaiyatab bogol kole kerib inendet , ak kigochin boroindo ; amat koete age tugul eng’ choronokyik koboisiechi inendet .
Ago kingobata betusiek alage , koit Peliki , koboto Drusila osotiondennyi , ne ki Chebyahudio , ak koyokto Paulo konyo , ak kigas eng’ inendet agobo kayanet eng’ Kristo Jesu . 
Ak ye kita kong’alali agobo imanda , ak ribetab ge , ak kiruoget ne nyonei , koiyweis Peliki , ak kowol kole , Ui korok ; ak ye tun anyoru boroindo ne mie , aguurin . 
Kiimang’u kole togot kogochi Paulo siling’isiek : kiguur anyun inendet konyil che chang’ , ak kong’alal koboto inendet .
Ago kingogesgei kenyisiek aeng’u , konam Porkio Pesto boisietab Peliki ; ak amu kimachei Peliki kobaibai Yahudik , kobagakta Paulo ko ratat .
Kingo kagoit Pesto koronoto , kotogosta Jerusalem kobunei Kaisaria , ko kagobata betusiek somogu . 
Ak kimwachi tisiik che eechen ak bik che toogunotin che bo Yahudik ng’alek che kiting’e Paulo ; ak kogaigai ichek inendet , 
kosom chamdaet agobo inendet , kole koyokto inendet kimut konyo Jerusalem; si kobiit korat oret kobar inendet. 
Ago kiwol Pesto kole kerib Paulo eng’ Kaisaria , ak kole , Negit si awa anendet oloto . 
Ak kole inendet , Ongechortege ak che eechen eng’ okwek , si ngo mi ng’olyo age tugul ne ya eng’ chichito , komwa ichek .
Ak kingo kagotebi eng’ kwenunywa koboto ichek eng’ betusiek che masiirei sisiit anan ko taman , kochortagei Kaisaria ; ak mutai kotebe ng’echeretab kiruoget , ak kong’at kole , kimut Paulo . 
Ak kingo kagoit , koyiem inendet Yahudik che kabunu Jerusalem , koibu ng’alek che chang’ che koromen che kiitaame inendet , che kima imuch kobor komie kit ne inet ; 
ago kimwa Paulo eng’ ng’alek che kisorunegei, kole, Tom ayai tengek agot kitigin agobo Ng’atutietab Yahudik, anan agobo hekalut, anan agobo Kaisari . 
Ago ye kimachei Pesto kobaibai Yahudik , kowolji Paulo , kolenji , Tos imache itogoste Jerusalem , si kiruogun eng’ oloto agobo tuguchu eng’ tainnyu ? 
Ago kile Paulo , Atononi eng’ taitab ng’echeretab kiruoget ne bo Kaisari, ole kanyol kiruogunena: tom ayachi kiy ne ya Yahudik, ko u ye ingen inye aginye komie . 
Ngo a kiptengekyo , ak ngot ko koayai kiy ne nyoljin meet , ko maesioi ame : ago ngot ko ma bo iman tuguchoto , che itaamjina bichu , ko mami chi ne imuchi kondea eunekwak . Arirjini Kaisari .
