Ak kingo kagong’alal anyun Pesto ak bikab kapkiruok , kowol kole , Kairirji Kaisari : ara anyun , iwendi gab Kaisari .
Ak kingo kagosiirto betusiek alage , koit laitoriat Agripa ak Bernike Kaisaria , si kogat Pesto . 
Ak ye kita kobeniei betusiek che chang’ , koborji Pesto laitoriat ng’alekab Paulo , kolenji , Mitei chi age ne kibagakta Peliki ko ratat : 
ne kimwawa ng’alekyik tisiik che eechen ak boisiekab Yahudik ye kiami Jerusalem , kisomei ng’alek che kigikyine inendet . 
Ak kiawolji ichek alenji , ma biteetab Romanik kigoito chi kotomo kogeergei kimni chito ne kitaami ak che itaamsei , ak konyor boroindo ne sorunegei eng’ ng’alek che kigitaamjin . 
Ye kingoyumgei anyun eng’ yu , ko mata agage , ago eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ atebe ng’echeretab kiruoget , ak ang’at kimut chichoto . 
Ak kingotononso icheget che kiitaami inendet , ko ma koib ng’olyo ne ya ne bo kagikyino agobo inendet ko u ye kiabwati ; 
ago kiting’e inendet teebutik agobo kayanenywa , ak agobo chi ne kilen Jesu , ne kigome , ne igiiljingei Paulo kole , sobei . 
Ago kialen agin ole teptoi ng’alechu kotemena , ateebe ngo machei kwo Jerusalem , si kiruokyi eng’ olindo agobo ng’alechuto . 
Ago kingorirji Paulo kotebi kole si kotil kiruoget bounindet ne o , ang’at ale kerib agoi tun ayokte kwo gab Kaisari . 
Ak kilenji Agripa Pesto , amache agas agane ng’alekab chichito . Kolenji , Igase mutai .
Ak mutai ko kagoit Agripa , koboto Bernike , eng’ etunatet ne o , ak ko kagoba got ne kigase ng’alek , koboto kiptainik che eechen , ak bik che toogunotin che bo nganaset , kimut Paulo eng’ ng’atutietab Pesto . 
Komwa Pesto anyun, kole , Laitoriat Agripa , ak bik tugul che kimi yu tugul , ogeere chichi , kigorirja tuiyet tugul ne bo Yahudik agobo inendet , eng’ Jerusalem ak eng’ olito , koboldos , kolen , manyol kota kosob . 
Ago kiageer ale ma yai kiy ne nyoljin meet : ak ko u ye kirirji inendet bounindet ne o , acham anyun ayokto inendet . 
Matinye ng’olyo ne bo iman ne asirjini kiptaiyandennyu agobo inendet . Noto anyun kamutu inendet konyo taing’wong’ , ak ne siirei ko konyo taing’ung’ , inye , laitoriat Agripa , si ye kageteepse , asich ng’olyot ne asire . 
Amu ageere ale , ma nyolu kiyokto kimonjororio , ama kibor tuguk che kigitaamjin .
Kolenji anyun Agripa Paulo , Kagichamun iwolu ng’aleguk . Kochuul anyun Paulo eunnyi , ak komwa ng’alek che sorunegei , kole : 
Abwati ale abaibai , ee laitoriat Agripa , amu amuchi asorge rani eng’ taing’ung’ agobo tuguk tugul che koitaamja Yahudik : 
ne siirei ko amu ingen komie bitonwek tugul ak teebutik tugul che tinyei Yahudik : noto anyun , kasomin ale igasa eng’ muitaet .
Ingen Yahudik tugul ateptab sobennyu , koboch ko a ming’in , ne kiatinye koboch ko kabiitu eng’ bororiennyu , ak eng’ Jerusalem ; 
ak kongena ichek koboch eng’ tai , nda chamei ichek kobaorian , ko u ye kia Parisaindet ne isubi biteet ne korom ne bo kayanennyo . 
Ak katonon nguno eng’ yu si kiruokwa agobo kamang’unet ne bo arorutiet ne kichopchi Jehovah kwanisiekyok ; 
noto ne imang’u ortinwekyok tamanu ak aeng’ kole nyoru , koboisiechin Jehovah eng’ kagiiletab ge bet ak kemoi . Kagogikya Yahudik agobo kamang’unonito , ee , laitoriandani ! 
Amu nee si kibwat kele maiyanaksei eng’ okwek kele , ing’eeti Jehovah che kigobek ? 
Kiabwati anendet iman ale kanyol ayai tuguk che chang’ che kirindoi kainetab Jesu ne bo Nasaret . 
Ak kiayai nito agine eng’ Jerusalem : ak atoorji korgorosiek bik che chang’ eng’ che tililen , ko kagogona kimnatet tisiik che eechen , ak kiachame ye kigibarei ichek . 
Ak kiabirote konyil che chang’ eng’ sunagogisiek tugul , abirjini kochubis ; ak ye kiga konyita ichek mising’ , ausote agoi nganasok che bo toek .
Ak ye kingawendi Damasko atinye kimnatet ak kayoktoet ne bo tisiik che eechen , 
ageer lapkeiyet ne kibunu kipsengwet , ne siirei kaluunetab asista , koluucha komoswek tugul koboto che kigibendi tugul , eng’ oret bet kwen , ee , laitoriandani . 
Ak kingo kagibutyi ng’ony tugul , agas kutit ne lenjina eng’ kutitab Hebranik , Saul , Saul , amu ne si iusa ? Bichii eng’ inye itiar kiplitwet . 
Ak kiale , I ng’o inye , Kiptaiyandani ? Kole Kiptaiyat , A Jesu ne iuse . 
Ago ng’eet , tonon eng’ kelyeguk : kang’ang’unge amu ni , ale andein iegu kiboitiot ak baoriatab tuguchu kaigeer agobo ane , ak tuguk che tun ang’ang’unenege ; 
asorun eng’ bik , ak eng’ Bororiosiek , ole tun ayoktoin iwe , 
si kobiit ing’any konyekwak , ak koweek eng’ mesundeito kobwanji lapkeiyet , ak eng’ kimnatetab Setani kobwanji Jehovah , si konyor ichek nyoetab kaat ne bo tengekwogik ak borotet eng’ ichek che kigitilil amu kayanet ne mi eng’ ane .
Noto anyun , ee , laitoriandani Agripa , ma abistoe kaborunet ne bo kipsengwet : 
ago kiaborji che mi Damasko korok , ak eng’ Jerusalem , ak eng’ emet komugul ne bo Judea , ak eng’ Bororiosiek agichek , si kosik ak koyan Jehovah , koyaei boisionik che nyoljin sigunet . 
Kinama anyun Yahudik eng’ hekalut amu nito , ak kotiem kobara . 
Ye kinganyoru toretet ne bunu Jehovah , atonon agoi rani abaorianjini che mengech ak che eechen , amamwae kiy age kobate che kimwa maotik ak Musa , kole tun bwanei ; 
kole kanyol konyalil Kristo , ak kole komwaita korok eng’ ng’eetyetab che kibek , lapkeiyet , komwachi bik ak Bororiosiek .
Ak ye kita kosorugei ko u noto , komwa Pesto eng’ kutit ne o , kole , Paulo , i kibiywa ; kagogonin iywek kanetetab ge ne o . 
Ago kile Paulo , Ma a kibiywa , ee Pesto ne i toogunot : ago amwae ng’alek che bo iman ak che bo ng’omnatet . 
Amu ingen laitoriat ng’alechuto , inendet ne ang’alaljini eng’ nyiganatet : amu angen komie , ale ma ung’otin ng’alechu eng’ inendet , agot agenge ; amu mayaak ng’olyondonito eng’ taban . 
Laitoriat Agripa , tos iyani inye maotik ? Angen ale iyani . 
Ak kilenji Agripa Paulo , Ka negit igaigaa eng’ ng’alek che ng’ering’ aek Kristianindet . 
Kole Paulo , Achame ko u noto eng’ Jehovah , ale ngo eng’ che ng’ering’ anan eng’ che chang’ , ma inye kityo , ago tugul agichek che kasa rani , ale kotebi ko u ane , ago ama eng’ ratutichu .
Kong’eet anyun laitoriat , ak bounindet ak Bernike , koboto ichek che kimi tugul : 
ak kingo kagoba , kong’alaljigei ichegei , kole , Ma yai chichi kiy ne nyoljin meet anan ratisiosiek . 
Kolenji anyun Agripa Pesto , Kota kitiachi chichi , nda kima rirji Kaisari .
Ak kingo katetil ng’alek kele kebun melit kebe Italia , kigigochi Julio kiptaiyatab bogol , ne bo lugetab Augusto , Paulo ak kimonjororinik alak . 
Kelany anyun melit ne bo Adramutio , ne kimachei kwo komoswek alak che mi ngegutab Asia , ak kebe nyanjet ak Aristarko Makedonianindet ne bo Tesalonike . 
Ak eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ keit Sidon : ak kirire Julio Paulo , ak kochamji kwo ole mi choronokyik si konyor toretet . 
Ak kigibun melit eng’ oloto ak kigitektaege Kupro , amu kigirindaech usonet . 
Ak ye kiga kebun melit kelande eng’ nyanjet ne bo Kilikia ak Pampulia , keit Mura , nganaset ne bo Lukia . 
Ak kinyorji oloto kiptaiyatab bogol melit ne bo Aleksandria , ne wendi Italia ; kondeech melit anyun .
Ak ye kiga kebe mutyo eng’ melit eng’ betusiek che chang’ , agoi keit Kanido eng’ bichiindo , koranyech usonet , kebe ketektaege Krete , ne itorjingei Salmone ; 
ak kigibun ngegut eng’ bichiindo agoi keit komosta age ne kiguure Luukwek che Miach ; ole negite nganasetab Lasea .
Ak kingo kagosiirto betusiek che chang’ , ak kobichiit bandab nyanjet , amu kiga kosiirto betusiekab Karugutetab ge , koteechi Paulo ichek , 
kolenji , Murenju , kaageer ale mitei ng’oiyondit ak luset eng’ banito bo nyanjet , ma ne bo melit kityo ak tuguk che mi orit , ago ne bo sobonwekyok agichek . 
Ago kigas kiptaiyatab bogol ng’alekab bounindet ak chitab kobo melit , kosiir ng’alek che kamwaei Paulo . 
Ak amu kima ko luita ne yamei ketebe eng’ betusiekab kaititiet , komwa che chang’ kole , Mie kota kinaakte eng’ olito , tamangab keit Poinike , si ketebe oloto eng’ betusiekab kaititiet ; noto ko ki luitab Krete , ne kitokyingei murot ne bo katam kitigin ak murot ne bo tai kitigin .
Ak ye kingous mutyo usonet ne bunu komostab tai , kolen ichek kagonyor kit ne kamachei , konem nanget ak kobun tabandab Krete , ye negit ngegut . 
Ak ne matenit kous chebwiwichet , ne kiguure Eurakulo : 
ak ye kingenam melit , ak mata komuch kotab usonet , keistochige , ak koonech . 
Ak kingeruai ketektaatege emet ne kiikwen beek ne kiguure Kauda , kimuch eng’ bichiindo keganab moinget ne ming’in : 
ak kingo kagotogosune moingonoto , koboisie tuguk che kitorete , koratune melit orit ; ak kingoiywei ichek kole si magiwirji Surti , kochoor angok , ak kion usonet koba . 
Ak ye kita keboisiei mising’ eng’ kagiiletab ge , ketabe usonoto o , ketau eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ kewirte tuguk che mi melit , 
ak eng’ betutab somok kowirta icheget eng’ eunekwak tuguk che kiboisie eng’ melit . 
Ak ye kimata koluuchech asista anan kecheik eng’ betusiek che chang’ , ak kogiichech usonet ne o , kogesgei anyun kamang’unet ne kigilen, tos kisoruech .
Ak ye kiga kotar betusiek che chang’ ama amis , kotonon Paulo eng’ kwenunywa , ak kole , Murenju , kita mie nda kigogasa , ak kita mie nda kima obwa eng’ Krete , ak onyoru nyalili ak lusoni . 
Amwawok nguno ale onyiganitu : amu mami chi ne meei eng’ okwek , kobate melit . 
Amu kotonon malaikaiyatab Jehovah eng’ ye negitena kemouni , ne a nenyi , ak ne aote , 
kole , Ameiyweisie , Paulo ; kanyol itonon eng’ taitab Kaisari : ak keero , kagogonin Jehovah tugul che obendi tugul eng’ melit . 
Ara anyun , murenju , onyiganitu : amu ayani Jehovah , ale yaaksei ko u ye kogomwawa . 
Ago kanyol kewirjech emet ne kiikwen beek .
Ago ye kingoit kemoutab taman ak ang’wan , ye kita kowirjinech usonet komosi ak komosi eng’ nyanjet ne kiguure Adria , ko kiibwati bikab melit olo bo kemoi kwen kolen kagorikta emet age ; 
ak kiirooch beek kit ne kikwaise , ak konyor kakwautik artam ; ak kita koba kitigin korooch beek kogeny kioto , konyor kakwautik sosom . 
Ak kingoiywei ichek kole abere togot kewirjech bitet ne mi ruandosiek , kounda nangaisiek ang’wan eng’ melit olo bo let , kosom kole nda kaech . 
Ak ye kimachei bikab melit komwaei kobagakta melit , ko kagochoorta moinget kwo nyanjet , kolen si kobwat bik kole wirtoi ichek nangaisiek eng’ olo bo melit tai , 
kolenji Paulo kiptaiyatab bogol ak askarik , Ngot ko matebi bichu eng’ melit , ko momuchi osopche . 
Kotil anyun askarik rogoosiek che bo moinget , ak kobagakta kobut . 
Ak ye kimachei koeech , kogaigai Paulo ichek tugul koamis , kolenjin , Rani ko betutab taman ak ang’wan ogeni ak ko ta orugutige , ak tom oam kiy . 
Noto anyun asomok ale oamisie : amu nito sobeng’wong’ ; amu mabetei sumeiyot agot agenge eng’ metitab chi age tugul eng’ okwek . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa ko u noto , ak konam makatiat , kogochi Jehovah kongoi eng’ taitab tugul : ak kiton , ak kotoi koamis . 
Konyiganitu anyun ichek tugul , ak koamis . 
Ak achek tugul ko kigiite bik bogol aeng’ ak tamanwogik tisab ak lo eng’ melit . 
Ak kingo kagobiyong’so , kowirji nyanjet nganok si kowisisit melit .
Ak kingo kagoeech , ko ma konai emonoto : kigeer luita age ne tinyei ng’aniek , ne kiibwati kole , ngomugak kokweri melit kwo oloto . 
Kotiach anyun nangaisiek , ak kobagakta eng’ nyanjet , ak kotiach rogoosiek che kigirate baoinik che kindochine melit ; ak ye kingo kagonamji barak anget ne mi olin bo tai kotokyi usonet , koba ngegut . 
Ago kingoit ye tuiyechin nyanjosiek aeng’u , kochunda ichek melit korieb ng’aniek ; ak kinamak melit ole bo tai kot ko ma kotwau , ago kitoi melit kong’asur eng’ ole bo let eng’ kimnatetab mildaetab ge ne bo beek .
Ak ng’olyot ne kitinyei askarik ko kobar kimonjororinik , kole si mabir beek alage eng’ ichek , kochililyo . 
Ago amu kimachei kiptaiyatab bogol kosor Paulo , koeete ichek si mayai kit ne kamachei ; ak kong’at ichek che kiimuchi kobirot beek kole, kowirjigei nyanjet , si kosib koit ngegut : 
ak kibun alage baoinik , kobun alage tuguk alak che bo melit . Kolong’ji anyun tugul emet kochamegei .
Ak ye kingo kagesopche , kenai anyun kele kigiguure emonoto kiikwen beek Melita . 
Ak kiyaiywech ne mie mising’ bikab emonoto : amu kiilaal mat , ak kotaachech achek tugul , amu kimi ropta ak kaititiet . 
Ago ye kingo kagoyum Paulo ratutiet ne bo kwenik , ak konde ma , komong’ anyun erenet amu mat , ak kotaachigei eunnyi . 
Ak kingogeer bikab emonoto erenet kosonginini eng’ eut , kolenjigei , Rumin chichi iman , agot nga kagosorgei eng’ nyanjet , ko machamjin inendet Imanda kosob . 
Ago kilelekta tionyoto kwo ma , ama am kiy Paulo . 
Ago kilen ichek abere tos ibwa , anan kobut ak kome ngunoto : ak ye kiga kogenis keny , ama kogeer kiy ne ya konyonji inendet , kowal kabwatutikwak , ak komwa kole , Inendet ko cheptalelit .
Kimi anyun eng’ ole negite yoto , korotinwekab chito ne o ne bo emonoto kiikwen beek , ne kigiguure Publio ; ne kitaachech eng’ chamnyet , ak koyaech keegu toekyik eng’ betusiek somok . 
Ak kimiani kwandab Publio koamei eset ak miandab moet ne bendi korotik : ak kiwa Paulo gotab chichoto , ak kosa , ak kogonoor eunekyik inendet ak kosoob . 
Ak kingo kagoyaak nito kobwa agichek che kimiandos eng’ kakwembeiyondonoto , ak kigisoob : 
ak kigonyitech eng’ teegisto ne o ; ak ye kingebe eng’ melit , kondewech melit tuguk che te che kigimakyinige .
Ak kingobata arawek somogu ketau banda eng’ melit ne bo Aleksandria , ne kiga tebe kakwembeiyondonoto eng’ betusiekab kaititiet , ne kaborunennyi ko ki Saramek che Muren . 
Ak kingeit Surakusa , ketebe yoto betusiek somok . 
Ak keng’eetye eng’ oloto kebe keyiematege , kot keit Regio : ak kingobata betut agenge kous usonetab murot ne bo tai , ak eng’ betut ne bo aeng’ keit Puteoli : 
ole kiginyorji tupchosiek , ak kiigaigaech ketebi ak icheget betusiek tisab : keit anyun Rom . 
Ak kingogas tupchosiek agobo achek eng’ oloto , kobwa kotorokwech kot koit Siret ne bo Apio , ak Gorik Somok che bo Toek : che kingogeer Paulo , komwachi Jehovah kongoi , ak konyiganit .
Ak kingeit Rom , kechamji Paulo kotebi inegei koboto askarindet ne kiribei inendet .
Ak kingo kagosiirto betusiek somogu koguur bik che eechen che bo Yahudik kotuiyo : ak kingo kagoyumgei , kolenji ichek , Che kitupche , agot ngo mayai ane kiy ne ya eng’ bik , anan eng’ bitonwekab kwanisiekyok , ko kigindea eunekab Romanik eng’ Jerusalem , ko a kimonjororio : 
ak kimachei kotiacha ichek , ko kagogin ng’alekyuk , amu kima komi kiy eng’ ane ne nyoljin meet . 
Ago ye kingogirinda Yahudik ng’olyondonoto , ageer ale kanyol arirji Kaisari ; ma kele kiatinye kiy ne ang’andoe bororiennyu . 
Amu nito anyun kasomok obwa kegeerge ak keng’alal tugul : amu a ratat eng’ sirimi agobo kamang’unetab Israel .
Ak kilenji inendet , Tomo kenyoru baronok che bunu Judea agobo inye , anan konyo oli age eng’ tupchosiek ak koboruech anan komwa kiy ne ya agobo inye . 
Ago kimache kegasenen kiy ne ibwati : amu kigonaak eng’ achek kele kimwaoti ne ya agobo bitonito eng’ komosta age tugul .
Ak ye kingo kagochob betut , kobwanji inendet che chang’ eng’ got ne kimenyei ; ak kiiborsechi komie , kobaoriani agobo bounatetab Jehovah , ak kogiiljingei koneti ichek agobo Jesu , eng’ Ng’atutiet ne bo Musa , ak eng’ maotik , koboch karon agoi koimen . 
Ak kiiyan alak tuguk che kigimwaei , ko ma iyan alak . 
Ak ye kimata kogasyin ichegei , koba , ko kagomwa Paulo ng’olyot agenge , kole , Kimwachi komie Tamirmiriet ne Tilil kwanisiekwok eng’ maotiot Isaia , kole ,
Ui oldab bichu , ak imwa ile , Eng’ kaset ogase , ago moguitosi agot kitigin ; Ak eng’ keeret ogeere , ago mobestosi agot kitigin :
Amu kwolilenotin mugulelwekab bichu , Ak magastoi komie itikwak , Ak kiger icheget konyekwak ; Si mageer eng’ konyekwak , Anan kogas eng’ itikwak , Anan koguiyo eng’ mugulelwekwak , Si koweek kogeny , Ak asoob ichek .
Ingonaak anyun eng’ okwek , ole , kiyokyin yetunoni bo Jehovah Bororiosiek : kasei agichek . 
Ak ye kingo kagomwa ng’alechu , koba Yahudik , koteebategei ichegei mising’ .
Ak kimeny eng’ kenyisiek aeng’ gonnyi ne kialei meng’et , ak kitaach tugul che kibwanjin inendet , 
koamdoi agobo bounatetab Jehovah , ak koneti tuguk agobo Kiptaiyat Jesu Kristo eng’ nyiganatet tugul , ama ete chi .
